### [1] [Global Dynamical Structure of Einstein$-$Scalar Cosmological Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04994)
*Prasanta Sahoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This work presents a global dynamical analysis of spatially flat FLRW cosmologies with a canonical scalar field, showing that the scalar field potential's steepness remains bounded at late times, leading to the existence of a compact global attractor. The asymptotic dynamics is governed by at most two effective degrees of freedom and exhibits structural stability and normal hyperbolicity, classified topologically via the Conley index.

本文对空间平坦的FLRW宇宙学中由正则标量场驱动的动力学进行了全局分析，证明了标量势的陡峭性在演化过程中始终保持有界，从而存在一个紧致的全局吸引子。晚期动力学至多由两个有效自由度支配，并通过Conley指标进行拓扑分类，揭示了系统的结构稳定性与常态双曲性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the late-time behavior of scalar field cosmologies is crucial for predicting cosmic evolution in models involving dark energy or inflation. Previous analyses often rely on specific potential forms; this paper aims to establish model-independent, global dynamical results under general assumptions on the potential's regularity and asymptotic structure.

理解标量场宇宙学的晚期行为对于预测暗能量或暴胀模型中的宇宙演化至关重要。以往研究通常依赖于特定形式的势能函数；本文旨在对标量势的正则性和渐近结构施加一般性假设，建立与具体模型无关的全局动力学结论。

Method: The authors employ techniques from finite-dimensional dissipative dynamical systems and invariant manifold theory. They formulate the Einstein$-$scalar field equations as a dynamical system on a suitable phase space, prove forward boundedness of trajectories using Lyapunov-type arguments, establish the existence of a compact absorbing set, and apply the theory of global attractors. Normal hyperbolicity and structural stability are analyzed using linearization and perturbation methods, while the Conley index is used for topological classification of asymptotic states.

作者采用有限维耗散动力系统与不变流形理论的方法，将Einstein$-$标量场方程表述为适当相空间上的动力系统，利用类Lyapunov方法证明轨迹的前向有界性，建立紧致吸收集的存在性，并应用全局吸引子理论。通过线性化与微扰方法分析常态双曲性与结构稳定性，使用Conley指标对渐近态进行拓扑分类。

Result: It is rigorously proven that the steepness $|V'(\phi)/V(\phi)|$ of the scalar potential $V(\phi)$ remains bounded along all forward-in-time trajectories, ensuring boundedness of the scalar sector. A compact global attractor exists, governing late-time dynamics. The flow asymptotically converges to a scalar-field-dominated invariant manifold, reducing effective dynamics to at most two dimensions (one dimension for asymptotically exponential potentials). This asymptotic structure is normally hyperbolic and structurally stable under smooth potential perturbations. Topological universality classes are identified via the Conley index, corresponding to one- and two-dimensional invariant sets.

严格证明了标量势$V(\phi)$的陡峭性$|V'(\phi)/V(\phi)|$在所有向前时间轨迹上保持有界，确保标量场部分的有界性。存在一个紧致的全局吸引子，支配晚期动力学。宇宙演化渐近趋向于一个标量场主导的不变流形，使有效动力学维度降至最多二维（对于渐近指数型势则降为一维）。该渐近结构具有常态双曲性，并在光滑势微扰下保持结构稳定性。通过Conley指标识别出对应于一维和二维不变集的拓扑普适类。

Conclusion: The late-time dynamics of spatially flat FLRW scalar field cosmologies is universally governed by a compact global attractor exhibiting dimensional reduction and structural stability. This provides a model-independent mechanism for asymptotic trapping in Einstein$-$scalar systems, with broad implications for dark energy and early universe scenarios.

空间平坦FLRW标量场宇宙学的晚期动力学普遍由一个展现维度约化与结构稳定性的紧致全局吸引子所支配。这为Einstein$-$标量系统中的渐近捕获提供了与模型无关的动力学机制，在暗能量与早期宇宙情景中具有广泛意义。

Abstract: In this work, a global dynamical analysis of spatially flat FLRW cosmologies driven by a canonical scalar field minimally coupled to gravity is presented. Under suitable regularity and asymptotic assumptions on the scalar field potential, it is shown that the Einstein$-$scalar evolution admits no forward trajectory along which the potential steepness becomes asymptotically unbounded. This establishes forward boundedness of the scalar sector and yields the existence of a compact absorbing set for the induced cosmological flow. Using techniques from invariant manifold theory and dissipative dynamical systems, the evolution is shown to admit a compact global attractor governing the late time dynamics of all physically admissible solutions. The asymptotic behavior is further characterized by convergence toward a scalar field dominated invariant manifold, leading to a reduction in effective dynamical dimensionality. In particular, the late time dynamics is governed by at most two independent degrees of freedom, with further reduction to one dimension for asymptotically exponential potentials. The resulting asymptotic structure is shown to be normally hyperbolic and structurally stable under smooth perturbations of the scalar field potential. A topological classification of the asymptotic dynamics is obtained using the Conley index, identifying universality classes corresponding to one and two dimensional invariant sets. These results provide a global characterization of late time scalar field cosmologies and establish a model independent dynamical mechanism for asymptotic trapping in Einstein$-$scalar systems.

</details>


### [2] [Revisiting The Gravitational Mirroring In Presence of Compact Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05009)
*Bikramarka S Choudhury,Aritra Sanyal,Md Khalid Hossain,Farook Rahaman*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We propose a new phenomenon called astrophysical mirroring in the Schwarzschild spacetime, where extremely compact objects create mirror-like images of light sources via extreme gravitational lensing; this effect arises from strong spacetime curvature near the object and can be analyzed through ray tracing.

我们提出了一种在史瓦西时空中的新现象，称为天体物理镜像效应：致密天体会通过极强的引力透镜作用产生光源的镜像；该效应源于物体附近强烈的时空曲率，并可通过光线追踪分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study is motivated by the need to better understand strong-field gravitational lensing effects near compact objects such as black holes and neutron stars, and to identify novel observable phenomena that arise from extreme spacetime curvature beyond standard weak-field approximations.

本研究的动机是更好地理解黑洞和中子星等致密天体附近的强场引力透镜效应，并识别出超越标准弱场近似的极端时空曲率下可能出现的新可观测现象。

Method: We employ the Schwarzschild metric to model spacetime around a spherically symmetric massive object. Null geodesics are solved analytically and numerically to trace light paths in strong gravitational fields. We analyze deflection angles $\Delta \phi$ approaching and exceeding $2\pi$, identifying conditions under which light rays loop around the object and reach distant observers from opposite directions, forming mirror images. Ray-tracing simulations are performed to visualize these effects.

我们采用史瓦西度规对球对称大质量天体周围的时空进行建模。通过解析和数值求解零测地线以追踪强引力场中的光路。我们分析了偏转角$\Delta \phi$接近甚至超过$2\pi$的情况，确定了光线绕天体循环并从相反方向到达远处观测者的条件，从而形成镜像。并通过光线追踪模拟可视化这些效应。

Result: We find that when the impact parameter $b$ approaches the critical value $b_c = 3\sqrt{3} r_s / 2$ (where $r_s$ is the Schwarzschild radius), light rays undergo multiple loops around the object, leading to highly magnified and delayed 'mirror' images located on the opposite side of the sky relative to the source. These mirroring events are most prominent for ultra-compact objects with radii close to or smaller than the photon sphere radius $r = 3GM/c^2$. The time delay between direct and mirrored images can be significant, scaling logarithmically with proximity to $b_c$.

我们发现，当撞击参数$b$接近临界值$b_c = 3\sqrt{3} r_s / 2$（其中$r_s$为史瓦西半径）时，光线会在天体周围多次环绕，导致在天空中相对于光源相反方向出现高度放大且延迟的“镜像”。这些镜像效应在半径接近或小于光子 sphere 半径$r = 3GM/c^2$的超紧凑天体中最显著。直接图像与镜像之间的时间延迟可能很大，并随接近$b_c$呈对数增长。

Conclusion: Astrophysical mirroring is a theoretically predicted phenomenon within general relativity that extends classical gravitational lensing into the ultra-strong field regime. It provides a new observational signature for probing the spacetime geometry near event horizons and could be detectable with future high-resolution very-long-baseline interferometry (VLBI) observations, particularly around supermassive black holes like M87* and Sgr A*.

天体物理镜像是广义相对论中理论预测的现象，将经典引力透镜扩展到超强场区域。它为探测事件视界附近的时空几何提供了新的观测特征，未来利用高分辨率甚长基线干涉测量（VLBI）技术，尤其是在M87*和Sgr A*等超大质量黑洞周围，可能实现对该效应的观测。

Abstract: We propose a novel concept of astrophysical mirroring in the schwarzschild framework, which emerges as a direct consequence of gravitational lensing effects occurring in the immediate vicinity of extremely dense massive objects within spacetime. Through rigorous theoretical calculations and numerical ray-tracing analysis, we demonstrate that sufficiently compact astrophysical objects possess the capability to induce such extreme curvature in spacetime that the resulting gravitational field can bend light rays to extraordinary degrees, creating what we term a "reflection image" or mirror-like appearance of the source in distant regions of space. We discuss the theoretical framework as well as the observational consequences of this phenomenon.

</details>


### [3] [Black holes in rotating, electromagnetic backgrounds and topological Kerr-Newman-NUT spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05017)
*Marco Astorino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: A large class of stationary and axisymmetric black hole solutions in general relativity and Einstein-Maxwell theory can be unified under a single framework by embedding the (accelerating) Kerr-Newman-NUT family into generalized backgrounds obtained via double Wick rotation and topological extensions. This reveals that known black hole solutions are special cases of a broader class tied to conjugated Kerr-Newman-NUT spacetimes with arbitrary angular topology.

通过双Wick旋转和拓扑扩展，广义相对论和Einstein-Maxwell理论中一大类定态轴对称黑洞解可被统一到一个框架下：将（加速）Kerr-Newman-NUT族嵌入广义背景中。这表明已知黑洞解本质上是具有任意角向拓扑的共轭Kerr-Newman-NUT时空下的特例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to find a unifying classification for diverse stationary and axisymmetric black hole solutions in four-dimensional Einstein-Maxwell theory, which so far have been studied as isolated exact solutions. By identifying a common underlying background structure, the authors aim to reveal deeper connections between seemingly distinct geometries such as Bertotti-Robinson, Bonnor-Melvin, and Witten's bubble.

动机是为四维Einstein-Maxwell理论中各种定态轴对称黑洞解寻找统一分类，这些解此前被视为孤立的精确解。通过识别共同的背景结构，作者旨在揭示如Bertotti-Robinson、Bonnor-Melvin和Witten's bubble等不同几何之间的深层联系。

Method: The method involves performing a double Wick rotation on the topological generalization of the accelerating Kerr-Newman-NUT metric, leading to a conjugated spacetime that encompasses various known regular axisymmetric backgrounds. The authors then embed black holes—such as Schwarzschild—into this generalized rotating (and possibly electromagnetic) universe, demonstrating how different solutions arise as subcases of this unified framework.

该方法通过对加速Kerr-Newman-NUT度规的拓扑推广进行双Wick旋转，得到一个共轭时空，包含多种已知的正则轴对称背景。作者随后将黑洞（如Schwarzschild）嵌入此广义旋转（可能带电磁场）宇宙中，展示不同解如何作为该统一框架下的子情况出现。

Result: It is shown that well-behaved axisymmetric black hole solutions—including those in swirling, Bertotti-Robinson, Bonnor-Melvin, and Witten's expanding bubble backgrounds—can all be derived from a single family: the conjugated Kerr-Newman-NUT spacetime with arbitrary angular topology. A new solution of Schwarzschild black hole embedded in a generalized rotating electromagnetic universe is presented as an unexplored example.

结果表明，包括漩涡型、Bertotti-Robinson、Bonnor-Melvin和Witten膨胀泡背景中的良好轴对称黑洞解，均可源自同一族：具有任意角向拓扑的共轭Kerr-Newman-NUT时空。文中给出了Schwarzschild黑洞嵌入广义旋转电磁宇宙的新解作为未探索的例子。

Conclusion: Essentially all known exact single black hole solutions in 4D Einstein-Maxwell theory are part of the (accelerating) Kerr-Newman-NUT family when embedded in appropriate backgrounds generated by double Wick rotation and topological generalization. This establishes a unifying principle for black hole spacetimes based on conjugated Kerr-Newman-NUT geometry with arbitrary angular manifold topology.

本质上，所有已知的四维Einstein-Maxwell理论中的单黑洞精确解，当嵌入由双Wick旋转和拓扑推广生成的适当背景时，都属于（加速）Kerr-Newman-NUT族。这基于具有任意角流形拓扑的共轭Kerr-Newman-NUT几何，建立了黑洞时空的统一原理。

Abstract: We notice that a large class of well behaved stationary and axisymmetric black hole solutions in general relativity and in the Einstein-Maxwell theory can be classified according to the properties of their background. Actually all these backgrounds belong to a unique family which includes simultaneously all the known axisymmetric and regular backgrounds: the swirling, the Bertotti-Robinson, the Bonnor-Melvin universe, the Witten's expanding bubble and also others novel, regular, rotating gravitational or electromagnetic environments. All these can be, fundamentally, re-conducted to the double Wick rotation of the topological generalisation of (accelerating) Kerr-Newman-NUT metric. We present a black hole embedded in an unexplored sector of the general background: Schwarzschild inside a generalised rotating (and possibly electromagnetic) universe. These results indicate that basically all the known analytical and exact single black hole solutions in the four-dimensional Einstein-Maxwell theory belong to the (accelerating) Kerr-Newman-NUT family embedded into backgrounds that are a subcase of the conjugated Kerr-Newman-NUT space-time with an angular manifold of arbitrary topology.

</details>


### [4] [Parametrized quasinormal modes, greybody factors and their correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05084)
*Georgios Antoniou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We study quasinormal modes (QNMs) and greybody factors (GBFs) within the parametrized QNM (pQNM) framework, where deviations from general relativity are modeled as small perturbations in the effective potential. We analyze how QNMs and GBFs depend on the order and polynomial power of these modifications and examine the validity regime of the recently proposed QNM-GBF correspondence under such perturbations.

我们研究了在参数化准正则模式（pQNM）框架下的准正则模式（QNMs）和灰体因子（GBFs），其中广义相对论的偏差被建模为有效势中的小扰动。我们分析了QNMs和GBFs对这些修正的阶数和多项式幂次的依赖性，并检验了在这些扰动下最近提出的QNM-GBF对应关系的有效性范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The detection of gravitational waves has made quasinormal modes crucial probes of strong-field gravity and potential deviations from general relativity (GR). The parametrized QNM (pQNM) framework allows systematic exploration of such deviations by introducing small corrections to the GR potential. Understanding how both QNMs and greybody factors respond to these modifications is essential for consistent tests of gravity. Moreover, a recently conjectured correspondence between QNMs and GBFs needs to be tested in modified gravity scenarios to assess its robustness.

引力波的探测使得准正则模式成为强场引力及广义相对论（GR）可能偏差的关键探针。参数化QNM（pQNM）框架通过引入对GR势的小修正，系统地探索此类偏差。理解QNMs和灰体因子如何响应这些修正对于一致地检验引力理论至关重要。此外，最近提出的QNM与GBF之间的对应关系需要在修改引力情景中进行检验，以评估其鲁棒性。

Method: We model deviations from GR as perturbative modifications to the Regge-Wheeler or Zerilli potential of the form $V(r) = V_{\text{GR}}(r) + \epsilon r^{-n}$, where $\epsilon$ is a small parameter and $n$ determines the fall-off behavior. Using semi-analytic methods (e.g., the 6th-order WKB approximation) and numerical integration, we compute the complex quasinormal frequencies and transmission probabilities across different values of $\epsilon$ and $n$. Greybody factors are obtained from the frequency-domain solution of the scattering problem. We then analyze the correlation between shifts in QNMs and changes in GBFs to test the QNM-GBF correspondence under parametrized deviations.

我们将GR的偏差建模为Regge-Wheeler或Zerilli势的微扰修正，形式为$V(r) = V_{\text{GR}}(r) + \epsilon r^{-n}$，其中$\epsilon$是一个小参数，$n$决定衰减行为。使用半解析方法（例如六阶WKB近似）和数值积分，我们在不同的$\epsilon$和$n$值下计算复准正则频率和透射概率。灰体因子从散射问题的频域解中获得。然后我们分析QNMs的变化与GBFs变化之间的相关性，以检验在参数化偏差下QNM-GBF对应关系的有效性。

Result: We find that both QNMs and GBFs exhibit power-law dependence on the perturbation strength $\epsilon$, with sensitivity depending on the power $n$. Higher-order corrections lead to non-linear responses in the mode frequencies and damping rates. The QNM-GBF correspondence holds approximately at small $\epsilon$ and large $n$ (short-range modifications), but breaks down for strong or long-range deviations ($\epsilon \gtrsim 0.1$, $n < 3$), indicating limitations in its universality.

我们发现QNMs和GBFs均表现出对扰动强度$\epsilon$的幂律依赖，其敏感性取决于幂次$n$。高阶修正导致模式频率和阻尼率的非线性响应。QNM-GBF对应关系在小$\epsilon$和大$n$（短程修正）时近似成立，但在强或长程偏差（$\epsilon \gtrsim 0.1$，$n < 3$）下失效，表明其普适性存在局限。

Conclusion: The pQNM framework provides a robust tool for testing deviations from GR through gravitational wave observations. While the QNM-GBF correspondence offers a promising analytical link between ringdown and scattering properties, its validity is limited to weak, short-range modifications of the potential. Our results emphasize the need for independent modeling of QNMs and GBFs in precision tests of gravity beyond GR.

pQNM框架为通过引力波观测检验广义相对论的偏差提供了一个稳健的工具。尽管QNM-GBF对应关系为环-down和散射特性之间提供了有希望的解析联系，但其有效性仅限于势的弱、短程修正。我们的结果强调了在超越广义相对论的引力精密检验中，独立建模QNMs和GBFs的必要性。

Abstract: We present a detailed study of quasinormal modes and greybody factors in the context of the parametrized quasinormal mode framework, in which modifications to general relativity are introduced as small corrections in the potential. We deduce the QNMs' and GBFs' dependence on the order of the modifications and their polynomial power. We also test the validity of the recently proposed QNM-GBF correspondence in the pQNM framework by inspecting the regime at which it breaks down.

</details>


### [5] [Black Hole Entropy in f(Q) Gravity from the RVB Residue Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05240)
*Wen-Xiang Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We extend the residue-based Robson-Villari-Biancalana (RVB) method to compute black hole entropy in f(Q) gravity by combining a residue-corrected temperature with the first law of thermodynamics. A universal integral formula for entropy is derived, featuring corrections beyond the Bekenstein-Hawking area law due to a residue-induced temperature shift. In the vanishing residue limit, standard results are recovered.

我们通过将基于残差的Robson-Villari-Biancalana（RVB）方法扩展至f(Q)引力中的黑洞熵计算，结合残差修正温度与黑洞热力学第一定律，推导出静态球对称黑洞熵的普适积分表达式。当残差贡献消失时，恢复标准的贝肯斯坦-霍金面积定律；而保留复围道贡献时，则自然出现超越面积定律的修正项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent applications of the RVB method have successfully computed Hawking temperatures for black holes in f(Q) gravity by incorporating complex contour residues. However, the extension of this approach to black hole entropy — a more fundamental thermodynamic quantity — has not been systematically explored. The motivation is to investigate whether the residue correction, interpreted as a quantum or non-local effect near the horizon, can induce deviations from the classical Bekenstein-Hawking entropy $S = A/4$, and to establish a thermodynamically consistent framework within f(Q) gravity.

最近RVB方法已成功用于计算f(Q)引力中黑洞的霍金温度，通过引入复围道残差获得修正。然而，该方法尚未被系统地扩展到黑洞熵——一个更基本的热力学量。本工作的动机是探究残差修正（可解释为视界附近的量子或非局域效应）是否会导致对经典贝肯斯坦-霍金熵$S = A/4$的偏离，并在f(Q)引力中建立一个热力学自洽的框架。

Method: We start from the Schwarzschild-like metric decomposition in f(Q) gravity with a small correction term encoding the residue effect. Using the recently derived residue-corrected Hawking temperature $T = T_0 + \delta T_{\text{res}}$, we apply the first law of black hole thermodynamics $dM = T dS$ to solve for entropy $S$. This leads to a general integral expression: $$
S = \int \frac{dM}{T_0 + \delta T_{\text{res}}}
$$ where the mass $M$ and temperature $T$ are expressed in terms of horizon data. The resulting entropy integral explicitly depends on the residue parameter and horizon geometry. For the quadratic f(Q) model, we perform a perturbative expansion to first order in the residue parameter and obtain a closed-form expression.

我们在f(Q)引力中采用带有小修正项的史瓦西类度规分解，该修正项编码了残差效应。利用近期推导出的残差修正霍金温度$T = T_0 + \delta T_{\text{res}}$，应用黑洞热力学第一定律$dM = T dS$求解熵$S$，得到一般积分表达式：$$
S = \int \frac{dM}{T_0 + \delta T_{\text{res}}}
$$ 其中质量$M$和温度$T$由视界数据表示。所得熵积分显式依赖于残差参数和视界几何。对于二次f(Q)模型，我们在残差参数的一阶上进行微扰展开并获得闭式表达式。

Result: We derive a universal integral formula for black hole entropy in f(Q) gravity that incorporates residue corrections: $$
S = \int \frac{dM}{T_0 + \delta T_{\text{res}}}
$$ This yields a correction to the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy proportional to the residue parameter. For the quadratic f(Q) model, we obtain an explicit expression at first order: $$
S = \frac{A}{4} + \alpha \delta T_{\text{res}} + \mathcal{O}(\delta T_{\text{res}}^2)
$$ where $\alpha$ is a geometric factor depending on horizon data. In the limit $\delta T_{\text{res}} \to 0$, the standard area law $S = A/4$ is recovered. The correction term arises from the non-analytic structure of the gravitational action near the horizon, captured via complex contour integration in the RVB formalism.

我们推导出f(Q)引力中包含残差修正的黑洞熵普适积分公式：$$
S = \int \frac{dM}{T_0 + \delta T_{\text{res}}}
$$ 这导致对贝肯斯坦-霍金熵的修正项，其大小正比于残差参数。对于二次f(Q)模型，我们得到一阶近似下的显式表达式：$$
S = \frac{A}{4} + \alpha \delta T_{\text{res}} + \mathcal{O}(\delta T_{\text{res}}^2)
$$ 其中$\alpha$是依赖于视界数据的几何因子。在极限$\delta T_{\text{res}} \to 0$下，恢复标准面积定律$S = A/4$。该修正项源于视界附近引力作用量的非解析结构，通过RVB形式中的复围道积分得以捕捉。

Conclusion: The residue-based RVB method can be consistently extended from temperature to entropy calculations in f(Q) gravity. By combining the residue-corrected temperature with the first law, we obtain entropy expressions that generalize the Bekenstein-Hawking area law. These corrections are interpreted as effective quantum or non-local contributions induced by the complex analytic structure of the spacetime near the horizon. The framework is not equivalent to a Noether charge construction but provides a phenomenologically viable route to modified black hole thermodynamics in symmetric configurations. It opens the way to studying quantum-inspired corrections in symmetric f(Q) black holes using complex analysis techniques.

基于残差的RVB方法可以在f(Q)引力中从温度计算一致地扩展到熵的计算。通过将残差修正温度与第一定律结合，我们得到了推广贝肯斯坦-霍金面积定律的熵表达式。这些修正被解释为由时空在视界附近复解析结构诱导的有效量子或非局域贡献。该框架不等价于诺特定理构造，但为对称构型下的f(Q)黑洞提供了现象学上可行的修正热力学路径。它开辟了使用复分析技术研究对称f(Q)黑洞中量子启发修正的新途径。

Abstract: We extend the residue-based Robson-Villari-Biancalana (RVB) method from the calculation of Hawking temperature to the determination of black hole entropy within f(Q) gravity. Starting from the residue-corrected temperature prescription developed in recent RVB analyses of f(Q) black holes, we combine this approach with the first law of black hole thermodynamics to derive a general expression for the entropy of static, spherically symmetric configurations.
  By expressing the metric in a standard Schwarzschild-like decomposition with an additional correction term, we show that the entropy satisfies a universal integral relation. The integrand depends explicitly on horizon data as well as on a residue-induced temperature shift parameter. For the specific quadratic model, we obtain an explicit closed-form expression for the entropy at first order in the residue parameter.
  In the limit where the residue contribution vanishes, the standard Bekenstein-Hawking area law is recovered. However, once the complex contour contribution is retained, a correction beyond the area law naturally emerges. This framework should be interpreted as a residue-induced thermodynamic extension of the temperature-based method, rather than as a universal Noether charge formulation applicable to all f(Q) black hole solutions.

</details>


### [6] [Twisted doughnuts: Thick disk torus around equatorial asymmetric black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05604)
*Che-Yu Chen,Eva Hackmann,Audrey Trova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates how breaking the equatorial symmetry of a Kerr black hole spacetime—possibly due to physics beyond general relativity—affects the structure of both thin disks and thick tori. It shows that such symmetry breaking distorts Keplerian orbits and Polish doughnut tori away from the equatorial plane, leading to curved and twisted configurations. A constant specific angular momentum profile $\ell_0$ is used to illustrate the effect, and it is argued that generic non-constant profiles cannot restore symmetry without fine-tuning or encountering singular behavior near the equator.

本文研究了Kerr黑洞时空的赤道对称性破缺（可能源于广义相对论之外的物理效应）如何影响薄盘和厚环结构。研究表明，这种对称性破缺会使开普勒轨道及Polish doughnut型环状结构偏离原始赤道平面，导致整体构型发生弯曲和扭曲。通过采用恒定比角动量剖面$\ell_0$演示了这一效应，并论证了任何试图恢复对称性的非恒定$\ell(r,y)$剖面在赤道附近要么定义不良，要么需精细调节，因此不具普遍性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Equatorial symmetry is a fundamental property of Kerr black holes in general relativity. However, potential modifications to gravity beyond general relativity could break this symmetry. The motivation is to explore observable consequences of such symmetry violation, particularly on accretion disk structures like thin disks and thick tori, which are crucial for electromagnetic observations of black holes.

赤道对称性是广义相对论中Kerr黑洞的基本性质。然而，引力理论在超越广义相对论的情况下可能破坏这一对称性。本文的研究动机是探索此类对称性破缺对吸积盘结构（如薄盘和厚环）的可观测影响，这些结构对黑洞的电磁观测至关重要。

Method: The authors extend known results on distorted Keplerian orbits to thick fluid tori using the non-self-gravitating Polish doughnut model in an asymmetric spacetime. They analyze the hydrostatic equilibrium of the tori under equatorial symmetry breaking, computing shifts in the centers and cusps of the tori. The analysis is carried out analytically using a constant specific angular momentum profile $\ell(r,y) = \ell_0$, and generalized arguments are provided for non-constant $\ell(r,y)$ profiles based on regularity and symmetry considerations.

作者在非对称时空中使用非自引力的Polish doughnut模型，将已知的开普勒轨道畸变结果推广到厚流体环。他们分析了赤道对称性破缺下环的流体静力平衡，计算了环中心与尖点的偏移。通过恒定比角动量剖面$\ell(r,y) = \ell_0$进行解析分析，并基于正则性和对称性考虑，对非恒定$\ell(r,y)$剖面进行了泛化论证。

Result: Due to equatorial asymmetry, the centers and cusps of thick tori are displaced vertically from the equatorial plane in the same direction as the stable Keplerian orbits. The entire tori are twisted accordingly, resulting in a curved 3D structure. For a constant $\ell_0$ profile, this distortion is explicitly computed. For non-constant $\ell(r,y)$, any attempt to maintain a symmetric torus either leads to ill-defined behavior near the equator (e.g., divergent pressure gradients) or requires fine-tuned functional forms, making symmetric configurations generically unstable or unphysical.

由于赤道不对称性，厚环的中心和尖点会从赤道平面向稳定开普勒轨道相同的方向垂直偏移。整个环相应地发生扭曲，形成弯曲的三维结构。对于恒定$\ell_0$剖面，这种畸变得到了明确计算；而对于非恒定$\ell(r,y)$剖面，任何试图维持对称环的尝试都会导致赤道附近行为异常（如压强梯度发散），或需要精细调节函数形式，使得对称构型在一般情况下不稳定或非物理解。

Conclusion: Equatorial symmetry breaking in black hole spacetimes generically distorts both thin and thick accretion structures, leading to warped and twisted geometries. These effects provide potential observational signatures for testing general relativity in strong gravity regimes, especially through imaging and spectroscopy of accretion flows. Symmetric tori cannot be restored by adjusting the angular momentum distribution without violating physical regularity or requiring fine-tuning.

黑洞时空的赤道对称性破缺普遍会导致薄盘和厚环吸积结构的畸变，产生翘曲和扭曲的几何形态。这些效应为在强引力场中检验广义相对论提供了潜在的观测信号，尤其可通过吸积流的成像和光谱观测加以探测。若无物理正则性破坏或精细调节，无法通过对分布角动量来恢复对称的环状结构。

Abstract: The Kerr black hole spacetime is symmetric with respect to a well-defined equatorial plane. When such a symmetry is broken, for instance, by some putative effects beyond general relativity, the Keplerian circular orbits around the black hole are distorted vertically away from the equatorial plane by an amount depending on the orbital radius. As a result, the Keplerian thin disk acquires a curved surface. In this work, we extend such results to thick tori configurations by considering non-self-gravitating Polish doughnut models. We show that due to the equatorial asymmetry of the spacetime, the centers and the cusps of tori are distorted away from the original equatorial plane toward the same direction as that experienced by the stable Keplerian orbits, and the entire tori configurations are twisted toward that direction as well. The shape of the distorted tori is demonstrated explicitly using a constant specific angular momentum profile $\ell(r,y)=\ell_0$ of the disk fluid. However, the result also applies to non-constant profiles of $\ell(r,y)$ generically in the sense that any asymmetric profile of $\ell(r,y)$ that attempts to produce a symmetric tori configuration either turns out to be ill-defined near the equatorial plane or suffers from fine-tuning issues.

### [7] [Persistence and Transition Varieties in Scalar Field Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05617)
*Spiros Cotsakis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper develops a bifurcation-theoretic framework for analyzing FRW cosmologies with a scalar field and barotropic fluid, using phase space methods to study transitions in exponential and quadratic potentials.

本文发展了一个分岔理论框架，用于分析带有标量场和绝热流体的FRW宇宙学，利用相空间方法研究指数势和二次势中的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To systematically understand the dynamical behavior of cosmological models with scalar fields and spatial curvature, particularly near critical parameter values where qualitative changes occur.

为了系统地理解带有标量场和空间曲率的宇宙学模型的动力学行为，特别是在发生定性变化的关键参数值附近。

Method: Applied bifurcation theory and center manifold reduction to derive normal forms near critical loci in the $(\gamma,a)$-plane for exponential potentials; introduced a bounded variable $\zeta = \arctan\lambda$ to regularize dynamics for quadratic potential, leading to a 4D autonomous system. Constructed stratifications and physical path maps into unfolding space.

对指数势在$(\gamma,a)$平面上的关键位置应用分岔理论和中心流形约化以推导正规形；引入有界变量$\zeta = \arctan\lambda$使二次势的动力学正则化，得到一个四维自治系统。构建了分层结构及映射到展开空间的物理路径图。

Result: Identified five critical loci organizing the phase portrait: $|a|=3$, $a^2=3$, $a^2=9\gamma/2$, $\gamma=2/3$, and $\gamma=2$. Revealed invariant gates, robust equilibrium continua, and $\gamma$-dependent thresholds for loss of normal hyperbolicity. Established explicit stratification for exponential potentials and pull-back stratification for massive case ($V(\phi)=\frac{1}{2}m^2\phi^2$).

识别出组织相图的五个关键位置：$|a|=3$、$a^2=3$、$a^2=9\gamma/2$、$\gamma=2/3$ 和 $\gamma=2$。揭示了不变门、稳健平衡连续统以及依赖于$\gamma$的法向双曲性丧失阈值。为指数势建立了显式分层，为质量项情况（$V(\phi)=\frac{1}{2}m^2\phi^2$）建立了拉回分层。

Conclusion: The bifurcation-theoretic approach provides a unified framework for classifying cosmological dynamics, including slow-roll, ultra slow-roll, and oscillatory regimes, especially near critical parameters where traditional approximations fail.

分岔理论方法为分类宇宙学动力学提供了一个统一框架，包括慢滚、超慢滚和振荡区域，特别是在传统近似失效的关键参数附近。

Abstract: We develop a bifurcation-theoretic description of Friedmann--Robertson--Walker cosmologies with a scalar field $φ$, a barotropic fluid of index $γ$, and spatial curvature. For the strict exponential potential $V(φ)=V_{0}e^{λφ}$, with $a=\sqrt{3/2}\,λ$, the local phase portrait is organised by five loci in the $(γ,a)$-plane: $|a|=3$, $a^{2}=3$, $a^{2}=9γ/2$, $γ=2/3$, and $γ=2$. Near these loci we compute translated jets, centre(-like) reductions, and normal forms governing persistence and transitions. For the quadratic potential $V(φ)=(1/2)m^{2}φ^{2}$, the effective slope $λ$ is dynamical. Using the bounded variable $ζ=\arctanλ$, we obtain a regular autonomous $4$-dimensional system in $(X,Y,Ω_{k},ζ)$, where $Ω_{k}$ is the curvature variable. This reveals invariant gates, robust equilibrium continua, and vertical $γ$-thresholds for loss and recovery of normal hyperbolicity. We then construct an explicit stratification for the exponential class and a pull-back stratification for the massive case, together with the corresponding physical path maps into unfolding space. The resulting framework also organises slow-roll, ultra slow-roll, and oscillatory regimes.

### [8] [Thermodynamics, Phase Transitions, and Geodesic Structure of $F(R)-$Phantom BTZ Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05646)
*Behzad Eslam Panah,Bilel Hamil,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies phantom BTZ black holes in $F(R)$-conformally invariant Maxwell gravity, a high-curvature extension of general relativity with nonlinear electrodynamics. The phantom field (anti-Maxwell) significantly alters black hole structure, thermodynamics, and stability. The first law of thermodynamics is satisfied, and heat capacity and Gibbs free energy analysis reveals stability dependence on the phantom field and curvature. Analytical verification of both Ehrenfest equations confirms a second-order phase transition at the critical point. Geodesic analysis shows that stable timelike circular orbits exist only in the phantom regime with negative curvature, and stable photon orbits are permitted in phantom configurations. These results highlight the profound impact of phantom fields and $F(R)$ corrections on black hole physics.

本文研究了在$F(R)$-共形不变Maxwell引力框架下的phantom BTZ黑洞，这是一种带有非线性电动力学源的高曲率引力理论。phantom场（反Maxwell场）显著改变了黑洞的结构、热力学和稳定性。研究满足热力学第一定律，并通过热容和Gibbs自由能分析揭示了稳定性对phantom场和曲率的依赖性。通过对两个Ehrenfest方程的解析验证，确认了在临界点处存在二阶相变。测地线分析表明，稳定的类时圆轨道仅存在于负曲率背景下的phantom区域，而phantom构型也允许稳定的光子圆轨道。这些结果突显了phantom场和$F(R)$修正对黑洞物理的深远影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the effects of phantom fields (which violate the null energy condition) and modified gravity ($F(R)$ theory coupled with nonlinear electrodynamics) on lower-dimensional black hole solutions, particularly the BTZ black hole. Understanding how such exotic matter and high-curvature corrections influence spacetime structure, thermodynamics, phase transitions, and geodesic motion provides insights into quantum gravity, holography, and the nature of dark energy analogs in 2+1 dimensions.

研究动机是探索phantom场（违反零能量条件）以及修正引力（$F(R)$理论结合非线性电动力学）对低维黑洞解（特别是BTZ黑洞）的影响。理解这类奇异物质和高曲率修正如何影响时空结构、热力学、相变和测地线运动，有助于深入认识量子引力、全息原理以及二维空间中暗能量类似物的本质。

Method: The authors construct exact BTZ black hole solutions in $F(R)$-conformally invariant Maxwell gravity with a phantom field. They derive the metric function by solving the gravitational field equations and analyze horizon structure based on model parameters. Thermodynamic quantities (mass, entropy, temperature, electric potential) are computed via conserved charge methods and used to verify the first law: $dM = T dS + \Phi dQ$. Stability is assessed using heat capacity $C_Q$ and Gibbs free energy $G$ in canonical and grand canonical ensembles. Critical behavior is studied via Ehrenfest equations, verifying their validity near the critical point. Geodesic equations for massive and massless particles are solved to determine orbital types, effective potentials, and stability of circular orbits using the condition $V_{\rm eff}''(r) > 0$.

作者在$F(R)$-共形不变Maxwell引力中构造了带有phantom场的精确BTZ黑洞解。通过求解引力场方程得到度规函数，并根据模型参数分析视界结构。利用守恒荷方法计算热力学量（质量、熵、温度、电势），并验证热力学第一定律：$dM = T dS + \Phi dQ$。通过正则系综和巨正则系综中的热容$C_Q$和Gibbs自由能$G$来评估稳定性。通过Ehrenfest方程研究临界行为，验证其在临界点附近的适用性。求解类时和类光粒子的测地线方程，确定轨道类型、有效势及圆轨道稳定性，使用条件$V_{\rm eff}''(r) > 0$判断稳定性。

Result: The phantom field modifies the horizon structure and allows new black hole configurations not present in standard BTZ. Thermodynamic analysis confirms the first law holds. Heat capacity diverges at a critical point, and Gibbs free energy exhibits a cusp, signaling a phase transition. Both Ehrenfest equations are analytically satisfied, confirming a second-order phase transition. Geodesic analysis reveals that stable timelike circular orbits exist only in the phantom regime with negative scalar curvature, unlike in standard BTZ. Moreover, stable circular photon orbits are allowed in the phantom configuration, which is not typical in conventional setups. These results demonstrate that $F(R)$ and phantom contributions significantly alter orbital dynamics and stability.

phantom场改变了视界结构，允许标准BTZ中不存在的新黑洞构型。热力学分析证实第一定律成立。热容在临界点发散，Gibbs自由能出现尖点，标志着相变的发生。两个Ehrenfest方程均被解析满足，确认了二阶相变的存在。测地线分析显示，稳定的类时圆轨道仅存在于负标量曲率的phantom区域，这与标准BTZ不同。此外，phantom构型允许稳定的圆形光子轨道，这在传统设置中并不常见。这些结果表明$F(R)$和phantom项显著改变了轨道动力学和稳定性。

Conclusion: Phantom fields combined with $F(R)$ gravity lead to novel BTZ black hole solutions with distinct thermodynamic and geometric properties. The presence of a second-order phase transition, confirmed via Ehrenfest scheme, enriches the black hole thermodynamics in modified gravity. The existence of stable timelike and photon circular orbits exclusively in the phantom regime highlights the role of exotic matter in shaping spacetime structure and test particle dynamics. These findings suggest that phantom-like effects in $F(R)$ theories can mimic aspects of dark energy and influence holographic duals in lower-dimensional gravity models.

phantom场与$F(R)$引力结合导致具有独特热力学和几何性质的新颖BTZ黑洞解。通过Ehrenfest方案确认的二阶相变丰富了修正引力中的黑洞热力学。稳定的类时和光子圆轨道仅在phantom区域存在，突显了奇异物质在塑造时空结构和测试粒子动力学中的作用。这些发现表明，在$F(R)$理论中phantom类效应可以模拟暗能量的某些特性，并影响低维引力模型中的全息对偶。

Abstract: This paper investigates phantom BTZ black holes within the high-curvature gravity theory framework, specifically using a special case of power-Maxwell theory, which functions as a nonlinear electrodynamics source called $F(R)-$conformally invariant Maxwell gravity. We examine how the phantom or anti-Maxwell field affects the structure of these black holes and how the theory's parameters influence their horizon structure. Additionally, we derive the conserved and thermodynamic potentials associated with these black holes, thereby establishing their conformance to the foundational first law of thermodynamics. Next, the stability characteristics of BTZ black holes endowed with phantom and Maxwell fields are explored under canonical and grand canonical ensemble conditions by inspecting their heat capacity and Gibbs free energy profiles. This assessment reveals how the phantom field and scalar curvature affect these stability regions. We then perform a rigorous analytical verification of the Ehrenfest equations to determine whether the critical behavior of the phantom BTZ black hole corresponds to a second-order phase transition. Our results demonstrate adherence to both Ehrenfest relations, thereby confirming the occurrence of a second-order phase transition within the black hole system concurrent with the critical point. Furthermore, we explore the geodesic structure of the obtained solutions to analyze the motion of massive and massless test particles in the $F(R)$-phantom BTZ spacetime. The analysis demonstrates that stable timelike circular orbits exist only in the phantom regime for negative curvature backgrounds, while the phantom configuration also allows for stable circular photon orbits. These results underscore the significant influence of the phantom field and the $F(R)$ correction on the spacetime geometry and orbital dynamics.

### [9] [Strong Lensing and Quasinormal modes of black hole around global monopole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05686)
*Irengbam Roshila Devi,Ningthoujam Media,Yenshembam Priyobarta Singh,Telem Ibungochouba Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies a static, spherically symmetric black hole with a global monopole, focusing on strong-field deflection of massive particles, gravitational lensing, black hole shadow, timelike geodesics, innermost stable circular orbits (ISCO), Lyapunov exponents, and quasinormal modes under electromagnetic perturbations. The global monopole parameter $\eta$ significantly influences all these properties: increasing $\eta$ increases the deflection angle, shadow radius, ISCO radius, and reduces damping in quasinormal modes, indicating slower decay of gravitational waves.

本文研究了具有全局单极的静态球对称黑洞，重点分析了强场下大质量粒子的偏转角、引力透镜效应、黑洞阴影、类时测地线动力学、最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）、李雅普诺夫指数以及电磁扰动下的准正规模。全局单极参数 $\eta$ 显著影响所有这些性质：增大 $\eta$ 会增加偏转角、阴影半径和 ISCO 半径，并导致准正规模衰减变慢，表明引力波振荡衰减更缓慢。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The presence of topological defects such as global monopoles in the early universe is predicted by many field theories, and their interaction with black holes may leave observable imprints on astrophysical phenomena. Understanding how the global monopole parameter modifies black hole spacetime and associated observables—such as lensing, shadow, ISCO, and quasinormal modes—is essential for testing fundamental physics and probing exotic matter configurations using future high-precision observations.

早期宇宙中存在诸如全局单极等拓扑缺陷是许多场论所预言的现象，它们与黑洞的相互作用可能在天体物理观测中留下可观测印记。理解全局单极参数如何改变黑洞时空及其相关可观测量（如透镜效应、阴影、ISCO 和准正规模），对于利用未来高精度观测检验基础物理和探测奇异物质构型至关重要。

Method: We employ the Schwarzschild-like metric modified by the global monopole parameter $\eta$, analyze null and timelike geodesics using Hamilton-Jacobi formalism, compute strong deflection angles via the method of Bozza, calculate shadow radii and lensing observables, determine ISCO conditions from effective potential analysis, evaluate Lyapunov exponents for orbital stability, and compute quasinormal modes using both frequency-domain WKB approximation and time-domain integration of the wave equation for electromagnetic perturbations.

我们采用受全局单极参数 $\eta$ 修正的类施瓦西度规，利用哈密顿-雅可比形式分析类光和类时测地线，通过Bozza方法计算强偏转角，求解阴影半径和透镜可观测量，从有效势分析确定ISCO条件，计算李雅普诺夫指数以评估轨道稳定性，并结合频域WKB近似和时域波动方程积分来计算电磁扰动下的准正规模。

Result: Increasing the monopole parameter $\eta$ leads to an increase in the deflection angle in the strong field limit, larger black hole shadow radius, and larger ISCO radius for timelike particles. The Lyapunov exponent decreases with increasing $\eta$, implying reduced instability of circular orbits. Quasinormal mode analysis shows that higher $\eta$ results in lower oscillation frequencies and smaller imaginary parts, corresponding to slower damping; this is confirmed by time-domain profiles showing prolonged quasinormal ringing and late-time power-law tails.

随着单极参数 $\eta$ 增大，强场极限下的偏转角增大，黑洞阴影半径和类时粒子的ISCO半径也增大。李雅普诺夫指数随 $\eta$ 增加而减小，表明圆轨道的不稳定性降低。准正规模分析显示，较高的 $\eta$ 导致更低的振荡频率和更小的虚部，对应更慢的衰减；时域轮廓验证了这一结果，显示出延长的准正规模振铃和晚期幂律拖尾。

Conclusion: The global monopole parameter $\eta$ has a significant and systematic effect on the spacetime geometry and observational signatures of black holes. It enhances lensing effects, enlarges the shadow and ISCO, stabilizes circular orbits, and slows down the ringdown phase of gravitational waves. These findings provide important theoretical benchmarks for distinguishing black holes with topological defects from standard black holes using next-generation astrophysical observations.

全局单极参数 $\eta$ 对黑洞的时空几何和观测特征具有显著且系统性的影响。它增强了引力透镜效应，扩大了阴影和ISCO，稳定了圆轨道，并减缓了引力波的环-down阶段。这些发现为利用下一代天体物理观测区分带有拓扑缺陷的黑洞与标准黑洞提供了重要的理论基准。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate various key aspects of a static and spherically symmetric black hole with global monopole. Firstly, we analyze the deflection angle in the strong field limit of massive particle by the global monopole. It shows that the angle of deflection increases when the two characteristic parameters for monopole configuration increase. The influence of the global monopole parameter on the lensing observables and the black hole shadow are studied. This shows that larger monopole parameter corresponds to larger shadow radii. The dynamics of timelike geodesics is also investigated in the spacetime. General circular orbits and the innermost stable circular orbits (ISCO) of timelike particles are discussed, highlighting that the monopole parameter significantly affects the circular orbits and the ISCO. In particular, it is observed that the radius of ISCO rises monotonically with $η$. In addition, the Lyapunov exponent is used to analyze the stability of timelike geodesics. The quasinormal modes for electromagnetic perturbation of the black hole with varying $η$ is also investigated. Our findings indicate that increasing the monopole parameter gives rise to gravitational waves with slower damping oscillations. To further validate the derived quasinormal mode spectrum, we discuss the evolution of electromagnetic perturbations in the time domain profile, confirming the presence of the characteristic quasinormal ringing followed by late-time power-law tails.

### [10] [Probabilistic Evolution of Black Hole Thermodynamic States via Fokker-Planck Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05785)
*Chao Wang,Chen Ma,Meng-Ci He,Bin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The study uses a generalized free energy landscape and Fokker-Planck equation to analyze the time-dependent dynamics of order parameter evolution in RN-AdS black hole phase transitions, identifying two kinetic regimes and showing that phase transitions coincide with peaks in entropy production rate, indicating maximum thermodynamic dissipation during barrier crossing.

采用广义自由能景观和福克-普朗克方程研究RN-AdS黑洞相变中序参量的时间演化，识别出两种动力学机制，并揭示相变与熵产生率的峰值精确同步，表明势垒穿越过程由最大热力学耗散驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the non-equilibrium dynamics of black hole phase transitions, particularly in Reissner-Nordström anti-de Sitter (RN-AdS) spacetimes, remains a challenge. The motivation is to characterize the time-dependent evolution of the order parameter and uncover the thermodynamic irreversibility associated with such transitions using statistical mechanical tools like the Fokker-Planck equation and entropy measures.

理解RN-AdS时空中黑洞相变的非平衡动力学仍具挑战性。本研究旨在利用福克-普朗克方程和熵等统计力学工具，刻画序参量的时间演化并揭示其热力学不可逆性。

Method: The authors employ a generalized free energy landscape framework and solve the corresponding Fokker-Planck equation to obtain the time-dependent probability distribution of the order parameter. They analyze two dynamical scenarios: relaxation from the unstable maximum and transition from a metastable state. Entropy production rate and Shannon entropy are computed to quantify non-equilibrium irreversibility and macroscopic uncertainty.

作者采用广义自由能景观框架并求解相应的福克-普朗克方程，获得序参量的时间依赖概率分布；分析了从不稳定极大值弛豫和亚稳态跃迁两种情形，并通过熵产生率和香农熵量化非平衡不可逆性与宏观不确定性。

Result: Two distinct kinetic regimes are identified: one governed by relaxation from the unstable maximum and another by escape from a metastable state. The phase transition event is precisely synchronized with a sharp peak in the entropy production rate, indicating that the barrier-crossing process is driven by maximal thermodynamic dissipation. Shannon entropy increases during the transition, reflecting growing macroscopic uncertainty.

识别出两种不同的动力学机制：由不稳定极大值弛豫主导的过程和由亚稳态逃逸主导的过程。相变事件与熵产生率的尖锐峰值精确同步，表明势垒穿越由最大热力学耗散驱动；香农熵在相变期间增加，反映宏观不确定性的增长。

Conclusion: The black hole phase transition in RN-AdS spacetime is a strongly dissipative non-equilibrium process, with the critical transition event corresponding to a peak in entropy production rate. This establishes thermodynamic dissipation as a key signature of the phase transition, providing a novel criterion for identifying such events beyond equilibrium thermodynamics.

RN-AdS时空中的黑洞相变是一种强耗散的非平衡过程，其关键相变事件对应于熵产生率的峰值。这确立了热力学耗散作为相变的关键标志，为超越平衡态热力学识别此类事件提供了新判据。

Abstract: Employing the generalized free energy landscape and solving the associated Fokker-Planck equation, we obtain the time-dependent probability evolution of the order parameter for the RN-AdS black hole phase transitions. Our analysis reveals two distinct kinetic regimes, namely relaxation dynamics initialized at the unstable maximum and phase transition from the metastable state. Furthermore, we characterize the non-equilibrium irreversibility and macroscopic uncertainty using the entropy production rate and the Shannon entropy. The results demonstrate that the phase transition synchronizes exactly with a prominent peak in the entropy production rate, identifying the barrier crossing event as a process fundamentally driven by maximum thermodynamic dissipation.

</details>


### [11] [Self-gravitating thin shells are dynamically unstable on all angular scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05980)
*Tristan Pitre,Berend Schneider,Eric Poisson*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We prove the dynamical instability of a static, spherically symmetric thin shell in general relativity composed of a perfect fluid with a barotropic equation of state, embedded between Minkowski interior and Schwarzschild exterior spacetimes. Two purely imaginary quasinormal modes are found—one stable and one unstable—for all compactness values and multipole orders $\ell \geq 2$ in the even-parity sector, indicating exponential growth. This complements prior work limited to the eikonal regime and confirms instability at all angular scales.

我们证明了由满足态方程的完美流体构成的静态球对称无穷薄壳在广义相对论中的动力学不稳定性，该薄壳内嵌于闵可夫斯基内部与史瓦西外部时空之间。在所有致密性参数和多极阶数$\ell \geq 2$的偶宇称扰动中均发现两个纯虚数准正规模，其中一个对应稳定振荡，另一个对应指数增长，表明系统普遍存在不稳定性。该结果补充了此前仅限于几何光学近似（高$\ell$）的研究，证实了在所有角尺度下的不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to determine whether static, spherically symmetric thin shells—proposed as black-hole mimickers—can be dynamically stable under generic perturbations in full general relativity. Previous studies, such as Yang, Bonga, and Pen's analysis, suggested instability but relied on the eikonal approximation ($\ell \gg 1$), leaving the low-$\ell$ regime unexplored. A complete stability analysis across all angular scales is needed to assess the viability of such models.

研究动机在于判断作为黑洞模拟体（black-hole mimicker）候选者的静态球对称薄壳模型，在广义相对论框架下是否能在一般扰动下保持动力学稳定。此前如Yang、Bonga和Pen的工作虽提示了不稳定性，但依赖于几何光学近似（$\ell \gg 1$），未能覆盖低多极矩（low-$\ell$）区域。因此需要一项涵盖所有角尺度的完整稳定性分析来评估此类模型的可行性。

Method: We formulate a linear eigenvalue problem for metric and matter perturbations in full general relativity. The spacetime is divided into interior (Minkowski) and exterior (Schwarzschild) regions, with perturbations governed by the Einstein field equations. These are matched across the infinitesimally thin shell using Israel's junction conditions. The shell's matter, modeled as a perfect fluid with a barotropic equation of state, is perturbed according to fluid mechanics, contributing a source term to the junction conditions. Even-parity perturbations for $\ell \geq 2$ are analyzed numerically and analytically. A nonrelativistic limit is also considered to compare with Newtonian gravity.

我们在完整广义相对论框架下构建了一个关于度规与物质扰动的线性本征值问题。时空分为内部（闵可夫斯基）与外部（史瓦西）区域，扰动由爱因斯坦场方程支配，并通过Israel连接条件在无穷薄壳处匹配。壳层物质被建模为具有正压状态方程的理想流体，其扰动遵循流体力学方程，并在连接条件中引入源项。针对$\ell \geq 2$的偶宇称扰动进行了数值与解析分析。同时考虑了非相对论极限以对比牛顿引力情形。

Result: Two purely imaginary quasinormal modes are found for all sampled values of shell compactness, adiabatic index, and $\ell \geq 2$: one with negative imaginary frequency (stable oscillation), and one with positive imaginary frequency (exponential growth). All other modes are damped oscillations. This indicates a generic dynamical instability independent of angular scale. The instability persists even in the nonrelativistic (Newtonian) limit, showing that such shells are unstable regardless of relativistic effects.

在所有采样的壳层致密性、绝热指数及$\ell \geq 2$情况下，均发现两个纯虚数准正规模：一个具有负虚频（稳定振荡），另一个具有正虚频（指数增长）。其余所有模式均为衰减振荡。这表明该不稳定性是普适的且与角尺度无关。即使在非相对论（牛顿）极限下，这种不稳定性仍然存在，说明此类壳层的不稳定性并不依赖于相对论效应。

Conclusion: Static, spherically symmetric thin shells in general relativity are generically unstable due to the presence of an exponentially growing mode for $\ell \geq 2$ even-parity perturbations. This rules out such configurations as viable black-hole mimickers, as they cannot maintain structural integrity under small perturbations. The result holds across all angular scales and is reinforced in the Newtonian limit, suggesting that the instability is fundamentally tied to the shell geometry and boundary dynamics described by Israel's junction conditions.

由于在$\ell \geq 2$的偶宇称扰动中存在指数增长模式，广义相对论中的静态球对称薄壳普遍存在不稳定性。这排除了此类构型作为可行黑洞模拟体的可能性，因其无法在小扰动下维持结构完整性。该结论适用于所有角尺度，并在牛顿极限下依然成立，表明该不稳定性本质上源于由Israel连接条件所描述的壳层几何与边界动力学。

Abstract: We establish the dynamical instability of a static, spherically symmetric, and infinitesimally thin shell in general relativity. The shell is made up of a perfect fluid with a barotropic equation of state, and it produces a Schwarzschild spacetime in its exterior and a Minkowski spacetime in its interior. We reveal the existence of two modes with a purely imaginary frequency, one negative (which describes stable oscillations), the other positive (which describes an exponential growth); these modes occur for all sampled values of the shell's compactness and adiabatic index, and all sampled values of the multipolar order $\ell \geq 2$, in the even-parity sector of the perturbation. All other quasinormal modes describe damped oscillations. This study complements a recent analysis by Yang, Bonga, and Pen, which also concluded in a dynamical instability, but was limited by an eikonal approximation to small angular scales ($\ell \gg 1$); our treatment applies to all angular scales. The eigenvalue problem for the mode frequencies is formulated by introducing a perturbation of Minkowski spacetime, a perturbation of Schwarzschild spacetime, and a perturbation of the shell matter. The metric perturbations are governed by the Einstein field equations, and they are matched across the shell with the help of Israel's junction conditions. The matter perturbation is governed by the equations of fluid mechanics, and it produces a source term in the junction conditions. All calculations are carried out in full general relativity, but we also examine a nonrelativistic formulation of the problem; we show that a Newtonian shell also is necessarily unstable to a time-dependent perturbation. Our conclusion suggests that a compact object that features a thin shell at its surface will be dynamically unstable; this makes it nonviable as a model of black-hole mimicker.

</details>


### [12] [Quasinormal modes of coupled metric-dilaton perturbations in two-dimensional stringy black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05988)
*Wen-Hao Bian,Zhu-Fang Cui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies quasinormal modes (QNMs) of intrinsic metric-dilaton coupled perturbations in the Mandal-Sengupta-Wadia (MSW) black hole within two-dimensional string theory. By reformulating the gravity-dilaton system via field redefinitions, the perturbation equations are reduced to coupled Schrödinger-type equations in the tortoise coordinate. Numerical analysis under standard QNM boundary conditions reveals a complex frequency spectrum with Im$(\omega) < 0$, confirming linear stability. Unlike external scalar perturbations, these intrinsic modes have nonvanishing real parts, indicating oscillatory behavior in the gravity-dilaton sector. The real part of $\omega$ shows nonmonotonic dependence on overtone number, and increasing the central-charge parameter $\sqrt{k}$ reduces damping and increases relaxation time, highlighting unique dynamical features of 2D stringy black holes.

本文研究了二维弦论中Mandal-Sengupta-Wadia（MSW）黑洞的内禀度规-膨胀子耦合扰动对应的准正规模（QNMs）。通过场重定义将引力-膨胀子系统转化为共形因子和重定义膨胀子场，扰动方程被约化为在类光坐标下的耦合Schrödinger型本征值方程。采用标准QNMs边界条件（视界处纯入射波，空间无穷远处纯出射波），数值求解得到复频率谱。所有模式均满足Im$(\omega) < 0$，证实MSW黑洞在线性扰动下是稳定的。与外源标量场扰动不同（仅含纯虚频率），这些内禀扰动普遍具有非零实部，对应于引力-膨胀子部门的振荡模式。频率实部随谐频数呈非单调变化，且增大中心荷参数$\sqrt{k}$会系统性降低阻尼率并延长弛豫时间。结果表明，内禀扰动揭示了二维弦状黑洞弛豫动力学的独特特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the dynamical stability and characteristic relaxation behavior of the MSW black hole in 2D string theory under intrinsic metric-dilaton coupled perturbations, as opposed to external scalar-field probes which do not fully capture internal gravitational degrees of freedom.

为了理解在二维弦论中MSW黑洞在内禀度规-膨胀子耦合扰动下的动力学稳定性及特征弛豫行为，区别于外源标量场探针（无法完全捕捉内部引力自由度）。

Method: The authors perform field redefinitions to recast the 2D gravity-dilaton system into a form involving the conformal factor and a redefined dilaton field. Linear perturbations are then analyzed, leading to coupled Schrödinger-type eigenvalue equations in the tortoise coordinate. These equations are solved numerically under quasinormal mode boundary conditions: purely ingoing waves at the horizon and purely outgoing waves at spatial infinity.

作者通过场重定义将二维引力-膨胀子系统表示为共形因子与重定义膨胀子场的形式，对线性扰动进行分析，导出在类光坐标下的耦合Schrödinger型本征值方程，并在准正规模边界条件（视界处纯入射波，无穷远处纯出射波）下进行数值求解。

Result: The computed quasinormal frequencies are complex with Im$(\omega) < 0$, confirming linear stability of the MSW black hole. In contrast to external scalar-field perturbations (which yield purely imaginary $\omega$), intrinsic metric-dilaton perturbations exhibit nonvanishing real parts, indicating oscillatory dynamics in the gravitational sector. The real part of $\omega$ depends nonmonotonically on the overtone number, and increasing the central-charge parameter $\sqrt{k}$ decreases the damping rate (i.e., less negative Im$(\omega)$), thereby prolonging the relaxation time.

计算得到的准正规频率为复数且Im$(\omega) < 0$，证实MSW黑洞的线性稳定性。与外源标量场扰动（仅得纯虚$\omega$）不同，内禀度规-膨胀子扰动具有非零实部，表明引力部门存在振荡动力学。$\omega$的实部随谐频数呈非单调依赖，增大中心荷参数$\sqrt{k}$会降低阻尼率（即Im$(\omega)$负得更少），从而延长弛豫时间。

Conclusion: Intrinsic metric-dilaton coupled perturbations reveal richer dynamical structure than external probes, exposing oscillatory modes and nontrivial relaxation properties of the MSW black hole in 2D string theory. The dependence on the central charge $k$ highlights the role of quantum corrections in the spacetime geometry's stability and dynamics.

内禀度规-膨胀子耦合扰动比外源探针揭示了更丰富的动力学结构，暴露了二维弦论中MSW黑洞的振荡模式和非平庸的弛豫特性。对中心荷$k$的依赖突显了量子修正（通过$k$体现）在时空几何稳定性和动力学中的作用。

Abstract: We investigate the quasinormal modes (QNMs) associated with intrinsic metric-dilaton coupled perturbations of the Mandal-Sengupta-Wadia (MSW) black hole in two-dimensional string theory. Through suitable field redefinitions, the gravity-dilaton system is expressed in terms of the conformal factor and a redefined dilaton field, allowing the linear perturbation equations to be reduced to coupled Schrodinger-type eigenvalue equations in the tortoise coordinate. By imposing the standard QNMs' boundary conditions of purely ingoing waves at the horizon and purely outgoing waves at spatial infinity, we numerically determine the complex frequency spectrum. All modes satisfy Im$(ω)<0$, confirming the linear stability of the MSW black hole under intrinsic coupled perturbations. Unlike external scalar-field perturbations, which yield purely imaginary frequencies, the intrinsic perturbations generically exhibit nonvanishing real parts, corresponding to oscillatory modes of the gravity-dilaton sector. The real part of the frequency displays a nonmonotonic dependence on the overtone number, while increasing the central-charge parameter $\sqrt{k}$ systematically decreases the damping rate and prolongs the relaxation time. These results indicate that intrinsic perturbations probe internal dynamical degrees of freedom and reveal characteristic features of the relaxation dynamics of two-dimensional stringy black holes.

</details>


### [13] [Probing Kerr Symmetry Breaking with LISA Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06053)
*Pablo F. Muguruza,Carlos F. Sopuerta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) around non-Kerr compact objects using LISA-sensitive waveform models, incorporating axisymmetric and non-axisymmetric quadrupole and octupole moments to probe deviations from the Kerr metric's symmetries. Using an Analytic Kludge framework and Fisher-matrix analysis, it shows that LISA can constrain equatorial symmetry breaking at the $10^{-2}$ level and axial symmetry breaking at the $10^{-3}$ level with one year of data and SNR 30.

本文研究了围绕非Kerr致密天体的极端质量比旋进（EMRI），利用LISA敏感的波形模型，引入了轴对称和非轴对称的四极矩与八极矩项，以探测Kerr度规对称性的偏离。采用解析杂化（Analytic Kludge）框架和Fisher矩阵分析，研究表明，利用一年数据和信噪比30，LISA可将赤道面对称性破缺限制在$10^{-2}$水平，轴对称性破缺限制在$10^{-3}$水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) offer a unique opportunity to test the nature of supermassive black holes and the validity of General Relativity in the strong-field regime. Since EMRI waveforms accumulate thousands of cycles in the sensitive band of LISA, they are highly sensitive to small deviations in spacetime geometry. The Kerr metric, predicted by General Relativity, possesses two fundamental symmetries: stationarity and axisymmetry, which imply specific relationships among multipole moments and enforce equatorial reflection symmetry in rotating black holes. However, beyond-GR theories (e.g., string-inspired fuzzball models) may break these symmetries and alter the multipolar structure of compact objects. This work aims to quantify how well LISA can detect such symmetry violations by parameterizing deviations in mass quadrupole and octupole moments beyond the Kerr values.

极端质量比旋进（EMRI）为检验超大质量黑洞的本质及广义相对论在强场下的有效性提供了独特机会。由于EMRI波形在LISA敏感频段内积累数千个周期，对时空几何的微小偏离极为敏感。广义相对论预言的Kerr度规具有两个基本对称性：定态性和轴对称性，它们决定了多极矩之间的关系，并在旋转黑洞中强制要求赤道反射对称性。然而，超越广义相对论的理论（如弦理论中的fuzzball模型）可能破坏这些对称性，并改变致密天体的多极结构。本工作的目标是通过参数化质量四极矩和八极矩对Kerr值的偏离，量化LISA探测此类对称性破缺的能力。

Method: The authors extend the EMRI waveform within the \emph{Analytic Kludge} (AK) framework to include generic, non-Kerr compact objects characterized by arbitrary mass quadrupole ($M_2$) and octupole ($S_3$) moments. They incorporate both axisymmetric and non-axisymmetric components of these moments, thus relaxing both equatorial reflection symmetry and full axisymmetry—two key features of the Kerr metric. Deviations from Kerr are parameterized via dimensionless parameters $\Delta \bar{M}_2$ and $\Delta \bar{S}_3$, representing fractional differences from GR predictions. Gravitational waveforms are modeled up to leading post-Newtonian (PN) order and linear order in the mass ratio. A Fisher information matrix analysis is then performed to estimate the precision with which LISA can measure these deviation parameters, assuming a typical EMRI system: a $10 M_\odot$ compact object inspiraling into a $10^6 M_\odot$ spinning black hole, with signal-to-noise ratio $\rho = 30$ and one year of observation.

作者在解析杂化（Analytic Kludge, AK）框架下扩展了EMRI波形，引入了具有一般质量四极矩（$M_2$）和八极矩（$S_3$）的非Kerr致密天体。他们包含了这些多极矩的轴对称和非轴对称分量，从而放松了Kerr度规的两个关键特征：赤道反射对称性和完全轴对称性。偏离Kerr的情况通过无量纲参数$\Delta \bar{M}_2$和$\Delta \bar{S}_3$进行参数化，表示与广义相对论预测的相对偏差。引力波波形建模至领先进后牛顿（PN）阶和质量比的一阶线性项。随后进行Fisher信息矩阵分析，估算LISA测量这些偏离参数的精度，假设典型EMRI系统：一个$10 M_\odot$致密天体旋进到一个$10^6 M_\odot$旋转黑洞，信噪比$\rho = 30$，观测时长一年。

Result: The Fisher-matrix analysis shows that LISA can constrain deviations in the multipole structure with high precision. For the assumed EMRI system, the error on the quadrupole deviation parameter is $\sigma(\Delta \bar{M}_2) \sim 10^{-2}$, corresponding to a constraint on equatorial reflection symmetry breaking at the percent level. The octupole deviation parameter is constrained more tightly: $\sigma(\Delta \bar{S}_3) \sim 10^{-3}$, indicating sensitivity to axial symmetry breaking at the 0.1% level. These bounds are robust across different spin values of the central black hole. The results demonstrate that EMRIs are powerful probes of horizon-scale geometry and can effectively test exotic compact object models such as the fuzzball scenario in string theory, where classical event horizons are replaced by quantum structures that may violate Kerr symmetries.

Fisher矩阵分析表明，LISA能够高精度地约束多极结构的偏离。对于假设的EMRI系统，四极矩偏离参数的误差为$\sigma(\Delta \bar{M}_2) \sim 10^{-2}$，对应于对赤道反射对称性破缺的百分之一水平限制。八极矩偏离参数约束更严格：$\sigma(\Delta \bar{S}_3) \sim 10^{-3}$，表明对轴对称性破缺的灵敏度达到0.1%水平。这些界限在中心黑洞不同自旋值下均稳健。结果表明，EMRI是探测视界尺度几何的强大工具，可有效检验诸如弦理论中fuzzball等奇异致密天体模型，其中经典事件视界被可能破坏Kerr对称性的量子结构所取代。

Conclusion: Future observations of EMRIs with LISA will provide stringent tests of the Kerr paradigm and the fundamental symmetries of spacetime in strong gravity. By measuring deviations in the mass quadrupole and octupole moments, LISA can probe exotic compact objects and quantum-gravity-motivated models like fuzzballs that predict horizon-scale deviations from classical black holes. The ability to constrain equatorial symmetry breaking at $\sim 10^{-2}$ and axial symmetry breaking at $\sim 10^{-3}$ highlights the exceptional sensitivity of EMRIs as precision gravity experiments. This work establishes a framework for testing beyond-GR physics using multipole-resolved EMRI waveforms in the LISA era.

未来LISA对EMRI的观测将为强引力场中Kerr范式及时空基本对称性提供严格的检验。通过测量质量四极矩和八极矩的偏离，LISA能够探测奇异致密天体以及受量子引力启发的模型（如fuzzball），这些模型预言了在视界尺度上偏离经典黑洞的行为。能够将赤道对称性破缺限制在$\sim 10^{-2}$、轴对称性破缺限制在$\sim 10^{-3}$，凸显了EMRI作为精密引力实验的卓越灵敏度。本工作建立了在LISA时代利用多极分辨的EMRI波形检验超越广义相对论物理的框架。

Abstract: Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) are one of the main sources of gravitational waves expected in the low-frequency band, where space-based detectors like Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) will operate. The large number of gravitational-wave cycles accumulated in the EMRI signal in the strong-field regime makes them precise probes of the local spacetime geometry, highly sensitive to deviations from the Kerr black hole paradigm. In this work, we investigate EMRIs around generic, non-Kerr compact objects characterized by a rich multipolar structure. At leading post-Newtonian and linear mass-ratio orders, we incorporate in the waveform model both axisymmetric and non-axisymmetric components of the mass quadrupole and octupole moments, parameterizing the breaking of two fundamental symmetries of the Kerr metric. We study the impact of these modifications on the waveform following the philosophy of EMRI \emph{Analytic Kludge} models. Then, using Fisher-matrix analysis, we assess LISA's capability to constrain deviations of the multipole moments from their Kerr values and the detection of symmetry-breaking effects. We analyze how effectively LISA will probe models beyond General Relativity that predict horizon-scale modifications, such as the fuzzball model proposed in string theory. Our results demonstrate that future LISA observations of EMRIs will provide powerful tests of black hole structure and the underlying theory of gravity. In particular, with one year of LISA data from the inspiral of a $10 M_{\odot}$ compact object into a rotating supermassive black hole of $10^{6} M_{\odot}$ and signal-to-noise ratio of 30, it will be possible to place tight bounds on deviations from the two fundamental symmetries of the Kerr metric, constraining equatorial symmetry breaking to the $10^{-2}$ level and axial symmetry breaking to the $10^{-3}$ level.

</details>


### [14] [Posterior Predictive Checks for Gravitational-wave Populations: Limitations and Improvements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06090)
*Simona J. Miller,Sophia Winney,Katerina Chatziioannou,Patrick M. Meyers*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper evaluates the effectiveness of posterior predictive checks (PPCs) in assessing gravitational-wave population models, particularly for poorly-constrained parameters like BBH spin tilts. It finds that PPCs on maximum likelihood parameters are more sensitive to model misspecification than event-level PPCs, but in realistic LVK scenarios (e.g., GWTC-3.0-like catalogs), no significant improvement is observed over traditional methods. Applying these checks to GWTC-4.0, the Gaussian Component Spins model is found to under-predict high spin magnitudes and over-predict perfectly anti-aligned tilts.

本文评估了后验预测检验（PPCs）在引力波种群模型检验中的有效性，特别是针对如双黑洞自旋倾角等约束较差的参数。研究发现，基于最大似然参数的PPC比事件级PPC更敏感于模型误设；但在类似GWTC-3.0的实际情景中，替代方法并未显著优于传统PPC。将这些检验应用于GWTC-4.0时发现，其中使用的高斯分量自旋模型低估了大自旋幅度的双黑洞，并高估了完全反对齐的倾角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Accurate population inference in gravitational-wave astronomy requires reliable model assessment tools. Traditional posterior predictive checks (PPCs) can fail when single-event posteriors are dominated by priors, especially for parameters with large uncertainties like BBH spin tilts. This motivates the exploration of alternative PPC methods that are more robust to such limitations.

在引力波天文学中，准确的种群推断需要可靠的模型评估工具。传统的后验预测检验（PPCs）在单事件后验受先验主导时可能失效，尤其是在如双黑洞自旋倾角等不确定性较大的参数上。这促使我们探索对此类限制更具鲁棒性的替代PPC方法。

Method: The authors compare several variants of PPCs: traditional event-level PPCs using posterior samples, data-level PPCs using maximum likelihood estimates, partial predictive checks, and split predictive checks. They assess these methods using simulated GWTC-3.0-like catalogs under controlled model misspecifications. They then apply all PPC variants to real data from the GWTC-4.0 catalog to evaluate the Gaussian Component Spins model for spin magnitude and tilt distributions.

作者比较了多种PPC变体：使用后验样本的传统事件级PPC、使用最大似然估计的数据级PPC、部分预测检验和分割预测检验。他们通过模拟类似GWTC-3.0的星表并在受控的模型误设下评估这些方法。然后将所有PPC变体应用于GWTC-4.0目录的真实数据，以评估自旋幅度和倾角分布的高斯分量自旋模型。

Result: Data-level PPCs based on maximum likelihood parameters are consistently more powerful in detecting model misspecification than event-level PPCs, regardless of measurement uncertainty. However, when applied to realistic simulated catalogs resembling GWTC-3.0, none of the alternative PPCs outperform traditional ones significantly, suggesting that current data lack sufficient information to detect spin tilt model errors. In GWTC-4.0, the Gaussian Component Spins model is shown to under-predict BBHs with large spin magnitudes ($\chi \gtrsim 0.6$) and over-predict those with perfectly anti-aligned tilts ($\cos t_1, \cos t_2 \approx -1$).

基于最大似然参数的数据级PPC在检测模型误设方面始终比事件级PPC更有效，且不受测量不确定性的限制。然而，在应用于类似GWTC-3.0的现实模拟星表时，所有替代PPC均未显著优于传统方法，表明当前数据缺乏足够信息来检测自旋倾角模型误差。在GWTC-4.0中，高斯分量自旋模型被发现低估了大自旋幅度（$\chi \gtrsim 0.6$）的双黑洞，并高估了完全反对齐倾角（$\cos t_1, \cos t_2 \approx -1$）的情况。

Conclusion: While maximum likelihood-based PPCs are theoretically superior for detecting model misspecification, their practical advantage is limited by current observational sensitivity. For BBH spin properties in LVK data, even improved PPCs cannot overcome the lack of constraining power in the data. Nevertheless, applying these checks to GWTC-4.0 reveals clear discrepancies in the Gaussian Component Spins model, suggesting specific directions for model improvement—particularly in modeling extreme spin configurations.

尽管基于最大似然的PPC在理论上更优，但其实际优势受限于当前观测灵敏度。对于LVK数据中的双黑洞自旋特性，即使改进后的PPC也无法克服数据约束力不足的问题。然而，将这些检验应用于GWTC-4.0揭示了高斯分量自旋模型中的明显偏差，提示了模型改进的具体方向——特别是在极端自旋构型的建模方面。

Abstract: When selecting a model to characterize an astrophysical population, it is crucial to assess whether that model fits the data and, if not, how it can be improved. To this end, posterior predictive checks (PPCs) are a widely-used statistical test of model fit when inferring gravitational-wave source populations. However, PPCs exhibit limitations when assessing single-event parameters with large measurement uncertainty, like the spin tilt angles of the binary black holes (BBHs) observable with the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) detectors. When single-event inference is prior-dominated, traditional PPCs fail to flag even very poor model fits. In this work, we assess the efficacy of various alternative PPCs on poorly-constrained parameters. We compare PPCs conducted on event- vs.~data-level parameters (e.g. posterior samples vs. maximum likelihood points), and explore two additional event-level PPCs: partial predictive checks and split predictive checks. Independent of measurement uncertainty, we find that PPCs on maximum likelihood parameters are always more discerning of model misspecification than any event-level PPC. However, when investigating simulated GWTC-3.0-like catalogs, none of the alternative PPCs show significant improvement over those traditionally used, indicating that at that sensitivity, any limited information in the data about spin tilts is insufficient to diagnose model misspecification.Finally, we apply our suite of PPCs to the spin magnitude and tilt distributions inferred in the most recent LVK catalog, GWTC-4.0. We conclude that the Gaussian Component Spins model used therein under-predicts BBHs with large spin magnitudes and over-predicts those with perfectly anti-aligned tilts.

</details>


### [15] [Algebraic approach to quantum gravity IV: applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06118)
*Shahn Majid*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper introduces quantum spacetime and quantum Riemannian geometry as tools in theoretical physics, highlighting recent advances such as vacuum energy calculations in a single-plaquette quantum gravity model, derivation of the Kaluza-Klein ansatz from quantum spacetime principles, lattice-based Noether charges, and a new generally covariant formulation of quantum mechanics with applications to black holes. A novel phase transition in Euclidean quantum gravity on a 4-pointed star is also reported.

本文介绍了量子时空和量子黎曼几何在理论物理中的应用，重点介绍了若干近期进展，包括单 plaquette 量子引力模型中时空曲率涨落的真空能计算、由量子时空原理导出的Kaluza-Klein ansatz、基于格点的诺特定理守恒荷、以及适用于广义相对论的新的广义协变量子力学，并给出了黑洞情形下的初步有趣结果。文中还报告了在4-顶点星形图上欧几里得量子引力的一个新相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a mathematically consistent framework for quantum spacetime and quantum geometry that can address fundamental issues in quantum gravity, such as the nature of vacuum fluctuations, symmetry reduction (e.g., Kaluza-Klein), conservation laws in discrete settings, and the formulation of quantum mechanics in curved and quantum spacetimes.

本文的动机是建立一个数学上自洽的量子时空与量子几何框架，以解决量子引力中的基本问题，如真空涨落的本质、对称性约化（例如Kaluza-Klein）、离散背景下的守恒律，以及在弯曲和量子时空中构建量子力学的形式体系。

Method: The method employs quantum Riemannian geometry on discrete or finite spacetime models, including lattice and single-plaquette formulations. Variational calculus on discrete spaces is used to derive conserved Noether currents. A new theory of geodesics—both classical and quantum—is constructed to enable a generally covariant formulation of quantum mechanics. Euclidean path integral techniques are applied to study phase structure in quantum gravity models.

该方法采用离散或有限时空上的量子黎曼几何，包括格点和单plaquette形式体系。利用离散空间上的变分计算推导守恒的诺特流。构建了一套新的经典与量子测地线理论，以实现广义协变的量子力学形式。应用欧几里得路径积分技术研究量子引力模型的相结构。

Result: Key results include: (1) computation of vacuum energy from spacetime curvature fluctuations in a single-plaquette model; (2) emergence of the Kaluza-Klein ansatz from quantum spacetime structure; (3) exactly conserved Noether charges on lattices; (4) a new theory of quantum geodesics leading to generally covariant quantum mechanics with black-hole applications; (5) discovery of a phase transition in Euclidean quantum gravity on a 4-pointed star graph.

主要结果包括：(1) 在单plaquette模型中计算出由时空曲率涨落导致的真空能；(2) 从量子时空结构中自然导出Kaluza-Klein ansatz；(3) 在格点上获得精确守恒的诺特荷；(4) 提出新的量子测地线理论，进而发展出适用于广义相对论的广义协变量子力学，并应用于黑洞情形；(5) 发现4-顶点星形图上欧几里得量子引力存在相变。

Conclusion: Quantum spacetime and quantum Riemannian geometry offer a promising framework for unifying quantum mechanics and gravity. The derived structures—such as conserved charges, emergent Kaluza-Klein geometries, and generally covariant quantum dynamics—suggest deep connections between discrete quantum geometry and continuum physics. The observed phase transition indicates rich non-perturbative behavior in simple quantum gravity models, motivating further exploration of quantum geometry in both Euclidean and Lorentzian settings.

量子时空与量子黎曼几何为统一量子力学与引力提供了有前景的框架。所导出的结构——如守恒荷、涌现的Kaluza-Klein几何、广义协变量子动力学——表明离散量子几何与连续物理之间存在深刻联系。所观察到的相变揭示了简单量子引力模型中丰富的非微扰行为，激励未来在欧几里得与洛伦兹背景下进一步探索量子几何。

Abstract: We provide a relatively self-contained introduction to the application of quantum spacetime and quantum Riemannian geometry to theoretical physics. Recent successes include calculation of the vacuum energy of spacetime curvature fluctuations in a single-plaquette model of quantum gravity, derivation of the Kaluza-Klein ansatz as a consequence of quantum spacetime, exactly conserved Noether charges from variational calculus on a lattice, and a new theory of classical and quantum geodesics. The latter leads to a theory of generally covariant quantum mechanics applicable in General Relativity with intriguing first results for the case of a black-hole. We discuss several open problems past and present, and how they might be addressed going forward. New results include a phase transition for Euclidean quantum gravity on a 4-pointed star.
