### [16] [A Survey through Conformal Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06120)
*Tahereh Aeenehvand,Ahmad Shariati*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper revisits conformal time $\eta$ in a spatially flat Friedmann--Robertson--Walker (FRW) universe using a simplified $1+1$-dimensional framework to clarify the relationships between cosmic time $t$, conformal time $\eta$, and the scale factor $a(t)$. It examines how these quantities influence particle geodesics and spacetime curvature in radiation-dominated, matter-dominated, and de Sitter universes. An affine-parameter formalism is developed for general spatially flat conformal metrics, with extension to $3+1$ dimensions outlined.

本文在空间平坦的Friedmann–Robertson–Walker（FRW）宇宙中重新审视共形时间$\eta$，采用简化的$1+1$维框架来阐明宇宙时间$t$、共形时间$\eta$和尺度因子$a(t)$之间的关系。研究这些量如何影响辐射主导、物质主导及纯真空de Sitter宇宙中的粒子测地线和时空曲率。文章为一般空间平坦共形度规建立了仿射参数形式，并概述了向$3+1$维的推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a clear, pedagogical understanding of the role of conformal time $\eta$ in cosmological spacetimes, especially how the relation $dt = a(\eta)d\eta$ governs both the geometry (curvature) and dynamics (geodesics) of expanding universes. By reducing to $1+1$ dimensions, the authors aim to make the mathematical structure transparent without sacrificing conceptual accuracy, clarifying common confusions about conformal time and its physical interpretation.

动机是提供对共形时间$\eta$在宇宙学时空中作用的清晰教学性理解，特别是关系式$dt = a(\eta)d\eta$如何支配膨胀宇宙的几何（曲率）和动力学（测地线）。通过降至$1+1$维，作者旨在使数学结构透明而不牺牲概念准确性，澄清关于共形时间及其物理诠释的常见误解。

Method: The method employs a $1+1$-dimensional spatially flat FRW metric $ds^2 = a^2(\eta)(-d\eta^2 + dx^2)$, where the transformation between cosmic and conformal time is explicitly used. The paper derives geodesic equations using the affine parameter formalism, computes the Ricci scalar $R = 2a^{-2}(\eta)(\partial_\eta^2 a)$, and analyzes the behavior of freely falling particles in radiation-, matter-, and vacuum-dominated eras. The treatment distinguishes exact solutions for $a(\eta)$ in each case and discusses their geometric implications.

方法采用$1+1$维空间平坦的FRW度规$ds^2 = a^2(\eta)(-d\eta^2 + dx^2)$，显式使用宇宙时间与共形时间之间的变换。论文利用仿射参数形式推导测地线方程，计算Ricci标量$R = 2a^{-2}(\eta)(\partial_\eta^2 a)$，并分析辐射主导、物质主导和真空主导时期自由下落粒子的行为。该方法区分每种情形下$a(\eta)$的精确解，并讨论其几何含义。

Result: The paper shows that different cosmic histories (radiation, matter, de Sitter) lead to distinct functional forms of $a(\eta)$, which in turn produce qualitatively different geodesic structures and curvature behaviors. For example, in the radiation-dominated case, $a \propto \eta$, leading to flat spacetime; in matter domination, $a \propto \eta^2$, yielding positive curvature; and in de Sitter space, $a \propto -1/\eta$, resulting in constant negative curvature. The affine parameter formalism is generalized for arbitrary $a(\eta)$, and the extension to $3+1$ dimensions is shown to preserve the same structural insights.

论文表明不同的宇宙历史（辐射、物质、de Sitter）导致$a(\eta)$的不同函数形式，进而产生定性上不同的测地线结构和曲率行为。例如，在辐射主导情况下，$a \propto \eta$，对应平坦时空；在物质主导下，$a \propto \eta^2$，产生正曲率；而在de Sitter空间中，$a \propto -1/\eta$，导致常负曲率。仿射参数形式被推广至任意$a(\eta)$，且向$3+1$维的扩展保持了相同的结构洞察。

Conclusion: Conformal time $\eta$ provides a powerful tool for analyzing cosmological spacetimes, particularly in simplifying the study of geodesics and curvature. The $1+1$-dimensional setting serves as an effective pedagogical model that captures essential features of higher-dimensional cosmology. The explicit treatment of exact solutions underscores how the interplay between $a(t)$ and $\eta$ shapes both geometry and dynamics, offering clarity on the physical meaning of conformal coordinates in expanding universes.

共形时间$\eta$为分析宇宙学时空提供了有力工具，特别是在简化测地线和曲率研究方面。$1+1$维设定作为一个有效的教学模型，捕捉了高维宇宙学的基本特征。对精确解的显式处理强调了$a(t)$与$\eta$之间相互作用如何塑造几何与动力学，从而阐明了膨胀宇宙中共形坐标的物理意义。

Abstract: We revisit conformal time $η$ in a spatially flat Friedmann--Robertson--Walker universe and use a $1+1$-dimensional setting as a technically transparent pedagogical arena. Our purpose is to clarify the relation among cosmic time $t$, conformal time $η$, and the scale factor $a(t)$, and then to follow how this relation governs the geodesics of freely moving particles and the curvature of the corresponding manifold. The radiation-dominated, matter-dominated, and exact vacuum-only de Sitter cases are treated separately, because each of them produces a distinct conformal-time dependence and therefore a distinct geodesic structure. We then write the affine-parameter formalism in a form that is genuinely general for any spatially flat conformal metric, and we record the straightforward extension to the spatially flat $3+1$ case. The presentation remains elementary in spirit, but the notation, the curvature formulas, and the de Sitter interpretation are kept explicit.

### [17] [Absorption and quasinormal modes by rotating acoustic black holes in Lorentz-violating background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06137)
*J. A. V. Campos,M. A. Anacleto,F. A. Brito,E. Passos,Amilcar R. Queiroz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This study explores the impact of Lorentz symmetry violation on the absorption cross section and quasinormal modes of a rotating acoustic black hole in (2+1) dimensions.

本研究探讨了洛伦兹对称性破缺对(2+1)维旋转声学黑洞吸收截面和准正规模的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand how Lorentz symmetry breaking affects key physical properties of analogue black holes, such as scattering and ringdown behavior, in lower-dimensional gravitational analogues.

为了理解洛伦兹对称性破缺如何影响类比黑洞的关键物理性质（如散射和铃宕行为）在低维引力类比系统中的表现。

Method: Analytical analysis of the absorption cross section in low- and high-frequency limits, combined with numerical integration of the radial equation; computation of quasinormal modes using appropriate boundary conditions in the presence of Lorentz violation.

在低频和高频极限下对吸收截面进行解析分析，并结合径向方程的数值积分；在存在洛伦兹破缺的情况下，利用适当的边界条件计算准正规模。

Result: Lorentz violation enhances the absorption cross section across all energy scales, with the rotation parameter $B$ contributing even at low frequencies. For quasinormal modes, symmetry breaking reduces the real part of the frequencies and increases the magnitude of the imaginary part, leading to faster damping of oscillations.

洛伦兹破缺在所有能量尺度上增强了吸收截面，且旋转参数$B$即使在低频下也有所贡献。对于准正规模，对称性破缺减小了频率的实部并增大了虚部的幅值，导致振荡衰减更快。

Conclusion: Lorentz symmetry violation has significant observable effects on both the scattering and ringdown characteristics of rotating acoustic black holes in (2+1) dimensions, suggesting its potential detectability in analogue gravity experiments.

洛伦兹对称性破缺对(2+1)维旋转声学黑洞的散射和铃宕特性具有显著可观测效应，表明其在类比引力实验中可能被探测到。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the effects of Lorentz symmetry violation on the absorption cross section and quasinormal modes of a rotating acoustic black hole in (2+1) dimensions. The absorption cross section was analyzed analytically, using the low and high frequency regimes, and numerically, through integration of the radial equation. The results showed that Lorentz violation increases the absorption cross section at all energy scales, with a contribution from the rotation parameter $B$ appearing even in the low frequency regime. For the quasinormal modes, we observed that symmetry breaking decreases the real part of the frequencies and increases the magnitude of the corresponding imaginary part, indicating a faster damping of the oscillations.

### [18] [Feynman integral reduction with intersection theory made simple](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05025)
*Li-Hong Huang,Yan-Qing Ma,Ziwen Wang,Li Lin Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper introduces a new method for reducing $L$-loop Feynman integrals using the branch representation in intersection theory, requiring at most $(3L-3)$ variables—significantly fewer than traditional methods—leading to improved computational efficiency, especially for multi-leg processes.

本文引入了一种基于分支表示和交截理论的新方法来约化$L$-圈费曼积分，最多只需$(3L-3)$个变量，相较于传统方法显著减少了变量数量，尤其提升了多腿过程的计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional integration-by-parts (IBP) methods and standard intersection theory approaches for Feynman integral reduction suffer from high computational complexity, particularly due to the large number of variables scaling with propagators in multi-loop and multi-leg diagrams. This limits their practical applicability. The motivation is to develop a more efficient reduction framework that drastically reduces the number of variables involved.

传统的分部积分（IBP）方法和标准交截理论在费曼积分约化中面临高计算复杂度的问题，尤其是在多圈多腿图中变量数随传播子数量增长，限制了实际应用。因此，亟需一种能大幅减少变量数的高效约化框架。

Method: The authors employ the recently developed \textit{branch representation} of Feynman integrals within the framework of intersection theory. In this representation, the reduction of $L$-loop integrals is formulated via intersection numbers computed in a space of at most $(3L-3)$ variables, independent of the number of external legs or propagators. The method leverages the geometric structure of the integrand to minimize the algebraic complexity.

作者在交截理论框架下采用新近发展的\textit{分支表示}（branch representation），将$L$-圈积分的约化表述为最多$(3L-3)$个变量空间中的交截数计算，该变量数与外腿或传播子数量无关。该方法利用被积函数的几何结构以最小化代数复杂度。

Result: Explicit calculations of two-loop diagrams show that the proposed method achieves correct integral reductions with far fewer variables than conventional approaches. It outperforms both standard intersection-theory computations and traditional IBP-based reduction in terms of speed and resource usage, demonstrating a substantial gain in computational efficiency.

通过对双圈图的显式计算表明，新方法以远少于传统方法的变量实现了正确的积分约化，在计算速度和资源使用上优于标准交截理论和传统基于IBP的约化方法，展现出显著的计算效率提升。

Conclusion: The branch representation enables a universal and efficient reduction of $L$-loop Feynman integrals by limiting the variable count to $(3L-3)$, marking a major advancement in the application of intersection theory to perturbative quantum field theory. This opens the door to tackling previously intractable multi-loop, multi-leg amplitudes.

分支表示通过将变量数限制在$(3L-3)$内，实现了$L$-圈费曼积分的普适高效约化，标志着交截理论在微扰量子场论应用中的一大进步，为处理以往难以解决的多圈多腿振幅开辟了道路。

Abstract: Feynman integral reduction based on intersection theory provides an alternative to the traditional integration-by-parts method, yet its practical application has been constrained by the large number of variables required in the computation. In this Letter, we demonstrate that by employing the recently introduced branch representation, the reduction of $L$-loop Feynman integrals with an arbitrary number of external legs can be achieved through the computation of at most $(3L-3)$-variable intersection numbers. This constitutes a significant simplification compared to existing approaches, particularly for multi-leg integrals where the number of variables in conventional methods scales with the total number of propagators. We validate the proposed method through explicit calculations of two-loop diagrams, demonstrating substantial improvements in computational efficiency relative to both traditional intersection-theory approaches and standard integration-by-parts reduction techniques.

</details>


### [19] [Quantum Solitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05026)
*Robie A. Hennigar,Ayan K. Patra,Simon F. Ross*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We construct geometries describing quantum backreaction of thermal fields in AdS$_3$ using branes in a 4D AdS C-metric, yielding two families of solutions—negative and positive asymptotic mass—interpreted via semiclassical gravity on the brane coupled to a dual CFT; the thermodynamics and first law are realized in a two-brane setup involving quantum BTZ and soliton branes.

我们利用四维AdS C-度规中的膜构造描述了AdS₃中热场量子反作用的几何，得到两类解——负和正渐近质量，通过膜上半经典引力与对偶CFT耦合进行解释；热力学和第一定律在包含量子BTZ膜和量子孤子膜的双膜设置中实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand how quantum effects of thermal conformal fields backreact on spacetime geometry in AdS$_3$, particularly extending previous studies of quantum-corrected BTZ black holes via a novel brane construction in higher-dimensional gravity.

旨在理解共形热场的量子效应如何在AdS₃中反作用于时空几何，特别是通过高维引力中的新膜构造扩展此前关于量子修正BTZ黑洞的研究。

Method: We derive solutions from branes embedded in a four-dimensional AdS C-metric, interpreting them as semiclassical geometries on the brane where 3D gravity is coupled to a CFT (holographically dual to the 4D bulk). A double analytic continuation relates this setup to prior quantum BTZ constructions. Thermodynamics is analyzed in a two-brane system including both the quantum BTZ brane and the new quantum soliton brane.

我们从嵌入四维AdS C-度规中的膜导出解，并将其解释为膜上的半经典几何，其中三维引力与CFT耦合（全息对偶于四维体）；通过双重解析延拓将此构造与先前的量子BTZ研究联系起来；热力学分析基于包含量子BTZ膜和新量子孤子膜的双膜系统。

Result: Two families of solutions are found: (1) negative asymptotic mass solutions representing thermal CFT backreaction on global AdS$_3$; (2) positive mass solutions where a classical horizon is replaced by a smooth origin upon backreaction. The brane geometry remains regular without singularities. Thermodynamic analysis confirms a consistent first law in the two-brane setup.

发现两类解：(1) 负渐近质量解，表示热CFT对全局AdS₃的反作用；(2) 正质量解，其经典视界在反作用后被光滑原点取代；膜几何保持正则无奇性；热力学分析证实双膜设置中存在一致的第一定律。

Conclusion: The brane-in-C-metric construction provides a controlled framework for studying quantum backreaction in AdS$_3$, yielding regular geometries and a well-defined thermodynamic interpretation via a two-brane system that unifies quantum solitons and quantum black holes within the EFTofLSS and holographic renormalization group.

C-度规中的膜构造为研究AdS₃中的量子反作用提供了可控框架，通过双膜系统获得正则几何和明确定义的热力学诠释，将量子孤子与量子黑洞统一于EFTofLSS和全息重整化群之中。

Abstract: We construct geometries describing the quantum backreaction of thermal fields in AdS$_3$. The solutions are obtained from branes in a four-dimensional AdS C-metric. They can be viewed as solutions of the semiclassical effective theory on the brane, which couples three-dimensional gravity to the CFT dual to the four-dimensional bulk. This brane construction is related by a double analytic continuation to earlier studies of quantum BTZ solutions. There are two families of solutions, labelled by the asymptotic mass. Solutions with negative mass correspond to the back-reaction of a thermal CFT state on global AdS$_3$. Solutions with positive mass have a horizon for zero back-reaction, which is replaced by a smooth origin in the back-reacted solution. We study the thermodynamics and first law on the brane, which we argue is realised in a two-brane setup where we include both the quantum BTZ brane and our quantum soliton brane.

</details>


### [20] [Worldline Images for Yang-Mills Theory within Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05082)
*Santiago Christiansen Murguizur,Lucas Manzo,Pablo Pisani*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We develop a worldline method using the image technique to study the effective action in Yang-Mills theories on manifolds with boundaries, incorporating relative and absolute boundary conditions for both vector and ghost fields. As applications, we compute the first three Seeley-DeWitt coefficients and calculate the gluon production rate in a chromoelectric field background near a boundary.

我们发展了一种基于像方法的世界线技术，用于研究具有边界的流形上杨-米尔斯理论的有效作用量，考虑了矢量场和鬼场的相对与绝对边界条件。作为应用，我们计算了前三个Seeley-DeWitt系数，并计算了在边界存在下色电场背景中的胶子产生率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Yang-Mills theories in the presence of boundaries require careful treatment of boundary conditions to preserve gauge invariance and ensure consistent quantization. Mixed boundary conditions such as relative and absolute ones are important in topological field theories and anomaly analysis, yet their implementation in quantum effective actions remains technically challenging. A worldline approach offers a powerful path-integral framework to systematically include boundary effects.

在存在边界的情况下，杨-米尔斯理论需要仔细处理边界条件以保持规范不变性并确保一致的量子化。相对和绝对等混合边界条件在拓扑场论和反常分析中很重要，但其在量子有效作用量中的实现仍具技术挑战。世界线方法为系统包含边界效应提供了一个强大的路径积分框架。

Method: We employ the worldline formalism combined with the method of images to model quantum fluctuations on manifolds with planar boundaries. The effective action is expressed as a path integral over closed worldlines, with boundary conditions implemented via image contributions. We apply this to vector and ghost fields under relative and absolute boundary conditions. The Seeley-DeWitt coefficients are extracted from the short-time expansion of the heat kernel. Gluon production rates are computed using the proper-time representation of the effective action in a constant chromoelectric field.

我们采用结合像方法的世界线形式体系，对具有平面边界的流形上的量子涨落进行建模。有效作用量被表示为闭合世界线上的路径积分，边界条件通过像贡献实现。我们将此方法应用于满足相对和绝对边界条件的矢量场和鬼场。Seeley-DeWitt系数从热核的短时间展开中提取。胶子产生率则通过在恒定色电场中有效作用量的固有时表示来计算。

Result: We successfully derive the first three Seeley-DeWitt coefficients $a_0$, $a_1$, and $a_2$ for both relative and absolute boundary conditions, confirming consistency with known heat kernel results. Using the worldline formalism, we obtain a finite expression for the imaginary part of the effective action, from which the gluon pair production rate per unit volume and time is calculated in the presence of a chromoelectric field and a boundary. The production rate shows dependence on the distance from the boundary and the type of boundary condition imposed.

我们成功推导了相对和绝对边界条件下前三个Seeley-DeWitt系数$a_0$、$a_1$和$a_2$，验证了与已知热核结果的一致性。利用世界线形式体系，我们得到了有效作用量虚部的有限表达式，由此计算出色电场和边界存在下的单位体积单位时间胶子对产生率。该产生率依赖于到边界的距离以及所施加的边界条件类型。

Conclusion: The worldline method combined with the method of images provides a robust and efficient framework for computing quantum effects in gauge theories on manifolds with boundaries. It correctly reproduces known geometric invariants (via Seeley-DeWitt coefficients) and enables physical predictions such as boundary-dependent gluon production, highlighting the role of boundaries in non-Abelian vacuum structure and particle creation.

结合像方法的世界线方法为计算具有边界流形上规范理论的量子效应提供了一个稳健且高效的研究框架。它不仅能正确复现已知几何不变量（通过Seeley-DeWitt系数），还能做出物理预测，例如依赖于边界的胶子产生，突显了边界在非阿贝尔真空结构和粒子产生中的作用。

Abstract: In this article we develop a worldline technique based on the method of images to study the effective action associated to Yang-Mills theories on manifolds with boundaries. We consider the possibility of having either relative or absolute boundary conditions, which are particular types of mixed boundary conditions. Both vector fields and ghost fields are taken into account in this analysis. As a check of our construction, we compute the first three Seeley-DeWitt coefficients of the heat kernel asymptotics. Finally, we employ our technique to calculate the rate of gluon production due to a chromoelectric field background in the presence of a boundary.

### [21] [Weak-Field Limits of Black Hole Metrics from the KMOC formalism: Schwarzschild, Kerr, Reissner-Nordström, and Kerr-Newman](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05094)
*Jacobo Hernández C*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates how the weak-field limits of four classical black hole metrics—Schwarzschild, Kerr, Reissner-Nordström, and Kerr–Newman—can be systematically derived using the KMOC (Kosower-Maybee-O'Connell) formalism by computing scattering amplitudes and extracting classical observables such as momentum impulses. The metric components are reconstructed to leading order in $ G $, $ a $, and $ Q^2 $, with special attention to interference effects in the Kerr–Newman case.

本文展示了如何通过KMOC（Kosower-Maybee-O'Connell）形式体系，利用散射振幅计算并提取动量冲量等经典可观测量，系统地推导出四种经典黑洞度规（Schwarzschild、Kerr、Reissner-Nordström和Kerr-Newman）的弱场极限。度规分量在$ G $、$ a $和$ Q^2 $的领头阶被重构，特别关注了Kerr-Newman情况下的干涉效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To demonstrate that classical black hole spacetimes can be recovered from quantum scattering amplitudes using the KMOC formalism, thereby strengthening the connection between quantum field theory and classical general relativity. The inclusion of both spin and charge allows for testing the framework in more physically rich settings, particularly in the presence of both gravitational and electromagnetic interactions.

旨在证明可以通过KMOC形式体系从量子散射振幅中恢复经典黑洞时空，从而加强量子场论与经典广义相对论之间的联系。包含自旋和电荷可允许在更丰富的物理场景下测试该框架，特别是在同时存在引力和电磁相互作用的情况下。

Method: Using three-point amplitudes with exponential spin structure for gravitons and photons, four-point scattering amplitudes are computed in the weak-field limit. The classical momentum impulse on a probe particle is extracted via the KMOC formula. This impulse is then matched to the geodesic motion in an ansatz metric, allowing reconstruction of the metric components $ g_{\mu\nu} $ to leading order in $ G $, $ a $ (angular momentum), and $ Q^2 $ (charge). Interference terms between gravity and electromagnetism are retained in the Kerr–Newman case.

使用具有指数型自旋结构的引力子和光子三点振幅，在弱场极限下计算四点散射振幅。通过KMOC公式提取探测粒子上的经典动量冲量。将此冲量与试探度规中的测地线运动匹配，从而在$ G $、$ a $（角动量）和$ Q^2 $（电荷）的领头阶重构度规分量$ g_{\mu\nu} $。在Kerr-Newman情况下保留引力与电磁之间的干涉项。

Result: The weak-field expansions of the Schwarzschild, Kerr, Reissner-Nordström, and Kerr–Newman metrics are successfully reproduced to leading order. Notably, in the Kerr–Newman case, a novel $ \frac{Q^2 a}{r^3} $ contribution to $ g_{t\phi} $ arises from interference between gravitational and electromagnetic interactions, which is absent in the pure Kerr or Reissner-Nordström limits. All results match known full metrics in the weak-field regime and are consistent with prior amplitude-based derivations (e.g., arXiv:1907.00431, arXiv:1908.04342).

成功重现了Schwarzschild、Kerr、Reissner-Nordström和Kerr-Newman度规的弱场展开式至领头阶。值得注意的是，在Kerr-Newman情况下，引力与电磁相互作用的干涉产生了对$ g_{t\phi} $的新型$ \frac{Q^2 a}{r^3} $贡献，这在纯Kerr或Reissner-Nordström极限中不存在。所有结果在弱场区域与已知完整度规一致，并与先前基于振幅的推导一致（例如arXiv:1907.00431，arXiv:1908.04342）。

Conclusion: The KMOC formalism provides a powerful and systematic method to derive classical spacetime geometries from quantum scattering amplitudes, even in the presence of charge and spin. The appearance of interference effects in the Kerr–Newman metric highlights the ability of the formalism to capture subtle classical corrections arising from mixed interactions. However, only weak-field expansions are obtained—not the full non-linear solutions.

KMOC形式体系提供了一种强大而系统的方法，即使在存在电荷和自旋的情况下，也能从量子散射振幅中推导出经典时空几何。Kerr-Newman度规中干涉效应的出现突显了该形式体系捕捉混合相互作用产生的微妙经典修正的能力。然而，仅得到了弱场展开式，而非完整的非线性解。

Abstract: The KMOC (Kosower-Maybee-O'Connell) formalism establishes a bridge between quantum scattering amplitudes and classical observables in gravitational systems. In this work, we show how the weak-field limits of the four classical black hole metrics - Schwarzschild, Kerr, Reissner-Nordstrom, and Kerr-Newman - can be reproduced within this formalism. Starting from three-point amplitudes with exponential spin structure for both gravitational and electromagnetic interactions, we compute four-point scattering amplitudes and extract the momentum impulse via the KMOC formula. Matching these results with geodesic motion in a general metric allows us to reconstruct the metric components to leading order in G, a, and Q^2. For the Kerr-Newman case, we include interference terms between gravitational and electromagnetic interactions, which produce a Q^2 a/r^3 contribution to g_{tφ} that does not appear in the Kerr or Reissner-Nordstrom weak-field limits separately. Our results are consistent with those of arXiv:1907.00431 [hep-th], where the Kerr-Newman metric is derived from minimal coupling amplitudes using the KMOC formalism arXiv:1908.04342 [hep-th]. All results are verified through their consistency with the well-known full metrics, though we emphasize that the KMOC formalism as applied here reproduces only the weak-field expansions, not the complete non-linear solutions.

### [22] [Untwisting the double copy: the zeroth copy as an optical seed](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05103)
*Damien A. Easson,Michael J. Falato*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper establishes a historical optical foundation for stationary vacuum Kerr–Schild spacetimes on a flat background and reformulates it using modern double-copy theory. A complex optical seed $\rho = -\theta - i\omega$, constructed from the expansion $\theta$ and signed twist $\omega$ of the Kerr–Schild null congruence, serves as a fundamental organizing object: it is harmonic, its inverse satisfies an eikonal equation, and it algebraically reconstructs the congruence. This seed acts as a normalized zeroth-copy field in the double-copy framework, with its real part giving the Kerr–Schild potential and its gradient producing the single-copy gauge field strength. This provides a spacetime-based realization—without twistor methods—of how a single complex scalar encodes gravity, gauge, and zeroth-copy data.

本文建立了静止真空Kerr–Schild时空在平直背景下的历史光学基础，并用现代双复制理论重新表述。一个由Kerr–Schild零测地线 congruence 的膨胀 $\theta$ 和符号化的扭率 $\omega$ 构成的复光学种子 $\rho = -\theta - i\omega$ 作为核心组织对象：它是调和的，其逆满足程差方程，并能代数地重构该测地线 congruence。此种子在双复制框架中充当归一化的零次复制场，其实部给出Kerr–Schild势，梯度生成单次复制规范场强。该构造无需旋量方法，即实现了单一复标量如何编码引力、规范场及零次复制几何信息的时空实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to bridge classical geometric optics interpretations of Kerr–Schild spacetimes with the modern double-copy paradigm in theoretical physics, which relates gravitational theories to gauge theories via algebraic structures. Historically, Kerr–Schild solutions were understood through null congruences with special optical properties (expansion and twist). The authors aim to reinterpret these geometric features in terms of modern amplitudes-based frameworks like the double copy, particularly exploring how a single complex scalar (the optical seed) can unify descriptions of gravity, gauge fields, and the so-called zeroth copy without relying on twistor theory.

动机是将Kerr–Schild时空的经典几何光学解释与现代双复制范式联系起来，后者通过代数结构将引力理论与规范理论关联。历史上，Kerr–Schild解通过具有特殊光学性质（膨胀和扭率）的零测地线来理解。作者旨在用基于散射振幅的现代框架（如双复制）重新解释这些几何特征，特别是探索单一复标量（光学种子）如何统一描述引力、规范场和所谓的零次复制，而不依赖旋量理论。

Method: The method relies on analyzing stationary vacuum Kerr–Schild spacetimes admitting a flat background and a geodesic, shear-free null congruence. The key object introduced is the complex scalar $\rho = -\theta - i\omega$, where $\theta$ is the expansion and $\omega$ the signed twist of the congruence. It is shown that $\rho$ is harmonic ($\Box \rho = 0$) and that $1/\rho$ satisfies the eikonal equation $(\partial_\mu (1/\rho)) (\partial^\mu (1/\rho)) = 0$, allowing reconstruction of the null vector field. The authors then connect this to the double-copy formalism by identifying $1/\rho$ as a representative of the zeroth-copy scalar field, the real part $-\theta$ as the Kerr–Schild profile function, and $\partial_\mu \rho$ as generating the field strength of a single-copy gauge field. All constructions are performed directly in spacetime, avoiding twistorial methods.

方法基于分析允许平直背景和测地无剪切零测地线的静止真空Kerr–Schild时空。引入的关键对象是复标量 $\rho = -\theta - i\omega$，其中 $\theta$ 是膨胀，$\omega$ 是符号化扭率。证明了 $\rho$ 是调和的（$\Box \rho = 0$），且 $1/\rho$ 满足程差方程（$(\partial_\mu (1/\rho))(\partial^\mu (1/\rho)) = 0$），从而可重构零矢量场。然后通过将 $1/\rho$ 识别为零次复制标量场的代表，实部 $-\theta$ 作为Kerr–Schild剖面函数，$\partial_\mu \rho$ 生成单次复制规范场强，连接到双复制形式体系。所有构造均在时空中直接完成，避免使用旋量方法。

Result: The main result is that the complex optical seed $\rho = -\theta - i\omega$ completely characterizes the local geometry of stationary vacuum Kerr–Schild spacetimes. It is harmonic, its inverse obeys the eikonal equation, and it reconstructs the null congruence algebraically. In the double-copy interpretation: $1/\rho$ serves as a normalized zeroth-copy field, $\mathrm{Re}(\rho) = -\theta$ gives the Kerr–Schild potential, and $\partial_\mu \rho$ generates the gauge field strength $F_{\mu\nu}$. This establishes a direct, spacetime-level correspondence between classical optical quantities in general relativity and the fields of the double-copy hierarchy, unifying geometric and quantum-inspired frameworks without invoking twistors.

主要结果是复光学种子 $\rho = -\theta - i\omega$ 完全刻画了静止真空Kerr–Schild时空的局部几何。它是调和的，其逆满足程差方程，并能代数重构零测地线。在双复制解释中：$1/\rho$ 作为归一化的零次复制场，$\mathrm{Re}(\rho) = -\theta$ 给出Kerr–Schild势，$\partial_\mu \rho$ 生成规范场强 $F_{\mu\nu}$。这建立了广义相对论中经典光学量与双复制层级场之间的直接时空对应，统一了几何与受量子启发的框架，而无需引入旋量。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the classical optical structure of stationary Kerr–Schild spacetimes is deeply compatible with the modern double-copy framework. A single complex harmonic seed $\rho = -\theta - i\omega$ organizes the full spacetime geometry, the associated gauge field, and the zeroth-copy data. This provides a concrete, spacetime-based realization of the double copy—linking general relativity, gauge theory, and scalar field theory—through purely classical geometric optics, enhancing conceptual understanding and offering new computational pathways in classical and quantum gravity.

论文结论是，静止Kerr–Schild时空的经典光学结构与现代双复制框架高度兼容。单一复调和种子 $\rho = -\theta - i\omega$ 可组织完整的时空几何、相关规范场及零次复制数据。这提供了双复制的具体时空实现——通过纯经典几何光学将广义相对论、规范理论与标量场理论联系起来，增强了概念理解，并为经典与量子引力研究提供了新的计算路径。

Abstract: We present a historical optical foundation for stationary vacuum Kerr--Schild spacetimes on a flat background and interpret it in modern double-copy language. In this setting, a complex optical seed \(ρ=-θ-iω\), built from the expansion and signed twist of the Kerr--Schild congruence, is harmonic, while its inverse obeys an eikonal equation and reconstructs the congruence algebraically. Thus the local stationary geometry is organized by a single complex seed. In the overlap of the stationary Kerr--Schild and Petrov type--D Weyl double-copy framework, this seed furnishes a normalized representative of the zeroth-copy data, while its real part yields the Kerr--Schild profile and its gradient generates the single-copy gauge-field strength. The construction provides, without recourse to twistor methods, a spacetime realization of how a single complex seed builds the congruence, organizes the associated spacetime and gauge fields, and encodes the geometric content of the zeroth copy.

### [23] [The double-logarithmic four-graviton Regge sector as a rank-two twisted period system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05139)
*Agustín Sabio Vera*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper reformulates the double-logarithmic four-graviton Regge sector in $N$-extended supergravity using a rank-two twisted period system, providing a unified framework via first-order differential equations and recursion in $N$, revealing connections to intersection theory and enabling a simple Hermite-polynomial construction for low-even supersymmetry theories.

本文通过秩为二的扭周期系统重构了$N$-扩展超引力中的双对数四引力子Regge区域，利用一阶微分方程和关于$N$的递推关系提供了统一框架，揭示了其与交叉理论的联系，并为低偶数超对称理论给出了简单的Hermite多项式构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To find a more structured and unified description of the four-graviton Regge scattering in $N$-extended supergravity, clarifying the underlying mathematical structure of known Mellin-space solutions and their dependence on the number of supersymmetries $N$.

为了为$N$-扩展超引力中四引力子Regge散射寻找更结构化且统一的描述，阐明已知Mellin空间解的潜在数学结构及其对超对称数目$N$的依赖性。

Method: The authors recast the known Mellin-space solution, originally expressed in terms of parabolic-cylinder functions, into a rank-two twisted period system defined by two weighted integrals. They derive a pair of first-order differential equations and a recursion relation in $N$, and use intersection theory to explain reduction rules and connect different integral representations (Euler vs. contour integrals).

作者将原本用抛物柱面函数表示的Mellin空间解重新表述为由两个加权积分定义的秩二扭周期系统。他们推导出一对一阶微分方程以及关于$N$的递推关系，并利用交叉理论解释约化规则，连接不同的积分表示（欧拉积分与围道积分）。

Result: A unified rank-two twisted period system is established for all $N$-extended supergravities, with explicit first-order differential equations and an $N$-recursion. The approach clarifies the relationship between Euler and contour integral representations via intersection theory and leads to a simple Hermite-polynomial construction in the cases of $N = 4$ and $N = 6$, highlighting special structures in low-even supersymmetry theories.

为所有$N$-扩展超引力建立了统一的秩二扭周期系统，具有显式的一阶微分方程和关于$N$的递推关系。该方法通过交叉理论阐明了欧拉积分与围道积分表示之间的关系，并在$N = 4$和$N = 6$的情况下导出了简单的Hermite多项式构造，突出了低偶数超对称理论中的特殊结构。

Conclusion: The twisted period system provides a powerful and geometrically natural framework for organizing high-energy gravitational scattering in supergravity, unifying the family of $N$-extended theories, simplifying known results, and revealing new algebraic and recursive structures, particularly for low-even $N$.

扭周期系统为组织超引力中高能引力散射提供了一个强大且几何自然的框架，统一了$N$-扩展理论族，简化了已知结果，并揭示了新的代数与递归结构，尤其针对低偶数$N$的情形。

Abstract: We study the double-logarithmic four-graviton Regge sector in $N$-extended supergravity. Its Mellin-space solution is already known in terms of parabolic-cylinder functions. We show that the same answer can be organized as a rank-two twisted period system, meaning that two closely related weighted integrals determine the full Mellin partial wave. These functions satisfy a simple pair of first-order differential equations and a recursion as the number of supersymmetries $N$ changes. This gives a uniform description of the full supergravity family, clarifies the relation between the positive-ray Euler integral and the earlier contour representation, and reproduces the same reduction rule through intersection theory. The reformulation also makes the special cases with four and six supersymmetries particularly transparent and yields a simple Hermite-polynomial construction for the low-even theories.

### [24] [New-born strings are tensionless](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05173)
*Sudip Karan,Bibhas Ranjan Majhi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: A new physical origin of tensionless strings is discovered by studying string dynamics in a finite-lifetime setting, where the string worldsheet is confined to a causal diamond in 2D Minkowski spacetime. Tensionless strings emerge only at the moment of birth, revealed through the ultra-shrinking limit of the causal diamond, leading to a novel phase with a global ultra-local Carrollian symmetry.

首次在有限寿命时空中构建弦动力学，发现无张力弦的物理起源：仅在弦诞生瞬间出现。通过二维闵可夫斯基时空中的因果金刚石的超收缩极限，揭示了一种具有全局超局部Carroll结构的新无张力弦相。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The conventional formulation of string theory assumes eternal strings propagating in infinite spacetime, which may not reflect realistic or quantum gravitational scenarios involving finite lifetimes or horizons. This work aims to explore string dynamics in finite-lifetime settings—such as those near black hole horizons or cosmological endpoints—to uncover new physical phases, particularly tensionless strings, whose origin has remained elusive within standard frameworks.

传统弦论基于永恒弦在无限时空传播的假设，难以描述涉及有限寿命或视界的现实场景（如黑洞或宇宙学末端）。本文旨在探索有限寿命下的弦动力学，以揭示无张力弦等新物理相的起源。

Method: We formulate string dynamics on a finite inertial worldsheet bounded by a causal diamond in two-dimensional Minkowski spacetime. By analyzing the geometric and conformal structure of this bounded region, we study the limit as the diamond size approaches zero—the 'ultra-shrinking limit'—which corresponds to the birth event of the string. In this limit, the Nambu-Goto action vanishes identically, leading to a tensionless regime. The resulting symmetry structure is analyzed using Carrollian geometry adapted to the null boundaries of the diamond.

在二维闵可夫斯基时空中构造一个被限制在因果金刚石内的惯性世界面，研究其几何与共形结构；通过取金刚石尺寸趋于零的“超收缩极限”（对应弦的诞生时刻），Nambu-Goto作用量严格消失，进入无张力区域，并利用适配于零边界 的Carroll几何分析所得对称结构。

Result: We find that tensionless strings do not persist throughout evolution but emerge exclusively at the moment of birth, when the worldsheet area vanishes. The ultra-shrinking limit yields a new phase of string theory characterized by a global, ultra-local Carrollian symmetry, distinct from previously known tensionless limits. This phase exhibits enhanced symmetries and non-relativistic scaling behavior consistent with Carrollian field theories.

发现无张力弦仅在世界面面积消失的诞生瞬间出现，而非持续存在。超收缩极限导出一种新的弦相，具有全局超局部Carroll对称性，区别于以往已知的无张力极限，展现出增强对称性和符合Carroll场论的非相对论标度行为。

Conclusion: Tensionless strings have a dynamical origin tied to the birth event of strings in finite-lifetime settings. Their emergence is governed by a novel ultra-local Carrollian structure on the shrinking worldsheet, providing a first-principles explanation for tensionless phases in string theory. This framework opens new avenues for understanding quantum gravity near singularities and horizons, where traditional string descriptions break down.

无张力弦的动力学起源源于有限寿命下弦的诞生事件，其出现由收缩世界面上的新型超局部Carroll结构支配，为弦论中的无张力相提供了第一性原理解释。该框架为理解视界与奇点附近的量子引力开辟了新路径。

Abstract: We report a physical origin of tensionless strings, obtained by formulating string dynamics in finite-lifetime settings for the first time. Departing from the conventional paradigm of eternal strings, we construct an inertial worldsheet confined to a finite region of two-dimensional Minkowski spacetime, known as a causal diamond. This reveals a striking result: tensionless strings arise only at the moment of their birth. The ultra-shrinking limit of the diamond worldsheet realizes this birth configuration, thereby uncovering a new tensionless string phase characterized by a global, ultra-local Carrollian structure.

### [25] [Residual Symmetries and Their Algebras in the Kerr-Schild Double Copy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05262)
*B. P. Holton*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The Kerr-Schild double copy (KSDC) does not map residual symmetries between Yang-Mills theory and gravity despite relating classical solutions; while the ansatz admits enlarged symmetry algebras, physical symmetries are recovered only after a cohomological reduction via a Weyl-compensated BRST complex, revealing a fundamental mismatch in symmetry structures.

克尔-席德尔双副本（KSDC）尽管关联了经典解，但并未在杨-米尔斯理论与引力之间建立残余对称性的映射；尽管试探形式具有扩展的对称代数，但物理对称性仅在通过韦尔补偿的BRST复形进行上同调约化后才得以恢复，揭示了杨-米尔斯与引力在残余对称性层面上的基本不匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: It is unclear whether the Kerr-Schild double copy (KSDC), which relates exact solutions in gauge theory and gravity, extends to a deeper correspondence between their underlying symmetry structures. This paper investigates if residual symmetries in the Kerr-Schild ansatz are mapped between Yang-Mills and gravity, addressing a key open question in the double copy program.

目前尚不清楚克尔-席德尔双副本（KSDC）——尽管它关联了规范理论与引力中的精确解——是否能推广为两者潜在对称结构之间的更深层对应关系。本文旨在探究克尔-席德尔试探形式下的残余对称性是否在杨-米尔斯理论与引力之间被映射，以解决双副本计划中的一个关键开放问题。

Method: We analyze the residual symmetries of the Kerr-Schild ansatz in both Yang-Mills theory and general relativity. In gauge theory, we identify an infinite-dimensional algebra of functions along null directions. In gravity, we study residual diffeomorphisms preserving the Kerr-Schild form of the Schwarzschild metric, which generate a conformal algebra on $S^2$ composed of Killing vectors and proper conformal Killing vectors (CKVs). To resolve the apparent contradiction arising from the infinite-dimensionality of CKVs, we construct a Weyl-compensated BRST complex and compute its cohomology.

我们在杨-米尔斯理论和广义相对论中分析了克尔-席德尔试探形式的残余对称性。在规范理论中，我们识别出沿零方向的无限维函数代数。在引力中，我们研究保持史瓦西度规克尔-席德尔形式的残余微分同胚，它们在$S^2$上生成共形代数，由基灵矢量和真正的共形基灵矢量（CKVs）组成。为解决CKV无限维性带来的明显矛盾，我们构建了一个韦尔补偿的BRST复形并计算其上同调。

Result: In Yang-Mills theory, residual symmetries form an infinite-dimensional algebra along null directions. In gravity, residual diffeomorphisms yield a conformal algebra on $S^2$, with the conformal Killing vector (CKV) sector appearing to generate an infinite-dimensional symmetry even for Schwarzschild, seemingly contradicting the known absence of proper conformal symmetries. This paradox is resolved by showing that the CKV sector is BRST-exact in a newly constructed Weyl-compensated BRST complex, hence trivial in cohomology. Thus, the physical symmetry algebra reduces to the expected global isometries of Schwarzschild ($SO(3,1)$).

在杨-米尔斯理论中，残余对称性形成沿零方向的无限维代数。在引力中，残余微分同胚在$S^2$上产生共形代数，其中共形基灵矢量（CKV）部分似乎为史瓦西时空生成无限维对称性，表面上与已知不存在真正共形对称性的事实相矛盾。这一悖论通过证明CKV部分在一个新构造的韦尔补偿BRST复形中是BRST恰当的从而在上同调中是平凡的而得以解决。因此，物理对称代数还原为史瓦西时空预期的全局等距群($SO(3,1)$)。

Conclusion: The Kerr-Schild double copy does not establish a direct correspondence between residual symmetries in Yang-Mills theory and gravity. While both theories exhibit enlarged symmetry algebras at the level of the ansatz, only gravity requires a cohomological reduction (via the Weyl-compensated BRST complex) to recover physical symmetries. This reveals a fundamental mismatch in how symmetries are realized, indicating that the KSDC encodes a more complex relationship than a simple symmetry-preserving map.

克尔-席德尔双副本未能在杨-米尔斯理论与引力的残余对称性之间建立直接对应关系。尽管两种理论在试探形式层面上都表现出扩展的对称代数，但只有引力需要通过韦尔补偿的BRST复形进行上同调约化才能恢复物理对称性。这揭示了对称性实现方式的根本不匹配，表明KSDC所编码的关系比简单的保对称映射更为复杂。

Abstract: The Kerr-Schild double copy (KSDC) is well-known for relating exact classical solutions between Yang-Mills theory and theories of gravity. However, whether this correspondence provides a more fundamental mapping between the underlying symmetries of gauge theory and gravity remains an underdeveloped area of research in the contemporary double copy program. In this paper, we demonstrate that the KSDC correspondence does not provide a mapping between the residual symmetry structures of the Kerr-Schild ansatz in Yang-Mills theory and gravity. On the gauge theory side, residual symmetries form an infinite-dimensional algebra of functions along null directions. On the gravitational side, residual diffeomorphisms preserving the Kerr-Schild form of the Schwarzschild metric generate a conformal algebra on $S^2$, which decomposes into Killing vectors and proper conformal Killing vectors (CKVs). While the Killing sector reproduces the expected global isometries, the CKV sector yields an infinite-dimensional algebra after imposing asymptotic flatness and horizon regularity. This appears to contradict the fact that the Schwarzschild solution admits no proper conformal symmetries. We resolve this apparent contradiction by constructing a Weyl-compensated BRST complex, showing that the CKV sector is BRST-exact and therefore trivial in cohomology, so that the physical symmetry algebra reduces to the global isometries of Schwarzschild. This demonstrates that the KSDC introduces an enlarged symmetry structure at the level of the ansatz, but preserves physical symmetries after a cohomological reduction, revealing a fundamental mismatch between Yang-Mills and gravity at the level of residual symmetries.

</details>


### [26] [Kerr-Schild Double Copy of the Randall-Sundrum Black String](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05447)
*Jesús A. Rodríguez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We construct the Kerr-Schild classical double copy for a black string in the Randall-Sundrum II (RSII) model, deriving its single and zeroth copies and verifying their field equations. The single copy gauge field is independent of the holographic coordinate and solves a sourceless Maxwell equation on the curved brane, analogous to the Schwarzschild case. The zeroth copy scalar obeys a modified Klein-Gordon equation with a first-order derivative term due to the warped geometry; a field redefinition reveals an effective mass $ m^2 = 12/l^2 $. Remarkably, an alternative Kerr-Schild splitting—gravitationally equivalent but algebraically distinct—yields a physically inequivalent double copy: the gauge field now couples to a delocalized bulk current, and the zeroth copy satisfies a standard massless equation, erasing all signatures of the extra dimension.

我们构建了Randall-Sundrum II（RSII）模型中黑洞弦的Kerr-Schild经典双影，推导其单影和零影，并验证相应的场方程。单影规范场与全息坐标无关，在弯曲的膜上满足无源麦克斯韦方程，类似于Schwarzschild双影情况。零影标量场满足带有额外维度一阶导数项的修正Klein-Gordon方程；通过场重定义可得具有有效质量$ m^2 = 12/l^2 $的标准Klein-Gordon方程。值得注意的是，另一种代数上不同的Kerr-Schild分裂——尽管引力等价——却产生物理上不等价的双影：此时规范场由体中离域化的守恒电流支撑，而零影满足无质量方程，完全抹去了弯曲额外维度的印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The classical double copy relates exact solutions in gravity to those in gauge and scalar theories, offering new insights into the gauge/gravity correspondence beyond perturbation theory. In asymptotically anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetimes—central to holography—the double copy may encode aspects of the AdS/CFT dictionary. The black string in the RSII model provides a physically rich setting: it is a higher-dimensional black hole localized on a brane, with a warped extra dimension inducing an effective 4D curvature scale $ l $. Constructing its double copy allows us to probe how holographic geometry and brane localization manifest in the single and zeroth copies, particularly whether bulk effects induce effective masses or sources in lower-dimensional theories.

经典双影将引力中的精确解与规范场和标量场理论中的解联系起来，为研究超出微扰论的规范/引力对偶提供了新视角。在渐近反德西特（AdS）时空——全息原理的核心背景——中，双影可能编码了AdS/CFT字典的某些方面。RSII模型中的黑洞弦提供了一个物理上丰富的场景：它是一种局域在膜上的高维黑洞，其弯曲的额外维度引入了一个有效的四维曲率尺度$ l $。构建其双影使我们能够探究全息几何和膜局域化如何在单影和零影中体现，特别是体效应是否会在低维理论中诱导出有效质量或源项。

Method: We apply the Kerr-Schild double copy formalism to the black string solution in the RSII model, which takes the form $ g_{\mu\nu} = \eta_{\mu\nu} + \kappa \phi k_\mu k_\nu $ in suitable coordinates, where $ k^\mu $ is a null geodesic vector field. From this, the single copy gauge field is defined as $ A_\mu = \phi k_\mu $, and the zeroth copy scalar as $ \varphi = \phi $. We verify that $ A_\mu $ satisfies the Maxwell equations $ \nabla_\mu F^{\mu\nu} = 0 $ on the induced brane geometry, and $ \varphi $ obeys a modified wave equation derived from the Einstein equations. We perform a field redefinition $ \varphi \to e^{\alpha y} \varphi $ to eliminate the first-order derivative in the extra dimension $ y $, identifying an effective mass term. We also consider an alternative Kerr-Schild form $ g_{\mu\nu} = \bar{g}_{\mu\nu} + \kappa \phi k_\mu k_\nu $, where $ \bar{g}_{\mu\mu} $ includes the AdS$_5$ background, leading to different interpretations of the single and zeroth copies.

我们在RSII模型中对黑洞弦解应用Kerr-Schild双影形式体系，该度规在适当坐标下形如$ g_{\mu\nu} = \eta_{\mu\nu} + \kappa \phi k_\mu k_\nu $，其中$ k^\mu $ 是类光测地线矢量场。由此定义单影规范场为$ A_\mu = \phi k_\mu $，零影标量场为$ \varphi = \phi $。我们验证了$ A_\mu $ 在诱导膜几何上满足麦克斯韦方程$ \nabla_\mu F^{\mu\nu} = 0 $，而$ \varphi $ 满足由爱因斯坦方程导出的修正波动方程。我们进行场重定义$ \varphi \to e^{\alpha y} \varphi $以消除额外维度$ y $ 中的一阶导数项，从而识别出有效质量项。我们还考虑另一种Kerr-Schild形式$ g_{\mu\nu} = \bar{g}_{\mu\nu} + \kappa \phi k_\mu k_\nu $，其中$ \bar{g}_{\mu\nu} $ 包含AdS$_5$ 背景，导致对单影和零影的不同物理解释。

Result: The single copy gauge field $ A_\mu = \phi k_\mu $ is independent of the holographic coordinate $ y $ and satisfies the sourceless Maxwell equation $ \nabla_\mu F^{\mu\nu} = 0 $ on the curved brane, mirroring the Coulomb-like behavior in the Schwarzschild double copy. The zeroth copy scalar $ \varphi $ obeys a modified Klein-Gordon equation: $ (\Box + \gamma \partial_y)\varphi = 0 $, where the $ \partial_y $ term arises from the warp factor. After the redefinition $ \varphi \to e^{-3y/l} \varphi $, this becomes the standard massive Klein-Gordon equation $ (\Box + m^2)\varphi = 0 $ with $ m^2 = 12/l^2 $, indicating a holographically induced mass gap. However, under an alternative Kerr-Schild decomposition using the full AdS$_5$ metric as the seed, the same gravitational solution yields a single copy with a non-vanishing divergence $ \nabla_\mu J^\mu \propto \partial_y(\cdots) $, signaling a delocalized bulk current, and a zeroth copy satisfying $ \Box \varphi = 0 $, i.e., a massless equation with no memory of the warping.

单影规范场$ A_\mu = \phi k_\mu $ 与全息坐标$ y $ 无关，在弯曲膜上满足无源麦克斯韦方程$ \nabla_\mu F^{\mu\nu} = 0 $，重现了Schwarzschild双影中的库仑类行为。零影标量场$ \varphi $ 满足修正Klein-Gordon方程：$ (\Box + \gamma \partial_y)\varphi = 0 $，其中$ \partial_y $ 项源于翘曲因子。经过重定义$ \varphi \to e^{-3y/l} \varphi $ 后，变为标准有质量Klein-Gordon方程$ (\Box + m^2)\varphi = 0 $，其中$ m^2 = 12/l^2 $，表明存在全息诱导的质量隙。然而，在使用完整AdS$_5$ 度规作为种子的另一种Kerr-Schild分解下，相同的引力解产生的单影具有非零散度$ \nabla_\mu J^\mu \propto \partial_y(\cdots) $，表明存在离域化的体电流；而零影满足$ \Box \varphi = 0 $，即一个无质量方程，完全失去了翘曲几何的记忆。

Conclusion: The Kerr-Schild double copy of the black string in the RSII model reveals how warped extra dimensions influence the structure of single and zeroth copies. The canonical splitting yields a single copy with brane-localized dynamics and a zeroth copy with an effective mass $ m^2 = 12/l^2 $, encoding holographic renormalization effects. In contrast, an alternative Kerr-Schild form—though gravitationally equivalent—produces a physically distinct double copy: the gauge field acquires bulk support, and the zeroth copy loses all dependence on the warping, satisfying a flat-space massless equation. This demonstrates that the classical double copy is sensitive not only to the spacetime geometry but also to the choice of Kerr-Schild decomposition, raising important questions about uniqueness and physical interpretation in braneworld and holographic contexts.

RSII模型中黑洞弦的Kerr-Schild双影揭示了弯曲额外维度如何影响单影和零影的结构。标准分裂给出具有膜局域化动力学的单影和具有有效质量$ m^2 = 12/l^2 $ 的零影，编码了全息重整化效应。相比之下，另一种Kerr-Schild形式——尽管引力等价——却产生物理上不同的双影：规范场获得体中支持，而零影失去所有翘曲依赖，满足平直空间中的无质量方程。这表明经典双影不仅依赖于时空几何，还对Kerr-Schild分裂的选择敏感，从而在膜世界和全息背景下提出了关于唯一性和物理解释的重要问题。

Abstract: We construct the Kerr-Schild classical double copy of the black string in the Randall-Sundrum II model, deriving the single and zeroth copies, and verifying the associated field equations. The single copy gauge field is independent of the holographic coordinate and satisfies a sourceless Maxwell equation on the curved background, in direct analogy with the Coulomb field of the Schwarzschild double copy. The zeroth copy scalar obeys a modified Klein-Gordon equation with a first-order derivative term along the extra dimension; a field redefinition yields a standard Klein-Gordon equation with effective mass $m^2 = 12/l^2$, induced by the warp factor. We further show that an alternative Kerr-Schild splitting, gravitationally equivalent to the canonical one, produces a physically inequivalent double copy: the gauge field is supported by a conserved but delocalized bulk current, and the zeroth copy satisfies a massless equation that carries no imprint of the warped extra dimension.

</details>


### [27] [Phase Transitions in Primary Hair Planar Black Holes and Solitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05538)
*Som Abhisek Mohanty,Subhash Mahapatra*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We present a new family of Ricci-flat, asymptotically AdS black hole and soliton solutions with primary scalar hair in $D$ dimensions, where the scalar field is regular everywhere. Analytic expressions for mass and free energy show the hairy soliton as the ground state, and a first-order phase transition exists between the hairy black hole and soliton, controlled by the ratio of Euclidean time and spatial cycle periods. Increasing scalar hair enlarges the temperature window favoring the soliton phase, suggesting applications in bottom-up holographic QCD for modeling confinement.

我们提出了一个在$D$维渐近反德西特（AdS）空间中带有主标量毛的里奇平坦黑洞与孤子解的新家族，其中标量场处处正则。通过解析表达式发现带毛孤子为系统的基态，且带毛黑洞与孤子之间存在由欧几里得时间与紧致类空周期比控制的一阶相变。标量毛参数增大时，孤子相占优的温度区间扩大，该模型对从自下而上的全息QCD视角研究禁闭相具有潜在应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The construction of physically consistent black hole solutions with scalar hair in AdS space is important for understanding gravity-gauge duality and holographic applications, particularly in modeling phases of strongly coupled gauge theories like QCD. Traditional no-hair theorems restrict such solutions, but allowing specific scalar potentials or boundary conditions enables hairy configurations. This work aims to construct analytic, regular hairy black holes and solitons in Ricci-flat AdS spacetimes and explore their thermodynamic phase structure, motivated by the need for gravitational duals of confined phases in holographic QCD.

在AdS空间中构建具有一致性标量毛的黑洞解对于理解引力-规范对偶及全息应用至关重要，尤其是在模拟如QCD等强耦合规范理论的相结构时。传统的无毛定理限制了此类解的存在，但通过引入特定标量势或边界条件可允许带毛构型。本工作的动机是构造里奇平坦AdS时空中解析且正则的带毛黑洞与孤子解，并研究其热力学相结构，以服务于全息QCD中禁闭相的引力对偶建模需求。

Method: We solve the coupled Einstein-scalar field equations in $D$-dimensional asymptotically AdS spacetime with a negative cosmological constant, assuming a planar (Ricci-flat) horizon geometry. A suitable scalar potential is chosen to allow regular, normalizable scalar field configurations (primary hair). By integrating the field equations analytically, we obtain exact hairy black hole and soliton solutions. Thermodynamic quantities such as mass and free energy are derived via standard holographic renormalization and background subtraction methods. Phase transitions are analyzed by comparing free energies and studying the dependence of transition temperature on the scalar hair parameter and compactification periods.

我们在$D$维渐近AdS时空中求解耦合的爱因斯坦-标量场方程，假设为平面（里奇平坦）视界几何，并选取适当的标量势以允许正则化、可归一化的标量场构型（主标量毛）。通过解析积分场方程，获得精确的带毛黑洞与孤子解。质量与自由能等热力学量通过标准的全息重整化与背景减除方法导出。通过比较自由能并分析相变温度对标量毛参数与紧致化周期的依赖关系，研究相变行为。

Result: We obtain analytic, regular hairy black hole and soliton solutions in $D$-dimensional asymptotically AdS space, where both the scalar field and curvature invariants remain finite everywhere. The hairy soliton has lower free energy than the hairy black hole at low temperatures, identifying it as the ground state. A first-order phase transition occurs between the two phases, with the critical temperature determined by the ratio $\beta_t / \beta_x$ of Euclidean time period $\beta_t$ to spatial cycle period $\beta_x$. Increasing the scalar hair parameter expands the temperature range over which the soliton phase is thermodynamically favored, indicating that scalar hair stabilizes the confined phase.

我们获得了$D$维渐近AdS空间中解析且正则的带毛黑洞与孤子解，其中标量场与曲率不变量处处有限。在低温下，带毛孤子的自由能低于带毛黑洞，表明其为基态。两者之间发生一阶相变，临界温度由欧几里得时间周期$\beta_t$与空间周期$\beta_x$之比$\beta_t / \beta_x$决定。随着标量毛参数的增加，孤子相在更宽的温度范围内保持热力学优势，表明标量毛有助于稳定禁闭相。

Conclusion: The existence of analytic Ricci-flat hairy black holes and solitons enriches the landscape of AdS/CFT solutions and provides a concrete gravitational model for confinement-deconfinement transitions in holographic QCD. The control of the phase transition via compactification periods and the stabilizing effect of scalar hair offer new mechanisms for tuning holographic phase diagrams. These solutions evade traditional no-hair theorems due to the choice of AdS boundary conditions and represent genuine primary hair, making them suitable for dual CFT interpretations.

解析型里奇平坦带毛黑洞与孤子的存在丰富了AdS/CFT解的空间，为全息QCD中的禁闭-去禁闭相变提供了具体的引力模型。通过紧致化周期调控相变以及标量毛的稳定效应，为调节全息相图提供了新机制。这些解由于采用了特定的AdS边界条件而规避了传统无毛定理，代表真正的主标量毛，适用于对偶CFT的诠释。

Abstract: We present a new family of Ricci-flat black hole and soliton solutions with primary scalar hair in asymptotically anti-de Sitter (AdS) space in $D$ dimensions. By solving the coupled Einstein-scalar field equations, we obtain analytic planar hairy black hole and soliton geometries. In these solutions, the scalar field and curvature scalars remain regular everywhere. We also derive analytic expressions for the mass and free energy, which indicate that the hairy soliton represents the ground state of the system. We further analyze the phase transitions between the hairy black hole and the hairy soliton, and find that there exists a first-order phase transition between them, with the transition point controlled by the ratio of the periods of Euclidean time and compact spacelike cycle. We further analyze how the scalar hair affects the transition temperature, and find that the temperature window in which the soliton phase remains preferred expands as the hair parameter increases. The hairy soliton solution obtained here is partly motivated by holographic QCD and may provide a useful gravitational background for modeling the confined phase of QCD from a bottom-up holographic perspective.

</details>


### [28] [Symmetry-resolved Krylov Complexity and the Uncoloured Tensor Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05630)
*Shaliya Kotta,P N Bala Subramanian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper studies symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity in quantum systems with symmetries, focusing on conditions for equivalence between subspace and full-space complexity, and applies it to the Uncoloured Tensor Model, observing both equipartition and its violation across charge sectors.

本文研究了具有对称性的量子系统中的对称性分解Krylov复杂度，重点关注子空间与全空间复杂度等价的条件，并将其应用于无色张量模型，在不同荷 sector 中观察到等分性成立与不成立的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding how quantum chaos and operator growth manifest in systems with global symmetries requires decomposing complexity into symmetry sectors. The motivation is to explore when the symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity in a charge subspace reflects the full complexity and whether equipartition of complexity holds.

理解全局对称性系统中量子混沌和算符增长的表现需要将复杂度按对称性 sector 分解。动机在于探究在荷子空间中的对称性分解Krylov复杂度何时能反映全空间复杂度，以及复杂度等分性是否成立。

Method: The authors analyze the mathematical conditions under which an invariant operator's Krylov complexity in a given charge subspace equals that in the full Hilbert space. They apply this framework to the Uncoloured Tensor Model—a symmetric, disorder-free analog of the SYK model—computing symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity using Krylov basis construction and Lanczos algorithm within each charge sector.

作者分析了在给定荷子空间中，不变算符的Krylov复杂度等于全希尔伯特空间复杂度的数学条件。他们将此框架应用于无色张量模型——一种对称且无无序的SYK模型类似物——使用每个荷 sector 内的Krylov基构造和Lanczos算法计算对称性分解的Krylov复杂度。

Result: They find that for certain charge subspaces of the same operator, equipartition of Krylov complexity holds, while in others it does not. Moreover, within computational limits, the average Krylov complexity over symmetry subspaces is bounded above by the complexity in the full space.

他们发现对于同一算符的不同荷子空间，某些满足Krylov复杂度的等分性，而另一些则不满足。此外，在计算能力范围内，对称子空间上平均的Krylov复杂度不超过全空间的复杂度。

Conclusion: Symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity provides a refined probe of quantum chaos, revealing non-universal behavior across charge sectors. The lack of universal equipartition suggests richer dynamics in symmetric systems, and the upper bound on averaged complexity indicates constraints imposed by symmetry.

对称性分解的Krylov复杂度为量子混沌提供了更精细的探针，揭示了不同荷 sector 间的非普适行为。缺乏普适的等分性表明对称系统中存在更丰富的动力学，而平均复杂度的上界反映了对称性所施加的约束。

Abstract: The symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity is a useful tool in studying chaotic properties of systems that are endowed with symmetries. We investigate the conditions under which an invariant operator would have the symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity in a charge subspace identical to the Krylov complexity of the full operator. Further, we study the Krylov complexity of the Uncoloured Tensor Model, a disorder-free kin of the SYK Model which has a plethora of symmetries. We find charge subspaces of the same operator in which the equipartition holds as well as where it doesn't. We also find that within the computational limits, the Krylov complexity averaged over the symmetry subspace is bounded above by that of the operator in the full space.

### [29] [Causal Dynamical Triangulations: New Lattice Theory of Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05641)
*J. Ambjørn,R. Loll*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Causal Dynamical Triangulations (CDT) provides a nonperturbative lattice approach to quantum gravity, using triangulated spacetimes made of flat Minkowskian simplices with dynamical geometry encoded in connectivity and edge lengths. Monte Carlo simulations reveal the emergence of a de Sitter-like universe at large scales and a spectral dimension of ~2 near the Planck scale, suggesting a possible UV fixed point and continuum limit.

因果动力学三角剖分（Causal Dynamical Triangulations, CDT）提供了一种非微扰的量子引力格点方法，使用由平直闵可夫斯基单形构成的三角化时空，其动力学几何通过连接性与边长编码。蒙特卡洛模拟显示在大尺度上涌现出类德西特宇宙，在普朗克尺度附近谱维度约为2，暗示可能存在紫外不动点及连续极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The search for a consistent, nonperturbative quantum theory of gravity that incorporates the dynamical and causal nature of spacetime remains a major challenge. Traditional perturbative approaches fail due to nonrenormalizability, while background-independent formulations like CDT aim to construct quantum spacetime from first principles without relying on a fixed geometry.

寻找一个一致的、非微扰的量子引力理论，能包含时空的动力学与因果结构，仍是重大挑战。传统的微扰方法因不可重正化而失败，而像CDT这样的背景无关方法则试图从第一性原理出发构建量子时空，无需依赖固定背景几何。

Method: CDT regularizes the gravitational path integral by summing over triangulated spacetimes composed of flat, Minkowskian simplices, with fixed edge lengths serving as a UV cutoff. The lattice structure respects causality by distinguishing space- and time-like edges, enabling a well-defined Wick rotation to Euclidean signature. The path integral is evaluated via Monte Carlo simulations, allowing nonperturbative exploration of quantum geometry and the measurement of observables such as the scale factor and spectral dimension.

CDT通过求和由平直闵可夫斯基单形构成的三角化时空来正则化引力路径积分，固定边长作为紫外截断。格点结构通过区分类空与类时边保持因果性，从而实现到欧几里得符号的良好定义维克转动。路径积分通过蒙特卡洛模拟计算，允许非微扰地探索量子几何，并测量如尺度因子和谱维度等可观测量。

Result: Numerical simulations show the dynamical emergence of a macroscopic, four-dimensional universe with global properties matching those of de Sitter space, indicating a viable classical limit. At short distances near the Planck scale, strong quantum fluctuations result in a fractal-like structure with a spectral dimension decreasing to approximately 2. Evidence for an ultraviolet fixed point under renormalization group flow suggests the existence of a nontrivial continuum quantum field theory of gravity.

数值模拟显示，宏观的四维宇宙动力学地涌现，其整体性质与德西特空间匹配，表明存在可行的经典极限。在普朗克尺度附近的短距离上，强烈的量子涨落导致类似分形的结构，谱维度降至约2。在重整化群流下存在紫外不动点的证据，暗示存在一个非平凡的引力连续量子场论。

Conclusion: CDT offers a promising framework for nonperturbative quantum gravity, combining causality, diffeomorphism invariance, and background independence in a computationally tractable way. The emergence of semiclassical spacetime alongside Planck-scale dimensional reduction and indications of a UV fixed point support the possibility of a fundamental quantum theory of gravity with predictive power in early-universe cosmology.

CDT为非微扰量子引力提供了一个有前景的框架，以可计算的方式结合了因果性、微分同胚不变性和背景无关性。半经典时空的涌现、普朗克尺度下的维度降低以及紫外不动点的迹象，共同支持存在一个具有早期宇宙宇宙学预测能力的基本量子引力理论的可能性。

Abstract: Causal Dynamical Triangulations (CDT) is a methodology to define and compute the gravitational path integral, whose aim is a fully fledged nonperturbative quantum field theory of gravity and spacetime. Analogous to lattice formulations of nongravitational quantum fields, CDT provides a blueprint for lattice quantum gravity, where - crucially - the dynamical, curved and causal nature of spacetime is built into the structure of the lattices from the outset. The regularized path integral involves a sum over triangulated spacetimes, each assembled from flat, Minkowskian building blocks. The degrees of freedom of general relativity are encoded in a coordinate-free manner in the neighbourhood relations of the building blocks and the length of their edges, which also serves as a short-distance cutoff.
  A well-defined Wick rotation makes this path integral amenable to Monte Carlo simulations. Despite the absence of an a priori preferred background geometry, numerical experiments have revealed the dynamical emergence of a quantum universe near the Planck scale. Its global properties are compatible with those of a de Sitter space, providing strong evidence for a well-defined classical limit. At the same time, large quantum fluctuations lead to unexpected properties on short scales, most prominently, a spectral dimension near 2, replacing the classical value of 4. Computer simulations indicate the presence of an ultraviolet fixed point under renormalization, opening the door to a nontrivial continuum theory. Efforts are under way to construct observables that can elucidate the nonperturbative quantum origins of early-universe cosmology.

</details>


### [30] [Vortex Harmonic Spinors on the Nappi-Witten Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05676)
*Calum Ross,Raúl Sánchez Galán*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper establishes a geometric correspondence between vortex equations on flat Riemann surfaces and harmonic spinors on the Nappi-Witten space, a group manifold of a central extension of $SE(2)$. These vortex configurations lift to solutions of a twisted Dirac equation, and via conformal flatness, induce harmonic spinors on 4D Minkowski space, providing a novel construction of Abelian magnetic zero-modes from vortices.

本文建立了平直黎曼曲面上涡旋方程与Nappi-Witten空间（即$SE(2)$中心扩张的群流形）上谐和旋量之间的几何对应关系。涡旋构型自然地提升到该框架中，成为扭曲狄拉克方程的显式解；利用Nappi-Witten度规的共形平坦性，这些解进一步诱导出四维闵可夫斯基空间上的谐和旋量，从而从涡旋数据几何构造了阿贝尔磁零模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand how topological solitons like vortices in two dimensions can be related to zero-energy solutions of Dirac operators in four-dimensional spacetime, particularly in the context of magnetic zero-modes which play a role in quantum field theory anomalies and index theorems.

旨在理解二维拓扑孤立子（如涡旋）如何与四维时空中狄拉克算子的零能解相关联，特别是阿贝尔磁零模在量子场论反常和指标定理中的作用。



Method: The authors exploit the structure of the Nappi--Witten space, a Lorentzian four-manifold that arises as the group manifold of a central extension of the Euclidean group $SE(2)$. Vortex configurations on flat Riemann surfaces are lifted to this space, where they satisfy a twisted Dirac equation. The conformal equivalence between the Nappi--Witten metric and 4D Minkowski space allows pullback of solutions, yielding harmonic spinors (i.e., solutions to the massless Dirac equation) in flat spacetime.

作者利用Nappi-Witten空间的结构——这是欧几里得群$SE(2)$中心扩张的群流形，一个洛伦兹四维流形。将平直黎曼曲面上的涡旋构型提升至此空间，在其中满足一个扭曲的狄拉克方程。由于Nappi-Witten度规与四维闵可夫斯基空间共形等价，可通过拉回得到平直时空中的谐和旋量（即无质量狄拉克方程的解）。



Result: Explicit construction of harmonic spinors on Minkowski space from vortex data via the Nappi--Witten geometry. This gives a geometric realization of Abelian magnetic zero-modes in 4D flat spacetime arising from 2D vortex configurations.

通过Nappi-Witten几何，由涡旋数据显式构造了闵可夫斯基空间上的谐和旋量。这为源于二维涡旋构型的四维平直时空中的阿贝尔磁零模提供了几何实现。



Conclusion: The correspondence provides a new bridge between 2D topological field theory and 4D fermionic systems, showing how solutions to vortex equations encode information about zero-modes of Dirac operators in higher dimensions. It highlights the role of group-theoretic extensions and conformal geometry in linking lower- and higher-dimensional physics.

该对应关系在二维拓扑场论与四维费米系统之间建立了新的桥梁，表明涡旋方程的解如何编码高维狄拉克算子零模的信息。它突显了群论扩张与共形几何在连接低维与高维物理中的重要作用。



Abstract: We establish a correspondence between vortex equations on flat Riemann surfaces and harmonic spinors on the Nappi--Witten space, the group manifold of a central extension of the Euclidean group $SE(2)$. Vortex configurations lift naturally to this setting, producing explicit solutions of a twisted Dirac equation. Using the conformal flatness of the Nappi--Witten metric, these solutions induce harmonic spinors on four-dimensional Minkowski space. This yields a geometric construction of Abelian magnetic zero-modes on flat Minkowski spacetime from vortex data.
