### [31] [Monodromy-Matrix Description of Extremal Multi-centered Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05696)
*Jun-ichi Sakamoto,Shinya Tomizawa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper develops a solution-generating framework using the Breitenlohner–Maison (BM) linear system for extremal, stationary biaxisymmetric black holes in 5D $U(1)^3$ supergravity, particularly over a Gibbons–Hawking base. It analyzes both BPS and almost-BPS configurations, including rotating black holes and two-center black rings, by reducing to a 3D coset sigma model with target space $SO(4,4)/[SO(2,2)\times SO(2,2)]$. The solutions are encoded in coset and monodromy matrices, which for BPS cases admit a nilpotent exponential representation. A factorization method resolves double poles in monodromy matrices, enabling solution reconstruction. This is extended to almost-BPS solutions, where two-center black rings exhibit higher-order poles that vanish under regularity. The extremal Rasheed–Larsen solution is analyzed: its fast-rotating branch is governed by idempotent elements, while the slow-rotating branch is shown to be duality-related via an explicit $SO(4,4)$ transformation to an almost-BPS solution. These results position the BM formalism as a unified framework for extremal multi-center black holes in five dimensions.

本文利用Breitenlohner–Maison (BM) 线性系统，为五维 $U(1)^3$ 超引力中基于Gibbons–Hawking基的极值、稳态双轴对称黑洞（包括BPS与almost-BPS构型）构建解生成框架。通过三维约化，系统被描述为靶空间为 $SO(4,4)/[SO(2,2)\times SO(2,2)]$ 的coset σ模型，其解由coset矩阵与单值矩阵编码。对于Bena–Warner BPS解，构造了相应的矩阵，并证明其可表示为幂零元控制的指数形式。尽管单值矩阵通常具有二阶极点，但可利用 $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ 的幂零代数显式分解，从而重构解。该方法推广至almost-BPS解，并导出了对应矩阵。单中心情形残差对易，而双环黑环则呈现更复杂的结构，出现三阶极点，但在正则性条件下消失。最后分析了Rasheed–Larsen解的极值极限：快转支由幂等元控制，慢转支则通过显式的 $SO(4,4)$ 对偶变换关联到单中心almost-BPS解。这些结果确立了BM形式体系作为五维极值多中心黑洞的统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The construction of extremal multi-center black hole solutions in five-dimensional supergravity remains challenging due to the complexity of solving non-linear coupled differential equations. While BPS solutions are well-understood through supersymmetry, almost-BPS and non-supersymmetric extremal solutions lack a unified generating technique. The Breitenlohner--Maison (BM) linear system offers a powerful integrability-based approach applicable to stationary biaxisymmetric systems. This work aims to extend and unify the application of the BM formalism to both BPS and almost-BPS extremal black holes—including rotating single-center and two-center black rings—by leveraging the underlying $SO(4,4)$ duality structure after three-dimensional reduction, thereby providing a systematic method for solution generation beyond supersymmetry.

在五维超引力中构造极值多中心黑洞解仍具挑战性，因其涉及求解非线性耦合微分方程组。虽然BPS解可通过超对称性良好理解，但almost-BPS及非超对称极值解缺乏统一的生成技术。Breitenlohner–Maison (BM) 线性系统为稳态双轴对称系统提供了强大的基于可积性的方法。本研究旨在通过三维约化后的 $SO(4,4)$ 对偶结构，拓展并统一BM形式体系在BPS与almost-BPS极值黑洞（包括旋转单中心与双环黑环）中的应用，从而提供一种超越超对称性的系统化解生成方法。

Method: The authors perform dimensional reduction from five to three dimensions for stationary biaxisymmetric solutions in $U(1)^3$ supergravity over a Gibbons--Hawking base, resulting in a coset sigma model with target space $SO(4,4)/[SO(2,2)\times SO(2,2)]$. Solutions are encoded in coset matrices $V$ and monodromy matrices $M$, which solve a linear system derived from the BM framework. For BPS solutions (e.g., Bena--Warner), they construct explicit $M$ matrices and show these admit an exponential form $M = \exp(N/\sigma)$ with $N$ nilpotent. They apply a pole structure analysis and use the nilpotent algebra of $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ to factorize double poles in $M$, reconstructing the physical fields. This method is extended to almost-BPS solutions, analyzing their monodromy structure. For two-center black rings, they examine the emergence of third-order poles and their cancellation under regularity. Finally, they analyze the extremal limits of the Rasheed--Larsen solution, identifying idempotent structures in the fast-rotating branch and constructing an explicit $SO(4,4)$ duality map from the slow-rotating branch to a single-center almost-BPS solution.

作者对基于Gibbons–Hawking基的五维 $U(1)^3$ 超引力中稳态双轴对称解进行五维到三维约化，得到靶空间为 $SO(4,4)/[SO(2,2)\times SO(2,2)]$ 的coset σ模型。解由coset矩阵 $V$ 和单值矩阵 $M$ 编码，后者满足BM框架导出的线性系统。对于BPS解（如Bena–Warner），他们构造显式的 $M$ 矩阵，并证明其可表示为 $M = \exp(N/\sigma)$ 形式，其中 $N$ 为幂零元。通过极点结构分析，利用 $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ 的幂零代数分解 $M$ 中的二阶极点，从而重构物理场。该方法推广至almost-BPS解，分析其单值结构。对于双环黑环，研究三阶极点的出现及其在正则性条件下的消除。最后分析Rasheed–Larsen解的极值极限，在快转支中识别出幂等结构，并构造从慢转支到单中心almost-BPS解的显式 $SO(4,4)$ 对偶映射。

Result: The paper constructs explicit coset and monodromy matrices for both BPS and almost-BPS extremal black hole solutions in 5D $U(1)^3$ supergravity. For BPS solutions, the monodromy matrix exhibits a double pole but can be factorized using nilpotent elements in $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$, enabling full reconstruction of the solution. In the almost-BPS case, similar techniques apply, though the algebraic structure differs. The two-center black ring solution displays a third-order pole in the monodromy matrix, which vanishes upon imposing smoothness and regularity conditions. For the extremal Rasheed--Larsen black hole, the fast-rotating branch is governed by idempotent elements in the monodromy matrix, while the slow-rotating branch is shown to be related via an explicit $SO(4,4)$ duality transformation to a single-center almost-BPS solution. These results demonstrate the robustness and generality of the BM linear system in describing diverse extremal black hole configurations.

本文为五维 $U(1)^3$ 超引力中的BPS与almost-BPS极值黑洞解构造了显式的coset矩阵与单值矩阵。对于BPS解，单值矩阵虽具二阶极点，但可通过 $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ 中的幂零元分解，实现解的完整重构。在almost-BPS情形下，类似技术适用，但代数结构不同。双环黑环解在单值矩阵中呈现三阶极点，但在施加光滑性与正则性条件后消失。对于极值Rasheed–Larsen黑洞，快转支由单值矩阵中的幂等元控制，而慢转支则通过显式 $SO(4,4)$ 对偶变换关联到单中心almost-BPS解。这些结果展示了BM线性系统在描述多种极值黑洞构型方面的稳健性与普适性。

Conclusion: The Breitenlohner--Maison linear system provides a unified and powerful framework for generating extremal, stationary biaxisymmetric black hole solutions in five-dimensional supergravity, encompassing both BPS and almost-BPS classes. By encoding solutions in coset and monodromy matrices within the $SO(4,4)/[SO(2,2)\times SO(2,2)]$ sigma model, and exploiting algebraic properties such as nilpotency and idempotency, the authors demonstrate systematic solution reconstruction—even in the presence of higher-order poles. The successful application to multi-center black rings and the extremal Rasheed--Larsen solution, including an explicit duality mapping, establishes the BM formalism as a comprehensive tool for exploring non-supersymmetric extremal black holes and paves the way for constructing new solutions in higher-dimensional gravity.

Breitenlohner–Maison线性系统为生成五维超引力中极值、稳态双轴对称黑洞解（涵盖BPS与almost-BPS类）提供了统一且强大的框架。通过在 $SO(4,4)/[SO(2,2)\times SO(2,2)]$ σ模型中以coset矩阵与单值矩阵编码解，并利用幂零性与幂等性等代数性质，作者实现了系统性的解重构，即使存在高阶极点亦然。该方法成功应用于多中心黑环与极值Rasheed–Larsen解（包括显式对偶映射），确立了BM形式体系作为探索非超对称极值黑洞的综合工具，为在高维引力中构造新解铺平道路。

Abstract: We study solution-generating techniques based on the Breitenlohner--Maison linear system for extremal, stationary biaxisymmetric black hole solutions in five-dimensional $U(1)^3$ supergravity. Focusing on multi-center configurations over a Gibbons--Hawking base, we analyze both BPS and almost-BPS solutions, including rotating single-center black holes and two-center black rings. After dimensional reduction to three dimensions, the system is described by a coset sigma model with target space $SO(4,4)/[SO(2,2)\times SO(2,2)]$, where solutions are encoded in coset and monodromy matrices. For Bena--Warner BPS solutions, we construct the coset and monodromy matrices and show that they admit an exponential representation governed by nilpotent elements. Although the monodromy matrices generically exhibit double poles, they can be factorized explicitly using the nilpotent algebra of $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$, reconstructing the solutions. We extend this to almost-BPS solutions and derive the corresponding matrices. While the single-center case exhibits commuting residues, the two-center black ring leads to a more intricate structure with a third-order pole, which disappears when regularity is imposed. Finally, we analyze the extremal limits of the Rasheed--Larsen solution, where the fast-rotating branch is governed by idempotent elements. We also construct an explicit $SO(4,4)$ duality transformation relating the slowly-rotating branch to a single-center almost-BPS solution. These results will provide the BM formalism as a unified framework for extremal multi-center black holes.

</details>


### [32] [Probing the Factorized Island Branch with the Capacity of Entanglement in JT Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05815)
*Raúl Arias,Agustín Tamis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that the capacity of entanglement, beyond the von Neumann entropy, captures finite-$n$ replica structure in Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity with a large-$c$ bath, revealing additional physical information in the island saddle that is invisible to entropy alone.

本文表明，在Jackiw-Teitelboim（JT）引力与大$c$浴耦合的框架下，纠缠容量除了冯诺依曼熵之外，还能捕捉到有限-$n$副本结构，揭示了岛屿鞍点中熵本身无法显示的额外物理信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While the von Neumann entropy ($n \to 1$ limit) is widely used to diagnose black hole islands, it may discard richer replica structure present at finite $n$. The authors aim to explore whether other quantum information measures—specifically the capacity of entanglement—can probe this finer structure within semiclassical gravity, particularly in the factorized island configuration of JT gravity.

尽管冯诺依曼熵（$n \to 1$极限）被广泛用于诊断黑洞岛屿，但它可能丢弃了有限$n$时更丰富的副本结构。作者旨在探索其他量子信息度量——特别是纠缠容量——是否能够探测半经典引力中这种更精细的结构，特别是在JT引力的因子化岛屿构型中。

Method: The authors compute the capacity of entanglement, defined as the second derivative of the replicated partition function with respect to $n$ at $n=1$, i.e., $C_E = \partial_n^2 \log Z_n|_{n=1}$, within the semiclassical JT gravity setup coupled to a large-$c$ conformal bath. They analyze both the entropy and the capacity in the late-time, high-temperature regime, focusing on the dominant factorized replica saddle. The gravitational path integral is evaluated using standard replica wormhole techniques.

作者在与大$c$共形浴耦合的半经典JT引力框架内计算纠缠容量，其定义为复制配分函数在$n=1$处对$n$的二阶导数，即$C_E = \partial_n^2 \log Z_n|_{n=1}$。他们在高温、晚期时间区域分析熵和容量，重点关注主导的因子化副本鞍点。引力路径积分通过标准的副本虫洞技术进行计算。

Result: The von Neumann entropy remains unchanged at leading nontrivial order in the late-time regime, consistent with the standard island formula. However, the capacity of entanglement acquires a definite correction at this order, signaling the presence of finite-$n$ replica structure within the same semiclassical saddle. This correction is calculable and physically meaningful, demonstrating that the replica geometry contains observable data beyond the $n=1$ limit.

冯诺依曼熵在晚期主导非平凡阶保持不变，符合标准的岛屿公式。然而，纠缠容量在此阶获得一个明确的修正，表明在同一半经典鞍点中存在有限-$n$副本结构。该修正是可计算且具有物理意义的，证明副本几何包含超越$n=1$极限的可观测数据。

Conclusion: The factorized island saddle in JT gravity encodes more information than what is captured by the von Neumann entropy alone. The capacity of entanglement serves as a sensitive probe of finite-$n$ replica effects, showing that the full replica geometry—and not just the $n\to1$ limit—contains physical content. This suggests a richer role for replica symmetry and finite-$n$ data in the semiclassical description of quantum gravity and black hole information.

JT引力中的因子化岛屿鞍点编码的信息超出了冯诺依曼熵单独所能捕捉的内容。纠缠容量作为有限-$n$副本效应的敏感探针，表明完整的副本几何——而不仅仅是$n\to1$极限——包含物理内容。这暗示了副本对称性和有限-$n$数据在量子引力和黑洞信息的半经典描述中具有更丰富的作用。

Abstract: Black hole islands are usually diagnosed through the von Neumann entropy, but the full replica saddle contains more information than survives in the limit $n \to 1$. In this paper we show that the capacity of entanglement can detect that extra structure already within the controlled factorized island branch of JT gravity coupled to a large-$c$ bath. In the late-time high-temperature regime, the entropy plateau remains unchanged at the first nontrivial order, while the capacity acquires a definite correction. This provides a sharp semiclassical example in which nearby replica data are physically meaningful even when the entropy itself appears rigid. Our result shows that the factorized island saddle already carries finite-$n$ information beyond the entropy, and that the capacity is a natural observable for exposing it. More broadly, it highlights that the physics of island saddles is not exhausted by the $n=1$ limit: the surrounding replica geometry can contain additional, and observable, information about how the semiclassical saddle is assembled.

</details>


### [33] [Exact WKB analysis of inverted triple-well: resonance, PT-symmetry breaking, and resurgence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05878)
*Syo Kamata,Tatsuhiro Misumi,Cihan Pazarbaşı,Hidetoshi Taya*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We analyze non-Hermitian quantum mechanics in an inverted triple-well potential using exact WKB methods, identifying three distinct quantum systems—PT-symmetric, resonance, and anti-resonance—defined by different Siegert boundary conditions. For each, we derive exact quantization conditions and trans-series solutions, revealing resurgent structures and median summation that determine reality or complexity of spectra. We establish connections to path integral saddles (bounces and bions), predict and prove PT-symmetry breaking via a simple algebraic condition at the exceptional point, and show vanishing non-perturbative corrections there while preserving resurgent structure. Resonance and anti-resonance systems have complex-conjugate spectra related by time reversal, no exceptional point, but share the same minimal trans-series. This work unifies non-Hermitian quantization through resurgence and semi-classical methods.

我们利用精确WKB方法研究倒置三势阱中的非厄米量子力学，通过不同的Siegert边界条件识别出三种不同的量子系统：PT对称、共振和反共振系统。对每种情况，我们推导了精确的量子化条件和超渐近级数解，揭示了重正结构和中位求和如何决定谱的实性或复性。我们建立了与路径积分鞍点（反弹子和双子）的联系，预测并证明了PT对称性破缺，并给出了分岔点处的一个简洁代数方程。在分岔点，中位求和的非微扰修正消失，但重正结构仍通过普适最小超渐近级数保留。共振与反共振系统的精确中位求和谱互为复共轭，对应时间反演关系，必然是复的，且无分岔点，但仍共享相同的最小超渐近结构。本工作通过重正理论与半经典方法为非厄米理论的量子化提供了统一而普适的视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Non-Hermitian quantum systems, particularly those with PT symmetry, have attracted significant attention due to their rich spectral properties and applications in open quantum systems, optics, and condensed matter. However, a complete understanding of their quantization, especially the interplay between boundary conditions, semiclassical approximations, and non-perturbative effects like instantons and bions, remains challenging. The inverted triple-well potential serves as a prototypical model to explore these features because it supports multiple saddle configurations (e.g., bounces and bions) in the path integral. Our goal is to develop a rigorous framework—using exact WKB and resurgence theory—to clarify how different physical scenarios (PT-symmetric vs. resonant) emerge from the same classical potential, when spectra are real or complex, and how PT-symmetry breaking occurs at exceptional points.

非厄米量子系统，特别是具有PT对称性的系统，因其丰富的谱性质及在开放量子系统、光学和凝聚态物理中的应用而受到广泛关注。然而，对其量子化的完整理解，尤其是边界条件、半经典近似以及瞬子、双子等非微扰效应之间的相互作用，仍具挑战性。倒置三势阱作为典型模型，支持路径积分中的多种鞍点构型（如反弹子和双子），适合探索这些特性。我们的目标是建立一个严格的框架——使用精确WKB和重正理论——以阐明从同一经典势如何产生不同物理情形（PT对称vs共振），谱何时为实或复，以及PT对称性如何在分岔点发生破缺。

Method: We employ the exact WKB method combined with Borel resummation and median summation to analyze the Schrödinger equation for an inverted triple-well potential under different Siegert boundary conditions. These conditions define three distinct quantum problems: PT-symmetric (bound states), resonance (outgoing waves), and anti-resonance (incoming waves). Using Voros symbols and alien calculus, we derive exact quantization conditions and construct trans-series solutions encoding perturbative and non-perturbative contributions (e.g., bounces and bions). We identify resurgent relations among different sectors and perform median summation to obtain unambiguous physical results. The connection to the semi-classical path integral is made explicit by identifying saddle-point configurations—bounce trajectories contributing to energy shifts and bion configurations responsible for level splitting. We analyze the analytic structure of the trans-series near the exceptional point and prove PT-symmetry breaking by deriving an exact algebraic condition involving the bounce and bion actions.

我们采用精确WKB方法结合Borel重求和与中位求和，分析在不同Siegert边界条件下倒置三势阱的薛定谔方程。这些条件定义了三个不同的量子问题：PT对称（束缚态）、共振（出射波）和反共振（入射波）。利用Voros符号和外星微积分（alien calculus），我们推导出精确量子化条件，并构建包含微扰与非微扰贡献（如反弹子和双子）的超渐近级数解。我们识别不同扇区间的重正关系，并进行中位求和以获得明确的物理结果。通过识别路径积分中的鞍点构型——反弹轨迹贡献于能量移动，双子构型导致能级分裂——我们显式建立了与半经典路径积分的联系。我们分析超渐近级数在分岔点附近的解析结构，并通过推导涉及反弹子与双子作用量的精确代数条件来证明PT对称性破缺。

Result: For the PT-symmetric system, we derive an exact quantization condition whose median-summed spectrum is real below the exceptional point and becomes complex above it, signaling spontaneous PT-symmetry breaking. At the exceptional point, defined by $ S_\text{bion} = 2 S_\text{bounce} $, the non-perturbative correction vanishes, yet the minimal trans-series persists, indicating survival of resurgence. For resonance and anti-resonance systems, the spectra are complex and related by complex conjugation (time-reversal symmetry), do not exhibit an exceptional point, but share the same minimal trans-series structure. We confirm our analytical predictions numerically and show that the resurgent cancellations ensure consistency across different lateral Borel resummations. The explicit link between bion and bounce actions provides a universal criterion for the onset of PT-symmetry breaking.

对于PT对称系统，我们推导出一个精确量子化条件，其经中位求和后的谱在分岔点以下为实，在以上变为复，标志着自发PT对称性破缺。在由 $ S_\text{bion} = 2 S_\text{bounce} $ 定义的分岔点处，非微扰修正消失，但最小超渐近级数仍然存在，表明重正结构得以保留。对于共振与反共振系统，其谱为复且互为复共轭（对应时间反演对称性），不出现分岔点，但仍共享相同的最小超渐近结构。我们通过数值计算验证了解析预测，并显示重正抵消确保了不同侧向Borel重求和之间的一致性。反弹子与双子作用量之间的显式联系为PT对称性破缺的起始提供了普适判据。

Conclusion: This work establishes a unified framework for quantizing non-Hermitian systems using exact WKB, resurgence, and path integral methods. It demonstrates that different physical behaviors—real vs complex spectra, presence or absence of PT-symmetry breaking—arise from distinct boundary conditions applied to the same classical potential. The exceptional point marking PT-symmetry breaking is governed by a simple algebraic relation between bounce and bion actions, $ S_\text{bion} = 2 S_\text{bounce} $. The survival of the minimal trans-series at the exceptional point reveals that resurgence persists even when spectral reality is lost. Resonance and anti-resonance systems, while spectrally distinct, share universal resurgent features, highlighting the robustness of trans-series structures across different physical contexts. Our results provide deep insights into the role of non-perturbative configurations in non-Hermitian theories and offer a general approach applicable to other multi-well potentials and open quantum systems.

本工作建立了利用精确WKB、重正理论和路径积分方法对非厄米系统进行量子化的统一框架。研究表明，不同的物理行为——谱的实性或复性、PT对称性破缺的存在与否——源于对同一经典势施加的不同边界条件。标记PT对称性破缺的分岔点由反弹子与双子作用量之间的简单代数关系 $ S_\text{bion} = 2 S_\text{bounce} $ 所支配。在分岔点处最小超渐近级数的存续表明，即使谱失去实性，重正结构依然保留。共振与反共振系统尽管谱上显著不同，却共享普适的重正特征，凸显了超渐近结构在不同物理情境下的鲁棒性。我们的结果深入揭示了非微扰构型在非厄米理论中的作用，并为其他多势阱及开放量子系统提供了普适的研究方法。

Abstract: We study non-Hermitian quantum mechanics of an inverted triple-well potential within the exact WKB framework. For a single classical potential, different Siegert boundary conditions define three distinct quantum problems: the PT-symmetric, resonance, and anti-resonance systems. For each case, we derive the exact quantization condition and construct the associated trans-series solution. By identifying the resurgent structures and cancellations in these non-Hermitian setups, we obtain the median-summed series, clarifying when the spectra are real or complex in accordance with the physical properties of each system. Establishing explicit links to the semi-classical path integral formalism, we elucidate the roles of bounce and bion configurations in these non-Hermitian systems. This analysis predicts PT-symmetry breaking, which we also verify numerically. Using the median quantization conditions, we prove the existence of this symmetry breaking and establish an exact equation for the exceptional point, which emerges as a remarkably simple algebraic relation between the bounce and bion actions. We further show that the median-summed non-perturbative correction to the spectrum vanishes at the exceptional point, while the resurgent structure survives through a universal minimal trans-series. For the resonance and anti-resonance systems, we find that the exact median-summed spectra are related by complex conjugation, representing time reversal in this setting, are necessarily complex, and do not exhibit an exceptional point. Although their spectra differ significantly from the PT-symmetric case, they share the same minimal trans-series. By maintaining explicit links with the path integral saddles and the formal theory of resurgence, our analysis provides a unified and general perspective on the quantization of non-Hermitian theories.

### [34] [Edge modes in Chern-Simons theory on a strip](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05889)
*Erica Bertolini,Michael Doyle,Nicola Maggiore,Conor Murphy,Carlotta Piras*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We study abelian Chern-Simons theory on a strip with two boundaries and show that consistent local boundary conditions lead to chiral bosonic edge modes described by Tomonaga-Luttinger actions, with opposite-moving currents and opposite central charges. A holographic-like bulk-boundary matching condition determines edge velocities, which are equal in magnitude but opposite in direction due to the boundary algebra structure, independent of strip width.

我们研究了在具有两个边界的条带几何上的阿贝尔Chern-Simons理论，表明一致的局域边界条件导致由Tomonaga-Luttinger型作用量描述的手性玻色子边缘模式，其沿两个边界以相反方向传播，并具有相反的中心电荷。一种类似全息的体-边界匹配条件决定了边缘速度，在对称设置中其大小相等、符号相反，且与条带宽度无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In topological field theories like Chern-Simons (CS) theory, physical edge states emerge when boundaries are present due to the breaking of gauge invariance. While the single-boundary case is well understood, the two-boundary setup—relevant for realistic quantum Hall devices—is less explored from a fully field-theoretic perspective. The goal is to derive edge dynamics directly from bulk CS theory with consistent boundary conditions, without relying on ad hoc assumptions about confining potentials or symmetry constraints.

在如Chern-Simons（CS）理论的拓扑场论中，当存在边界时由于规范不变性的破缺会出现物理边缘态。尽管单边界情况已被充分理解，但双边界情形——与真实的量子霍尔器件相关——从完全场论的角度尚缺乏深入研究。本工作的目标是从具有自洽边界条件的体CS理论直接导出边缘动力学，而不依赖于关于限制势或对称性约束的特设假设。

Method: We apply Symanzik's framework for power-counting consistent local boundary conditions to abelian Chern-Simons theory on a strip. By analyzing the residual gauge transformations at the boundary, we derive a broken gauge Ward identity that fixes the boundary dynamics. Canonical quantization leads to Kac-Moody current algebras on each edge with opposite central charges $c = \pm k$, where $k$ is the CS level. The resulting boundary actions are Tomonaga-Luttinger liquids supporting chiral bosons. A consistency condition between bulk equations and boundary terms yields a holographic-like matching that determines physical edge velocities.

我们将Symanzik的局域边界条件幂次计数框架应用于条带上的阿贝尔Chern-Simons理论。通过分析边界处的剩余规范变换，推导出破缺的规范Ward恒等式，从而确定边界动力学。正则量子化导致每个边缘上具有相反中心电荷$c = \pm k$（其中$k$为CS层级）的Kac-Moody流代数。所得边界作用量为支持手性玻色子的Tomonaga-Luttinger液体。体方程与边界项之间的一致性条件给出决定物理边缘速度的类全息匹配关系。

Result: The bulk equations of motion induce boundary dynamics through a broken gauge symmetry, leading to two-dimensional chiral boundary actions of Tomonaga-Luttinger type. Each edge supports a Kac-Moody current algebra with central charges $c = +k$ on one edge and $c = -k$ on the other. The edge modes are chiral bosons propagating in opposite directions with velocities $v_+ = -v_-$. These velocities are determined entirely by a bulk-boundary matching condition involving the CS coupling and boundary parameters, and are independent of the strip width. In symmetric setups, the equality and opposite sign of velocities arise purely from the algebraic structure of the boundary conditions.

体运动方程通过对称性破缺诱导出边界动力学，产生二维Tomonaga-Luttinger型的手性边界作用量。每条边缘支持一个Kac-Moody流代数，中心电荷分别为$c = +k$和$c = -k$。边缘模式为以相反方向传播的手性玻色子，速度满足$v_+ = -v_-$。这些速度完全由涉及CS耦合常数和边界参数的体-边界匹配条件决定，且与条带宽度无关。在对称设置中，速度大小相等、符号相反的性质纯粹源于边界条件的代数结构。

Conclusion: We provide a complete field-theoretic derivation of chiral edge dynamics in abelian Chern-Simons theory on a strip with two boundaries. The emergence of counter-propagating chiral bosons with opposite central charges is enforced by consistency of local boundary conditions with bulk gauge structure, via a broken Ward identity. The edge velocities are fixed by a holographic-like bulk-boundary correspondence, rather than by microscopic details or geometry. This establishes a robust realization of bulk-boundary correspondence in systems with two edges, applicable to quantum Hall physics and topological hydrodynamics.

我们给出了在具有两个边界的条带上阿贝尔Chern-Simons理论中手性边缘动力学的完整场论推导。通过对称性破缺的Ward恒等式，局域边界条件与体规范结构的一致性强制产生了具有相反中心电荷的反向传播手性玻色子。边缘速度由类全息的体-边界对应关系确定，而非由微观细节或几何决定。这建立了适用于量子霍尔物理和拓扑流体力学的双边缘系统中体-边界对应的稳健实现。

Abstract: We investigate abelian Chern-Simons gauge theory on a strip geometry with two spatial boundaries. In the presence of boundaries, gauge invariance is broken by boundary conditions, leading to physical edge excitations. By deriving the most general local boundary conditions consistent with power counting in the sense of Symanzik, we show that the bulk equations of motion determine the boundary degrees of freedom through a broken gauge Ward identity, yielding boundary Kac-Moody current algebras with opposite central charges on the two edges. The corresponding two-dimensional boundary actions are of Tomonaga-Luttinger type and describe chiral bosons propagating in opposite directions along the two boundaries. A consistency condition, interpreted as a holographic-like bulk-boundary matching, relates the Chern-Simons coupling constant and the boundary parameters to the physical edge velocities. Within this framework, the equality and opposite sign of the two velocities in a symmetric setup follow directly from the boundary structure rather than from model-dependent assumptions about confining potentials, and the velocities are independent of the strip width. Our analysis provides a fully field-theoretic realization of bulk-boundary correspondence in Chern-Simons theory with two boundaries, with direct applications to edge physics in quantum Hall systems and related topological/hydrodynamic settings.

</details>


### [35] [Geodesics from Quantum Field Theory: A Case Study in AdS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05901)
*Vaibhav Burman,Chethan Krishnan,Livesh Parajuli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper develops two rigorous implementations of geodesic motion for localized one-particle states in quantum field theory on curved spacetime, tested in global AdS₃. First, a covariant center-of-mass trajectory is defined via the stress tensor expectation $\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle$, shown to follow the geodesic equation under the monopole approximation using $\nabla_\mu\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle = 0$. Second, position operators are constructed from the Klein--Gordon inner product and mode completeness, with expectation values computed in single-particle wave packets. Explicit normalizable wave packets in AdS₃ are built, demonstrating both analytically and numerically that they reproduce timelike and null geodesics (radial, circular, elliptical-like). A controlled ultra-relativistic crossover from timelike to null behavior is identified, along with limits where geodesic localization breaks down. On the CFT side, bulk localization—particularly radial information—is encoded in the distribution over global descendants of the dual primary operator.

本文提出了在弯曲时空量子场论中单粒子局域态遵循测地线运动的两种严格实现方案，并在全局AdS₃中进行了详细检验。首先，通过应力张量算符期望值$\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle$定义了一个协变的“质心”轨迹，并利用$\nabla_\mu\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle = 0$证明其在单极近似下满足测地线方程，从而将经典广义相对论中的Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon框架推广至QFT-in-curved-spacetime。其次，基于Klein-Gordon内积和模完备性构造了位置算符，并计算了一般单粒子波包态下的期望值。作者构建了AdS₃中具有可调能量与角动量的显式可归一波包，解析与数值结果均表明两种方法能复现预期的类时与类光测地线（径向、圆形、椭圆型）。研究还识别出一个自然的超相对论极限，其中波包轨迹从类时平滑过渡到类光行为，并明确了局域化测地线描述失效的精确界限。在CFT侧，体空间中的局域化——特别是径向信息——由对偶原初算符的全局后裔分布所刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In quantum field theory in curved spacetime, the notion of particle localization and its classical correspondence—specifically whether localized quantum states follow geodesics—is not rigorously defined. While often assumed heuristically, a precise formulation connecting semiclassical one-particle states to geodesic motion is lacking. The motivation is to establish well-defined, covariant prescriptions for the trajectory of a localized quantum state and to verify their consistency with general relativity's predictions in a controlled setting such as global AdS₃, where exact computations are feasible. This bridges formal QFT concepts with semiclassical gravity intuition and informs holographic correspondences, particularly how bulk localization is encoded in boundary CFT data.

在弯曲时空量子场论中，粒子局域化的概念及其经典对应——即局域量子态是否遵循测地线——尚未被严格定义。尽管通常作为启发式假设使用，但目前仍缺乏将半经典单粒子态与测地线运动精确关联的公式体系。本文旨在建立良好定义且协变的局域量子态轨迹描述方案，并在如全局AdS₃这样可进行精确计算的受控环境中验证其与广义相对论预测的一致性。这有助于连接形式化的QFT概念与半经典引力直觉，并深化对全息对偶的理解，尤其是体空间局域化如何编码于边界CFT数据之中。

Method: Two distinct methods are developed: (1) A covariant center-of-mass trajectory is defined through the stress-energy tensor expectation value $\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle$. Using the conservation law $\nabla_\mu \langle T^{\mu\nu} \rangle = 0$, it is shown that in the monopole approximation (where higher multipole moments are neglected), the resulting trajectory satisfies the geodesic equation $\ddot{x}^\mu + \Gamma^\mu_{\alpha\beta} \dot{x}^\alpha \dot{x}^\beta = 0$ in general curved spacetimes. (2) Position operators are constructed using the Klein--Gordon inner product and the completeness of field modes. Expectation values of these operators are computed in generic single-particle wave packet states. Explicit Gaussian-like normalizable wave packets for a free scalar field in global AdS₃ are engineered with tunable energy and angular momentum. Both analytical solutions and numerical simulations are used to track the evolution of these wave packets and compare their trajectories to known geodesics. On the CFT side, the correspondence between bulk radial localization and the distribution over global descendants of the dual primary operator is analyzed.

发展了两种不同的方法：(1) 通过应力-能量张量期望值$\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle$定义协变的质心轨迹。利用守恒律$\nabla_\mu \langle T^{\mu\nu} \rangle = 0$，证明在单极近似（忽略高阶多极矩）下，该轨迹在一般弯曲时空中满足测地线方程$\ddot{x}^\mu + \Gamma^\mu_{\alpha\beta} \dot{x}^\alpha \dot{x}^\beta = 0$。(2) 基于Klein-Gordon内积与场模的完备性构造位置算符，并计算其在一般单粒子波包态中的期望值。在全局AdS₃中为自由标量场设计了具有可调能量和角动量的显式高斯型可归一波包。结合解析求解与数值模拟追踪波包演化，并将其轨迹与已知测地线进行比较。在CFT侧，分析了体空间径向局域化与对偶原初算符的全局后裔分布之间的对应关系。

Result: Both methods successfully reproduce expected timelike and null geodesics in AdS₃, including radial, circular, and elliptical-like orbits. Analytical and numerical evidence confirms that the center-of-mass trajectory derived from $\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle$ follows geodesic motion under the monopole approximation. Similarly, the position operator approach yields trajectories matching classical geodesics for appropriately localized wave packets. A natural ultra-relativistic regime is identified where the wave packet transitions smoothly from timelike to null geodesic behavior, reflecting the massless limit. Precise limits—such as large spatial extent or high delocalization—are identified where the geodesic interpretation breaks down. Furthermore, on the CFT side, it is shown that the radial profile of bulk localization correlates with the distribution of the state over global descendants of the dual primary operator, providing a microscopic CFT diagnosis of bulk position.

两种方法均成功复现了AdS₃中的预期类时与类光测地线，包括径向、圆形及椭圆型轨道。解析与数值证据证实，由$\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle$导出的质心轨迹在单极近似下遵循测地线运动。同样，位置算符方法也对适当局域化的波包给出了与经典测地线一致的轨迹。研究识别出一个自然的超相对论区域，其中波包从类时行为平滑过渡到类光测地线行为，反映了无质量极限。同时明确了局域化解释失效的精确界限，例如当波包空间展宽过大或高度非局域时。此外，在CFT侧发现，体空间局域化的径向分布与对偶原初算符的全局后裔分布相关联，从而提供了体空间位置的微观CFT判据。

Conclusion: The work establishes a rigorous foundation for interpreting localized one-particle states in QFT as following geodesic trajectories in curved spacetime. The two proposed prescriptions—one based on $\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle$ and the other on position operators from mode decomposition—are shown to be consistent with classical geodesic dynamics in AdS₃ under appropriate localization conditions. This provides a QFT generalization of the Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon framework and clarifies the semiclassical limit of particle motion. The breakdown of geodesic behavior at finite delocalization highlights quantum limitations to classical trajectory concepts. Finally, the connection to CFT descendant distributions offers a novel holographic dictionary entry relating bulk localization to boundary operator content.

本工作为解释弯曲时空中QFT中局域单粒子态沿测地线运动奠定了严格基础。所提出的两种方案——一种基于$\langle T^{\mu\nu}\rangle$，另一种基于模分解的位置算符——在适当的局域条件下均被证明与AdS₃中的经典测地线动力学一致。这实现了对Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon框架的QFT推广，并澄清了粒子运动的半经典极限。有限非局域化下测地线行为的失效揭示了经典轨迹概念的量子局限性。最后，与CFT后裔分布的联系提供了一条新的全息词典条目，将体空间局域化与边界算符内容相联系。

Abstract: Localized one-particle states of a quantum field theory--whether in flat space or on a curved background--are expected to exhibit geodesic motion in an appropriate semiclassical regime. This expectation is often invoked heuristically: in this work we develop two precise implementations and test them in detail in global AdS$_3$. First, we define a covariant ''center-of-mass'' trajectory from the expectation value of the stress tensor operator and show, using only $\nabla_μ\langle T^{μν}\rangle=0$, that it obeys the geodesic equation in the monopole (sufficiently localized) approximation in a general spacetime. This provides a QFT-in-curved-spacetime generalization of the Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon framework in classical general relativity. Second, we construct position operators from the Klein--Gordon inner product and mode completeness, and compute their expectation values in generic single-particle wave packet states. We then build explicit normalizable wave packets of a free scalar field in empty AdS$_3$ with tunable energy and angular momentum, and demonstrate analytically and numerically that both prescriptions reproduce the expected radial, circular, and elliptical-like timelike and null geodesics. Our discussion also isolates a natural ultra-relativistic regime in which the wave packet trajectory exhibits a controlled crossover from timelike to null geodesic behavior. We identify precise limits where the localized geodesic interpretation of the wave packet breaks down. On the CFT side, we show that bulk localization--specifically the radial data--is captured by how the state is distributed over global descendants of the dual primary.

</details>


### [36] [${\cal N}=4$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills thermodynamics to order $λ^{5/2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05919)
*Margaret E. Carrington,Gabor Kunstatter,Ubaid Tantary*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We compute the resummed perturbative free energy of $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM$_{44}$ up to order $\lambda^{5/2}$ at finite temperature, showing cancellation of infrared divergences and obtaining a UV- and IR-finite result. This is the highest possible order in perturbation theory due to nonperturbative effects at $\lambda^3$. We compare regularization schemes (RDR vs DR), construct a generalized Pad\'e approximant, and demonstrate superior convergence compared to QCD.

我们计算了四维 $\mathcal{N} = 4$ 超对称杨-米尔斯理论（SYM$_{44}$）在有限温度下的重求和自由能，直至't Hooft耦合的 $\lambda^{5/2}$ 阶。包含环图贡献后，红外发散完全抵消，结果在紫外和红外区域均为有限。这是微扰论中可达到的最高阶，因在 $\lambda^3$ 阶会出现与磁质量尺度相关的非微扰效应。我们比较了保持超对称的减维正则化（RDR）与标准维数正则化（DR），构建了匹配弱耦合（$\lambda^2$）与大$N_c$强耦合（$\lambda^{-3/2}$）极限的广义Pad\'e逼近，并表明SYM$_{44}$相比QCD具有更优的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The calculation of thermodynamic quantities in strongly coupled gauge theories is challenging. $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM$_{44}$ provides a unique testing ground due to its conformal invariance and supersymmetry, allowing high-order perturbative calculations and comparisons with holographic (AdS/CFT) strong coupling results. Understanding the convergence of perturbation theory and the role of infrared physics is essential for assessing its reliability.

计算强耦合规范理论中的热力学量具有挑战性。由于共形不变性和超对称性，$\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM$_{44}$为高阶微扰计算及与全息（AdS/CFT）强耦合结果的对比提供了独特平台。理解微扰论的收敛性以及红外物理的作用对于评估其可靠性至关重要。

Method: We perform hard thermal loop (HTL)-resummed perturbation theory in the imaginary-time formalism at finite temperature. Infrared divergences are regulated by including ring diagrams that capture long-wavelength fluctuations. Calculations are carried out to order $\lambda^{5/2}$ using both dimensional reduction (RDR) and canonical dimensional regularization (DR). A generalized Pad\'e approximant is constructed using known weak-coupling $\mathcal{O}(\lambda^2)$ and strong-coupling $\mathcal{O}(\lambda^{-3/2})$ limits.

我们在有限温度的虚时形式下采用硬热圈（HTL）重求和微扰论。通过引入包含长波涨落的环图来调控红外发散。使用减维正则化（RDR）和标准维数正则化（DR）进行至 $\lambda^{5/2}$ 阶的计算。利用已知的弱耦合（$\mathcal{O}(\lambda^2)$）与强耦合（$\mathcal{O}(\lambda^{-3/2})$）极限构建广义Pad\'e逼近。

Result: The resummed free energy is ultraviolet and infrared finite to order $\lambda^{5/2}$. Infrared divergences cancel between daisy and superdaisy diagrams when ring contributions are properly included. Results from RDR and DR agree when supersymmetry-preserving counterterms are used. The generalized Pad\'e approximant interpolates well between weak and strong coupling. The $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM$_{44}$ free energy shows better convergence than QCD, with smaller higher-order corrections.

重求和后的自由能在 $\lambda^{5/2}$ 阶是紫外和红外有限的。当正确包含环图贡献时，‘雏菊’与‘超级雏菊’图之间的红外发散相互抵消。使用保持超对称的抵消项时，RDR与DR的结果一致。广义Pad\'e逼近在弱耦合与强耦合之间实现了良好插值。$\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM$_{44}$的自由能相比QCD表现出更优的收敛性，高阶修正更小。

Conclusion: Perturbation theory in $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM$_{44}$ remains reliable up to $\lambda^{5/2}$, with controlled infrared behavior due to resummation. The agreement between RDR and DR (with proper counterterms) confirms consistency of regularization schemes in supersymmetric contexts. The improved convergence relative to QCD highlights the beneficial role of supersymmetry and conformal symmetry in organizing perturbative expansions. Nonperturbative effects enter at $\lambda^3$, setting a natural limit for perturbative methods.

在 $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM$_{44}$ 中，由于重求和的作用，微扰论在 $\lambda^{5/2}$ 阶内仍可靠且红外行为受控。RDR与DR（配合适当抵消项）的一致性验证了超对称背景下正则化方案的自洽性。相较于QCD的更优收敛性凸显了超对称与共形对称在组织微扰展开中的积极作用。非微扰效应在 $\lambda^3$ 阶进入，标志着微扰方法的自然极限。

Abstract: We calculate the resummed perturbative free energy of ${\cal N} = 4$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills in four spacetime dimensions (SYM$_{44}$) to order $λ^{5/2}$ in the 't Hooft coupling at finite temperature and zero chemical potential. All infrared divergences cancel when we include contributions from SYM$_{44}$ ring diagrams and the final result is both ultraviolet and infrared finite. Our result has special significance since order $λ^{5/2}$ is the highest order calculation that can be done with perturbation theory, because there are nonperturbative effects associated with the magnetic mass scale that come into play at order $λ^3$. We compare results obtained with regularization by dimensional reduction (RDR), which preserves supersymmetry, and canonical dimensional regularization (DR). We also compare with a generalized Padé approximant constructed by matching the weak coupling result at order $λ^2$ and the large $N_c$ strong coupling result at order $λ^{-3/2}$. Finally we make a comparison between our result and the QCD free energy and show that SYM$_{44}$ has better convergence properties.

### [37] [$ξRφ^2$ non-minimal coupling, and the long range gravitational potential for different spin fields from 2-2 scattering amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06062)
*Avijit Sen Majumder,Ayan Kumar Naskar,Sourav Bhattacharya*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We compute the long-range gravitational potential arising from the non-minimal curvature-scalar coupling $\xi R \phi^2$ in perturbative quantum gravity up to $\mathcal{O}(G^2 \xi)$, finding a leading $r^{-4}$ behavior in the non-relativistic limit, with extensions to scalar--massive spin-1 and spin-1/2 interactions showing spin-dependent effects.

我们计算了非最小耦合 $\xi R \phi^2$ 在微扰量子引力框架下产生的长程引力势，至 $\mathcal{O}(G^2 \xi)$ 阶，发现在非相对论极限下主导项为 $r^{-4}$ 行为，并推广到标量—大质量自旋-1 和自旋-1/2 散射，展示了自旋与极化依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The non-minimal coupling $\xi R \phi^2$ is naturally required for renormalization of scalar field theories in curved spacetime and may have significant long-range gravitational consequences. While prior work included cosmological constant effects, we study the case with vanishing cosmological constant to isolate the pure $\xi$-dependent quantum corrections to the gravitational potential.

非最小耦合 $\xi R \phi^2$ 在弯曲时空标量场论的重整化中自然出现，可能带来显著的长程引力效应。尽管先前研究包含了宇宙学常数的影响，本文研究宇宙学常数为零的情形，以分离出纯 $\xi$ 相关的量子修正对引力势的贡献。

Method: Using perturbative quantum gravity, we compute 2-2 scattering amplitudes involving scalars with non-minimal $\xi R \phi^2$ coupling up to $\mathcal{O}(G^2 \xi)$, including one-loop Feynman diagrams. The long-range potential is extracted via the non-relativistic limit and Fourier transform of the scattering amplitude. We extend the analysis to massive spin-1 and spin-1/2 fields using appropriate propagators and polarization sums.

在微扰量子引力框架下，我们计算了包含 $\xi R \phi^2$ 耦合的标量2-2散射振幅至 $\mathcal{O}(G^2 \xi)$，包括单圈费曼图；通过散射振幅的非相对论极限和傅里叶变换提取长程势；并使用适当的传播子和极化求和将分析推广至大质量自旋-1 和 自旋-1/2 场。

Result: The leading-order contribution to the potential appears at one-loop $\mathcal{O}(G^2 \xi)$, as tree-level $\mathcal{O}(G\xi)$ vanishes. The resulting potential exhibits a $\sim r^{-4}$ long-range behavior, distinct from Newtonian $r^{-1}$. For spinning particles, the potential acquires spin and polarization dependence, explicitly shown in scalar--vector and scalar--fermion cases.

由于树图阶 $\mathcal{O}(G\xi)$ 消失，势的领头贡献出现在单圈 $\mathcal{O}(G^2 \xi)$ 阶；所得势具有 $\sim r^{-4}$ 的长程行为，不同于牛顿势的 $r^{-1}$；对于有自旋粒子，势表现出自旋与极化依赖性，在标量—矢量和标量—费米子情形中被明确展示。

Conclusion: The $\xi R \phi^2$ non-minimal coupling generates a distinctive $r^{-4}$ gravitational potential at $\mathcal{O}(G^2 \xi)$ in the absence of a cosmological constant, indicating novel long-range quantum gravitational effects. These results suggest that such couplings could play a measurable role in low-energy precision gravity experiments or astrophysical observations, particularly when spin-dependent interactions are considered.

在无宇宙学常数时，$\xi R \phi^2$ 非最小耦合在 $\mathcal{O}(G^2 \xi)$ 阶产生独特的 $r^{-4}$ 引力势，表明存在新的长程量子引力效应；这些结果暗示此类耦合可能在低能精密引力实验或天体物理观测中（尤其是考虑自旋相关相互作用时）发挥可观测作用。

Abstract: In this paper we investigate the long range gravitational effect of curvature-scalar field non-minimal coupling, in the form of $ξR φ^2$, in the perturbative quantum gravity framework. Such coupling is most naturally motivated from the renormalisation of a scalar field theory with a quartic self interaction in a curved spacetime background. This coupling results in two scalar-$n$ graviton vertices which contain no explicit momenta of the scalar, qualitatively different from the usual, e.g. $κh^{μν}T_{μν}$-type minimal matter-graviton vertices. Assuming the dimensionless coupling parameter $ξ$ to be small, we compute the 2-2 scattering Feynman amplitudes between such scalars up to ${\cal O}(G^2 ξ)$. From the non-relativistic limit of these amplitudes, we compute the corresponding long range gravitational potential. There exists no tree level contribution $({\cal O}(ξG))$ here, and hence the one loop ${\cal O}(G^2 ξ)$ result is leading. Recently, the effect of a cosmological constant in such non-minimal interaction and the subsequent gravitational potential was computed. In this work we take the cosmological constant to be vanishing. The resulting potential is found to have $r^{-4}$ leading behaviour. We further extend these results for scalar-massive spin-1 and massive spin-1/2 scattering. Spin and polarisation dependence of the two body potential have been explicitly demonstrated. We discuss some possible physical implications of these results.

### [38] [The 't Hooft loop from a center-vortex wave functional](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05950)
*D. R. Junior,L. E. Oxman,H. Reinhardt*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper calculates the spatial 't Hooft loop in $SU(N)$ Yang-Mills theory using an infrared vacuum wave functional peaked at thin center vortices, finding a perimeter law, consistent with confinement as per 't Hooft's criterion.

本文利用一种峰值位于薄中心涡旋的红外真空波泛函，计算了$SU(N)$杨-米尔斯理论中的空间't Hooft环，发现其遵循周长律，符合't Hooft对禁闭的判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To further test the validity of the proposed infrared vacuum wave functional for $SU(N)$ Yang-Mills theory in describing confinement, beyond the Wilson loop area law.

为进一步检验所提出的$SU(N)$杨-米尔斯理论红外真空波泛函在描述禁闭方面的有效性，超越威尔逊环的面积律之外。

Method: Using the previously constructed vacuum wave functional that is peaked at thin center vortices, the authors compute the expectation value of the spatial 't Hooft loop operator in the infrared regime.

使用先前构建的、峰值位于薄中心涡旋的真空波泛函，作者计算了空间't Hooft环算符在红外区域的期望值。

Result: The spatial 't Hooft loop exhibits a perimeter law, $\langle T(C) \rangle \sim \exp(-\mu L)$ where $L$ is the perimeter of the loop $C$, consistent with 't Hooft's dual criterion for confinement.

空间't Hooft环呈现出周长律，$\langle T(C) \rangle \sim \exp(-\mu L)$，其中$L$是环路$C$的周长，符合't Hooft对禁闭的对偶判据。

Conclusion: The perimeter law result supports the confining nature of the vacuum described by the vortex-peaked wave functional and confirms its consistency with 't Hooft's duality-based confinement criterion.

周长律的结果支持了由峰值在涡旋上的波泛函所描述的真空的禁闭性质，并验证了其与基于't Hooft对偶性的禁闭判据的一致性。

Abstract: Previously, we proposed an infrared vacuum wave functional for $SU(N)$ Yang-Mills theory peaked at thin center vortices and showed that it yields an area law for the Wilson loop. In this work, we use this wave functional to calculate the spatial 't Hooft loop, for which we find a perimeter law, in accordance with 't Hooft's criterion for confinement.

### [39] [Massive Exchange and the Sign of the Equilateral Bispectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06145)
*Diptimoy Ghosh,Suvashis Maity,Farman Ullah*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The study revisits the inflationary bispectrum from massive scalar exchange in the Effective Field Theory (EFT) of inflation using bootstrap methods, showing that the commonly assumed universal negativity of the equilateral bispectrum is not generic when higher-order EFT operators are included. The sign depends on the relative strength of interactions, with a derived critical ratio determining the transition between positive and negative signals. Modifications due to reduced sound speed and multi-particle exchange further allow for positive equilateral non-Gaussianity even when subdominant operators dominate.

该研究使用bootstrap方法重新审视了有效场论（EFT）中由大质量标量粒子交换产生的暴胀三谱，表明当包含高阶算符时，通常假设的正三角三谱普遍负性并非普适。其符号取决于相互作用系数的相对强度，并导出了决定正负转变的临界比值。声速降低和多粒子交换的修正进一步允许即使在高阶算符次主导的情况下也出现正的正三角非高斯信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: It has been previously established that in the EFT of inflation with only the leading boost-breaking operator, the equilateral bispectrum from tree-level exchange of a principal-series massive scalar is universally negative, regardless of the coupling sign. This apparent universality suggests a possible fundamental constraint on observable signatures in inflationary models. However, this result was derived under a restricted operator basis. The motivation of this work is to generalize the analysis to the full EFT operator basis to determine whether the negativity is truly universal or an artifact of truncating the operator expansion.

先前研究表明，在仅存在主导破boost对称算符的有效场论（EFT）框架下，主级数大质量标量交换所产生的正三角三谱普遍为负，与耦合符号无关。这种表观普适性暗示暴胀模型可观测信号可能存在某种基本限制。然而，这一结论基于受限的算符基底得出。本工作的动机是将分析推广到完整的EFT算符基底，以确定负号特性究竟是普适规律还是算符展开截断的人为结果。

Method: The authors employ cosmological bootstrap techniques to construct the de Sitter-invariant seed four-point function for the inflaton-hidden sector system. Using weight-shifting operators, they uplift solutions from lower-weight correlators and extract the inflationary bispectrum via a soft-limit procedure. They include all relevant EFT operators up to cubic order in perturbations, going beyond the leading $\dot{\pi}^3$ interaction. The analysis incorporates corrections from reduced sound speed ($c_s < 1$) and extends to multi-particle exchange by summing over multiple exchanged states in the conformal partial wave expansion.

作者采用宇宙学bootstrap方法构建暴胀子-隐含 sector 系统的dS不变种子四点函数。利用权重提升算符（weight-shifting operators），从低权重关联函数提升解，并通过软极限程序提取暴胀三谱。他们包含了直至扰动三次项的所有相关EFT算符，超越了主导的$\dot{\pi}^3$相互作用。分析中纳入了声速降低（$c_s < 1$）的修正，并通过在共形部分波展开中对多个交换态求和，推广至多粒子交换情形。

Result: While the equilateral bispectrum remains strictly negative when only the leading EFT operator is present, the inclusion of higher-order operators introduces new cubic structures that contribute comparably in the equilateral limit. These contributions can overcome the negativity, leading to a positive equilateral bispectrum depending on the ratio of coupling coefficients. A critical ratio $\Lambda_{\rm crit}$ is derived that separates positive and negative regions. For $c_s < 1$, this critical ratio is modified due to altered kinematics. In the case of multi-particle exchange, constructive interference allows a positive signal even when the higher-order operator is subdominant, demonstrating that positivity is achievable under physically plausible conditions.

当仅存在主导EFT算符时，正三角三谱仍严格为负；但引入高阶算符后，新的立方结构在正三角极限下产生可比拟的贡献，这些贡献可克服原有负性，导致正的正三角三谱，具体取决于耦合系数之比。文中导出了分隔正负区域的临界比值$\Lambda_{\rm crit}$。对于$ c_s < 1 $的情况，由于运动学改变，该临界比值被修正。在多粒子交换情况下，建设性干涉使得即使高阶算符次主导也能产生正信号，表明在物理上合理的条件下正性是可以实现的。

Conclusion: The universal negativity of the equilateral bispectrum from massive scalar exchange in inflation is not a robust prediction of the full EFT of inflation, but rather a consequence of restricting to the leading-order operator. When the complete set of EFT operators is considered, the sign of the bispectrum becomes model-dependent, governed by the relative strengths of different interactions. This result lifts a previously assumed theoretical constraint and expands the space of allowed non-Gaussian signatures in inflationary cosmology, particularly opening the possibility of detectable positive equilateral non-Gaussianity from heavy particle exchange.

大质量标量交换在暴胀中产生的正三角三谱的普遍负性并非完整EFTofLSS的稳健预测，而是局限于领头阶算符的结果。当考虑完整的EFT算符集时，三谱的符号变为依赖于不同相互作用相对强度的模型依赖量。这一结果解除了此前假设的理论约束，拓展了暴胀宇宙学中允许的非高斯信号空间，特别是开启了由重粒子交换产生可观测正的正三角非高斯性的可能性。

Abstract: We study the inflationary bispectrum generated by the tree-level exchange of a massive hidden-sector scalar during inflation. When the interaction between the inflaton and the hidden sector arises only from the leading boost-breaking operator of the Effective Field Theory (EFT) of inflation, the equilateral bispectrum for principal-series scalar exchange is known to be universally negative, independent of the sign of the coupling. We revisit this result within the full EFT operator basis. Using bootstrap methods, we construct the de Sitter-invariant seed four-point function and obtain the inflationary bispectrum via weight-shifting operators and a soft-limit procedure. While the equilateral bispectrum remains strictly negative when only the leading interaction is present, additional operators generate independent cubic structures whose contributions compete in the equilateral configuration. As a result, the sign of the bispectrum is no longer universal. We derive a critical ratio of interaction coefficients that separates regions of positive and negative equilateral bispectrum. We further study the effects of reduced sound speed $c_s<1$ and the exchange of multiple particles. In both cases, the critical ratio is modified, and for multi-particle exchange a positive equilateral bispectrum can arise even when the higher-order operator is subdominant. Our results show that the negativity of the equilateral bispectrum from massive exchange is not generic, but reflects a restricted operator structure in the EFT of inflation.

</details>


### [40] [Holographic entanglement entropy, Wilson loops, and neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05970)
*Veselin G. Filev*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We apply artificial neural networks to solve the holographic inverse problem by reconstructing bulk geometry from boundary entanglement entropy, using the Ryu--Takayanagi area functional as a differentiable loss. The method achieves high accuracy in recovering metric functions, resolves degeneracies via Wilson loop data, and introduces a three-network variational approach for multi-observable integration.

我们应用人工神经网络解决全息逆问题，通过边界纠缠熵重构体几何，使用Ryu-Takayanagi面积泛函作为可微损失函数。该方法在恢复度规函数方面实现了高精度，通过威尔逊环数据解决了简并性，并引入了三网络变分方法以整合多可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The holographic inverse problem—reconstructing bulk geometry from boundary data—is central to understanding quantum gravity via gauge/gravity duality. While entanglement entropy provides geometric information through the Ryu--Takayanagi formula, it often leads to ambiguities (e.g., degenerate metric reconstructions). We aim to resolve such degeneracies and enable precise, flexible reconstruction using machine learning.

全息逆问题——从边界数据重构体几何——是通过规范/引力对偶理解量子引力的核心。虽然纠缠熵通过Ryu-Takayanagi公式提供几何信息，但常导致模糊性（例如度规重构的简并性）。我们的目标是利用机器学习解决这些简并性并实现精确且灵活的重构。

Method: We use artificial neural networks trained with the Ryu--Takayanagi area functional as a differentiable loss to reconstruct bulk metrics from boundary entanglement entropy. For degeneracy resolution, we incorporate holographic Wilson loop data sensitive to the timelike metric component. A semi-analytical inversion is developed using Bilson's and Hashimoto's formulas, and a three-network variational method minimizes both the area and Nambu--Goto actions simultaneously.

我们使用以Ryu-Takayanagi面积泛函为可微损失的人工神经网络，从边界纠缠熵中重构体度规。为解决简并性，我们引入对类时度规分量敏感的全息威尔逊环数据。我们发展了一种半解析反演方法，结合Bilson和Hashimoto公式，并采用三网络变分法同时最小化面积和Nambu-Goto作用量。

Result: On the AdS-Schwarzschild background, the neural network reconstructs the blackening factor $f(r)$ with 1.7% error. In the Gubser--Rocha model, strip entanglement entropy alone determines only the spatial metric function; adding Wilson loop data resolves the one-function degeneracy. The three-network method achieves sub-0.2% accuracy in reconstructing both metric components, even without closed-form derivatives.

在AdS-Schwarzschild背景下，神经网络以1.7%的误差重构出黑化因子$f(r)$。在Gubser-Rocha模型中，仅带状纠缠熵只能确定空间度规函数；加入威尔逊环数据后解除了单函数简并性。三网络方法在两个度规分量的重构中均达到低于0.2%的误差，即使在没有闭式导数关系的情况下亦然。

Conclusion: Artificial neural networks provide a powerful and flexible framework for solving the holographic inverse problem. By combining multiple holographic observables—entanglement entropy and Wilson loops—and leveraging differentiable geometric functionals, we achieve high-precision metric reconstruction and resolve exact degeneracies, paving the way for data-driven exploration of quantum gravity.

人工神经网络为求解全息逆问题提供了强大而灵活的框架。通过结合多种全息可观测量——纠缠熵与威尔逊环——并利用可微几何泛函，我们实现了高精度的度规重构并解决了精确简并性，为数据驱动的量子引力研究铺平了道路。

Abstract: We apply artificial neural networks to the holographic inverse problem, reconstructing bulk geometry from boundary entanglement entropy by using the Ryu--Takayanagi area functional as a differentiable loss. Validated on the AdS-Schwarzschild background, this approach recovers the blackening factor to 1.7% accuracy. For finite-density backgrounds like the Gubser--Rocha model, we demonstrate that strip entanglement entropy determines only the spatial metric. We resolve this exact one-function degeneracy by incorporating holographic Wilson loop data, which couples to the timelike metric. We present a semi-analytical inversion combining Bilson's and Hashimoto's formulas, alongside a general three-network variational method minimizing the combined area and Nambu--Goto actions. The neural network achieves sub-0.2% accuracy for both metric functions without closed-form derivative relations, establishing a flexible framework for integrating multiple holographic observables.

### [41] [Background Fields Meet the Heat Kernel: Gauge Invariance and RGEs without diagrams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05972)
*Debanjan Balui,Joydeep Chakrabortty,Christoph Englert,Subhendra Mohanty,Tushar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We present a novel method combining the Heat Kernel and Background Field Method to compute gauge-invariant and gauge-parameter-independent quantities—such as the effective potential, anomalous dimensions, and renormalization group equations—using only background field dynamics, without input from traditional Feynman diagrams. By consistently handling open and closed derivatives in Heat Kernel expansions, we derive $\beta$ functions and demonstrate their gauge independence when background fields are on-shell, validated in Scalar QED, Yukawa theory, and the bosonic sector of the Standard Model.

本文提出一种结合热核（Heat Kernel）与背景场方法的新方法，仅利用背景场动力学计算规范不变且规范参数无关的物理量（如有效势、反常量纲和重整化群方程），无需传统费曼图计算的额外输入。通过在热核展开中一致处理开导数与闭导数，我们在背景场满足运动方程时推导出$\beta$函数并证明其规范参数无关性，该方法在标量QED、Yukawa理论及标准模型的玻色子部分得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional methods for computing quantum corrections in gauge theories often rely on diagrammatic perturbation theory and suffer from gauge dependence, requiring additional steps (e.g., Nielsen identities) to ensure physical results. The need for a purely background-field-based, manifestly gauge-invariant framework motivates the development of a method that avoids explicit diagrammatics and ensures gauge parameter independence intrinsically.

在规范场论中，传统量子修正计算通常依赖于微扰图方法，并存在规范依赖问题，需借助Nielsen恒等式等额外手段确保结果的物理性。因此，亟需发展一种完全基于背景场、显式规范不变且内禀保证规范参数无关性的计算框架。

Method: We employ the Heat Kernel (HK) technique within the Background Field Method, focusing on the proper treatment of open and closed covariant derivatives in the HK expansion. This allows us to extract gauge-invariant quantities directly from the background field effective action. By ensuring consistency between open and closed derivative structures, we obtain renormalization group coefficients such as $\beta$ functions and anomalous dimensions without input from standard diagrammatic calculations. The formalism is applied to Scalar QED, Yukawa theory, and the bosonic sector of the Standard Model.

我们在背景场方法中采用热核（Heat Kernel）技术，重点在于热核展开中开协变导数与闭协变导数的一致处理。这种方法使我们能直接从背景场有效作用量中提取规范不变量，通过保持开导数与闭导数组合结构的一致性，在无需标准费曼图计算输入的情况下获得$\beta$函数、反常量纲等重整化群系数。该形式体系应用于标量QED、Yukawa理论以及标准模型的玻色子部分。

Result: We derive the $\beta$ functions and anomalous dimensions in a fully gauge-parameter-independent manner when the background fields are on-shell. The results match known expressions in Scalar QED and Yukawa theory. For the bosonic sector of the Standard Model, we obtain complete one-loop $\beta$ functions solely from background field dynamics, confirming the validity and robustness of our approach.

当背景场满足运动方程时，我们以完全规范参数无关的方式导出了$\beta$函数和反常量纲。结果与标量QED和Yukawa理论中的已知表达式一致。对于标准模型的玻色子部分，我们仅从背景场动力学中得到了完整的一圈$\beta$函数，验证了该方法的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: The combination of the Heat Kernel and Background Field Method, with consistent treatment of open and closed derivatives, provides a powerful and self-contained framework for computing physical, gauge-invariant quantities without reliance on diagrammatics. This opens a new pathway toward first-principles computations in quantum field theory, particularly in gravitational and non-perturbative settings where diagrammatic methods are less effective.

热核与背景场方法的结合，通过一致处理开导数与闭导数，提供了一个强大且自洽的框架，可在无需依赖费曼图的情况下计算物理的、规范不变的量。这为量子场论中的第一性原理计算开辟了新路径，尤其适用于图方法较弱的引力与非微扰体系。

Abstract: We introduce a new method that exploits the combination of the Heat Kernel (HK) and Background Field Method to compute gauge-invariant and gauge parameter-independent quantities such as the effective potential, anomalous dimensions, and renormalization group equations. In contrast to currently employed techniques, these results are obtained exclusively from the dynamics of the background fields, without relying on supplementary input from, e.g., traditional diagrammatic calculations. This is achieved by a consistent treatment of open and closed derivatives in the HK expansions. In this way, we compute the standard quantities such as $β$ functions and their gauge-parameter independence when background fields are on-shell. We demonstrate this formalism for instructive examples such as Scalar QED and Yukawa theory. Full results for the bosonic part of the Standard Model provide further validation of our approach.

### [42] [Are Black Holes Fuzzballs? Probing Horizon-Scale Structure with LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06009)
*Pablo F. Muguruza,Carlos F. Sopuerta*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: LISA observations of EMRIs can tightly constrain deviations from the Kerr metric, particularly higher multipole moments, providing unprecedented tests of quantum gravity models like the fuzzball proposal.

LISA对EMRI的观测能够严格限制偏离Kerr度规的效应，特别是高阶多极矩，为fuzzball等量子引力模型提供了前所未有的检验手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The strong-field regime of gravity near black holes is a key testing ground for quantum gravity. The fuzzball proposal challenges the classical black hole paradigm by replacing horizons with quantum structures; however, it lacks direct observational constraints. Gravitational waves from extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) offer a unique opportunity to probe the near-horizon geometry with high precision, enabling tests of such alternatives to Kerr black holes.

黑洞附近强引力场区域是检验量子引力理论的关键场所。fuzzball提议用量子结构取代事件视界，挑战了经典黑洞范式，但目前缺乏直接观测约束。极端质量比旋进（EMRI）产生的引力波为高精度探测近视界几何提供了独特机会，从而可检验Kerr黑洞的替代理论。

Method: We introduce generic multipolar deformations to the Kerr metric to parameterize potential symmetry breakings in the spacetime geometry. Using waveform models that include these deformations, we perform a systematic Fisher matrix-based parameter estimation analysis for EMRI signals detectable by LISA. This allows us to forecast the sensitivity of LISA to deviations in mass and current multipoles, especially in the quadrupole and octupole sectors, including both axisymmetric and non-axisymmetric cases.

我们引入对Kerr度规的通用多极形变以参数化时空几何中潜在的对称性破缺。利用包含这些形变的波形模型，基于Fisher矩阵方法对LISA可观测的EMRI信号进行系统性的参数估计分析，从而预测LISA对质量与电流多极矩（尤其是四极和八极项，包括轴对称与非轴对称情形）偏离的灵敏度。

Result: For realistic EMRI signals with astrophysically motivated signal-to-noise ratios, LISA can constrain non-axisymmetric mass quadrupole deformations at the $10^{-3}$ level and axisymmetric mass octupole deformations at the $10^{-2}$ level—orders of magnitude tighter than current electromagnetic or ground-based gravitational-wave bounds. These sensitivities are sufficient to probe characteristic signatures of fuzzball geometries and rule out or support specific quantum-gravity-motivated models.

对于具有天体物理典型信噪比的EMRI信号，LISA能够以$10^{-3}$精度限制非轴对称质量四极形变，以$10^{-2}$精度限制轴对称质量八极形变——比现有电磁或地面引力波观测的限制高出数个数量级。该灵敏度足以探测fuzzball几何的特征信号，进而排除或支持特定的量子引力驱动模型。

Conclusion: Precision measurements of EMRI waveforms by LISA will open a new observational window into horizon-scale physics, enabling direct empirical tests of quantum-gravity-inspired models such as the fuzzball proposal. This positions LISA as a fundamental physics laboratory, capable of constraining beyond-Kerr dynamics and offering the first data-driven insights into the quantum nature of compact objects.

LISA对EMRI波形的精确测量将打开通向视界尺度物理的新观测窗口，实现对fuzzball等量子引力启发模型的直接实证检验。这使LISA成为基础物理实验室，有能力限制超越Kerr的动力学，并提供关于致密天体量子本质的首批数据驱动见解。

Abstract: Gravitational waves provide a unique probe of the strong-field regime of gravity, offering access to physics beyond the classical black hole paradigm. We explore how space-based observations of extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) by the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) can be used to test the fuzzball proposal, a quantum gravity-inspired alternative to Kerr black holes. By introducing generic multipolar deformations encoding potential symmetry breakings and performing a systematic parameter estimation analysis, we forecast LISA's ability to constrain deviations from the Kerr geometry in the near-horizon region. We show that EMRI signals with realistic signal-to-noise ratios can constrain multiple higher-order multipoles at levels orders of magnitude beyond current electromagnetic and ground-based gravitational-wave bounds, opening a new observational window onto horizon-scale structure. In particular, we find that LISA can constrain generic non-axisymmetric mass quadrupole deformations at the $10^{-3}$ level and axisymmetric mass octupole deformations at the $10^{-2}$ level, providing concrete observational targets for identifying fuzzball geometries. Our results demonstrate that precision measurements of EMRI waveforms will transform LISA into a powerful laboratory for fundamental physics and offer the first direct empirical constraints on quantum-gravity-motivated models of compact objects.

### [43] [Comments on Symmetry Operators, Asymptotic Charges and Soft Theorems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06088)
*Luigi Tizzano*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that emergent 1-form symmetries in QED, in both massive (HQET) and massless (SCET) effective field theory regimes, lead to an infinite-dimensional Abelian algebra of conserved charges with a central extension. These charges are related to asymptotic symmetries and imply the leading electric and magnetic soft photon theorems. The central term fixes a contact term in amplitudes with two soft photons of mixed polarization, and the framework is extended to inclusive observables relevant for QED photon detectors.

本文证明了在QED中，无论是大质量（HQET）还是无质量（SCET）有效场论区域，涌现的1-形式对称性导致了一个具有中心扩张的无限维阿贝尔守恒荷代数。这些荷与渐近对称性相关，并导出了主导的电和磁软光子定理。该代数中的中心项固定了两个混合极化软光子散射振幅中的一个接触项，并且该构造被推广到适用于QED光子探测器的含入观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Soft theorems in quantum field theory are deeply connected to asymptotic symmetries and memory effects. However, the role of higher-form symmetries—particularly 1-form symmetries—in gauge theories like QED has only recently been explored. This work aims to clarify how emergent 1-form symmetries in different kinematic limits of QED (HQET for massive particles, SCET for massless) give rise to soft photon theorems and whether they form a richer algebraic structure involving central extensions.

量子场论中的软定理与渐近对称性和记忆效应密切相关。然而，高阶形式对称性——特别是1-形式对称性——在如QED这类规范理论中的作用直到最近才被探索。本研究旨在阐明QED在不同运动学极限下（大质量粒子的HQET，无质量粒子的SCET）涌现的1-形式对称性如何导致软光子定理，以及它们是否形成包含中心扩张的更丰富代数结构。

Method: The authors analyze the structure of the soft sector in QED within the frameworks of HQET (Heavy Quark Effective Theory) and SCET (Soft-Collinear Effective Theory). They identify electric and magnetic 1-form symmetries in the respective regimes and construct associated conserved charges. By integrating over appropriate hypersurfaces in Minkowski spacetime, they relate these charges to asymptotic symmetry generators. They derive the algebra of these charges, revealing a central extension, and connect it to soft photon theorems via Ward identities. They also compute the contact term in two-soft-photon amplitudes implied by the central charge and extend the analysis to inclusive observables using detector models in QED.

作者在HQET（重夸克有效理论）和SCET（软-共线有效理论）框架下分析QED中软区间的结构。他们在相应区域识别出电和磁的1-形式对称性，并构建相关的守恒荷。通过在闵可夫斯基时空中对适当超曲面进行积分，将这些荷与渐近对称性生成元联系起来。他们推导了这些荷的代数结构，揭示了其存在中心扩张，并通过Ward恒等式将其与软光子定理关联。他们还计算了由中心荷决定的双软光子振幅中的接触项，并利用QED中的探测器模型将分析扩展到含入观测量。

Result: The soft sector of QED in both HQET and SCET exhibits electric and magnetic 1-form symmetries. These generate an infinite-dimensional Abelian algebra of conserved charges with a non-trivial central extension. Upon reduction to asymptotic hypersurfaces, these charges reproduce the standard asymptotic symmetry charges and imply the leading soft photon theorems for both electric and magnetic sectors. The central term fixes a specific contact term in scattering amplitudes with two soft photons of mixed electric-magnetic polarization. The construction is generalized to inclusive observables, providing a symmetry basis for modeling photon detectors in QED.

在HQET和SCET中的QED软区间表现出电和磁的1-形式对称性。这些对称性生成一个具有非平凡中心扩张的无限维阿贝尔守恒荷代数。当约化到渐近超曲面时，这些荷重现标准的渐近对称性荷，并导出电和磁部门的主导软光子定理。中心项固定了具有混合电-磁极化的两个软光子散射振幅中的特定接触项。该构造被推广到含入观测量，为QED中光子探测器的建模提供了对称性基础。

Conclusion: Emergent 1-form symmetries in effective descriptions of QED play a fundamental role in organizing soft dynamics and underlie soft photon theorems. The presence of a centrally extended infinite-dimensional charge algebra suggests a deeper algebraic structure in gauge theories, analogous to Kac-Moody or Virasoro algebras in 2D CFTs. This structure not only explains known soft theorems but also predicts new constraints on multi-soft-photon amplitudes and provides a symmetry-based foundation for detector physics in QED.

在QED的有效描述中，涌现的1-形式对称性在组织软动力学中起着根本作用，并构成了软光子定理的基础。具有中心扩张的无限维荷代数的存在表明规范理论中存在更深的代数结构，类似于二维CFT中的Kac-Moody或Virasoro代数。这一结构不仅解释了已知的软定理，还预测了对多软光子振幅的新约束，并为QED中的探测器物理提供了基于对称性的基础。

Abstract: We study the relation between emergent 1-form symmetries and soft photon theorems in QED. We show that in the relevant massive and massless kinematic regimes, described respectively by HQET and SCET, the soft sector admits electric and magnetic 1-form symmetries. We then show that these symmetries give rise to an infinite-dimensional Abelian algebra of ordinary conserved charges, with a central extension. In Minkowski spacetime, suitable choices of hypersurfaces reduce these charges to the familiar asymptotic symmetry charges and imply the leading electric and magnetic soft photon theorems. We further show that the central term in this algebra fixes a contact term appearing in scattering amplitudes involving two soft photons with mixed electric-magnetic polarizations. Finally, we extend the same construction to inclusive observables and apply it to QED photon detectors.

</details>

### [44] [Unquenched Radially Excited $P$-wave Charmonia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04991)
*George Rupp*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: First radial excitations of P-wave charmonia are studied using the Resonance-Spectrum Expansion, including all OZI-allowed decay channels via a generalized $^{3}P_0$ model to avoid spectral distortions.

使用共振谱展开方法研究P波粲偶素的首次径向激发态，包含所有OZI允许的衰变道，并通过推广的$^{3}P_0$模型计算耦合常数以避免能谱畸变。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The mass pattern of P-wave charmonia in the 3.85–3.95 GeV region deviates significantly from quenched quark model predictions, with unexpected states like two scalar $χ_{c0}$ resonances; this calls for inclusion of dynamical decay effects beyond static models.

在3.85–3.95 GeV区域的P波粲偶素质量分布显著偏离静态夸克模型预测，出现如两个标量$χ_{c0}$态等异常现象，需引入超出静态模型的动力学衰变效应。

Method: The Resonance-Spectrum Expansion (RSE) is employed, incorporating all OZI-allowed open-charm decay channels through a generalized $^{3\!}P_0$ model for consistent coupling constant computation across different positive-parity charmonia.

采用共振谱展开（Resonance-Spectrum Expansion, RSE）方法，通过推广的$^{3\!}P_0$模型包含所有OZI允许的开粲衰变道，以一致地计算各类正宇称粲偶素的耦合常数。

初步结果显示，基于推广$^{3\!}P_0$模型的RSE引入动力学衰变效应后，能显著改变预期的质量谱，可能解决诸如两个$χ_{c0}$态共存及能级结构畸变等问题。

Conclusion: Dynamical strong-decay effects are essential for understanding the spectroscopy of radially excited P-wave charmonia, and the generalized $^{3\!}P_0$-RSE approach provides a consistent framework to incorporate these without introducing artificial spectral distortions.

动力学强衰变效应对理解径向激发P波粲偶素的谱结构至关重要，推广的$^{3\!}P_0$-RSE方法为无畸变地纳入这些效应提供了自洽框架。

Abstract: The ground-state positive-parity charmonia $χ_{c0}(1P)$, $χ_{c1}(1P)$, $h_c(1P)$, and $χ_{c2}(1P)$ are generally well described in static (``quenched'') quark models, in which dynamical effects of actual or virtual strong decay are neglected. In contrast, the five PDG candidates for $P$-wave charmonia in the energy region 3.85-3.95 GeV, probably including the first radial excitations of the above ones, display a totally different and quite disparate mass pattern. Moreover, two scalar states are listed, viz. $χ_{c0}(3860)$ and $χ_{c0}(3915)$, the former one apparently being very broad.
  Preliminary results will be presented here for the first radial excitations of the lowest $P$-wave $c\bar{c}$ states, obtained with the Resonance-Spectrum Expansion while including in the calculation all OZI-allowed decay channels of the most relevant charm-meson pairs. Employing a generalised scheme of computing coupling constants for decays based on the ${}^{3\!}P_0$ model ensures that no distortion of the spectra will occur due to the different classes of allowed decay channels for the various positive-parity charmonia.

### [45] [Electroweak Doublet Dark Matter for a Galactic Halo Gamma-Ray Excess](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05016)
*Yasunori Nomura,Tomonori Totani*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates minimal extensions of the Standard Model to explain a claimed indirect-detection signal of dark matter in the 400–800 GeV mass range, showing that an electroweak doublet dark matter model with Higgs-portal interactions provides a natural explanation through dominant annihilation into longitudinal gauge bosons and allows for inelastic scattering consistent with direct-detection anomalies.

本文研究了标准模型的最小扩展，以解释在400–800 GeV质量范围内暗物质的潜在间接探测信号，表明具有Higgs-portal相互作用的电弱二重态暗物质模型可通过主导的纵向规范玻色子湮灭提供自然解释，并允许与直接探测反常一致的非弹性散射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: A recent claim of an indirect-detection signal from the Galactic halo, potentially due to dark matter annihilation, motivates the need to revisit minimal dark matter models that can explain this signal while satisfying existing experimental and cosmological constraints, particularly for weakly interacting massive particles (WIMPs) in the 400–800 GeV mass range.

银河系晕中最近声称的间接探测信号（可能源于暗物质湮灭）促使人们重新审视能够解释该信号并同时满足现有实验和宇宙学约束的最小暗物质模型，特别是针对400–800 GeV质量范围内的弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMPs）。

Method: The authors analyze the simplest extensions of the Standard Model, focusing on electroweak doublet dark matter coupled via Higgs-portal interactions. They compute the thermal relic abundance, annihilation channels (especially into longitudinal gauge bosons), branching fractions, and implications for direct detection, including inelastic dark matter scenarios with small mass splittings. They also explore enhancements to the present-day annihilation rate using a simple extension involving a light scalar field.

作者分析了标准模型的最简扩展，聚焦于通过Higgs-portal相互作用耦合的电弱二重态暗物质。他们计算了热遗迹丰度、湮灭通道（特别是到纵向规范玻色子）、分支比以及对直接探测的影响，包括具有小质量分裂的非弹性暗物质情形。此外，他们还探讨了引入轻标量场的简单扩展对当前湮灭率增强的可能性。

Result: Electroweak doublet dark matter with Higgs-portal interactions naturally explains the observed relic abundance and the claimed indirect-detection signal via dominant annihilation into $W_L^+ W_L^-$ and $Z_L Z_L$ final states. The model predicts characteristic branching fractions and allows for a mass splitting of order $\sim 100\ \text{keV}$, consistent with a recent direct-detection anomaly. A light scalar mediator can enhance the annihilation rate today without violating constraints from dwarf spheroidal galaxies if its mass is appropriately chosen.

具有Higgs-portal相互作用的电弱二重态暗物质可通过主导的$W_L^+ W_L^-$和$Z_L Z_L$末态湮灭自然地解释观测到的遗迹丰度和所声称的间接探测信号。该模型预测了特征性的分支比，并允许约$\sim 100\ \text{keV}$的质量分裂，与最近的直接探测反常一致。若选择合适的质量，轻标量传播子可增强当今的湮灭率，同时不违反来自矮椭球星系的约束。

Conclusion: The electroweak doublet dark matter model with Higgs-portal interactions provides a minimal, self-consistent framework that explains both the thermal relic abundance and the potential indirect-detection signal around 400–800 GeV, while remaining compatible with direct-detection results through inelastic scattering. It represents a well-motivated benchmark for future collider, direct, and indirect searches.

具有Higgs-portal相互作用的电弱二重态暗物质模型提供了一个极小且自洽的框架，既能解释热遗迹丰度，也能解释400–800 GeV附近的潜在间接探测信号，同时通过非弹性散射与直接探测结果兼容。它为未来的对撞机、直接和间接搜寻提供了有说服力的基准模型。

Abstract: Weakly interacting massive particles provide a well-motivated framework for dark matter, naturally reproducing the observed relic abundance through thermal freeze-out. A recent claim of an indirect-detection signal from the Galactic halo, consistent with dark matter annihilation in the mass range 400--800 GeV, motivates a reexamination of minimal models that can account for such a signal while remaining consistent with existing constraints. In this paper, we analyze the simplest extensions of the Standard Model capable of explaining the signal. We show that electroweak doublet dark matter with Higgs-portal interactions provides a natural and economical explanation. The model predicts annihilation predominantly into longitudinal gauge bosons with characteristic branching fractions and allows for inelastic dark matter with a mass splitting of order 100 keV, intriguingly consistent with a recent direct-detection anomaly. Possible enhancements of the present-day annihilation rate relative to the thermal value are also discussed, including a simple extension with a light scalar field, whose mass can be chosen such that the enhancement is suppressed in dwarf galaxies.
