### [46] [Signals of Doomsday III: Cosmological signatures of the late time $U(1)_{EM}$ symmetry breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05023)
*Amartya Sengupta,Dejan Stojkovic*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates the astrophysical signatures of a late-time breaking of $U(1)_{\rm EM}$ via a first-order phase transition mediated by a massive scalar field, leading to the nucleation of true-vacuum bubbles. Particle production occurs through two channels: vacuum mismatch and thermal dissipation at terminal wall velocity, generating detectable high-energy photons and neutrinos as precursors to the bubble wall arrival.

本文研究了通过一个大质量标量场介导的相变导致$U(1)_{\rm EM}$在晚期破缺的天体物理信号。该相变为一级相变，产生真真空泡核化。粒子产生通过两个通道：真空失配和泡壁达到终端速度后的热耗散，生成可观测的高能光子与中微子，作为泡壁到达前的前兆信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While $SU(3)_c$ and $U(1)_{\rm EM}$ are currently unbroken gauge symmetries, there is no fundamental reason for their permanence. The possibility of late-time symmetry breaking—particularly of electromagnetism—remains unexplored in terms of observable consequences. This work aims to probe whether such a dramatic event could leave detectable astrophysical imprints, especially through precursor signals before the actual arrival of the phase transition front.

尽管$SU(3)_c$和$U(1)_{\rm EM}$是当前未破缺的规范对称性，但并无基本原理保证其永久性。电磁对称性在晚期破缺的可能性及其可观测效应尚未被充分探索。本研究旨在探讨这种剧烈事件是否可能留下可探测的天体物理印记，特别是相变前锋到达前的前兆信号。

Method: We construct a model with a new massive scalar field coupled to electromagnetism, where a first-order phase transition proceeds via bubble nucleation. Using the vacuum-mismatch method, we compute particle production (photons and massive photons) prior to the bubble wall reaching terminal velocity. We also model frictional effects that halt acceleration, leading to thermal production of scalars and massive photons at terminal velocity. Event generators are used to simulate decays into Standard Model particles, tracing final-state photons and neutrinos after hadronization and secondary decays.

我们构建了一个包含新大质量标量场并与电磁相互作用耦合的模型，其中一级相变通过泡核化进行。利用真空失配方法，在泡壁达到终端速度之前计算粒子（光子与大质量光子）的产生。我们还建模了摩擦效应导致泡壁加速度停止，进而在终端速度下热产生大量标量粒子与大质量光子。使用事件生成器模拟这些粒子衰变为标准模型粒子的过程，并追踪强子化及不稳定粒子衰变后的终态光子与中微子。

Result: Two distinct particle production mechanisms are identified: (1) non-thermal vacuum mismatch radiation during early wall propagation, and (2) thermal production of scalars and massive photons at terminal velocity, which persists after the mismatch channel shuts off. Simulations yield energy spectra of final-state photons and neutrinos, showing they dominate the signal. These particles can arrive significantly earlier than the bubble wall due to subluminal wall speeds, providing observable precursors. For conservative parameters, the thermal channel produces macroscopic bursts of high-energy photons and neutrinos.

识别出两种不同的粒子产生机制：(1) 泡壁早期传播期间的非热真空失配辐射；(2) 泡壁达到终端速度后标量粒子与大质量光子的热产生，该过程在失配通道关闭后仍持续。模拟给出了终态光子与中微子的能量谱，显示它们主导信号。由于泡壁亚光速传播，这些粒子可比泡壁早得多到达，形成可观测前兆。在保守参数下，热通道产生宏观尺度的高能光子与中微子爆发。

Conclusion: A late-time breaking of $U(1)_{\rm EM}$ could produce detectable multi-messenger signals in the form of high-energy photons and neutrinos, generated both by vacuum mismatch and thermal processes at terminal wall velocity. These signals may serve as observable precursors to the arrival of the phase transition front, offering a novel probe of dynamical gauge symmetry breaking in the late universe. Present and future multi-messenger observatories could potentially detect such signals from nearby cosmological bubbles.

$U(1)_{\rm EM}$的晚期破缺可能通过真空失配与终端速度下的热过程产生可观测的多信使信号——高能光子与中微子。这些信号可作为相变前锋到达的前兆，为晚期宇宙中动力学规范对称性破缺提供新的探针。当前及未来的多信使观测设施有可能探测到来自邻近宇宙泡的此类信号。

Abstract: Of the universe's original gauge symmetries, only $SU(3)_c$ (quantum chromodynamics) and $U(1)_{\rm EM}$ (electromagnetism) remain unbroken today. There is, however, no reason to assume that these symmetries are permanent. This paper explores the potential astrophysical observational signatures of a late-time breaking of $U(1)_{\rm EM}$. We present a model with a new massive scalar field whose potential supports a first-order phase transition through the nucleation of true-vacuum bubbles. If the propagation of the bubble walls slows down due to interactions with the surrounding matter and radiation, these signals can reach us before the bubble wall itself arrives. Using the vacuum-mismatch method, we calculate the spectrum of particles produced by such a bubble until the terminal velocity is reached. In addition, we show that frictional dissipation at terminal wall velocity generates a large population of thermally produced scalars and massive photons, which continues even after the mismatch channel shuts off. We then use event generators to simulate the decays of the new scalar and the massive photon into Standard Model particles and obtain, as the final result, the energy spectra of photons and neutrinos. Since the dominant final decay products after hadronization and the decay of unstable particles are photons and neutrinos, they act as long-range signatures of the transition. We also estimate the possible lead time of these photon and neutrino signals relative to the arrival of the bubble wall itself, showing that even a modest subluminal wall velocity can in principle provide an observable precursor. For the conservative set of parameters used here, the thermal channel produces a macroscopically large burst of high-energy photons and neutrinos, which could in principle be detectable from sufficiently nearby bubbles with present or future multi-messenger facilities.

### [47] [Learning to Unscramble Feynman Loop Integrals with SAILIR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05034)
*David Shih*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: SAILIR introduces a self-supervised machine learning approach using transformers to perform integration-by-parts (IBP) reduction of Feynman integrals, achieving bounded memory usage regardless of integral complexity by leveraging a scramble/unscramble training procedure and beam search.

SAILIR提出了一种基于自监督机器学习的Feynman积分分部积分（IBP）约化方法，使用transformer模型，通过“打乱/解乱”训练流程和束搜索实现内存占用与积分复杂度无关的约化过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional IBP reduction algorithms like Laporta's require solving large systems of linear equations, leading to exponential growth in memory consumption as integral complexity increases—this limits the feasibility of high-precision calculations in high-energy physics for complex topologies.

传统的Laporta类IBP约化算法需要求解大规模线性方程组，导致内存消耗随积分复杂度指数增长，限制了高能物理中复杂拓扑高精度计算的可行性。

Method: SAILIR employs a transformer-based classifier trained in a self-supervised manner: synthetic training data is generated by scrambling known reduction identities in reverse, and the model learns to unscramble them step-by-step. Reduction proceeds online using beam search and a parallelized, asynchronous, single-episode strategy, avoiding the need to store large equation systems.

SAILIR采用基于transformer的分类器，通过自监督方式训练：利用已知约化恒等式反向打乱生成合成数据，模型学习逐步还原；约化过程在线进行，结合束搜索和高度并行、异步、单幕策略，避免存储大型方程组。

Result: On two-loop triangle-box integrals, SAILIR maintains nearly constant per-worker memory usage across increasing complexity, while Kira's memory consumption grows rapidly. For the most complex cases, SAILIR uses only 40\% of Kira's memory with comparable reduction time, albeit slower in wall-clock when not fully optimized.

在双圈三角-盒子积分上，SAILIR的每工作单元内存使用几乎不随复杂度增加而增长，而Kira则迅速上升；在最复杂情况下，SAILIR仅用Kira 40\%的内存，约化时间相当（未完全优化时壁钟时间稍慢）。

Conclusion: SAILIR demonstrates that machine learning can overcome the memory bottleneck of traditional Laporta-style IBP reduction, enabling scalable, high-weight integral reductions with bounded memory—a paradigm shift toward tractable high-precision computations in high-energy physics.

SAILIR表明，机器学习可克服传统Laporta型IBP约化的内存瓶颈，实现内存有界的高权积分约化，标志着迈向可处理高精度高能物理计算的新范式。

Abstract: Integration-by-parts (IBP) reduction of Feynman integrals to master integrals is a key computational bottleneck in precision calculations in high-energy physics. Traditional approaches based on the Laporta algorithm require solving large systems of equations, leading to memory consumption that grows rapidly with integral complexity. We present SAILIR (Self-supervised AI for Loop Integral Reduction), a new machine learning approach in which a transformer-based classifier guides the reduction of integrals one step at a time in a fully online fashion. The classifier is trained in an entirely self-supervised manner on synthetic data generated by a scramble/unscramble procedure: known reduction identities are applied in reverse to build expressions of increasing complexity, and the classifier learns to undo these steps. When combined with beam search and a highly parallelized, asynchronous, single-episode reduction strategy, SAILIR can reduce integrals of arbitrarily high weight with bounded memory. We benchmark SAILIR on the two-loop triangle-box topology, comparing against the state-of-the-art IBP reduction code Kira across 16 integrals of varying complexity. While SAILIR is slower in wall-clock time, its per-worker memory consumption remains approximately flat regardless of integral complexity, in contrast to Kira whose memory grows rapidly with complexity. For the most complex integrals considered here, SAILIR uses only 40\% of the memory of Kira while achieving comparable reduction times. This demonstrates a fundamentally new paradigm for IBP reduction in which the memory bottleneck of Laporta-based approaches could be entirely overcome, potentially opening the door to precision calculations that are currently intractable.

### [48] [Aspects of a Five-Dimensional $U(1)_{L_μ- L_τ}$ Model at Future Muon-Based Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05041)
*Dibyendu Chakraborty,Arindam Chatterjee,AseshKrishna Datta,Ayushi Kaushik,Kenji Nishiwaki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates a 5D $U(1)_{L_\mu-L_\tau}$ gauge model with bulk gauge field $V$ generating Kaluza-Klein (KK) excitations $V^{(n)}$, which couple preferentially to muons and tau leptons. The study focuses on probing this scenario at future muon-based colliders—such as $\mu$TRISTAN and a muon collider—through processes like elastic $\mu^+\mu^+ \to \mu^+\mu^+$ scattering via off-shell KK exchange, bremsstrahlung production of $V^{(n)}$ followed by decays into neutrinos and $\mu^-\mu^+$, and resonant $\mu^-\mu^+ \to \mu^-\mu^+$ scattering. These facilities can access previously unreachable parameter space, probing TeV-scale KK bosons with large couplings and MeV-scale ones with very weak couplings ($g_D \sim 10^{-5}$), offering $2\sigma$ exclusion sensitivity across a wide mass range.

本文研究了一个五维$U(1)_{L_\mu-L_\tau}$规范模型，其体内的规范场$V$产生卡鲁扎-克莱因（KK）激发态$V^{(n)}$，优先耦合到缪子和陶轻子。研究重点是在未来的缪子对撞机（如$\mu$TRISTAN和缪子对撞机）上通过弹性$\mu^+\mu^+ \to \mu^+\mu^+$散射（通过虚KK交换）、$V^{(n)}$的轫致辐射产生及其衰变为中微子和$\mu^-\mu^+$，以及共振$\mu^-\mu^+ \to \mu^-\mu^+$散射等过程探测该模型。这些设施能够探测此前实验无法触及的参数空间，涵盖大耦合下TeV质量尺度的KK玻色子和弱至$g_D \sim 10^{-5}$耦合下MeV质量尺度的粒子，在广泛质量范围内提供$2\sigma$排除灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The $U(1)_{L_\mu-L_\tau}$ extension of the Standard Model is motivated by its ability to explain the long-standing muon $g-2$ anomaly while being anomaly-free and minimally coupled to SM fields. Embedding this symmetry in a 5D framework allows for Kaluza-Klein (KK) towers of gauge bosons $V^{(n)}$, enhancing phenomenological reach. Unlike models relying on kinetic mixing with hypercharge, this setup can be directly probed at high-energy muon colliders without such assumptions, making it ideal for testing the gauge structure independently. Future low-energy experiments are limited in sensitivity to light but weakly coupled states; thus, high-energy muon colliders offer a complementary and powerful probe.

标准模型的$U(1)_{L_\mu-L_\tau}$扩展因其能解释长期存在的缪子$g-2$反常现象，且无反常、与标准模型场最小耦合而受到关注。将此对称性嵌入五维框架可产生卡鲁扎-克莱因（KK）规范玻色子塔$V^{(n)}$，增强现象学覆盖范围。不同于依赖与超荷动能混合的模型，该设置可在高能缪子对撞机上直接探测，无需此类假设，适合独立检验规范结构。未来低能实验对轻但弱耦合态的灵敏度有限，因此高能缪子对撞机提供了有力且互补的探测手段。

Method: We analyze three key processes at future muon-based colliders: (1) Elastic $\mu^+\mu^+ \to \mu^+\mu^+$ scattering mediated by off-shell KK gauge bosons $V^{(n)}$, computed using effective field theory techniques in the 5D bulk; (2) Bremsstrahlung-like production of KK modes $V^{(n)}$ in $\mu^+\mu^-$ collisions at $\mu$TRISTAN, with subsequent decays into $\nu_\mu \bar{\nu}_\mu$ and $\mu^-\mu^+$, modeled via full 5D propagator sums; (3) Resonant production of $V^{(n)}$ in $\mu^-\mu^+$ annihilation at a high-energy muon collider, where center-of-mass energy matches the mass of individual KK modes. We compute cross sections, apply detector simulations and background estimates, and derive $2\sigma$ exclusion limits in the $(m_{V^{(n)}}, g_D)$ parameter space.

我们在未来的缪子对撞机上分析三个关键过程：（1）由离壳KK规范玻色子$V^{(n)}$介导的弹性$\mu^+\mu^+ \to \mu^+\mu^+$散射，使用五维体中的有效场论技术计算；（2）在$\mu$TRISTAN上$\mu^+\mu^-$碰撞中类似轫致辐射地产生KK模$V^{(n)}$，随后衰变为$\nu_\mu \bar{\nu}_\mu$和$\mu^-\mu^+$，通过完整的五维传播子求和建模；（3）在高能缪子对撞机上$\mu^-\mu^+$湮灭中共振产生$V^{(n)}$，当质心能量匹配单个KK模质量时发生。我们计算截面，应用探测器模拟和背景估计，并在$(m_{V^{(n)}}, g_D)$参数空间中推导出$2\sigma$排除极限。

Result: We find that future muon colliders can probe KK gauge bosons $V^{(n)}$ over a wide mass range—from MeV to TeV scales—with gauge couplings as small as $g_D \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-5})$. For $\mu$TRISTAN, the bremsstrahlung process offers sensitivity to light $V^{(n)}$ decaying to neutrinos or dimuons, even when couplings are too weak for detection in fixed-target or beam-dump experiments. At a multi-TeV muon collider, resonant production enables precise reconstruction of individual KK modes, allowing discrimination between the $U(1)_{L_\mu-L_\tau}$ signal and SM backgrounds. The combination of these channels provides complementary coverage, surpassing current and projected low-energy constraints by several orders of magnitude in certain regions.

我们发现未来的缪子对撞机能够在从MeV到TeV质量尺度的广泛范围内探测KK规范玻色子$V^{(n)}$，即使耦合小至$g_D \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-5})$。对于$\mu$TRISTAN，轫致辐射过程对衰变为中微子或双缪子的轻$V^{(n)}$具有灵敏度，即使在固定靶或束流倾倒实验中无法探测的弱耦合下亦然。在多TeV缪子对撞机上，共振产生允许精确重建单个KK模，从而区分$U(1)_{L_\mu-L_\tau}$信号与标准模型背景。这些通道的组合提供了互补覆盖，在某些区域超越当前及预期低能限制数个数量级。

Conclusion: Muon-based colliders offer a uniquely powerful and direct probe of 5D $U(1)_{L_\mu-L_\tau}$ models through multiple observable channels. They can test both heavy KK states inaccessible to low-energy experiments and extremely light, weakly coupled ones that evade traditional searches. This makes them essential for fully exploring the phenomenology of anomaly-free, gauged lepton flavor models. The absence of reliance on kinetic mixing enhances the theoretical cleanliness of the test, enabling unambiguous verification or exclusion of the model's gauge sector.

基于缪子的对撞机通过多个可观测通道为探测五维$U(1)_{L_\mu-L_\tau}$模型提供了独特而强大的手段。它们既能测试低能实验无法触及的重KK态，也能探测传统搜索难以发现的极轻且弱耦合态。这使其成为全面探索无反常规范轻子味模型现象学的关键工具。由于不依赖动能混合，该检验具有更高的理论清晰度，可明确验证或排除该模型的规范部分。

Abstract: We study a five-dimensional (5D) framework based on the \(U(1)_{L_μ-L_τ}\) gauge symmetry, where the associated gauge field \(V\) propagates in the bulk, giving rise to an infinite tower of Kaluza--Klein (KK) excitations \(V^{(n)}\) that couple selectively to the second- and third-generation leptons. Originally motivated by its potential to address the muon \(g-2\) anomaly, this framework remains of interest as a minimal, anomaly-free, phenomenologically well-motivated extension of the Standard Model (SM) of particle physics. We focus on high-energy muon-based colliders, which could directly probe the gauge structure without relying on the kinetic mixing between the SM hypercharge gauge boson and the 5D gauge boson \(V\). We explore a set of complementary processes: the elastic $μ^+μ^+ \to μ^+μ^+$ scattering via off-shell exchange of KK (gauge) excitations \(V^{(n)}\); the bremsstrahlung production of \(V^{(n)}\) followed by their decays into neutrinos and into $μ^-μ^+$ at a future $μ$TRISTAN collider. Further, we study the $μ^-μ^+ \to μ^-μ^+$ scattering via resonant KK excitation(s) at a future muon collider. Our results show that these future muon-based colliders could offer sensitive and complementary probes into regions in the parameter space of the scenario that are beyond the reach of low-energy experiments. In particular, such experiments would be able to probe both heavier such KK gauge bosons with TeV-scale masses for relatively large gauge couplings, as well as the much lighter ones with masses in the MeV-scale for couplings as weak as \(g_D \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-5})\), thereby offering a promising $2σ$ exclusion reach for such KK excitations, over an extensive range of masses, at these facilities.

</details>


### [49] [The chromomagnetic moment of a heavy quark with hyperasymptotic precision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05044)
*Cesar Ayala,Antonio Pineda*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We determine the normalization of the leading infrared renormalon in the chromomagnetic moment of a heavy quark and use it to compute hyperfine splittings in $B$ and $D$ mesons with hyperasymptotic precision. By fitting to experimental data within the operator product expansion (OPE), we extract the pole-subtracted chromomagnetic parameter $\hat \mu^2_{G,\rm PV} = 0.507(7)\, {\rm GeV}^2$ for the ground state.

我们确定了重夸克色磁矩中主导红外幺正化的归一化，并利用它以超渐近精度计算了$B$和$D$介子的超精细分裂。通过在算符乘积展开（OPE）框架内拟合实验数据，我们提取了减除后的色磁参数$\hat \mu^2_{G,\rm PV} = 0.507(7)\, {\rm GeV}^2$（基态）。



<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Infrared renormalons introduce ambiguities in perturbative QCD predictions, limiting the precision of theoretical calculations. Understanding and quantifying the leading infrared renormalon in the chromomagnetic operator allows for resummation beyond fixed-order perturbation theory and improves predictions for physical observables like hyperfine splittings in heavy mesons.

红外幺正化在微扰QCD预言中引入不确定性，限制了理论计算的精度。理解和量化色磁算符中的主导红外幺正化有助于超越固定阶微扰论的求和方法，并提升对重介子超精细分裂等物理观测量的预测精度。


Method: We compute the normalization of the leading infrared renormalon in the chromomagnetic moment using operator product expansion and resurgence theory. The hyperfine splitting is calculated with hyperasymptotic precision by including the leading terminant associated with the first infrared renormalon. A fit to experimental data is performed using the OPE prediction with $\hat \mu^2_{G,\rm PV}$ as the sole free parameter.

我们使用算符乘积展开（OPE）和突现理论（resurgence theory）计算色磁矩中主导红外幺正化的归一化。通过包含与第一红外幺正化相关的主导终项（terminant），以超渐近精度计算超精细分裂。利用OPE理论预言并以$\hat \mu^2_{G,\rm PV}$为唯一自由参数对实验数据进行拟合。


Result: The normalization of the leading infrared renormalon is determined, enabling estimation of higher-order perturbative coefficients. The hyperfine splitting of $B$ and $D$ mesons is computed with improved theoretical precision. Fitting to data yields $\hat \mu^2_{G,\rm PV} = 0.507(7)\, {\rm GeV}^2$ for the ground state, which is more precise than previous determinations.

确定了主导红外幺正化的归一化，从而可以估计高阶微扰系数。以更高的理论精度计算了$B$和$D$介子的超精细分裂。拟合数据得到基态下的$\hat \mu^2_{G,\rm PV} = 0.507(7)\, {\rm GeV}^2$，比以往的测定更为精确。


Conclusion: The inclusion of renormalon-based resummation via hyperasymptotic expansions significantly improves the precision of QCD predictions for heavy-quark systems. The extracted value of $\hat \mu^2_{G,\rm PV}$ provides a robust nonperturbative input for future calculations in heavy quark effective theory (HQET).

通过超渐近展开包含基于幺正化的重求和显著提升了对重夸克系统QCD预言的精度。提取出的$\hat \mu^2_{G,\rm PV}$值为未来重夸克有效理论（HQET）中的计算提供了可靠的非微扰输入。


Abstract: We determine the normalization of the leading infrared renormalon of the chromomagnetic moment of a heavy quark. Estimates of higher order coefficients of the perturbative series are given. We compute the hyperfine splitting of the $B$ and $D$ mesons for the ground state with hyperasymptotic precision by including the leading terminant, associated with the first infrared renormalon. We fit the experimental data to the operator product expansion theoretical prediction with $\hat μ^2_{G,\rm PV}$ as the free parameter. We obtain $\hat μ^2_{G,\rm PV}=0.507(7)$ GeV$^2$ for the ground state.

</details>


### [50] [Gravitational Waves from Matter Perturbations of Spectator Scalar Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05078)
*Marcos A. G. Garcia,Angel Garcia-Vega,Sarunas Verner*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We compute the stochastic gravitational wave (GW) background generated at second order by a spectator scalar field $\chi$ coupled to the inflaton via a portal interaction $\sigma\phi^2\chi^2$, including quartic self-interactions $\lambda_\chi \chi^4/4!$. In the large portal coupling regime ($\sigma/\lambda \gg 1$), parametric resonance during reheating strongly amplifies $\chi$ fluctuations, producing a detectable high-frequency GW signal sourced by $\partial_a\chi\,\partial_b\chi$. We derive a master formula factorizing the GW spectrum into spectral and temporal components, validate it against lattice simulations, and find a peak amplitude $\Omega_{\rm GW}h^2 \sim 10^{-11}$ at $f \sim 10^7$–$10^8\,{\rm Hz}$ for benchmark parameters.

我们计算了由通过门户相互作用 $\sigma\phi^2\chi^2$ 与暴胀子耦合的旁观者标量场 $\chi$ 在二阶产生的随机引力波背景，包含四次自相互作用 $\lambda_\chi \chi^4/4!$。在大门户耦合区域（$\sigma/\lambda \gg 1$），再加热期间的参数共振强烈放大 $\chi$ 涨落，由 $\partial_a\chi\,\partial_b\chi$ 产生可探测的高频引力波信号。我们推导出将引力波谱分解为谱和时间分量的主公式，并通过格点模拟验证该框架，在基准参数下得到峰值幅度 $\Omega_{\rm GW}h^2 \sim 10^{-11}$，频率范围 $f \sim 10^7$–$10^8\,{\rm Hz}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Detecting stochastic gravitational wave backgrounds from early universe physics offers a unique probe of high-energy processes beyond CMB and collider reach. Spectator fields during inflation can evade isocurvature constraints if sufficiently massive, but may still leave imprints via nonlinear couplings during reheating. We aim to quantify the GW signal from a minimally coupled spectator with a renormalizable portal interaction, where strong parametric resonance — regulated by quartic self-interactions — generates large-scale fluctuations without violating observational bounds.

探测来自早期宇宙物理的随机引力波背景为超出CMB和对撞机能量范围的高能过程提供了独特探针。暴胀期间的旁观者场若足够重可避免同曲率约束，但仍可能通过对再加热期间的非线性耦合留下印记。我们的目标是量化具有可重整化门户相互作用的最小耦合旁观者产生的引力波信号，其中强参数共振（由四次自相互作用调节）在不违反观测限制的情况下生成大尺度涨落。

Method: We solve the second-order Einstein equations with source term $T_{ab}^{(2)} \supset \partial_a\chi\,\partial_b\chi$, computing the GW energy density $\Omega_{\rm GW}$ as a convolution of the spectator's power spectrum. Using the Hartree approximation to handle backreaction from $\lambda_\chi$, we evolve the spectator field through reheating, subtracting vacuum contributions to isolate physical modes. A master formula is derived that separates the GW spectrum into a spectral integral over the frozen spectator spectrum and a time integral over the post-inflationary expansion history. This framework is validated against full nonlinear lattice simulations using classical statistical methods.

我们求解包含源项 $T_{ab}^{(2)} \supset \partial_a\chi\,\partial_b\chi$ 的二阶爱因斯坦方程，将引力波能量密度 $\Omega_{\rm GW}$ 计算为旁观者功率谱的卷积。使用Hartree近似处理来自 $\lambda_\chi$ 的反作用，我们在再加热过程中演化旁观者场，并减去真空贡献以分离物理模式。推导出一个主公式，将引力波谱分解为对冻结旁观者谱的谱积分和对后暴胀膨胀历史的时间积分。该框架通过使用经典统计方法的完整非线性格点模拟进行验证。

Result: In the large portal regime ($\sigma/\lambda \gg 1$), parametric resonance amplifies the spectator spectrum by many orders of magnitude within the resonance band, limited by Hartree-level backreaction from $\lambda_\chi$. The resulting GW spectrum peaks at high frequencies $f \sim 10^7$–$10^8\,{\rm Hz}$ with amplitude $\Omega_{\rm GW}h^2 \sim 10^{-11}$ for $\sigma/\lambda \simeq 10^4$ and $T_{\rm reh} = 2 \times 10^{14}\,{\rm GeV}$. Scaling relations show $\Omega_{\rm GW} \propto T_{\rm reh}^{8/3}$, strong dependence on $\sigma$, and weak sensitivity to $m_\chi$. Increasing $\lambda_\chi$ has a non-monotonic effect: small values enhance GW production via rescattering, while large values suppress it by detuning the resonance.

在大门户区域（$\sigma/\lambda \gg 1$），参数共振在共振带内将旁观者谱放大多个数量级，受 $\lambda_\chi$ 的Hartree级反作用限制。对于 $\sigma/\lambda \simeq 10^4$ 和 $T_{\rm reh} = 2 \times 10^{14}\,{\rm GeV}$，产生的引力波谱在高频 $f \sim 10^7$–$10^8\,{\rm Hz}$ 处达到峰值，幅度为 $\Omega_{\rm GW}h^2 \sim 10^{-11}$。标度关系显示 $\Omega_{\rm GW} \propto T_{\rm reh}^{8/3}$，对 $\sigma$ 强依赖，对 $m_\chi$ 弱敏感。增加 $\lambda_\chi$ 具有非单调效应：小值通过再散射增强引力波产生，而大值则通过失谐共振抑制它。

Conclusion: A spectator field with a renormalizable portal coupling can generate a potentially observable high-frequency stochastic gravitational wave background during reheating, provided the coupling ratio $\sigma/\lambda$ is large enough to trigger strong parametric resonance. The signal is regulated by quartic self-interactions through Hartree backreaction, which naturally limits growth and avoids overproduction. Our master formula provides an efficient analytic tool for computing second-order GWs, complementary to numerical lattice simulations. Future detectors sensitive to MHz–GHz frequencies could test such scenarios, probing otherwise inaccessible reheating dynamics.

具有可重整化门户耦合的旁观者场在再加热期间可以产生潜在可观测的高频随机引力波背景，前提是耦合比 $\sigma/\lambda$ 足够大以触发强参数共振。该信号通过Hartree反作用下的四次自相互作用自然调节，限制涨落增长并避免过度产生。我们的主公式为计算二阶引力波提供了一种高效的解析工具，与数值格点模拟互补。未来对MHz–GHz频率敏感的探测器可检验此类情景，探索其他方式无法触及的再加热动力学。

Abstract: We compute the stochastic gravitational wave background sourced at second order by a spectator scalar field $χ$ coupled to the inflaton $φ$ through a portal interaction $σφ^2χ^2$ and with quartic self-interaction $λ_χχ^4/4!$. In the large portal coupling regime ($σ/λ\gg 1$, with $λ$ the inflaton normalization), parametric resonance during reheating amplifies the spectator power spectrum by many orders of magnitude near the resonance band until Hartree backreaction from the quartic coupling detunes the instability, while the large inflationary effective mass suppresses superhorizon power and ensures compatibility with CMB isocurvature bounds. We focus on the direct field-gradient source $\partial_aχ\,\partial_bχ$ in the second-order Einstein equations and derive a master formula that factorizes into a spectral integral over the frozen, vacuum-subtracted spectator spectrum and a time integral encoding the post-inflationary expansion history. For our benchmark reheating history we obtain analytic scaling relations, including a peak amplitude $Ω_{\rm GW}\propto T_{\rm reh}^{8/3}$, strong dependence on the portal strength, and weak sensitivity to $m_χ$. We validate the framework against nonlinear lattice simulations, demonstrating complementarity: the Hartree treatment captures superhorizon evolution inaccessible to the lattice, while the lattice resolves rescattering and fragmentation near the spectral peak. For $σ/λ\simeq 10^4$ and $T_{\rm reh}=2 \times 10^{14}\,\mathrm{GeV}$, the signal reaches $Ω_{\rm GW}h^2\sim 10^{-11}$ at $f\sim10^{7}$-$10^{8}\,\mathrm{Hz}$. Increasing $λ_χ$ at fixed $σ$ has a non-monotonic effect: small values enhance the signal via rescattering, whereas larger values suppress it by detuning the resonance.

### [51] [Probing Gluon TMD Models with Drell--Yan Structure Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05154)
*Jan Ferdyan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We compute Drell-Yan structure functions in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{S} = 8 \mathrm{TeV}$ using high-energy factorization and two partonic channels, comparing predictions from four gluon TMD models (Gaussian, WW, KMR, JH) and their phenomenologically improved variants against ATLAS 2016 data. The modified Weizsäcker--Williams model provides the best fit, as quantified by $\chi^2$/dof, offering guidance for future gluon TMD parametrizations.

我们使用高能因式分解法计算了在$\sqrt{S} = 8 \mathrm{TeV}$质子-质子碰撞中Drell-Yan过程的结构函数，采用两个部分子通道，并比较了四种胶子TMD模型（高斯型、WW、KMR、JH）及其现象学改进版本对ATLAS 2016数据的预测。经$\chi^2$/dof评估，改进的Weizsäcker--Williams模型拟合最优，为未来胶子TMD参数化提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The precise description of Drell--Yan structure functions is essential for understanding transverse momentum distributions in hard processes and for constraining Transverse Momentum Dependent (TMD) parton distribution functions, especially the gluon TMDs which are less constrained than quark TMDs. This work aims to assess the predictive power of different gluon TMD models in the context of high-energy factorization and identify key features needed for improved TMD parametrizations.

精确描述Drell--Yan结构函数对于理解硬散射过程中的横向动量分布以及约束横向动量依赖（TMD）部分子分布函数至关重要，尤其是胶子TMD比夸克TMD更缺乏约束。本研究旨在评估不同胶子TMD模型在高能因式分解框架下的预测能力，并识别改进TMD参数化所需的关键特征。

Method: We employ the high-energy factorization formalism with off-shell partonic matrix elements at tree level, considering two subprocesses: $q_\mathrm{val} g^* \to q V^*$ and $g^* g^* \to q \overline{q} V^*$. Four standard gluon TMD models -- Gaussian, Weizs\"acker--Williams (WW), Kimber--Martin--Ryskin (KMR), and Jung--Hautmann (JH) -- are used, along with phenomenological modifications (e.g., adjustable parameters or form factors). Structure functions are computed differentially in dilepton rapidity and transverse momentum, and compared to ATLAS 2016 data. A $\chi^2$ per degree of freedom analysis is performed to quantify agreement.

我们采用高能因式分解形式，基于树图水平的离壳部分子矩阵元，考虑两个子过程：$q_\mathrm{val} g^* \to q V^*$ 和 $g^* g^* \to q \overline{q} V^*$。使用了四种标准胶子TMD模型——高斯型、Weizs\"acker--Williams (WW)、Kimber--Martin--Ryskin (KMR) 和 Jung--Hautmann (JH)，并结合现象学修正（如可调参数或形状因子）。结构函数在双轻子快度和横向动量上微分计算，并与ATLAS 2016数据对比，通过每自由度$\chi^2$分析量化一致性。

Result: Significant differences are observed among predictions from different TMD models, both for individual structure functions and the full dataset. The best agreement with ATLAS data is achieved by a phenomenologically modified Weizs\"acker--Williams (WW) model, yielding the lowest $\chi^2/\mathrm{dof}$. Other models, including standard WW and KMR, show larger deviations. The comparison reveals sensitivity of structure functions to the infrared behavior and $k_T$-dependence of the gluon TMD.

不同TMD模型的预测结果在单个结构函数和完整数据集上均表现出显著差异。经过现象学修正的Weizs\"acker--Williams (WW)模型与ATLAS数据的一致性最佳，其$\chi^2/\mathrm{dof}$最低。其他模型（包括标准WW和KMR）则偏差较大。该比较揭示了结构函数对胶子TMD红外行为和$k_T$依赖性的敏感性。

Conclusion: The structure functions in Drell--Yan production are sensitive probes of gluon TMD modeling. Our $\chi^2$ analysis demonstrates that a modified Weizs\"acker--Williams gluon TMD provides the most accurate description of ATLAS data, suggesting that proper treatment of low-$k_T$ dynamics and evolution effects is crucial. This work provides guidance for future global fits of gluon TMDs within high-energy factorization and TMD factorization frameworks.

Drell--Yan产生中的结构函数是探测胶子TMD建模的敏感工具。我们的$\chi^2$分析表明，修正的Weizs\"acker--Williams胶子TMD对ATLAS数据的描述最为准确，表明低-$k_T$动力学和演化效应的恰当处理至关重要。本研究为在高能因式分解和TMD因式分解框架下进行胶子TMD全局拟合提供了指导。

Abstract: We compute structure functions for the Drell--Yan process in proton-proton collisions at the center of mass energy $\sqrt{S} = 8 \mathrm{TeV}$ both parity conserving and parity breaking. For this calculation, we use the high-energy factorization formalism. The hard scattering matrix elements used in our derivation consist of two channels -- $q_\mathrm{val} g^* \to q V^*$ and $g^* g^* \to q \overline{q} V^*$, both at the tree level. We consider four types of gluon TMD models: Gaussian, Weizsäcker--Williams (WW), Kimber--Martin--Ryskin (KMR), and Jung--Hautmann (JH). We also consider the models with phenomenological adjustments to improve the data description. We derive and compare the structure functions calculated for different gluon TMD models with the ATLAS 2016 data. Based on this comparison, we calculate $χ^2$ per number of degrees of freedom for each of the predictions. This assessment shows clear differences between the predictions obtained with different TMD models, both in the description of the full data set and in the case of individual structure functions. The best description of the structure functions data is obtained with one of the modified WW models. Our analysis can serve to identify the features of the TMD model that should be considered in future gluon TMD fits.

### [52] [$b \to c$ semileptonic sum rule: SU(3)$_{\rm{F}}$ symmetry violation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05186)
*Syuhei Iguro*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: An extended semileptonic sum rule for $b\to c$ transitions, incorporating $B_s\to D_s^{(*)} l\overlineν$ and $Ξ_b\to Ξ_c l\overlineν$, is developed based on heavy quark and SU(3) flavor symmetries. The size of symmetry violations is numerically evaluated and found to be smaller than projected experimental uncertainties, supporting the robustness of the sum rule. Additional new physics-agnostic sum rules are proposed for consistency checks.

扩展了基于重夸克对称性和SU(3)味对称性的$b\to c$半轻子衰变求和规则，纳入了$B_s\to D_s^{(*)} l\overlineν$和$Ξ_b\to Ξ_c l\overlineν$过程。数值评估表明对称性破缺效应小于预期实验误差，验证了该求和规则的可靠性，并提出了新的无新物理假设的预测性求和规则用于一致性检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Deviations in $b\to cτ\overlineν$ processes have sparked interest in potential new physics. The existing sum rule for $\{B\to D^{(*)} l\overlineν,\,Λ_b\to Λ_c l\overlineν\}$ provides a model-independent test based on heavy quark symmetry (HQS), but its applicability is limited. Extending it to include strange hadronic channels like $B_s\to D_s^{(*)} l\overlineν$ and $Ξ_b\to Ξ_c l\overlineν$ allows for more comprehensive cross-checks. However, both HQS and SU(3) flavor symmetry are broken in nature, so quantifying these corrections is essential to validate the extended sum rule.

在$b\to cτ\overlineν$过程中观测到的偏差引发了对新物理的关注。现有的$\{B\to D^{(*)} l\overlineν,\,Λ_b\to Λ_c l\overlineν\}$求和规则基于重夸克对称性（HQS）提供了模型无关的检验，但其适用范围有限。将其扩展至包含奇异强子道如$B_s\to D_s^{(*)} l\overlineν$和$Ξ_b\to Ξ_c l\overlineν$可实现更全面的交叉检验。然而，HQS和SU(3)味对称性在现实中均被破缺，因此量化这些修正对于验证扩展后的求和规则至关重要。

Method: The sum rule is derived using heavy quark symmetry and SU(3) flavor symmetry, relating inclusive semileptonic decay rates across different beauty baryons and mesons. Symmetry-breaking effects are evaluated numerically using chiral perturbation theory, which accounts for finite quark mass corrections and SU(3) breaking. Theoretical predictions are compared with projected experimental sensitivities from future facilities such as Belle II and LHCb.

利用重夸克对称性和SU(3)味对称性推导求和规则，关联不同底强子（介子与重子）的半轻子衰变宽度。通过对包含有限夸克质量修正和SU(3)破缺的动量有效理论（chiral perturbation theory）进行数值计算，评估对称性破缺效应。理论预测结果与Belle II和LHCb等未来实验的预期灵敏度进行比较。

Result: The numerical evaluation shows that SU(3) and HQS violating corrections to the extended sum rule are smaller than the expected experimental uncertainties at current and near-future experiments. This supports the validity of the sum rule as a reliable consistency test. Furthermore, additional sum rules independent of new physics assumptions are constructed, enhancing the toolkit for probing anomalies in $b\to c$ transitions.

数值计算表明，扩展求和规则中的SU(3)和HQS破缺修正小于当前及近期未来实验的预期不确定度，支持该求和规则作为可靠一致性检验的有效性。此外，构建了不依赖于新物理假设的额外求和规则，增强了探测$b\to c$跃迁反常现象的工具集。

Conclusion: The extended semileptonic sum rule including strange hadronic channels remains robust against symmetry-breaking effects, making it a viable and model-independent probe for testing the consistency of $b\to cτ\overlineν$ data. The construction of new physics-agnostic sum rules further strengthens the theoretical framework for interpreting current and future measurements in heavy-flavor physics.

包含奇异强子道的扩展半轻子求和规则对对称性破缺效应具有鲁棒性，可作为检验$b\to cτ\overlineν$数据一致性的可行且模型无关的探针。构建无新物理假设的求和规则进一步强化了重味物理中当前与未来测量结果解释的理论框架。

Abstract: To clarify possible deviations in $b\to cτ\overlineν$ processes, the $b\to c$ semileptonic sum rule provides a valuable tool. This relation, derived based on heavy quark symmetry (HQS), offers a powerful consistency check among experimental results. In this work, we extend the previously proposed sum rule for $\{B\to D^{(*)} l\overlineν,\,Λ_b\to Λ_c l\overlineν\}$ to include $\{B_s\to D_s^{(*)} l\overlineν,\,Ξ_b\to Ξ_c l\overlineν\}$, thereby enabling more useful cross-checks. Although the relation is supported by HQS and SU(3) flavor symmetry, both symmetries are broken in reality, and the size of the violation needs to be quantified to assess the validity of the sum rule. While the violation is expected to be moderate based on chiral perturbation theory, we perform a numerical evaluation and compare it with future experimental sensitivities. We find that the violation remains smaller than the expected experimental uncertainty. Therefore another new physics agnostic and predictive sum rules are constructed to check the consistency.

Abstract: Huang and Li [arXiv:2603.00885] have raised the following two points regarding our previous work [arXiv:2502.18029]:(1) The real-value conditions associated with $μ$-$τ$ reflection symmetry were overlooked. In contrast, they argue that IO remains viable when considering the effective neutrino mass, $|M_{ee}|$. While IO may indeed remain allowed in light of the latest $|M_{ee}|$ data, it is still in tension with the experimental bounds on $\sum m_ν$ under approximate $μ-τ$ symmetry within the discussed model parameter space.

### [54] [Gamma-Ray Signatures of Thermal Misalignment Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05326)
*Koichi Hamaguchi,Ryoichiro Hayakawa,Hiroki Takahashi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Thermal misalignment provides a dark matter production mechanism where a scalar field acquires misalignment via thermal effects; we study the case with photon coupling $\phi F^{\mu\nu}F_{\mu\nu}$ and derive gamma-ray constraints on the scalar mass.

热误配准是一种通过热效应产生暗物质的可行机制；我们研究了标量场与光子耦合的情形，并推导了伽马射线对质量的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The thermal misalignment mechanism offers an alternative to traditional dark matter production scenarios like freeze-out or vacuum misalignment. It allows for feebly interacting scalars to be produced in the early universe through interactions with the thermal bath, motivating the study of its observational consequences, especially when the scalar couples to photons.

热误配准机制为冻结或真空误配等传统暗物质产生机制提供了替代方案。它允许弱相互作用标量通过与热浴的相互作用在早期宇宙中产生，激励我们研究其可观测效应，特别是当标量与光子耦合时。

Method: We consider a scalar dark matter candidate $\phi$ coupled to photons via the operator $\phi F^{\mu\nu}F_{\mu\nu}$, which induces decays into two photons. We compute the thermal abundance of $\phi$ generated through thermal misalignment and analyze current gamma-ray data (e.g., from Fermi-LAT, H.E.S.S.) to constrain the decay rate and thus the scalar mass and coupling.

我们考虑一个通过算符 $\phi F^{\mu\nu}F_{\mu\nu}$ 与光子耦合的标量暗物质候选者 $\phi$，该耦合诱导其衰变为两个光子。我们计算了通过热误配准产生的 $\phi$ 的热丰度，并分析当前伽马射线数据（如来自Fermi-LAT、H.E.S.S.）以约束其衰变率，从而限制标量质量和耦合强度。

Result: Current gamma-ray observations impose a robust upper bound on the scalar mass of $\mathcal{O}(1)\,\mathrm{GeV}$. The most sensitive region is in the MeV--GeV range, where future gamma-ray telescopes (e.g., e-ASTROGAM, AMEGO) will significantly improve sensitivity and probe previously unconstrained parameter space.

当前伽马射线观测对标量质量施加了严格的上限，约为 $\mathcal{O}(1)\,\mathrm{GeV}$。最敏感的区域位于MeV至GeV范围，未来的伽马射线望远镜（如e-ASTROGAM、AMEGO）将显著提高灵敏度并探测此前未受约束的参数空间。

Conclusion: Thermal misalignment with photon-coupled scalars is testable via gamma-ray searches. The metastability of the scalar leads to observable decays, and upcoming observatories will critically test this scenario in the MeV--GeV window.

通过伽马射线搜寻可检验与光子耦合的热误配准标量模型。标量的亚稳态导致可观测衰变，即将到来的观测设备将在MeV至GeV窗口内对此情景进行关键性检验。

Abstract: Thermal misalignment is a viable dark matter scenario where the misalignment of a dark matter scalar, feebly coupled to the Standard Model particles, is generated through thermal effects from the primordial plasma. In this framework, the scalar is generically metastable, and its decay can leave observable signatures. In this work, we focus on the case in which the scalar $φ$ is coupled to photons through $φF^{μν} F_{μν}$, and examine its observational signatures. We find that current gamma-ray constraints place a robust upper bound on the scalar mass of $\mathcal O(1)\,\mathrm{GeV}$. We also find that future observations can further probe the parameter region, particularly in the MeV--GeV range, an energy band expected to be explored by various gamma-ray observatories in the coming decades.

</details>


### [55] [Rare B meson decays in the Minimal R-symmetric Supersymmetric Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05357)
*Ke-Sheng Sun,Kui-Wen Guan,Hao-Yi Liu,Jin-Lei Yang,Tie-Jun Gao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies lepton flavor violating (LFV) decays of $B^0_d$ mesons in the minimal R-symmetric supersymmetric standard model (MRSSM), focusing on the decay $B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$. The branching ratio predictions are significantly influenced by $\tan\beta$ and off-diagonal elements in slepton and squark mass matrices. While the predicted rate for $B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$ is currently four orders of magnitude below future experimental sensitivity, it remains one of the more promising channels for potential observation.

本文在最小R对称超对称标准模型（MRSSM）框架下研究了B介子的轻子味破坏（LFV）衰变，重点关注$B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$过程。分支比的预测强烈依赖于$\tan\beta$以及slepton和squark质量矩阵中的非对角项。尽管当前预测的$B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$衰变率比未来实验灵敏度低四个数量级，但它仍是未来最有可能被观测到的衰变道之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lepton flavor violation in $B$ meson decays is a clear signature of physics beyond the Standard Model, as such processes are highly suppressed in the Standard Model. The MRSSM offers a theoretically motivated extension with R-symmetry that stabilizes the electroweak scale and modifies supersymmetric particle interactions. This work aims to explore how LFV $B$ decays, particularly $B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$, are affected in this specific SUSY framework, taking into account up-to-date experimental constraints.

B介子衰变中的轻子味破坏是超出标准模型新物理的明确信号，因为此类过程在标准模型中被高度压低。MRSSM是一种具有R对称性的理论上有吸引力的扩展，可稳定电弱尺度并改变超对称粒子的相互作用。本工作的目的是在这一特定SUSY框架下，结合最新的实验限制，研究LFV B衰变（特别是$B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$）的行为。

Method: The authors calculate the branching ratios for $B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$ within the MRSSM framework. They incorporate constraints from existing experimental data on lepton radiative decays (e.g., $\mu \rightarrow e\gamma$) to limit the off-diagonal entries in the slepton mass matrix, and use low-energy $B$-physics observables (e.g., $B$ mixing, rare $B$ decays) to constrain the squark mass matrix off-diagonal elements. The dependence of the predicted rates on $\tan\beta$ and these flavor-violating parameters is systematically analyzed.

作者在MRSSM框架内计算了$B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$的分支比。他们利用轻子辐射衰变（如$\mu \rightarrow e\gamma$）的实验数据限制slepton质量矩阵的非对角元，并利用低能B物理观测量（如B介子混合、稀有B衰变）约束squark质量矩阵的非对角元。系统分析了预测衰变率对$\tan\beta$及这些味破坏参数的依赖性。

Result: The branching ratio for $B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$ is found to be suppressed, lying approximately four orders of magnitude below the projected sensitivity of future experiments. However, among the possible LFV $B$ decays, $B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$ exhibits relatively enhanced rates due to favorable helicity and $\tan\beta$ enhancement factors, making it one of the most promising channels for future detection in the MRSSM context.

$B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$的分支比被发现受到显著压低，大约比未来实验预期灵敏度低四个数量级。然而，在所有可能的LFV B衰变中，由于有利的手征性和$\tan\beta$增强因子，$B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$表现出相对较高的衰变率，使其成为MRSSM框架下未来探测最有希望的通道之一。

Conclusion: While the MRSSM predicts $B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$ to be unobservably small with current and near-future sensitivities, the analysis highlights the importance of $\tan\beta$ and flavor structure in supersymmetric models. The relative enhancement of $B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$ compared to other LFV modes suggests it should remain a key target for next-generation B physics experiments searching for supersymmetry.

尽管MRSSM预测的$B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$在当前和近期未来的实验灵敏度下无法观测，但该分析凸显了$\tan\beta$和超对称模型中味结构的重要性。相比其他LFV模式，$B^0_d \rightarrow \mu\tau$的相对增强表明，它应继续作为下一代B物理实验搜寻超对称性的关键目标。

Abstract: Taking into account the constraints imposed by experimental data on the parameter space, we analyze the lepton flavor violating decays of B meson in the scenario of the minimal R-symmetric supersymmetric standard model. The prediction of the branching ratios is strongly affected by $\tanβ$ and the off-diagonal entries in the slepton and squark mass matrices. The off-diagonal entries in the slepton mass matrix are constrained by the experimental limits of radiative two body decays of leptons. The off-diagonal entries in the squark mass matrix are constrained by the experimental limits of low energy observables related to B meson physics. The branching ratio of $B^0_d\rightarrow μτ$ is predicted to be four orders of magnitude below the future experimental sensitivity and the decay $B^0_d\rightarrow μτ$ has a higher chance of being observed in the future.

### [56] [Towards Testable Type-III Leptogenesis in Non-Standard Early Universe Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05362)
*Simran Arora,Devabrat Mahanta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores triplet fermion leptogenesis in non-standard cosmological scenarios, showing that a faster-expanding early Universe or scalar-tensor gravity can allow successful leptogenesis with TeV to hundred-TeV scale triplet fermions, significantly lowering the required mass scale compared to standard radiation-dominated cosmology.

本文研究了在非标准宇宙学背景下三重态费米子轻子生成机制，发现早期宇宙快速膨胀或标量-张量引力理论下，可在TeV至数百TeV能标实现成功轻子生成，显著降低标准辐射主导宇宙所需的质量尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Leptogenesis is a compelling mechanism to explain the baryon asymmetry of the Universe through lepton number violation linked to neutrino masses. While minimal models use heavy Majorana neutrinos, triplet fermion decay offers testable signatures but typically requires masses around $10^{10}$ GeV due to strong gauge annihilations and neutrino constraints in standard cosmology. This work aims to relax these stringent mass requirements by considering non-standard cosmological histories prior to big bang nucleosynthesis.

轻子生成机制通过与中微子质量相关的轻子数破坏来解释宇宙重子不对称性，具有吸引力。尽管最小模型使用重马约拉纳中微子，三重态费米子衰变提供了可检验的信号，但在标准宇宙学下由于强规范湮灭和中微子约束通常需要约$10^{10}$ GeV的质量。本研究旨在通过考虑大爆炸核合成前的非标准宇宙历史来放宽这些严格的质量限制。

Method: The authors analyze triplet fermion leptogenesis in two alternative cosmological scenarios: (1) a fast-expanding Universe where the Hubble rate $H$ is enhanced relative to the standard radiation-dominated case, and (2) a scalar-tensor theory of gravity modifying the expansion history. They solve the Boltzmann equations governing the evolution of triplet fermion abundance and lepton asymmetry, incorporating gauge interactions, decays, and inverse processes, while adjusting $H(T)$ to reflect the modified cosmologies.

作者分析了两种替代宇宙学场景下的三重态费米子轻子生成机制：（1）快速膨胀宇宙，其哈勃率$H$相对于标准辐射主导情况增强；（2）修改膨胀历史的标量-张量引力理论。他们求解控制三重态费米子丰度和轻子不对称之演化的Boltzmann方程，包含规范相互作用、衰变和逆过程，并调整$H(T)$以反映修正后的宇宙学。

Result: In the fast-expanding Universe scenario, successful leptogenesis can be achieved with triplet fermion masses as low as a few TeV due to earlier freeze-out and suppressed washout processes. In the scalar-tensor gravity model, the allowed mass is relaxed to a few hundred TeV. These reductions are attributed to an increased Hubble rate $H(T)$, which modifies thermal production and out-of-equilibrium dynamics crucial for generating the observed baryon asymmetry.

在快速膨胀宇宙情景中，由于更早的冻结和被抑制的冲刷过程，三重态费米子质量低至几TeV即可实现成功的轻子生成。在标量-张量引力模型中，允许的质量放宽至几百TeV。这些降低归因于增强的哈勃率$H(T)$，其修改了热产生和非平衡动力学，这对生成观测到的重子不对称性至关重要。

Conclusion: Non-standard cosmological histories, such as a faster-than-standard expansion or scalar-tensor gravity, can significantly lower the mass scale of triplet fermions required for successful leptogenesis. This opens up prospects for experimental detection at collider and precision experiments, bridging high-scale phenomenology with observable physics.

非标准宇宙学历史（如比标准更快的膨胀或标量-张量引力）可显著降低成功轻子生成所需三重态费米子的质量尺度。这为对撞机和精密实验中的实验探测开辟了前景，架起了高能现象学与可观测物理之间的桥梁。

Abstract: Leptogenesis is an elegant way to explain the baryon asymmetry of the Universe in connection to the neutrino mass and mixing. Although leptogenesis from the decay of a heavy Majorana neutrino has been the minimal set up, it is also motivating to look for leptogenesis from the decay of triplet fermion as it can have detectable signatures in the experiments. However, due to strong gauge annihilations and constraints from neutrino sector, the triplet fermions have to be as heavy as $10^{10}$ GeV or more to generate the observed baryon asymmetry. While this prediction is based on the standard radiation dominated history of the early Universe, it is also possible to have a non-standard expansion history of the Universe prior to the big-bang nucleosynthesis. In this work we study triplet leptogenesis in two non-standard cosmological scenarios, where the Universe expands faster than radiation and a scalar tensor theory of gravity. We show that it is possible to have successful leptogenesis with a few TeV triplet fermion for fast expanding Universe and a few hundered TeV for a scalar tensor gravity theory.

### [57] [Gauge coupling unification and doublet-triplet splitting via GUT dynamical breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05509)
*Isabella Masina,Mariano Quiros*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores gauge coupling unification in $SU(5)$ Grand Unified Theories by introducing higher-dimensional operators ($d \geq 5$) affecting gauge field kinetics. It examines fermionic condensates in various representations, finding that $5$-representation condensates are ruled out by proton decay, while $10$ and $24$ representations allow viable models, linking unification to the doublet-triplet splitting problem in dynamical symmetry breaking.

本文通过引入影响规范场动力学的高维算符（$d \geq 5$）研究了$SU(5)$大统一理论中的规范耦合统一问题。文章分析了不同表示下的费米子凝聚，发现$5$表示因质子衰变限制被排除，而$10$和$24$表示可构造成功模型，并在动力学对称性破缺框架下将耦合统一与二重态-三重态分裂问题联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gauge coupling unification is a key motivation for Grand Unified Theories (GUTs). In minimal $SU(5)$, unification fails under Standard Model renormalization group evolution. The authors aim to achieve unification via non-renormalizable operators modifying gauge kinetic terms, and explore whether such frameworks can simultaneously address the doublet-triplet splitting problem in dynamical GUT models.

规范耦合统一是大统一理论（GUTs）的核心动机之一。在最小$SU(5)$模型中，标准模型的重整化群演化无法实现统一。作者旨在通过修改规范场动能项的不可重整算符实现统一，并探索此类框架是否能在动力学GUT模型中同时解决二重态-三重态分裂问题。

Method: The method involves analyzing effective field theory (EFT) extensions of the Standard Model with higher-dimensional operators of dimension $d \geq 5$ that correct the gauge field strength terms. The renormalization group equations (RGEs) are modified by these operators. The authors examine fermion condensates in different $SU(5)$ representations ($5$, $10$, $24$) under a dynamical symmetry breaking scenario, computing their impact on gauge coupling running and constraints from proton decay.

该方法基于在标准模型上引入维度$d \geq 5$的高维算符，修正规范场强项，构建有效场论（EFT）。这些算符修改了重整化群方程（RGEs）。作者在动力学对称性破缺框架下分析$SU(5)$不同表示（$5$、$10$、$24$）中的费米子凝聚，计算其对规范耦合跑动的影响以及质子衰变的限制。

Result: Operators from $5$-representation condensates lead to rapid proton decay and are excluded. In contrast, condensates in the $10$ and $24$ representations generate suitable threshold corrections to gauge couplings, enabling successful unification while avoiding excessive proton decay rates. These models naturally link the scale of unification with the solution to the doublet-triplet splitting problem via dynamical mechanisms.

来自$5$表示凝聚的算符导致过快的质子衰变，因而被排除。相反，$10$和$24$表示的凝聚能产生合适的阈值修正，实现成功的耦合统一，同时避免过大的质子衰变率。这些模型通过动力学机制自然地将统一尺度与二重态-三重态分裂问题的解决方案联系起来。

Conclusion: Non-renormalizable operators from fermion condensates in $10$ and $24$ representations of $SU(5)$ provide a viable path to gauge coupling unification while addressing the doublet-triplet splitting problem dynamically. This framework enhances the phenomenological viability of GUTs beyond minimal constructions.

来自$SU(5)$群$10$和$24$表示中费米子凝聚的不可重整算符为规范耦合统一提供了可行路径，同时以动力学方式解决了二重态-三重态分裂问题。该框架提升了大统一理论相较于最小模型的唯象可行性。

Abstract: An interesting framework to achieve gauge coupling unification consists in adding to the Standard Model Lagrangian non-renormalizable operators of $d \geq 5$, which affect the kinetic term of gauge fields. We first review the phenomenology related to this framework in the context of $SU(5)$, identifying which are the most interesting representations for the sake of achieving coupling unification. Secondly, we point out that in the case of a dynamical breaking pattern, it is possible to relate gauge coupling unification with the doublet-triplet splitting problem. We show that condensates of fermions in the $5$ representation do not lead to viable models because of proton decay constraints. At difference, we point out that successful models can be obtained by considering condensates of fermions in the $10$, as well as in the $24$ representations.

### [58] [Cosmological collider signals of modular spontaneous CP breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05548)
*Shuntaro Aoki,Alessandro Strumia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper proposes a modular-invariant extension of the Standard Model where the modulus acts as the inflaton. During inflation, CP-violating phases in Yukawa couplings evolve, generating a Higgs condensate and enhancing cosmological collider signals via fermion loops with chemical potentials. Precise one-loop results for Dirac fermions in de Sitter space are derived, showing detectability in future experiments even for sub-Planckian decay constants.

该论文提出了一种模不变的标准模型扩展，其中模量作为暴胀子。在暴胀期间，汤川耦合中的CP破坏相位演化，导致希格斯凝聚的产生，并通过带化学势的费米子圈增强宇宙学对撞机信号。推导了德西特空间中狄拉克费米子在化学势下的精确单圈结果，表明即使在次普朗克衰变常数下，下一代实验也可探测到该信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore the cosmological implications of modular invariance in the Standard Model, particularly how dynamical moduli during inflation can generate observable signatures such as enhanced cosmological collider signals through CP violation and fermionic chemical potentials.

探索标准模型中模不变性的宇宙学意义，特别是暴胀期间动力学模量如何通过CP破坏和费米子化学势产生可观测的宇宙学对撞机信号。

Method: The authors employ a modular-invariant framework where the modulus field drives inflation. They analyze the time evolution of CP-violating phases in Yukawa couplings during inflation, compute the resulting Higgs condensate, and calculate one-loop contributions of Dirac fermions with finite chemical potentials in de Sitter space using quantum field theory in curved spacetime.

作者采用一个模量驱动暴胀的模不变框架，分析暴胀期间汤川耦合中CP破坏相位的时间演化，计算由此产生的希格斯凝聚，并利用弯曲时空中的量子场论计算德西特空间中带化学势狄拉克费米子的单圈贡献。

Result: The evolving CP phases induce a non-zero Higgs condensate, which enhances the one-loop cosmological collider signal mediated by SM fermions. The enhancement is due to finite chemical potentials arising from the modulus coupling. Analytical expressions for the fermion loop contributions in de Sitter space are derived, showing that next-generation cosmological observations can probe modulus decay constants below the Planck scale.

演化的CP相位诱导出非零希格斯凝聚，增强了由标准模型费米子介导的单圈宇宙学对撞机信号。这种增强源于模量耦合产生的有限化学势。推导了德西特空间中费米子圈贡献的解析表达式，表明下一代宇宙学观测可探测低于普朗克尺度的模量衰变常数。

Conclusion: Modular invariance with a modulus-driven inflation provides a rich mechanism for generating observable cosmological signatures. The interplay between CP violation, chemical potentials, and Higgs dynamics during inflation leads to enhanced non-Gaussianities detectable via cosmological collider physics, even for sub-Planckian parameters.

模不变性与模量驱动的暴胀为产生可观测宇宙学信号提供了丰富机制。暴胀期间CP破坏、化学势与希格斯动力学的相互作用导致可被宇宙学对撞机物理探测到的增强非高斯性，即使在次普朗克参数下亦然。

Abstract: We consider a modular-invariant extension of the Standard Model. Assuming that the modulus is the inflaton, the CP-violating phases of the Yukawa couplings evolve during inflation. This dynamics favours a Higgs condensate, so that Standard Model fermions mediate a one-loop cosmological collider signal enhanced by chemical potentials. Next-generation experiments can probe sub-Planckian values of the modulus decay constant. We provide precise expressions for Dirac fermions with chemical potentials in de Sitter.

### [59] [Deuteron normalization and channel-dependent formation dynamics in pion and kaon color transparency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05612)
*Byung-Geel Yu,Kook-Jin Kong,Tae Keun Choi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The Jefferson Lab data on nuclear transparency in $A(e,e'π^+) $ and $A(e,e'K^+) $ reveal that the onset of color transparency is reaction-dependent, with distinct normalization effects and in-medium dynamics: pion production is well described by quantum diffusion ($\Delta M^2_\pi \simeq 0.7~\mathrm{GeV}^2$), while kaon production shows faster geometric expansion tied to $R_K \sim \sqrt{\sigma_{KN}/\pi}$, indicating different formation mechanisms.

Jefferson Lab 关于 $A(e,e'π^+) $ 和 $A(e,e'K^+) $ 反应中核透明度的数据表明，色透明性的 onset 具有反应依赖性：π介子产生可用量子扩散模型（$\Delta M^2_\pi \simeq 0.7~\mathrm{GeV}^2$）描述，而K介子产生则表现出与 $R_K \sim \sqrt{\sigma_{KN}/\pi}$ 相关的更快几何膨胀，揭示了不同的介质内形成机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand whether the onset of color transparency—a predicted reduction in hadron-nucleus interactions due to small color-singlet configurations—exhibits universal behavior across different hadronic channels, or if it depends on the specific reaction and hadron type.

旨在探究色透明性的 onset 是否在不同强子通道间具有普适性，或是否依赖于具体反应和强子类型。

Method: Analyze and compare Jefferson Lab measurements of nuclear transparency in semi-inclusive $A(e,e'π^+) $ and $A(e,e'K^+) $ reactions, focusing on the role of deuterium normalization and the $Q^2$ dependence of transparency. Use the quantum diffusion model for pions and test its applicability to kaons; alternatively, consider a geometric expansion model based on hadron-nucleon cross sections.

分析并比较 Jefferson Lab 在 $A(e,e'π^+) $ 和 $A,e,e'K^+)$ 反应中的核透明度测量数据，重点关注氘核归一化的作用及透明度的 $Q^2$ 依赖性；对π介子使用量子扩散模型，并检验其对K介子的适用性，或改用基于强子-核子截面的几何膨胀模型。

Result: In $A(e,e'π^+) $, missing-mass selection suppresses neutron-induced $\Delta$ production, making the deuterium baseline effectively proton-only. In $A(e,e'K^+) $, hyperon channels remain significant, so deuterium represents a true proton--neutron average. The $Q^2$ dependence shows pion transparency follows quantum diffusion with $\Delta M^2_\pi \simeq 0.7~\mathrm{GeV}^2$, while kaon transparency requires a faster expansion scale $R_K \sim \sqrt{\sigma_{KN}/\pi}$ and is underestimated by the pion-like model.

在 $A(e,e'π^+) $ 中，缺失质量选择强烈抑制中子诱导的 $\Delta$ 产生，使氘核基准近似为仅质子贡献；而在 $A(e,e'K^+) $ 中，超子通道仍显著，故氘核反映真实的质子-中子平均。$Q^2$ 依赖性显示，π介子透明度符合 $\Delta M^2_\pi \simeq 0.7~\mathrm{GeV}^2$ 的量子扩散模型，而K介子透明度需更快的膨胀尺度 $R_K \sim \sqrt{\sigma_{KN}/\pi}$，且被π介子类模型显著低估。

Conclusion: The onset of color transparency is not universal but reaction-dependent, differing both in normalization (due to channel-specific final-state interactions) and in-medium propagation dynamics (quantum diffusion for pions vs. geometric expansion for kaons). This implies that hadron formation and color coherence development are sensitive to the specific quark-gluon structure and production mechanism.

色透明性的 onset 并非普适，而是依赖于反应类型，在归一化（源于末态相互作用的通道特异性）和介质内传播动力学（π介子为量子扩散，K介子为几何膨胀）上均有差异。这表明强子形成与色相干性的发展对特定的夸克-胶子结构及产生机制敏感。

Abstract: A combined view of the Jefferson Lab data on nuclear transparency in $A(e,e'π^+)$ and $A(e,e'K^+)$ reveals two simple but nontrivial features of the onset of color transparency. First, normalization to deuterium does not play the same role in the two reactions. In pion electroproduction, the missing-mass selection suppresses the neutron-induced $Δ$ channel so strongly that the deuteron baseline becomes effectively proton dominated. In kaon electroproduction, the nearby hyperon channels cannot be removed in the same way, and the deuteron retains a genuine proton--neutron average. Second, the $Q^2$ dependence indicates different in-medium formation dynamics. The pion transparency is well reproduced by the standard quantum diffusion model with $ΔM^2_π\simeq 0.7~\mathrm{GeV}^2$, whereas the kaon data favor a faster geometric expansion characterized by the scale $R_K \sim \sqrt{σ_{KN}/π}$ and are strongly underestimated by the same pion-like diffusion scale. These results suggest that the pion and kaon data already contain evidence that the onset of color transparency is reaction dependent both in normalization and in propagation through nuclear matter.

</details>


### [60] [Pion Parton Distribution Functions in the Light-Cone Quark Model and Experimental Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05762)
*Hari Govind P,Satyajit Puhan,Abhishek K. P,Reetanshu Pandey,Harleen Dahiya,Arvind Kumar,Suneel Dutt*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We calculate the valence quark parton distribution functions (PDFs) of the pion using the light-cone quark model, evolve them via DGLAP equations to higher energy scales, and find good agreement with experimental and theoretical data. We predict the pion's $F_2$ structure function at NLO accuracy, compare it with ZEUS and H1 data from DESY-HERA, and study the forward pion production cross-section in the Drell-Yan process. The results are consistent with existing measurements and provide predictions for the electron-ion collider era.

我们使用光锥夸克模型计算了π介子的价夸克部分子分布函数（PDFs），并通过DGLAP方程将其演化到更高能标，发现与实验和理论提取数据吻合良好。我们首次在NLO精度下预测了π介子的$F_2$结构函数，并与DESY-HERA的ZEUS和H1实验数据进行比较，同时研究了Drell-Yan过程中由π介子引起的前向π介子产生截面。结果与现有测量一致，并为电子-离子对撞机时代的实验提供了预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The internal structure of the pion, as a fundamental pseudoscalar meson, is crucial for understanding non-perturbative QCD dynamics. However, experimental access to pion PDFs is limited due to the lack of free pion targets. Therefore, a reliable theoretical framework like the light-cone quark model is needed to compute valence quark distributions and related observables such as the $F_2$ structure function and Drell-Yan cross-sections, enabling comparison with indirect data and future collider experiments.

作为基本的赝标量介子，π介子的内部结构对于理解非微扰QCD动力学至关重要。然而，由于缺乏自由π介子靶，实验上对π介子PDFs的获取受限。因此，需要像光锥夸克模型这样的可靠理论框架来计算价夸克分布以及相关的可观测量（如$F_2$结构函数和Drell-Yan截面），以便与间接实验数据及未来的对撞机实验进行比较。

Method: Valence quark PDFs of the pion are computed from the quark-quark correlation function within the light-cone quark model. These initial PDFs are evolved to higher energy scales using the DGLAP evolution equations at next-to-leading order (NLO). The $F_2$ structure function is calculated from the evolved PDFs and compared with ZEUS and H1 data. Forward pion production in the Drell-Yan process is computed using the calculated pion PDFs and nucleon PDFs from LHAPDF. Predictions are also made for the kinematics of the upcoming electron-ion collider.

在光锥夸克模型中，通过夸克-夸克关联函数计算π介子的价夸克PDFs。利用NLO精度下的DGLAP演化方程将这些初始PDFs演化到更高能标。由演化的PDFs计算$F_2$结构函数，并与ZEUS和H1数据进行比较。使用计算得到的π介子PDFs和LHAPDF中的核子PDFs计算Drell-Yan过程中前向π介子的产生。还针对未来电子-离子对撞机的运动学区域做出了预测。

Result: The evolved valence quark PDFs show good agreement with available experimental and theoretical extractions. The predicted $F_2$ structure function at NLO matches ZEUS and H1 data across a wide range of energy scales. The forward pion production cross-section in the Drell-Yan process is presented, and predictions for the electron-ion collider kinematics are provided, demonstrating consistency between the light-cone quark model and empirical observations.

演化的价夸克PDFs与现有的实验和理论提取结果符合良好。在NLO下预测的$F_2$结构函数在广泛的能标范围内与ZEUS和H1数据匹配。展示了Drell-Yan过程中前向π介子产生的截面，并提供了电子-离子对撞机运动学区域的预测，表明光锥夸克模型与实证观测之间具有一致性。

Conclusion: The light-cone quark model provides a consistent and predictive framework for studying the pion's valence quark structure. The successful description of PDFs, $F_2$ structure function, and Drell-Yan cross-sections validates the approach, supporting its use for future precision studies at facilities like the electron-ion collider.

光锥夸克模型为研究π介子的价夸克结构提供了一个自洽且具有预测能力的框架。该方法成功描述了PDFs、$F_2$结构函数和Drell-Yan截面，验证了其有效性，支持其在未来如电子-离子对撞机等设施上的高精度研究中应用。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the valence quark parton distribution functions (PDFs) of the pion within the light-cone quark model. The initial quark PDFs are calculated by solving the quark-quark correlation function for the pseudoscalar mesons. The initial quark PDFs have been evolved to higher energy scales through the Dokshitzer,Gribov,Lipatov,Altarelli,Parisi (DGLAP) evolution equations. We also find that our calculated evolved PDFs match experimental and available theoretical extraction data. For the first time, we have also predicted the $F_2$ structure function at next-to-leading (NLO) order accuracy. The calculated $F_2$ structure function has been compared with the available ZEUS and H1 experimental data at DESY-HERA over a wide range of energy scales. Additionally, we display the forward pion production cross-section for the Drell-Yan process caused by pions using the pion PDFs that were calculated and the target nucleon PDFs from the LHAPDF nucleus datasets. The evolved $F_2$ structure function of the pion have been studied at the upcoming electron-ion collider energy kinematics. Overall, it was observed that the quark PDFs of pions computed using the light-cone quark model consistent with the experimental results.

### [61] [Scalar axion field of toroidal electromagnetic pulses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05791)
*Wangke Yu,Nikitas Papasimakis,Nikolay I. Zheludev,Yijie Shen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Structured toroidal light pulses in free space create localized regions with $\bm{E}\cdot\bm{B} \ne 0$, inducing a co-propagating pseudoscalar field via axion electrodynamics—without producing real axion particles.

结构化的环形光脉冲在自由空间中产生局域的 $\bm{E}\cdot\bm{B} \ne 0$ 区域，通过轴子电动力学诱导出共传播的伪标量场，而非产生真实的轴子粒子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Axion electrodynamics introduces a coupling between electromagnetism and a hypothetical pseudoscalar axion field through the $\theta \bm{E} \cdot \bm{B}$ term. While no fundamental axion has been detected, exploring classical consequences of this extension helps clarify the physical interpretation of such theories and identify observable signatures in structured electromagnetic fields.

轴子电动力学通过 $\theta \bm{E} \cdot \bm{B}$ 项引入电磁场与假想的伪标量轴子场的耦合。尽管尚未探测到基本轴子，探索该扩展的经典效应有助于澄清此类理论的物理诠释，并识别结构化电磁场中的可观测特征。

Method: The authors analyze superpositions of toroidal electromagnetic pulses propagating in free space using classical axion electrodynamics. They compute $\bm{E}\cdot\bm{B}$ for these structured fields and solve the effective equation for the induced pseudoscalar field $\theta(x,t)$ assuming it is sourced by this invariant, within the framework where $\partial_\mu\partial^\mu\theta \propto \bm{E}\cdot\bm{B}$.

作者利用经典轴子电动力学分析在自由空间中传播的环形电磁脉冲叠加，计算这些结构化场的 $\bm{E}\cdot\bm{B}$，并在 $\partial_\mu\partial^\mu\theta \propto \bm{E}\cdot\bm{B}$ 的框架下求解由该不变量驱动的有效伪标量场 $\theta(x,t)$ 方程。

Result: It is shown that toroidal pulse superpositions yield localized spacetime regions where $\bm{E} \cdot \bm{B} \ne 0$, leading to a nontrivial, co-propagating solution for the pseudoscalar field $\theta(x,t)$. The induced $\theta$ field is classical and does not correspond to quantized axion particles.

研究表明，环形脉冲叠加会产生局域的时空区域，其中 $\bm{E} \cdot \bm{B} \ne 0$，从而导致非平凡的、共传播的伪标量场 $\theta(x,t)$ 解。该诱导场为经典场，不对应于量子化的轴子粒子。

Conclusion: Axion electrodynamics predicts that structured light with nonzero $\bm{E}\cdot\bm{B}$ can support a classical, localized pseudoscalar field that evolves self-consistently with the electromagnetic field. This provides a novel platform to explore effective axionic responses in classical optics without requiring quantum axions.

轴子电动力学预言，具有非零 $\bm{E}\cdot\bm{B}$ 的结构光可支持一个与电磁场自洽演化的经典局域伪标量场。这为在无需量子轴子的情况下探索经典光学中的有效轴子响应提供了新平台。

Abstract: Axion electrodynamics extends Maxwell's theory by postulating a hypothetical pseudoscalar axion field sourced by a scalar product of electric and magnetic fields. In this work, we demonstrate that a superposition of toroidal electromagnetic pulses propagating in free space naturally exhibits localized regions, where $\bm{E}\cdot\bm{B}\ne0$. As a consequence of axion electrodynamics, these structured light pulses generate a space-time localized pseudoscalar field co-propagating with the pulses. This result should not be interpreted as a mechanism for generating axion particles by light, but rather as a consequence of adopting the axion electrodynamics extension to Maxwell's equations.

### [62] [Thermodynamic and Transport Properties of Quark-Gluon Plasma at Finite Chemical Potential with a DNN framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05858)
*Rishabh Kumar Tiwari,Kangkan Goswami,Suraj Prasad,Captain R. Singh,Raghunath Sahoo,Mohammad Yousuf Jamal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A deep-learning-assisted quasi-particle model (DLQPM) is developed to study the thermodynamic and transport properties of the quark-gluon plasma (QGP) at finite baryon chemical potential $\mu_B$, using neural networks trained on lattice QCD data; the model successfully reproduces equation of state and predicts quantities like speed of sound, specific heat, viscosity, and conductivity with good agreement to existing results.

采用基于深度学习的准粒子模型（DLQPM），结合在格点QCD数据上训练的神经网络，研究有限重子化学势$\mu_B$下夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）的热力学与输运性质；该模型成功复现状态方程，并准确预测声速、比热、黏度和电导率等物理量，结果与其他计算一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The quark-gluon plasma at finite baryon density is difficult to access via first-principles lattice QCD simulations due to the sign problem, and traditional effective models often lack precision in extrapolating thermodynamic and transport properties to finite $\mu_B$. This work aims to bridge the gap by constructing a data-driven, deep neural network (DNN)-assisted quasi-particle model that accurately captures non-perturbative effects from lattice QCD while enabling reliable predictions at finite baryon chemical potential.

由于符号问题，通过第一性原理的格点QCD模拟难以直接研究有限重子密度下的夸克-胶子等离子体，而传统有效模型在向有限$\mu_B$外推时往往缺乏精度。本研究旨在构建一个数据驱动的、基于深度神经网络（DNN）的准粒子模型，以精确捕捉来自格点QCD的非微扰效应，并实现对有限重子化学势下性质的可靠预测。

Method: Temperature $T$ and baryon chemical potential $\mu_B$-dependent thermal masses of quasiparticles are modeled using deep neural networks (DNNs), which are trained to reproduce the lattice QCD equation of state expanded around $\mu_B = 0$ up to second order in a Taylor-like series. The resulting DLQPM serves as an effective emulator for the QGP, allowing computation of thermodynamic observables (e.g., pressure, entropy) and transport coefficients (e.g., shear viscosity $\eta$, electrical conductivity $\sigma$) via standard kinetic theory relations. All quantities are consistently derived from the DNN-generated spectral functions and distribution functions.

使用深度神经网络（DNN）建模准粒子的温度$T$和重子化学势$\mu_B$依赖的热质量，训练目标是复现围绕$\mu_B = 0$展开至二阶泰勒类级数的格点QCD状态方程。所得DLQPM作为QGP的有效模拟器，通过标准动理学理论关系计算热力学观测量（如压强、熵）和输运系数（如剪切黏滞系数$\eta$、电导率$\sigma$）。所有物理量均自洽地由DNN生成的谱函数和分布函数导出。

Result: The DLQPM successfully reproduces lQCD results for the equation of state at $\mu_B = 0$ and provides smooth extrapolations to finite $\mu_B$. Predictions for the speed of sound $c_s^2$, specific heat $c_v$, shear viscosity to entropy ratio $\eta/s$, and electrical conductivity $\sigma/T$ show good agreement with available lattice data and other phenomenological models. Notably, $\eta/s$ exhibits a minimum near the pseudo-critical temperature $T_{\mathrm{pc}}$, consistent with expectations for a strongly coupled fluid.

DLQPM成功复现了$\mu_B = 0$时格点QCD的状态方程，并能平滑外推至有限$\mu_B$。对声速$c_s^2$、比热$c_v$、剪切黏滞比$\eta/s$及电导率$\sigma/T$的预测与现有格点数据和其他唯象模型吻合良好。值得注意的是，$\eta/s$在拟临界温度$T_{\mathrm{pc}}$附近出现极小值，符合强耦合流体的预期行为。

Conclusion: The integration of deep learning with physical modeling offers a powerful and efficient framework for studying the QGP in regions inaccessible to direct lattice simulations. The DLQPM demonstrates that DNN-based emulators can reliably capture non-perturbative dynamics and provide accurate predictions for both thermodynamic and transport properties at finite baryon density, paving the way for more precise hydrodynamic simulations of heavy-ion collisions.

将深度学习与物理建模相结合，为研究无法通过直接格点模拟访问区域的QGP提供了强大且高效的框架。DLQPM表明，基于DNN的模拟器能够可靠捕捉非微扰动力学，并在有限重子密度下准确预测热力学与输运性质，为更精确的重离子碰撞流体力学模拟铺平道路。

Abstract: The characteristics of a thermal system depend strongly on its response to thermal gradients and the underlying microscopic interactions among constituents. In the present study, we investigate the thermodynamic and transport properties of the quark-gluon plasma (QGP) at finite baryon chemical potential within a deep-learning-assisted quasi-particle model (DLQPM). The temperature ($\mathrm{T}$) and baryon chemical potential ($μ_B$)-dependent thermal masses of quasi-particles are estimated using neural networks trained to reproduce lattice QCD (lQCD) results for the equation of state, obtained via a Taylor-like expansion around vanishing baryon chemical potential. The trained model acts as an effective emulator, enabling us to estimate the thermodynamic and transport properties at finite $μ_B$. We compute the speed of sound, specific heat, viscosity, and conductivity of the deconfined medium. Our findings are in good agreement with available lattice calculations and other phenomenological models. The present study demonstrates that a DNN-based approach provides an efficient framework for studying the properties of the QGP at finite baryon density.
