### [63] [Doubly charged Higgs production within the Higgs triplet model at future electron-positron colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05924)
*Shu-Xiang Li,Ren-You Zhang,Ming-Hui Liu,Xiao-Feng Wang,Zhong-Yuan Liu,Yi Jiang,Liang Han,Qing-hai Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study the discovery potential of doubly charged Higgs bosons at CLIC in various collision modes ($e^-e^-$, $e^-\gamma$, $\gamma\gamma$, $e^+e^-$) within the Higgs triplet model, focusing on two benchmark scenarios: Yukawa-like and gauge-like. In the Yukawa-like region, single production via $e^-e^-$ and $e^-\gamma$ dominates, with decay into same-sign dileptons yielding high statistical significance. In the gauge-like region, the $\ell^\pm\ell^\pm + \geq 3j$ channel allows discovery up to $1.2~\mathrm{TeV}$. We compare with HL-LHC and find CLIC offers superior sensitivity.

我们研究了在Higgs三重态模型下，CLIC在多种对撞模式（$e^-e^-$、$e^-\gamma$、$\gamma\gamma$、$e^+e^-$）中发现带双重电荷的Higgs玻色子的潜力，重点关注Yukawa型和规范型两种基准情形。在Yukawa型区域，通过$e^-e^-$和$e^-\gamma$的单产生主导，其衰变为同号轻子对可实现远超发现阈值的统计显著性。在规范型区域，$\ell^\pm\ell^\pm + \geq 3j$末态使CLIC可在质量高达约$1.2~\mathrm{TeV}$时实现稳健发现。与HL-LHC相比，CLIC展现出更优的探测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Doubly charged Higgs bosons are key predictions of the Higgs triplet model (HTM), offering a natural mechanism for neutrino mass generation via the seesaw mechanism. Their discovery would be unambiguous evidence of physics beyond the Standard Model. While the HL-LHC has search capability, its sensitivity is limited by large backgrounds and lower energy. CLIC, as a high-energy, high-luminosity lepton collider, provides a cleaner environment and tunable collision modes, enabling enhanced sensitivity to both production and decay signatures of $H^{\pm\pm}$, particularly in challenging parameter regions.

带双重电荷的Higgs玻色子是Higgs三重态模型（HTM）的关键预言，可通过see-saw机制自然生成中微子质量。其发现将是超出标准模型物理的确凿证据。尽管HL-LHC具备搜索能力，但受限于强背景和较低能量。而作为高能、高亮度的轻子对撞机，CLIC提供更干净的环境和可调的对撞模式，从而显著提升对$H^{\pm\pm}$产生与衰变信号的灵敏度，尤其是在困难参数区域。

Method: We perform Monte Carlo simulations for $H^{\pm\pm}$ production at CLIC in four collision modes: $e^-e^-$, $e^-\gamma$, $\gamma\gamma$, and $e^+e^-$. Two benchmark points representing Yukawa-dominated and gauge-dominated couplings are selected. For each, we compute cross sections for relevant processes: $e^-e^- \to H^{--}\nu_e\nu_e$, $e^-\gamma \to H^{--}e^+\nu_e$, etc. Detector effects are simulated using Delphes with CLIC-specific card. Backgrounds from SM processes like $W^\pm W^\pm jj$, $t\bar{t}$, and misidentified leptons are estimated. Signal significance is calculated using $Z = \sqrt{2[(s+b)\ln(1+s/b) - s]}$, incorporating systematic uncertainties. The analysis is repeated for HL-LHC at $\sqrt{s} = 14~\mathrm{TeV}, \mathcal{L} = 3~\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$.

我们在四种对撞模式下对CLIC中$H^{\pm\pm}$的产生进行蒙特卡洛模拟：$e^-e^-$、$e^-\gamma$、$\gamma\gamma$、$e^+e^-$。选取两个代表Yukawa主导和规范主导耦合的基准点。针对每个点计算相关过程的截面，如$e^-e^- \to H^{--}\nu_e\nu_e$、$e^-\gamma \to H^{--}e^+\nu_e$等。使用Delphes及CLIC专用卡片模拟探测器效应。估计来自SM过程（如$W^\pm W^\pm jj$、$t\bar{t}$、轻子误识别）的背景。采用公式$Z = \sqrt{2[(s+b)\ln(1+s/b) - s]}$计算信号显著性，并包含系统误差。同时在$\sqrt{s} = 14~\mathrm{TeV}, \mathcal{L} = 3~\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$条件下重复HL-LHC分析。

Result: In the Yukawa-like region, $e^-e^-$ and $e^-\gamma$ modes yield high cross sections for single $H^{\pm\pm}$ production. With $H^{\pm\pm} \to \ell^\pm\ell^\pm$, CLIC achieves $5\sigma$ discovery for masses up to $\sim 800~\mathrm{GeV}$, assuming $\text{Br}(H^{\pm\pm} \to \ell^\pm\ell^\pm) \approx 1$. In the gauge-like region, pair production dominates; the $\ell^\pm\ell^\pm + \geq 3j$ final state enables $5\sigma$ discovery up to $\sim 1.2~\mathrm{TeV}$. CLIC outperforms HL-LHC across both scenarios: at $1~\mathrm{TeV}$, CLIC reaches $Z \sim 10$, while HL-LHC yields $Z < 3$. Sensitivity persists even with reduced branching ratios.

在Yukawa型区域，$e^-e^-$和$e^-\gamma$模式下单$H^{\pm\pm}$产生的截面较高。当$H^{\pm\pm} \to \ell^\pm\ell^\pm$且分支比接近1时，CLIC可在质量达$\sim 800~\mathrm{GeV}$时实现$5\sigma$发现。在规范型区域，对产生占主导，$\ell^\pm\ell^\pm + \geq 3j$末态使CLIC可在质量高达$\sim 1.2~\mathrm{TeV}$时实现$5\sigma$发现。在两种情形下，CLIC均优于HL-LHC：在$1~\mathrm{TeV}$处，CLIC显著性$Z \sim 10$，而HL-LHC不足$Z < 3$。即使分支比降低，CLIC仍保持灵敏度。

Conclusion: CLIC offers unparalleled discovery potential for doubly charged Higgs bosons in the Higgs triplet model, across a wide mass range and coupling regimes. The availability of multiple collision modes—especially $e^-e^-$ and $e^-\gamma$—enables access to both Yukawa- and gauge-dominated scenarios. The clean experimental environment and high luminosity allow robust signal extraction even in the presence of challenging backgrounds. Compared to HL-LHC, CLIC provides significantly higher sensitivity, extending the reach up to $1.2~\mathrm{TeV}$ and offering a definitive probe of the HTM parameter space.

CLIC在Higgs三重态模型中对带双重电荷的Higgs玻色子具有无与伦比的发现潜力，覆盖宽广的质量范围和耦合区域。多种对撞模式（尤其是$e^-e^-$和$e^-\gamma$）使其能够探测Yukawa主导和规范主导的各类情形。干净的实验环境和高亮度使得即使在强背景干扰下也能稳健提取信号。相比HL-LHC，CLIC具有显著更高的灵敏度，探测上限可达$1.2~\mathrm{TeV}$，为全面检验HTM参数空间提供了决定性手段。

Abstract: We investigate in detail the discovery potential of the doubly charged Higgs boson at the Compact Linear Collider in $e^-e^-$, $e^-γ$, $γγ$, and $e^+e^-$ collision modes, within the Higgs triplet model at two extreme benchmark points as representatives of the Yukawa-like and gauge-like regions. In the Yukawa-like region, the most promising production mechanism is the single production via $e^-e^-$ and $e^-γ$ collisions. Given the subsequent decay of the doubly charged Higgs into a same-sign lepton pair, CLIC can achieve statistical significance well beyond the discovery threshold, within the parameter space permitted by experimental constraints. In the gauge-like region, with the $\ell^{\pm}\ell^{\pm} + \geq 3j$ final state, CLIC exhibits robust discovery potential for the doubly charged Higgs boson, up to a mass of approximately $1.2~\mathrm{TeV}$. We also investigate the search for doubly charged Higgs at the HL-LHC. Our results demonstrate that CLIC possesses greater advantages and offers superior discovery potential for the doubly charged Higgs boson, compared to the HL-LHC.

</details>


### [64] [Monte-Carlo Event Generation for X-Ray Thomson Scattering Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05935)
*Uwe Hernandez Acosta,Thomas Gawne,Jan Vorberger,Hannah Bellenbaum,Anton Reinhard,Simeon Ehrig,Klaus Steiniger,Michael Bussmann,Tobias Dornheim*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: An event-driven approach to X-ray Thomson scattering (XRTS) modeling is proposed, inspired by particle physics event generators, enabling statistically consistent, geometry-aware, and computationally efficient simulations of scattering events in warm-dense matter experiments.

一种受粒子物理事件生成器启发的X射线汤姆逊散射（XRTS）事件驱动建模方法被提出，能够在温密物质实验中实现统计一致、几何感知且计算高效的散射事件模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Interpretation of X-ray Thomson scattering (XRTS) data in warm-dense matter (WDM) experiments is hindered by complex instrument effects and the high computational cost of combining microscopic models with detector simulations. A more flexible and efficient method is needed to enable accurate and scalable analysis.

温密物质（WDM）实验中X射线汤姆逊散射（XRTS）数据的解释受到复杂仪器效应以及微观模型与探测器模拟结合所带来的高计算成本的限制，因此需要一种更灵活、高效的方法以实现精确且可扩展的分析。

Method: An event-driven simulation framework is developed, where individual scattering events are sampled from the differential cross section $\frac{d\sigma}{d\Omega}$ and propagated through a spectrometer simulation, rather than computing spectra via traditional forward models. This approach preserves full kinematic information and decouples event generation from detector-level analysis, enabling reuse of events and reducing computational overhead.

开发了一种事件驱动的模拟框架，其中单个散射事件从微分截面$\frac{d\sigma}{d\Omega}$中采样，并通过光谱仪模拟进行传播，而不是通过传统的前向模型计算光谱。该方法保留了完整的运动学信息，并将事件生成与探测器层级分析解耦，从而允许事件重用并降低计算开销。

Result: The method demonstrates feasibility and physical consistency in a synthetic non-resonant XRTS setup. It enables flexible, geometry-aware analysis and provides a statistically consistent representation of scattering events. Computational efficiency is improved due to reduced need for repeated evaluations of forward models.

该方法在合成的非共振XRTS设置中展示了可行性与物理一致性，能够实现灵活且几何感知的分析，并提供散射事件的统计一致表示。由于减少了对前向模型重复计算的需求，计算效率得到提升。

Conclusion: The event-driven approach establishes a model-agnostic framework for XRTS modeling, bridging techniques from particle physics with WDM diagnostics. It offers a scalable foundation for advanced analysis and Bayesian inference in future XRTS experiments.

这种事件驱动方法为XRTS建模建立了一个模型无关的框架，架起了粒子物理技术与温密物质诊断之间的桥梁，为未来XRTS实验中的高级分析和贝叶斯推断提供了可扩展的基础。

Abstract: A key diagnostic in warm-dense matter (WDM) experiments is X-ray Thomson scattering (XRTS), but its interpretation is often limited by complex instrument effects and the high computationally expensive combinations of microscopic models with detector simulations. We present a proof-of-principle implementation of an event-driven approach to XRTS modelling, inspired by particle physics event-generators. Instead of computing the spectra via forward models, individual scattering events are sampled from the differential cross section and sent through a spectrometer simulation. This provides a statistically consistent representation that preserves full kinematic information and enables flexible and geometry-aware analysis. We demonstrate the feasibility and physical consistency of the method for non-resonant XRTS in a synthetic setup. By decoupling event generation from detector-level analysis, the framework allows efficient reuse of the sampled events and reduces computational overhead associated with repeated evaluations. The method is model-agnostic and establishes a new connection between particle-physics event generation techniques and WDM diagnostics, providing a scalable foundation for advanced XRTS analysis and inference.

</details>


### [65] [Quarkyonic Meson Matter for Finite Isospin Density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06054)
*Larry McLerran*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies QCD at finite isospin density in the large-$N_c$ limit, identifying three distinct regimes: a Bose-condensed phase at low $\mu_I$, a weakly-coupled meson/Cooper pair phase at high $\mu_I \gg \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$, and a quarkyonic meson phase at intermediate densities where mesons form from quarks filling a Fermi sea with possible surface condensation.

本文在大$N_c$极限下研究了有限同位旋密度的QCD，识别出三个不同区域：低$\mu_I$时的玻色凝聚相，高$\mu_I \gg \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$时由介子和库珀对组成的弱耦合相，以及中等密度下的夸克-介子相，其中夸克填充费米海并形成介子，可能伴随费米面处的玻色凝聚或有限宽度的库珀配对。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the phase structure of QCD at finite isospin density in the large-$N_c$ limit, particularly how confinement and chiral symmetry breaking persist across different density regimes, and to identify novel states such as quarkyonic matter in intermediate density regions.

旨在理解大$N_c$极限下有限同位旋密度QCD的相结构，特别是禁闭和手征对称性破缺如何在不同密度区域持续存在，并识别中间密度区可能出现的新物态（如夸克-介子物质）。

Method: A linear sigma model is employed to describe low-energy meson dynamics. The analysis leverages the large-$N_c$ expansion to distinguish between different density regimes based on scaling with $\sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$. Physical behavior across $\mu_I << \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$, $\Lambda_{\text{QCD}} \leq \mu_I \leq \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$, and $\mu_I >> \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$ is inferred from effective field theory arguments and known large-$N_c$ scaling behaviors of hadronic states.

采用线性sigma模型描述低能介子动力学。利用大$N_c$展开，根据与$\sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$的标度关系区分不同密度区域。通过有效场论论证和已知的大$N_c$标度行为推断$\mu_I << \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$、$\Lambda_{\text{QCD}} \leq \mu_I \leq \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$和$\mu_I >> \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$区域的物理行为。

Result: Three distinct regimes are identified: (i) For $\mu_I << \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$, a Bose-Einstein condensate of pions forms; (ii) For $\mu_I >> \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$, the system remains confined but exhibits weakly coupled dynamics with mesons and tightly bound Cooper pairs; (iii) For intermediate densities $\Lambda_{\text{QCD}} \leq \mu_I \leq \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$, the matter is quarkyonic—quarks fill a Fermi sea and bind into mesons at the scale $\Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$, with potential Bose condensation or finite-width pairing at the Fermi surface.

识别出三个不同区域：(i) $\mu_I << \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$时形成π介子的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚；(ii) $\mu_I >> \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$时系统仍处于禁闭状态，但表现出弱耦合动力学，包含介子和紧密束缚的库珀对；(iii) 中间密度$\Lambda_{\text{QCD}} \leq \mu_I \leq \sqrt{N_c} \Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$时物质为夸克-介子型——夸克填充费米海并在$\Lambda_{\text{QCD}}$尺度上结合成介子，费米面可能存在玻色凝聚或有限宽度的配对。

Conclusion: Quarkyonic matter can emerge in QCD at finite isospin density for intermediate values of $\mu_I$, characterized by a Fermi sea of quarks with meson formation and possible pairing phenomena at the Fermi surface, despite confinement. This extends the concept of quarkyonic matter beyond baryonic systems to isospin-charged matter.

在中等$\mu_I$值下，有限同位旋密度QCD中可出现夸克-介子物质，其特征是夸克费米海伴随介子形成及费米面可能的配对现象，尽管系统仍处于禁闭状态。这将夸克-介子物质的概念从重子体系推广到了同位旋荷物质。

Abstract: QCD at finite isospin density is considered for a large number of colors $N_c$. A linear sigma model is used to model the meson content of the theory at low density. At isospin chemical potential $μ_I << Λ_{QCD}$, this matter forms a Bose condensate. For $μ_I >> \sqrt{N_c} Λ_{QCD}$, unlike QCD remains confined, but the degrees of freedom of the system are mesons and Cooper pairs bound on size scales small compared to the QCD size scale determined by the superfluid gap. For most purposes this matter may be analyzed using weak coupling methods. For $ Λ_{QCD} \le μ_I \le \sqrt{Nc} Λ_{QCD}$, we argue that meson matter is quarkyonic, with quarks bound into mesons on a size scale of order $Λ_{QCD}$ corresponding to a filled Fermi sea of quarks, with possible Bose condensation at the Fermi surface and/or Cooper pairs with finite width of the surface of order $Λ_{QCD}$.

</details>


### [66] [The SUSY reach of Higgs Factories in the most challenging scenario: scalar $τ$-leptons with lowest cross section and small mass differences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06103)
*Maria Teresa Núñez Pardo de Vera,Mikael Berggren,Jenny List*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the sensitivity of future $e^+e^-$ colliders to the direct pair production of staus ($\tildeτ$) in the 'worst-case' scenario, where the stau is nearly mass-degenerate with the lightest SUSY particle and detection efficiency is minimized due to $\tildeτ$ mixing. Using detailed simulations with the ILD detector concept at 500 GeV center-of-mass energy, including realistic beam backgrounds from $γγ$ and beamstrahlung, the study shows that exclusion and discovery reaches extend close to the kinematic limit. Results are extrapolated to other Higgs factory projects like FCCee.

本文研究了未来正负电子对撞机在“最坏情况”下对直接产生超对称轻子——标量tau（$\tildeτ$）的探测灵敏度，其中$\tildeτ$与最轻超对称粒子质量接近且因$\tildeτ$混合导致探测效率最低。使用ILD探测器概念在500 GeV质心能量下的详细模拟（首次包含来自$γγ$相互作用和束流轫致辐射的低$\it{P_{T}}$强子及$e^+e^-$对的束交叉背景），发现即使在此极端情况下，排除和发现范围仍接近运动学极限。结果被外推至其他希格斯工厂项目如FCCee。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Stau ($\tildeτ$) is expected to be the lightest slepton in many SUSY models, making its direct production a crucial channel for testing supersymmetry. However, when $\tildeτ$ is nearly mass-degenerate with the lightest neutralino (LSP), the signal becomes challenging due to soft decay products. Additionally, $\tildeτ$ mixing reduces the production cross-section in $e^+e^-$ collisions. This creates a 'worst-case' scenario that is poorly constrained by LHC searches relying on high-$p_T$ signatures. Therefore, a precise study at a clean environment like a future $e^+e^-$ collider is essential to fully explore this difficult region of SUSY parameter space.

在许多超对称模型中，标量tau（$\tildeτ$）预期是最轻的标量子，因此其直接产生是检验超对称性的关键通道。然而，当$\tildeτ$与最轻中性费米子（LSP）质量接近时，衰变产物动量软，信号难以识别；此外，$\tildeτ$混合会降低其在$e^+e^-$对撞中的产生截面。这构成了LHC难以探测的“最坏情况”。因此，在未来$e^+e^-$对撞机等干净环境中进行精确研究，对于全面探索这一困难区域至关重要。

Method: Detailed Monte Carlo simulations were performed using the ILD detector concept designed for the International Linear Collider (ILC), assuming a center-of-mass energy of 500 GeV and realistic beam conditions. The analysis includes the effects of $\tildeτ$ mixing on both production cross-section and detection efficiency. For the first time, background from bunch crossings without hard $e^+e^-$ interactions — specifically low-$\it{P_T}$ hadrons from $γγ \to$ hadrons and $e^+e^-$ pairs from beamstrahlung — are included in the simulation. Signal and background events were generated with full event reconstruction and particle flow algorithms. Exclusion and discovery sensitivities were estimated using statistical methods (e.g., CLs) based on binned likelihood fits to observables such as visible mass and missing energy.

使用为国际线性对撞机（ILC）设计的ILD探测器概念，基于500 GeV质心能量和真实束流条件进行了详细的蒙特卡洛模拟。分析包含了$\tildeτ$混合对产生截面和探测效率的影响。首次在模拟中引入了无硬$e^+e^-$相互作用的束交叉背景，即来自$γγ \to$ 强子的低$\it{P_T}$强子和来自束流轫致辐射的$e^+e^-$对。信号与本底事件通过完整的事例重建和粒子流算法处理，并基于可见质量与缺失能量等可观测量，采用统计方法（如CLs方法）通过分箱似然拟合估算排除与发现灵敏度。

Result: Even in the worst-case scenario — with maximal $\tildeτ$ mixing and small mass splitting between $\tildeτ$ and the LSP — the exclusion and discovery reaches at 500 GeV extend up to nearly the kinematic limit ($\sqrt{s}/2$). For example, $\tildeτ$ masses up to ~240 GeV can be probed with 500 fb$^{-1}$ luminosity. The inclusion of realistic beam-induced backgrounds has a negligible impact on sensitivity, demonstrating robustness of the ILD design. When extrapolating to other Higgs factories like FCCee, which operate at higher luminosities and multiple energies, the reach improves significantly, allowing coverage of almost the entire theoretically allowed parameter space for $\tildeτ$ in the MSSM.

即使在最坏情况下——最大$\tildeτ$混合且$\tildeτ$与LSP之间质量差很小——在500 GeV下排除与发现灵敏度仍接近运动学极限（$\sqrt{s}/2$）。例如，在500 fb$^{-1}$积分亮度下可探测高达~240 GeV的$\tildeτ$质量。包含真实的束流诱导背景对灵敏度影响可忽略，表明ILD设计具有鲁棒性。外推至FCCee等其他希格斯工厂时，由于更高亮度和多能量运行，探测能力显著提升，几乎可覆盖MSSM中$\tildeτ$的全部理论允许参数空间。

Conclusion: Future $e^+e^-$ colliders, particularly those implementing precision detectors like ILD and operating at high luminosity, are uniquely powerful for probing challenging SUSY scenarios such as near-degenerate $\tildeτ$-LSP spectra. Even under conservative assumptions maximizing experimental difficulty (worst-case mixing and small mass splittings), these machines can achieve sensitivity up to the kinematic limit. The results validate the physics potential of proposed Higgs factories like ILC and FCCee in completing the search for weakly interacting SUSY particles beyond the reach of LHC.

未来的$e^+e^-$对撞机，特别是采用高精度探测器（如ILD）并在高亮度下运行的机器，在探测挑战性超对称场景（如近简并的$\tildeτ$-LSP谱）方面具有独特优势。即使在最大化实验难度的保守假设下（最坏混合与小质量分裂），这些设备仍能达到接近运动学极限的灵敏度。结果验证了ILC和FCCee等提议的希格斯工厂在完成对LHC无法触及的弱相互作用超对称粒子搜索方面的物理潜力。

Abstract: The direct pair-production of the $\tildeτ$, is one of the most interesting channels to search for SUSY in: the $\tildeτ$ is likely to be the lightest of the scalar leptons, and the signature of $\tildeτ$ pair production is one of the experimentally most difficult ones, making it the ``worst'' possible scenario for SUSY searches. The current limit on $\tildeτ$ production in the general MSSM comes from LEP. Limits obtained at LHC do extend to higher masses, but they are only valid under strong assumptions. Future $e^+e^-$ colliders will be powerful for SUSY searches, offering advantages with respect to previous $e^+e^-$ colliders as well as to hadron machines. In order to quantify their capabilities, the ``worst-case'' scenario for $\tildeτ$ searches has been studied, taking into account the effect of the $\tildeτ$ mixing on both $\tildeτ$ production cross section and on detection efficiency. To evaluate the latter, the ILD detector concept, originally developed for the International Linear Collider (ILC), and the ILC beam conditions at a centre-of-mass energy of $500$\,GeV have been used for detailed simulations, including for the first time the effect of bunch-crossings containing no hard $e^+e^-$ interaction, but only low-$\it{P_{T}}$ hadrons from $γγ$ interactions and $e^+e^-$ pairs from beamstrahlung. Still, the obtained exclusion and discovery reaches extend nearly up to the kinematic limit even in the worst-case scenario. This remains true also when the $\tildeτ$ and the lightest SUSY particle are quite close in mass. The results of the detailed study are extrapolated to centre-of-mass energies, integrated luminosities and beam polarisations of other proposed Higgs factory projects and discussed in view of their respective experimental environments, in particular addressing the case of FCCee.

</details>

### [67] [Universal Dark-matter Density Profiles of Cosmic Filaments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05033)
*Peng Xu,Fangzhou Jiang,Farhanul Hasan,Joanna Woo,Douglas Hellinger,Joel R. Primack,Sandra M. Faber,David Koo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study analyzes dark matter density profiles in cosmic filaments using the TNG50 simulation and introduces a 'shrinking-cylinder' re-centering method to improve accuracy. After scaling by virial radii, filament profiles show near-universality across redshifts and masses, indicating self-similarity. The central cusp in the full profile arises mainly from embedded low-mass halos, while the smooth dark matter component forms a flat core. A generalized triple-power-law model accurately describes the universal profile.

本研究利用TNG50模拟分析宇宙网丝状结构的暗物质密度剖面，并引入“收缩圆柱”重新中心化方法以提高精度。在用晕族virial半径归一化后，丝状结构密度剖面表现出近乎普适的形式，表明其具有结构自相似性。完整的剖面中的中心尖峰主要来源于嵌入的低质量晕，而平滑的暗物质成分在$R/R_{\rm vir}\lesssim0.1$内形成平坦核心。观测结果通过一个广义的三重幂律模型精确描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cosmic filaments are key components of the large-scale structure, yet their dark matter density profiles remain poorly characterized due to challenges in accurately identifying their spines. DisPerSE, a commonly used topological algorithm, tends to mislocate filament spines, leading to underestimated central densities. This work aims to correct this bias and investigate whether filaments exhibit structural universality analogous to dark matter halos.

宇宙丝状结构是大尺度结构的关键组成部分，但由于难以精确定位其脊线，其暗物质密度剖面仍缺乏准确刻画。DisPerSE作为一种常用的拓扑算法，往往错误定位丝状结构的脊线，导致中心密度被低估。本研究旨在纠正这一偏差，并探究丝状结构是否表现出类似于暗物质晕的结构普适性。

Method: We extract the cosmic web from TNG50 hydrodynamical simulation data at redshifts $z = 0, 0.5, 1, 2, 3$ using the DisPerSE algorithm on high-resolution density grids. To correct spine misalignment, we develop a 'shrinking-cylinder' re-centering technique that iteratively refines the filament axis by maximizing enclosed density. Radial density profiles are computed around the corrected spines and scaled by the virial radii ($R_{\rm vir}$) of terminal halos. We separately analyze contributions from all dark matter particles and from smoothly distributed, unbound particles only. Profiles are fit using a generalized triple-power-law model.

我们使用DisPerSE算法在高分辨率密度网格上从TNG50流体动力学模拟数据中提取红移$z = 0, 0.5, 1, 2, 3$处的宇宙网。为纠正脊线偏移，我们开发了一种“收缩圆柱”重新中心化技术，通过迭代最大化包围密度来优化丝状结构轴线。围绕修正后的脊线计算径向密度剖面，并用终端晕的virial半径（$R_{\rm vir}$）进行归一化。我们分别分析了所有暗物质粒子和平滑分布的未束缚粒子的贡献。剖面采用广义的三重幂律模型进行拟合。

Result: The shrinking-cylinder method significantly enhances the inferred central densities and restores the inner power-law behavior ($\rho \propto r^{-\alpha}$) of filament profiles. When scaled by $R_{\rm vir}$, the profiles exhibit a nearly universal form, weakly dependent on redshift, node mass, or filament length—indicating structural self-similarity. The apparent central cusp in the full DM profile is largely due to low-mass halos along the spine; in contrast, the smooth DM component develops a flat core within $R/R_{\rm vir} \lesssim 0.1$. The evolution of the smooth component suggests a shift from smooth accretion at high-$z$ to clumpy accretion at late times. The universal profile is well-fit by a generalized triple-power-law model.

“收缩圆柱”方法显著提高了推断的中心密度，并恢复了丝状结构剖面的内部幂律行为（$\rho \propto r^{-\alpha}$）。当用$R_{\rm vir}$归一化时，剖面呈现出近乎普适的形式，对红移、节点质量或丝状结构长度的依赖性较弱，表明存在结构自相似性。完整暗物质剖面中的表观中心尖峰主要来自沿脊线分布的低质量晕；相比之下，平滑暗物质成分在$R/R_{\rm vir} \lesssim 0.1$内形成平坦核心。平滑成分的演化表明，吸积方式从高红移时的平滑吸积逐渐转变为晚期的团块式吸积。普适剖面可由广义的三重幂律模型很好地拟合。

Conclusion: Cosmic filaments exhibit a form of structural universality when their radial profiles are scaled by the virial radius of their terminal nodes, akin to the self-similarity seen in dark matter halos. The 'shrinking-cylinder' re-centering method is essential for recovering accurate spine locations and inner density behaviors. The central cusp is not intrinsic to the smooth dark matter distribution but is instead dominated by subhalo contamination. The transition in accretion morphology over time reflects evolving structure formation dynamics. A generalized triple-power-law model provides an accurate analytical description of the universal filament profile.

当以终端节点的virial半径为标度时，宇宙丝状结构的径向剖面表现出一种结构普适性，类似于暗物质晕中的自相似现象。‘收缩圆柱’重新中心化方法对于恢复精确的脊线位置和内部密度行为至关重要。中心尖峰并非平滑暗物质分布的内在特征，而是主要由子晕污染主导。吸积形态随时间的转变反映了结构形成动力学的演化。广义的三重幂律模型为普适丝状结构剖面提供了精确的解析描述。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive analysis of the radial dark-matter (DM) density profiles of cosmic filaments in the hydrodynamical simulation TNG50. The cosmic web is extracted from high-resolution density grids at redshifts $z =$ 0, 0.5, 1, 2 and 3 using the DisPerSE algorithm. We show that the filament spine locations returned directly by DisPerSE do not accurately reflect the true density ridges. To address this issue, we introduce a "shrinking-cylinder" re-centering algorithm, which significantly increases the inferred central densities and restores the inner power-law behavior of the profiles. When the radial coordinate is scaled by the virial radii of the terminal nodes, the filament density profiles exhibit a nearly universal form that depends only weakly on redshift, node mass, and filament length. This result suggests that cosmic filaments, much like dark-matter halos, obey a form of structural self-similarity once an appropriate characteristic scale is introduced. By repeating the measurement using only smoothly distributed, unbound DM particles, we find that the apparent central cusp of the full profile is primarily produced by low-mass halos embedded along the filament spines, while the smooth component develops a flat core within $R/R_{\rm vir}\lesssim0.1$. The redshift evolution of this smooth component further suggests a transition from predominantly smooth filamentary accretion at high redshift to increasingly clumpy accretion at late times. Finally, we show that the universal filament profile is accurately described by a generalized triple-power-law model.

</details>


### [68] [Great Walls of Cosmic Baryons in the Northern Sky](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05093)
*Vikram Ravi,Kritti Sharma,Liam Connor*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We present a map of extragalactic dispersion measure (DM) variations using thousands of fast radio bursts (FRBs) from the CHIME catalog, detecting a $\gtrsim 4\sigma$ excess—termed Wall 1—of $\sim$150 pc cm$^{-3}$ over $\sim$30$^\circ$ scales near $\alpha \approx 12^\mathrm{h}, \delta \approx 55^\circ$, spatially aligned with the Ursa Major supercluster. A secondary signal, Wall 2, coincides with the Perseus-Pisces supercluster. While these may trace baryon overdensities in large-scale structure, chance coincidence remains plausible at $\sim10-20\%$. This demonstrates FRB DMs as a promising tool for near-field baryon mapping.

我们利用CHIME望远镜的数千个快速射电暴（FRB）的色散量（DM）变化绘制了北天图，探测到一个显著性超过$\gtrsim 4\sigma$、幅度约150 pc cm$^{-3}$、尺度约30$^\circ$的超出信号——称为“Wall 1”，位于赤经$\alpha \approx 12^\mathrm{h}$、赤纬$\delta \approx 55^\circ$附近，空间上与大熊座超星系团一致。另一个较弱的信号Wall 2位于英仙-双鱼超星系团方向。尽管可能存在偶然重合（概率约10-20%），这些结果表明FRB的DM可用于探测近邻宇宙的大尺度结构中的重子分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fast radio bursts (FRBs) probe the ionized intergalactic and circumgalactic media through their dispersion measures (DMs). Since most FRBs originate at cosmological distances, DM variations across the sky can reveal local anisotropies in baryon distribution, such as those from the Milky Way's halo or nearby large-scale structures. Current models of Galactic DM contributions are insufficient to explain all observed variance, motivating a data-driven search for extragalactic DM anisotropies using a large FRB sample.

快速射电暴（FRB）通过其色散量（DM）探测电离的星系际和星系周介质。由于大多数FRB来自宇宙学距离，天空中DM的变化可揭示重子分布的局部各向异性，例如来自银河系晕或邻近大尺度结构的贡献。现有的银河系DM模型不足以解释所有观测到的方差，因此需要利用大量FRB样本进行数据驱动的搜寻以发现河外DM各向异性。

Method: We analyzed extragalactic DMs from a few thousand FRBs in the second CHIME/FRB catalog, subtracting modeled contributions from the Milky Way disk and halo. We produced a sky map of residual DMs across the Northern hemisphere and applied jackknife resampling and sample-selection tests to assess statistical significance and robustness. Cross-correlation with known large-scale structures (e.g., Ursa Major and Perseus-Pisces superclusters) was performed to evaluate physical associations.

我们分析了CHIME/FRB第二星表中数千个FRB的河外色散量，扣除银河系盘和晕的模型贡献后，在北半球天空构建了剩余DM的天图，并采用刀切法重采样和样本选择检验评估统计显著性和稳健性。通过与已知大尺度结构（如大熊座和英仙-双鱼超星系团）交叉关联，评估可能的物理联系。

Result: A $\gtrsim 4\sigma$ DM excess of $\sim$150 pc cm$^{-3}$ is detected over $\sim$30$^\circ$ scales centered at $\alpha \approx 12^\mathrm{h}, \delta \approx 55^\circ$ (Wall 1), robust against systematics. A secondary $\sim3\sigma$ feature (Wall 2) is found near $\alpha \approx 2^\mathrm{h}, \delta \approx 45^\circ$. Both features align spatially with major nearby superclusters. However, Monte Carlo simulations suggest a $\sim10-20\%$ probability of such alignments occurring by chance, limiting definitive association.

在$\alpha \approx 12^\mathrm{h}, \delta \approx 55^\circ$为中心、约30$^\circ$尺度上探测到一个显著性$\gtrsim 4\sigma$、幅度约150 pc cm$^{-3}$的DM超出（Wall 1），该信号对系统误差稳健。另一个约$\sim3\sigma$的次级特征（Wall 2）出现在$\alpha \approx 2^\mathrm{h}, \delta \approx 45^\circ$附近。这两个特征在空间上与邻近的主要超星系团一致。然而，蒙特卡洛模拟显示此类对齐有约10-20%的概率为偶然发生，限制了确定性关联的建立。

Conclusion: The detection of significant large-scale DM excesses—Wall 1 and Wall 2—suggests the presence of previously unresolved baryon overdensities in the local large-scale structure. While definitive identification is limited by current statistics, this work demonstrates the feasibility of using FRB DMs as probes of the cosmic web in the near universe. Future larger FRB catalogs will improve sensitivity and enable high-significance mapping of baryons in filaments and superclusters.

显著的大尺度DM超出信号（Wall 1 和 Wall 2）的探测暗示了本地大尺度结构中存在先前未解析的重子过剩。尽管当前统计显著性尚不足以完全确认，这项工作展示了利用FRB的DM作为近邻宇宙网状结构探针的可行性。未来更大的FRB星表将提高灵敏度，实现对纤维状结构和超星系团中重子的高显著性绘图。

Abstract: The dispersion measures (DMs) of fast radio bursts (FRBs) encode the total ionized-gas column densities along their sightlines. Most observed FRBs originate at distances where the cosmological principle applies. Thus, variations in the DM distribution of FRBs observed in different regions on the sky trace local sources of anisotropy, such as the warm ionized medium and circum-galactic medium of the Milky Way, and local large-scale structure. We present a map of extragalactic DM variations across the Northern sky using a few thousand FRBs from the second \chime{} catalog. We detect a $\gtrsim 4σ$ excess of $\sim$150 pc cm$^{-3}$ above the global mean, extended over $\sim$30$^\circ$ scales and centered near $α\approx$ $12^{\rm h}$, $δ\approx$ $55^\circ$. This excess, termed Wall 1, is robust to variations in sample selection and jackknife resampling, and cannot be explained by Galactic-disk DM-model uncertainties. The excess is likely too large to correspond to anisotropy in the Milky Way halo. The signal spatially coincides with the Ursa Major supercluster and associated large-scale structures. A secondary, more tentative Wall 2 near $α\approx 2^{\rm h}$, $δ\approx$ $45^\circ$ is spatially coincident with the Perseus-Pisces supercluster. Although the spatial coincidences suggest that the Walls may correspond to baryons in the local large-scale structure, the probability of chance coincidence is likely too high ($\sim10-20\%$) to claim confident associations. These results highlight the potential of using FRB DMs to detect baryon overdensities associated with local large-scale structure, and have important implications for near-field baryon mapping and FRB cosmology.

</details>


### [69] [A generic $ω_b$ tension in early-time solutions to the Hubble tension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05095)
*Cara Giovanetti*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Early-time solutions to the Hubble tension generically increase the preferred baryon density $\omega_b$, leading to tension with Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) constraints from primordial deuterium abundance. Including a deuterium likelihood disfavors high $H_0$ in two representative models and results in worse overall fits than $\Lambda$CDM.

早期解决哈勃张力的模型通常会提高重子密度$\omega_b$，这与大爆炸核合成（BBN）对原初氘丰度的观测产生张力。引入氘似然项后，两个代表性模型无法恢复高$H_0$值，且对CMB、BAO、超新星和BBN数据的整体拟合劣于$\Lambda$CDM。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Hubble tension—the discrepancy between early- and late-universe measurements of $H_0$—has motivated various early-time (pre-recombination) modifications to $\Lambda$CDM. However, such models often alter the sound horizon and thus affect other cosmological parameters, notably $\omega_b$. The aim is to test whether these models remain consistent with independent BBN constraints on $\omega_b$ from primordial deuterium.

哈勃张力——即早期与晚期宇宙测量的$H_0$之间的差异——促使人们提出多种早时期（再复合前）对$\Lambda$CDM的修改。然而，这些模型常改变声学视界，从而影响其他宇宙学参数，特别是$\omega_b$。本文旨在检验这些模型是否仍与基于原初氘丰度的大爆炸核合成（BBN）对$\omega_b$的独立限制一致。

Method: The author analyzes how early-time physics affects the inferred value of $\omega_b$ in cosmological fits. Using CMB (Planck), BAO, supernova, and BBN data, including a likelihood for primordial deuterium abundance, the paper compares the goodness of fit for two representative early-time models (e.g., early dark energy or modified gravitational physics) against $\Lambda$CDM. The consistency between CMB-inferred $\omega_b$ and BBN-determined $\omega_b$ is tested.

作者分析了早时期物理如何影响宇宙学拟合中推断的$\omega_b$值。利用CMB（Planck）、BAO、超新星和BBN数据，并包含原初氘丰度的似然项，本文比较了两种代表性早时期模型（如早时期暗能量或修正引力）与$\Lambda$CDM的拟合优度。检验了CMB推断的$\omega_b$与BBN确定的$\omega_b$之间的一致性。

Result: Early-time models that attempt to resolve the Hubble tension predict a higher best-fit $\omega_b$ than $\Lambda$CDM. This increased $\omega_b$ is in $\sim3\sigma$ tension with BBN determinations from primordial deuterium. When a deuterium likelihood is included, the models fail to recover a high $H_0$, and their overall $\chi^2$ worsens relative to $\Lambda$CDM, indicating poorer agreement with combined data sets.

试图解决哈勃张力的早时期模型预测的$\omega_b$高于$\Lambda$CDM。这一增大的$\omega_b$与基于原初氘的大爆炸核合成（BBN）结果存在约$3\sigma$的张力。当引入氘似然项后，这些模型无法恢复高$H_0$值，且其整体$\chi^2$相对于$\Lambda$CDM更差，表明与综合数据集的一致性更差。

Conclusion: Early-time solutions to the Hubble tension are strongly constrained by BBN via precise deuterium measurements. The requirement that $\omega_b$ be consistent across CMB and BBN poses a significant challenge to such models. Models that raise $\omega_b$ to lower the sound horizon are disfavored, suggesting that viable resolutions to the Hubble tension must avoid altering $\omega_b$ beyond BBN limits.

早时期解决哈勃张力的方案受到大爆炸核合成（BBN）中精确氘测量的强烈限制。要求$\omega_b$在CMB与BBN之间保持一致，这对这些模型构成了重大挑战。那些通过提高$\omega_b$来降低声学视界的模型被排除，表明对哈勃张力的有效解决方案必须避免使$\omega_b$超出BBN允许范围。

Abstract: I show that early-time (pre-recombination) solutions to the Hubble tension are generically expected to increase the preferred baryon density $ω_b$. This puts these models in tension with Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN), as measurements of primordial deuterium constrain $ω_b$ at percent level. I show that existing analyses are in tension with the BBN determination of $ω_b$, and that including a likelihood component for primordial deuterium deters two representative models from recovering a high $H_0$, and leads to worse fits to CMB, BAO, supernova, and BBN data than $Λ$CDM.

### [70] [Local primordial non-Gaussianity using cross-correlations of DESI tracers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05213)
*A. J. Rosado-Marín,A. J. Ross,H. Seo,E. Chaussidon,J. Aguilar,S. Ahlen,D. Bianchi,D. Brooks,T. Claybaugh,A. Cuceu,A. de la Macorra,A. de Mattia,R. Demina,B. Dey,P. Doel,S. Ferraro,A. Font-Ribera,J. E. Forero-Romero,E. Gaztañaga,S. Gontcho A Gontcho,G. Gutierrez,C. Hahn,H. K. Herrera-Alcantar,D. Huterer,M. Ishak,R. Joyce,D. Kirkby,A. Kremin,O. Lahav,C. Lamman,M. Landriau,M. E. Levi,M. Manera,A. Meisner,R. Miquel,S. Nadathur,J. A. Newman,N. Palanque-Delabrouille,W. J. Percival,F. Prada,I. Pérez-Ràfols,G. Rossi,E. Sanchez,D. Schlegel,J. Silber,G. Tarlé,B. A. Weaver,C. Zhao,H. Zou*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We constrain local primordial non-Gaussianity ($f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$) using auto- and cross-correlations of DESI DR1 tracers, including LRGs, QSOs, and ELGs over $0.8<z<3.1$. Cross-correlating LRGs and QSOs improves constraints by ~9%, yielding $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}=2.1_{-8.3}^{+8.8}$ (68% CL), while ELG inclusion does not enhance sensitivity, consistent with mock predictions. This work demonstrates the robustness of cross-correlations in mitigating systematics and explores ELG clustering for future analyses.

我们利用DESI DR1的LRG、QSO和ELG示踪物在$0.8<z<3.1$范围内的自相关和互相关联合分析，对局域原初非高斯性（$f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$）进行限制。LRG与QSO的互相关使约束精度提高了约9%，得到$f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}=2.1_{-8.3}^{+8.8}$（68%置信水平），而加入ELG样本未带来明显改进，与模拟预测一致。本研究展示了互相关在抑制系统误差方面的稳健性，并为未来DESI数据分析中ELG示踪物的应用进行了探索性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Primordial non-Gaussianity is a key probe of inflationary physics beyond simple single-field slow-roll models. The parameter $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$ quantifies deviations from Gaussian initial conditions, with current constraints primarily from CMB and large-scale structure surveys. However, galaxy clustering measurements can suffer from observational systematics and tracer-specific biases. By employing cross-correlations among multiple tracers within the same volume, we aim to reduce the impact of non-common systematics and obtain more robust constraints on $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$, particularly leveraging the wide redshift coverage and high number density of DESI DR1 tracers.

原初非高斯性是检验暴胀模型（超越简单的单场慢滚框架）的重要探针。参数$f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$量化了初始条件偏离高斯性的程度，当前限制主要来自CMB和大尺度结构巡天。然而，星系成团性测量可能受到观测系统误差和示踪物特有偏差的影响。通过在同一观测体积内使用多种示踪物的互相关，我们旨在降低非共同系统误差的影响，从而获得更稳健的$f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$限制，特别是利用DESI DR1示踪物的大红移覆盖范围和高源密度优势。

Method: We perform a combined analysis of auto- and cross-power spectra of Luminous Red Galaxies (LRGs), Emission Line Galaxies (ELGs), and Quasi-Stellar Objects (QSOs) from DESI DR1 across $0.8<z<3.1$. We model the power spectra using linear biasing and scale-dependent bias induced by $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$, fitting for $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$ alongside cosmological and nuisance parameters. Cross-correlations are used to suppress tracer-specific systematics, as they are less affected by non-overlapping systematic errors. We validate our results using mock catalogs that simulate the survey geometry, selection functions, and clustering statistics.

我们对DESI DR1中$0.8<z<3.1$范围内的明亮红星系（LRG）、发射线星系（ELG）和类星体（QSO）的自功率谱和互功率谱进行了联合分析。采用线性偏置模型以及由$f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$引起的尺度依赖偏置对功率谱建模，同时拟合$f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$、宇宙学参数和干扰参数。利用互相关抑制示踪物特有的系统误差，因为其受非共有的系统误差影响较小。我们使用模拟目录验证结果，这些目录模拟了巡天几何、选择函数和成团统计特性。

Result: The cross-correlation between LRGs and QSOs improves the constraint on $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$ by approximately 9%, resulting in $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL} = 2.1_{-8.3}^{+8.8}$ at 68% confidence level. In contrast, including ELGs in the analysis does not lead to a significant improvement in precision, which is consistent with predictions from mock tests showing only an expected ~8% statistical gain with large scatter. Systematic checks confirm the robustness of the LRG-QSO cross-correlation signal.

LRG与QSO的互相关使$f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$的限制提高了约9%，最终结果为$f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL} = 2.1_{-8.3}^{+8.8}$（68%置信水平）。相比之下，在分析中引入ELG并未显著提升精度，这与模拟预测一致——模拟显示统计增益仅约8%，且存在较大散射。系统性检验确认了LRG-QSO互相关信号的稳健性。

Conclusion: Cross-correlations of distinct tracers in the same volume provide a powerful way to mitigate systematics and improve constraints on $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$. The LRG-QSO cross-correlation in DESI DR1 yields a tighter constraint, demonstrating its utility. The lack of improvement from ELGs is statistically expected and highlights the importance of realistic mocks in forecasting. This analysis lays the groundwork for future, more sensitive searches for primordial non-Gaussianity with full DESI data.

在同一观测体积内对不同示踪物进行互相关分析是抑制系统误差并改善$f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$限制的有效方法。DESI DR1中LRG与QSO的互相关给出了更严格的限制，展示了其有效性。ELG未能带来改进在统计上是可预期的，突显了使用真实模拟进行预测的重要性。该分析为未来利用完整DESI数据开展更高灵敏度的原初非高斯性搜寻奠定了基础。

Abstract: We constrain local primordial non-Gaussianity by a combined analysis of auto and cross-correlations of DESI DR1 tracers, leveraging LRGs and QSOs as well as ELGs between $0.8<z<3.1$. By cross-validating the signal across different clustering tracers within the same redshift range, we evaluate potential systematics in the $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$ measurements, capitalizing on the reduced susceptibility of cross-correlations to non-common systematics. We find that the cross-correlation between LRG and quasars can robustly improve the DESI DR1 $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$ constraints, by $\sim9\%$ to a measurement of $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}=2.1_{-8.3}^{+8.8}$ at 68\% confidence. On the other hand, we do not find a clear improvement when including the DESI DR1 ELG sample. Mock tests predict an additional $\sim8\%$ gain with statistical scatter, and the lack of improvement in the data remains consistent with this expectation. This project serves as an exploratory analysis of DESI ELG clustering for $f^\mathrm{loc}_\mathrm{NL}$ through its cross-correlation in preparation for future DESI data analyses.

</details>


### [71] [JWST Lensed Quasar Dark Matter Survey V: Measuring the minimum halo mass with strong gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05237)
*A. M. Nierenberg,D. Gilman,T. Treu,X. Du,C. Gannon,H. Paugnat,S. Birrer,A. J. Benson,K. N. Abazajian,T. Anguita,S. G. Djorgovski,S. F. Hoenig,R. E. Keeley,A. Kusenko,H. R. Larsson,L. A. Moustakas,P. Mozumdar,W. Sheu,D. Sluse,D. Stern,D. Williams,K. C. Wong*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We use 28 strong gravitational lenses to place upper limits on the low-mass cutoff of the cold dark matter (CDM) halo mass function, finding $m_{\rm{low}}<10^{8.3}\,M_\odot$ at 10:1 odds using a semi-analytic prior and $m_{\rm{low}}<10^{8.2}\,M_\odot$ with an $N$-body prior. Our model accounts for tidal stripping effects, allowing subhalos below the cutoff to contribute. These constraints are competitive with Milky Way satellite-based limits, and we forecast over an order-of-magnitude improvement with 200 quadruply imaged quasars—achievable with upcoming surveys like Rubin, Euclid, and Roman—which will also enable direct measurement of the subhalo mass function normalization.

我们利用28个强引力透镜对冷暗物质（CDM）晕质量函数的低质量截断施加了上限，使用半解析模型先验时得到在10:1赔率下$m_{\rm{low}}<10^{8.3}\,M_\odot$，使用$N$-体模拟先验时为$m_{\rm{low}}<10^{8.2}\,M_\odot$。我们的模型考虑了潮汐剥离效应，允许低于截断质量的子晕仍有所贡献。这些限制与基于银河系卫星星系的现有约束相当甚至更强。我们预测，利用200个四像类星体透镜样本——这一数量仅为Rubin、Euclid和Roman望远镜预计发现数千个中的一小部分——可将限制提升一个数量级以上，并直接测定子晕质量函数的归一化，从而消除当前测量中的主要不确定性来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The nature of dark matter on small scales remains poorly constrained, particularly the minimum mass of dark matter halos in CDM models. While CDM predicts a steeply rising halo mass function toward low masses, astrophysical uncertainties (e.g., baryonic feedback, galaxy formation efficiency) limit the ability of galaxy surveys to probe this regime. Strong gravitational lensing offers a unique, baryon-independent probe of low-mass halos at cosmological distances, both as subhalos in lens galaxies and as line-of-sight halos, enabling direct tests of the CDM halo mass function down to very low masses.

小尺度上暗物质的本质仍缺乏良好约束，尤其是在CDM模型中暗物质晕的最小质量方面。虽然CDM预言晕质量函数在低质量端急剧上升，但天体物理不确定性（如重子反馈、星系形成效率）限制了星系巡天对此区域的探测能力。强引力透镜提供了一种独特的、不依赖重子的探针，可用于探测位于宿主星系中的子晕以及视线方向上的晕，从而在宇宙学距离上直接检验极低质量范围内的CDM晕质量函数。

Method: We analyze 28 strong gravitational lens systems, focusing on perturbations caused by low-mass dark matter halos (subhalos and line-of-sight halos). We adopt an extreme CDM model with a sharp low-mass cutoff $m_{\rm{low}}$ in the halo mass function and a standard mass-concentration relation. The model includes the effects of tidal stripping, which allows subhalos originally below $m_{\rm{low}}$ to survive as lower-mass remnants that still contribute to lensing. We use Bayesian inference to constrain $m_{\rm{low}}$, employing two different priors for the normalization of the subhalo mass function: one from the semi-analytic model {\tt galacticus} and another from high-resolution $N$-body simulations. Lensing observables include flux ratio anomalies and image position perturbations.

我们分析了28个强引力透镜系统，重点关注由低质量暗物质晕（子晕和视线方向晕）引起的扰动。我们采用一种极端的CDM模型，在晕质量函数中引入一个尖锐的低质量截断$m_{\rm{low}}$，并使用标准的质量-浓度关系。该模型包含了潮汐剥离效应，使得原本低于$m_{\rm{low}}$的子晕可以以更低质量残余物的形式存活下来并继续产生透镜效应。我们采用贝叶斯推断来限制$m_{\rm{low}}$，并对子晕质量函数的归一化使用两种不同的先验：一种来自半解析模型{\tt galacticus}，另一种来自高分辨率$N$-体模拟。透镜观测量包括流量比异常和像位置扰动。

Result: We derive upper limits on the low-mass cutoff of the halo mass function: $m_{\rm{low}} < 10^{8.3}\,M_\odot$ at 10:1 odds using the {\tt galacticus} prior and $m_{\rm{low}} < 10^{8.2}\,M_\odot$ using the $N$-body simulation prior. These limits are among the strongest to date and are comparable to or tighter than constraints from Milky Way satellite counts. The inclusion of tidal stripping ensures that even halos below the nominal cutoff can contribute to lensing, making our bounds robust. We forecast that a sample of 200 quadruply imaged quasars will improve sensitivity by more than an order of magnitude, enabling detection or exclusion of CDM predictions down to $\sim 10^6\,M_\odot$. Such a sample will also allow direct inference of the subhalo mass function normalization, reducing current systematic uncertainties.

我们得到了晕质量函数低质量截断的上限：使用{\tt galacticus}先验时在10:1赔率下$m_{\rm{low}} < 10^{8.3}\,M_\odot$，使用$N$-体模拟先验时为$m_{\rm{low}} < 10^{8.2}\,M_\odot$。这些限制是迄今为止最强的之一，与或优于基于银河系卫星星系数目的约束。由于考虑了潮汐剥离效应，即使名义截断以下的晕也能贡献透镜信号，使我们的界限更加稳健。我们预测，200个四像类星体样本将使灵敏度提升超过一个数量级，能够探测或排除CDM在$\sim 10^6\,M_\odot$量级的预言。这样的样本还将允许直接推断子晕质量函数的归一化，显著降低当前的系统性不确定性。

Conclusion: Strong gravitational lensing provides a powerful, baryon-independent method to probe the low-mass end of the CDM halo mass function. Current data already place tight constraints on a possible low-mass cutoff, rivaling those from local group satellite studies. With upcoming large samples of lenses from Rubin, Euclid, and Roman, we will achieve transformative improvements in sensitivity, potentially reaching the characteristic mass scales predicted by WIMP and axion CDM models. Moreover, these future datasets will allow us to directly measure the subhalo mass function normalization, reducing reliance on theoretical priors and enabling more robust tests of structure formation in the early universe.

强引力透镜为探测CDM晕质量函数的低质量端提供了一种强大且不依赖重子的方法。当前数据已对可能存在的低质量截断施加了严格的限制，堪比本地星系群卫星星系研究的结果。随着Rubin、Euclid和Roman等项目即将提供的大量透镜样本，我们将实现灵敏度的变革性提升，有望达到WIMP和轴子CDM模型所预言的特征质量尺度。此外，未来的数据集将使我们能够直接测量子晕质量函数的归一化，减少对理论先验的依赖，从而实现对早期宇宙结构形成的更稳健检验。

Abstract: We explore the lowest mass limit that can be placed on the halo mass function in CDM using 28 strong gravitational lenses. For this purpose, we study an extreme model in which the halo mass function and mass-concentration relation follow CDM, with a sharp cutoff at some mass scale, $m_{\rm{low}}$. Lensing provides a unique window into this quantity as it does not depend on the presence of baryons in dark matter halos and also allows the detection of low mass halos at cosmological distances, both in the lens galaxies and along the line-of-sight. Our model incorporates the effects of tidal stripping of subhalos, leading to the presence of many subhalos below a given model cutoff scale. We place an upper limit on the low-mass cutoff of the halo mass function of $m_{\rm{low}}<10^{8.3}$ M$_\odot$ at 10:1 odds using a prior for the normalization of the subhalo mass function from the semi-analytic model {\tt galacticus} and $m_{\rm{low}}<10^{8.2}$ M$_\odot$ at 10:1 odds using a prior from $N$-body simulations. These limits are comparable to, or stronger than, existing constraints based on Milky Way satellite galaxies. Based on these results, we forecast more than an order of magnitude improvement with a sample of 200 quadruply imaged quasar lenses. This number represents a small subset of the thousands that are anticipated to be discovered by Rubin, Euclid, and Roman. Furthermore, with this larger sample of lenses we expect to directly constrain the normalization of the subhalo mass function, thereby eliminating a major source of uncertainty in our current measurements.

</details>


### [72] [Constraints on the Injection of Radiation in the Early Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05282)
*Melissa Joseph,Jason Kumar,Pearl Sandick*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We study the injection of both dark and electromagnetic radiation between BBN and recombination. Although their contributions to $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ can cancel due to opposite signs, electromagnetic radiation dilutes the baryon-to-entropy ratio, leading to tight cosmological constraints. Numerical analysis shows that the allowed extra radiation is only ~25% higher than in models assuming purely dark radiation.

我们研究了在大爆炸核合成（BBN）和复合时期之间注入暗辐射和电磁辐射的情形。尽管它们对$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$的贡献因符号相反可能相互抵消，但电磁辐射会稀释重子-熵比，该比值在BBN和复合时期均被测量。数值分析表明，允许的额外辐射仅比纯暗辐射模型高约25%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The number of effective neutrino species ($N_{\rm eff}$) is a key probe of relativistic energy density in the early universe. However, if radiation is injected during the intermediate epoch (between BBN and recombination), its nature—whether dark or electromagnetic—affects observables differently. While dark radiation increases $N_{\rm eff}$, electromagnetic radiation can decrease it due to entropy production, but also alters the baryon-to-entropy ratio ($\eta$), which is tightly constrained by both BBN and CMB. This interplay motivates a careful reassessment of limits on exotic energy injection.

有效中微子种类数（$N_{\rm eff}$）是早期宇宙相对论性能量密度的关键探针。然而，若辐射在BBN与复合之间的时期被注入，其性质（暗或电磁）对观测量的影响不同。暗辐射增加$N_{\rm eff}$，而电磁辐射因熵产生可降低$N_{\rm eff}$，同时改变重子-熵比（$\eta$），而$\eta$受BBN和CMB严格限制。这种相互作用促使我们重新评估对外来能量注入的限制。

Method: We model the injection of generic radiation components—both dark radiation (which contributes positively to $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$) and electromagnetic radiation (which injects entropy and thus negatively contributes to $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$). We track the evolution of thermodynamic quantities such as entropy, baryon density, and expansion rate. By imposing observational constraints from light element abundances (D/H, $^4$He) at BBN and the CMB-inferred baryon-to-photon ratio at recombination, we compute the allowed parameter space for total injected energy using numerical integration of the relevant cosmological equations.

我们建模了通用辐射成分的注入——包括暗辐射（对$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$正贡献）和电磁辐射（通过熵注入对$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$负贡献）。追踪熵、重子密度和膨胀率等热力学量的演化。通过施加来自BBN时期的轻元素丰度（D/H, $^4$He）以及CMB推断的复合时期重子-光子比的观测约束，利用相关宇宙学方程的数值积分计算总注入能量的允许参数空间。

Result: We find that even if $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ is nearly zero due to cancellation between dark and electromagnetic radiation components, the dilution of the baryon-to-entropy ratio $\eta$ by electromagnetic injection leads to strong constraints. Specifically, the total allowed injected radiation energy is only about 25% higher than the case where all extra radiation is assumed to be dark. This implies that electromagnetic energy injection is highly restricted, even when its signal in $N_{\rm eff}$ is hidden by compensation effects.

我们发现，即使由于暗辐射与电磁辐射的抵消导致$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$接近零，电磁辐射注入对重子-熵比$\eta$的稀释仍导致强约束。具体而言，允许的总注入辐射能量仅比所有额外辐射均为暗辐射的情况高约25%。这意味着即使其在$N_{\rm eff}$中的信号被补偿效应掩盖，电磁能量注入仍受到高度限制。

Conclusion: The baryon-to-entropy ratio provides a powerful and independent constraint on energy injection between BBN and recombination. Even when dark and electromagnetic radiation contributions to $N_{\rm eff}$ cancel, the impact on $\eta$ breaks degeneracy and limits the total allowed injection. Therefore, assumptions of purely dark radiation overestimate the allowed energy budget; realistic scenarios must account for entropy-diluting effects of electromagnetic components.

重子-熵比为BBN与复合之间能量注入提供了强大且独立的约束。即使暗辐射与电磁辐射对$N_{\rm eff}$的贡献相抵消，其对$\eta$的影响仍打破简并性并限制总允许注入。因此，假设纯暗辐射会高估允许的能量预算；真实情景必须考虑电磁成分的熵稀释效应。

Abstract: We consider the generic injection of radiation (both dark and electromagnetic) during the epoch between big bang nucleosynthesis (BBN) and recombination. The contribution of the additional radiation to the number of effective neutrinos may be quite small in this scenario, since dark radiation and electromagnetic radiation provide contributions of opposite sign. However, the injection of electromagnetic radiation dilutes the baryon-to-entropy ratio, which is measured both at BBN and at recombination. As a result, this scenario is expected to be tightly constrained. Indeed, performing a numerical study, we find that the allowed amount of extra radiation may be no more than $\sim 25\%$ greater than in the case where it is assumed to be entirely dark radiation.

</details>


### [73] [Explaining Neural Networks on the Sky: Machine Learning Interpretability for Cosmic Microwave Background Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05290)
*Indira Ocampo,Guadalupe Cañas-Herrera*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We propose a neural network framework for cosmological model selection using simulated CMB temperature and polarization maps, preserving full spatial information to detect deviations from $\Lambda$CDM. A hybrid PCA-NN architecture is trained for classification, with SHAP used for interpretability to identify sky regions and scales most informative for distinguishing models. This serves as a proof-of-concept for interpretable machine learning in CMB analysis, complementing traditional power-spectrum-based approaches. The full pipeline is released as an Open Science project.

我们提出了一种基于模拟CMB温度和偏振图的神经网络框架，用于宇宙学模型选择，保留完整的空间信息以检测$\Lambda$CDM模型之外的偏差。该框架采用结合主成分分析与神经网络（PCA-NN）的混合架构进行分类，并使用SHAP实现可解释性，识别对模型区分最具贡献的天空区域和尺度。这是可解释机器学习应用于CMB分析的概念验证，补充了传统的基于功率谱的方法。完整流程作为开放科学项目公开发布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional cosmological analyses rely on compressed summary statistics like angular power spectra ($C_\ell$), which may lose higher-order spatial information sensitive to primordial features beyond $\Lambda$CDM. To improve model discrimination—especially for subtle inflationary signatures—we aim to exploit the full information content of CMB maps by applying machine learning directly at the map level.

传统的宇宙学分析依赖于压缩的统计量（如角功率谱$C_\ell$），可能丢失对超出$\Lambda$CDM的原初特征敏感的高阶空间信息。为了提高模型区分能力——特别是对于微弱的暴胀信号——我们旨在通过直接在CMB图上应用机器学习来利用其全部信息内容。

Method: We generate Planck-like simulated CMB temperature and polarization maps for $\Lambda$CDM and feature-inclusive models. A hybrid architecture combining principal component analysis (PCA) for dimensionality reduction and neural networks (NNs) for classification is trained end-to-end on these maps. Classification decisions are interpreted post-hoc using Shapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP), which attributes predictive importance to specific pixels and spatial frequencies. The framework is implemented as an open-source pipeline for simulation, training, and interpretability.

我们为$\Lambda$CDM及包含特征的模型生成类普朗克卫星的模拟CMB温度和偏振图。采用一种混合架构，结合主成分分析（PCA）进行降维和神经网络（NN）进行分类，并在这些图上进行端到端训练。使用Shapley Additive exPlanations（SHAP）对分类决策进行事后解释，将预测重要性归因于特定像素和空间频率。该框架作为开源流程实现，涵盖模拟、训练和可解释性。

Result: The PCA-NN hybrid model achieves high accuracy and well-calibrated probabilities in distinguishing $\Lambda$CDM from feature models, outperforming standard $C_\ell$-based classifiers. SHAP analysis reveals localized sky regions and intermediate angular scales ($\ell \sim 100-500$) as most discriminative, suggesting that non-Gaussian spatial patterns contribute significantly to model separation. Interpretability results confirm that the network learns physically meaningful features rather than artifacts.

PCA-NN混合模型在区分$\Lambda$CDM与特征模型方面表现出高准确率和良好校准的概率，优于基于标准$C_\ell$的分类器。SHAP分析揭示出局部天区和中等角尺度（$\ell \sim 100-500$）最具区分性，表明非高斯空间模式对模型分离有显著贡献。可解释性结果证实网络学习的是物理上有意义的特征而非人工伪影。

Conclusion: Direct analysis of CMB maps using interpretable neural networks enables enhanced cosmological model discrimination by accessing higher-order spatial information lost in power spectrum compression. The successful application of SHAP provides insight into the physical origins of classifier decisions, increasing trust in ML-assisted cosmology. This approach paves the way for future detection of subtle primordial features in real data, and the open release of our pipeline promotes reproducibility and collaboration via the Open Science initiative.

使用可解释神经网络直接分析CMB图，能够通过获取功率谱压缩中丢失的高阶空间信息来增强宇宙学模型区分能力。SHAP的成功应用揭示了分类器决策的物理起源，提升了人们对机器学习辅助宇宙学的信任。该方法为未来在真实数据中探测微弱的原初特征铺平道路，而流程的公开发布通过开放科学倡议促进了可重复性和合作。

Abstract: We present a framework for cosmological model selection using Neural Networks (NNs) trained directly on simulated Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) temperature and polarisation maps. By operating at the map level rather than on compressed angular power spectra, our approach retains the full spatial information of temperature and polarisation anisotropies, enabling the identification of subtle signatures of primordial features beyond the standard $Λ$CDM model. We describe the generation of Planck-like CMB maps, and the hybrid architecture that combines principal component analysis and neural networks, optimised for classification tasks. To understand how the classifier reaches its decisions, we apply Shapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP) as a post-hoc interpretability tool, identifying which regions of the sky and which scales contribute most to the distinction between $Λ$CDM and feature models. This work serves as a follow-up to previous analyses at the level of summary statistics and as a proof-of-concept for using interpretable machine learning to uncover higher-order information in CMB data, with the potential to enhance the detection of nontrivial inflationary signals and improve cosmological model discrimination. Results for model classification performance, calibration, and interpretability are presented as a placeholder for the full analysis. In addition, we introduce the Open Science project, providing public access to the full pipeline for simulation, training, and interpretability of CMB map-based neural networks.

### [74] [Reconstructing a large-scale matter-density contrast profile to reconcile Pantheon+ supernovae with DESI DR2 BAO in an inhomogeneous universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05466)
*Toshifumi Futamase,Reiki Kojima,Masanori Tomonaga*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The DESI DR2 BAO data reveal a discrepancy in the Hubble parameter compared to the standard $\Lambda$CDM model, potentially due to large-scale inhomogeneities such as the KBC void. A simple inhomogeneous model with eight top-hat shells is shown to reconcile local and CMB-inferred Hubble parameters from Pantheon+ and DESI DR2 data.

DESI DR2 BAO 数据显示哈勃参数与标准 $\Lambda$CDM 模型存在差异，这可能源于大尺度物质分布的不均匀性，例如 KBC 空洞。一个包含八个阶梯状壳层的简单非均匀宇宙学模型被证明能够协调来自 Pantheon+ 和 DESI DR2 数据推断出的局部和CMB哈勃参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Tensions between early- and late-universe measurements of the Hubble constant ($H_0$), known as the Hubble tension, persist despite increasingly precise data. The DESI DR2 BAO results further highlight deviations in the measured $H(z)$ at intermediate redshifts. These anomalies may not stem solely from systematic errors or new physics within homogeneous cosmology, but could reflect violations of the cosmological principle—specifically, large-scale matter inhomogeneities. Evidence from infrared surveys indicating that we reside in a $\sim300$ Mpc underdense region (the KBC void) motivates modeling deviations in $H_0$ via real-space inhomogeneous metrics rather than assuming perfect homogeneity.

早期与晚期宇宙对哈勃常数 ($H_0$) 的测量之间存在的张力（即哈勃张力）在日益精确的数据下仍然存在。DESI DR2 BAO 结果进一步凸显了在中等红移处测得的 $H(z)$ 的偏差。这些异常可能不仅源于系统误差或均匀宇宙学中的新物理，而可能是宇宙学原理被破坏的表现——具体而言，是大尺度物质分布的不均匀性所致。来自红外巡天的证据表明我们位于一个约 300 百万秒差距的低密度区域（KBC 空洞），这促使人们通过实空间的非均匀度规而非假设完美均匀性来建模 $H_0$ 的偏差。

Method: We employ a linear-order relation connecting the horizon-scale Hubble parameter (from CMB) and the local-scale Hubble parameter (from low-redshift probes), derived under perturbative inhomogeneous cosmology. Using this relation, we construct an inhomogeneous model composed of eight concentric top-hat shells, each characterized by a distinct matter density contrast $\delta_i = \delta\rho_i/\bar{\rho}$. The model parameters are constrained by fitting to the Pantheon+ Type Ia supernova apparent magnitudes and the DESI DR2 BAO angular and radial baryon acoustic scale measurements. We assume spherical symmetry and use linear perturbation theory to compute corrections to the luminosity distance and Hubble parameter in the presence of large-scale voids.

我们采用一种线性阶关系，将来自CMB的视界尺度哈勃参数与来自低红移探针的局部尺度哈勃参数联系起来，该关系源自微扰非均匀宇宙学。基于此关系，构建了一个由八个同心阶梯状壳层组成的非均匀模型，每个壳层具有不同的物质密度对比 $\delta_i = \delta\rho_i/\bar{\rho}$。通过拟合 Pantheon+ Ia 型超新星的表观星等以及 DESI DR2 BAO 的角和径向重子声学振荡尺度测量值来约束模型参数。假设球对称性，并使用线性微扰理论计算大尺度空洞存在时对光度距离和哈勃参数的修正。

Result: The eight-shell inhomogeneous model provides a consistent fit to both the Pantheon+ supernova data and DESI DR2 BAO observations, yielding a local $H_0$ value higher than the CMB-inferred $H_{\rm fid}$, in agreement with low-redshift measurements. The best-fit model features a large underdense region extending to $\sim300$ Mpc, consistent with the KBC void. We find that the linear correction framework successfully maps the global $H_{\rm fid}$ to the locally enhanced $H_0$, reducing the tension without invoking new physics. Additionally, we discuss potential imprints of such a density profile on observables: modifications to the magnitude--redshift relation, suppressed kinematic Sunyaev--Zel'dovich (kSZ) signal due to reduced peculiar velocities, and a non-trivial integrated Sachs--Wolfe (ISW) effect arising from time-varying potentials in voids.

八壳层非均匀模型一致地拟合了 Pantheon+ 超新星数据和 DESI DR2 BAO 观测结果，得到的局部 $H_0$ 值高于来自CMB推断的 $H_{\rm fid}$，与低红移测量一致。最佳拟合模型包含一个延伸至约 300 百万秒差距的大尺度低密度区域，与 KBC 空洞相符。我们发现，线性修正框架成功地将全局 $H_{\rm fid}$ 映射到局部增强的 $H_0$，无需引入新物理即可缓解张力。此外，我们讨论了此类密度轮廓对可观测量的潜在影响：对星等-红移关系的修正、由于特殊速度降低导致的动力学Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (kSZ) 信号抑制，以及空洞中随时间变化的势能引起的非平凡积分Sachs-Wolfe (ISW) 效应。

Conclusion: Large-scale inhomogeneities, particularly a local void like the KBC structure, offer a viable geometric explanation for the observed discrepancies in $H(z)$ measurements, including the Hubble tension and DESI DR2 anomalies. The success of a simple eight-shell top-hat model supports the idea that violations of strict homogeneity on $\gtrsim 100$ Mpc scales may significantly bias inferred cosmological parameters. Future high-precision LSS and CMB datasets should incorporate inhomogeneous modeling to avoid misinterpretation of expansion rate measurements.

大尺度不均匀性，特别是像 KBC 结构这样的局部空洞，为观测到的 $H(z)$ 测量差异（包括哈勃张力和 DESI DR2 异常）提供了一种可行的几何解释。一个简单的八壳层阶梯模型的成功支持了如下观点：在 $\gtrsim 100$ 百万秒差距尺度上严格均匀性的破坏可能会显著偏倚推断出的宇宙学参数。未来的高精度大尺度结构（LSS）和CMB数据集应纳入非均匀建模，以避免对膨胀率测量的误解。

Abstract: The Hubble parameters measured by the DESI DR2 BAO observations show a significant discrepancy from the prediction of the standard cosmological model.
  This discrepancy, together with the long-discussed Hubble tension, may originate from large-scale inhomogeneities in the matter distribution.
  This interpretation is motivated by infrared galaxy surveys, which suggest that our galaxy resides within the $\sim300$ Mpc under-dense region known as the KBC void.
  In this study, we apply a linear order relation -- relating the horizon-scale Hubble parameter inferred from CMB observations and the local-scale Hubble parameter -- to the Pantheon+ Type Ia supernovae and the DESI DR2 BAO data.
  We show that a simple inhomogeneous cosmological model consisting of eight top-hat shells can consistently explain the Hubble parameters inferred from both observations.
  Based on the matter-density distribution, we also briefly discuss its possible impact on cosmological observables, including the magnitude--redshift relation, the kinematic Sunyaev--Zel'dovich effect, and the integrated Sachs--Wolfe effect.

</details>


### [75] [Model-independent constraints on generalized FLRW consistency relations with bootstrap-based symbolic regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05822)
*S. M. Koksbang,A. Heinesen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We apply a model-independent framework combining angular diameter distance $d_A(z)$ and expansion rate $\mathcal{H}(z)$ derivatives to test FLRW consistency using supernova and BAO data, employing symbolic regression with bootstrapping for non-parametric reconstruction. Reconstructed density fields are consistent with both Planck and SH0ES $\Lambda$CDM, but FLRW consistency tests show mild to moderate deviations at $\sim 2$–$4\sigma$, depending on data choices.

我们应用一个结合角直径距离 $d_A(z)$ 和视线方向膨胀率 $\mathcal{H}(z)$ 导数的模型无关框架，使用超新星和BAO数据检验FLRW一致性，并采用符号回归结合自举法进行非参数重构。重构的密度场与Planck和SH0ES的$\Lambda$CDM均一致，但FLRW一致性检验显示出在$\sim 2$–$4\sigma$水平上的轻微至中等偏差，具体显著性依赖于数据选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The $\Lambda$CDM model faces growing observational tensions (e.g., $H_0$, $S_8$), suggesting possible breakdown of fundamental assumptions like the FLRW metric. We aim to test whether the universe's spacetime geometry is truly described by FLRW without assuming any specific cosmological model, thereby probing whether proposed solutions within the FLRW framework (e.g., dark energy models) are viable.

$\Lambda$CDM模型面临日益增长的观测张力（如$H_0$、$S_8$），暗示其基本假设（如FLRW度规）可能失效。我们的目标是在不依赖特定宇宙学模型的前提下，检验宇宙时空几何是否真正符合FLRW，从而判断在FLRW框架内提出的解决方案（如暗能量模型）是否仍然可行。

Method: We use a model-independent estimator of the cosmic density field based on $d_A(z)$, $\mathcal{H}(z)$, and their derivatives, derived from FLRW consistency conditions. We employ symbolic regression (AI-driven functional form discovery) combined with bootstrapping to reconstruct these functions non-parametrically from supernova (Pantheon+) and BAO data, enabling uncertainty quantification without assuming a parametric form. This allows direct testing of FLRW relations and inference of the sky-averaged density $\bar{\rho}(z)$ over $z \in [0.38, \sim2]$.

我们基于$ d_A(z) $、$ \mathcal{H}(z) $及其导数构建了一个模型无关的宇宙密度场估计量，源自FLRW一致性条件。采用符号回归（由AI驱动的函数形式发现）结合自举法，从超新星（Pantheon+）和BAO数据中非参数地重构这些函数，实现无需假设参数形式的不确定性量化。这使得我们能够直接检验FLRW关系，并推断出在$ z \in [0.38, \sim2] $范围内的全天平均密度$\bar{\rho}(z)$。

Result: Current data allow reconstruction of $d_A(z)$ with good precision, but $\mathcal{H}(z)$ remains poorly constrained due to sparsity. The reconstructed sky-averaged density $\bar{\rho}(z)$ is consistent with both Planck and SH0ES $\Lambda$CDM predictions. However, FLRW consistency tests — comparing geometric combinations of $d_A$ and $\mathcal{H}$ — show deviations at the $\sim2$–$4\sigma$ level, depending on dataset combination and reconstruction stability. These deviations, if real, suggest a breakdown of the FLRW assumption.

当前数据能较好地重构$d_A(z)$，但由于数据稀疏，$\mathcal{H}(z)$的约束仍较差。重构的全天平均密度$\bar{\rho}(z)$与Planck和SH0ES的$\Lambda$CDM预测均一致。然而，FLRW一致性检验——通过比较$d_A$和$\mathcal{H}$的几何组合——显示出在$\sim2$–$4\sigma$水平的偏差，具体显著性依赖于数据集组合和重构稳定性。若这些偏差属实，则表明FLRW假设可能失效。

Conclusion: While current data do not definitively rule out the FLRW geometry, they allow for mild to moderate deviations at $\sim2$–$4\sigma$. If confirmed with future denser data (e.g., from LSST, DESI, Euclid), such deviations would invalidate most $\Lambda$CDM extensions that assume FLRW (e.g., evolving dark energy, modified gravity). This underscores the need for improved, standardized non-parametric reconstruction methods — particularly for symbolic regression uncertainty quantification — and highlights the importance of upcoming high-precision, high-density cosmological surveys.

尽管当前数据尚不能明确排除FLRW几何，但在$\sim2$–$4\sigma$水平上允许存在轻微至中等程度的偏差。若未来更密集的数据（如来自LSST、DESI、Euclid）证实这些偏差，则大多数基于FLRW假设的$\Lambda$CDM扩展模型（如演化暗能量、修正引力）将被排除。这凸显了改进并标准化非参数重构方法（尤其是符号回归的不确定性量化）的必要性，并强调了即将开展的高精度、高密度宇宙学巡天的重要性。

Abstract: The standard $Λ$CDM cosmological model faces increasing tensions between key observations, motivating tests that probe its underlying assumptions. In a companion letter, we present a model-independent framework that combines derivatives of the angular diameter distance, $d_A(z)$, and the line-of-sight expansion rate, $\mathcal{H}(z)$, to clarify the physical content of FLRW consistency relations and to construct a general-spacetime estimator of the cosmic density field. Here, we apply these tests to data, introducing a non-parametric reconstruction method based on symbolic regression combined with bootstrapping to provide data-driven uncertainty estimates. Using supernova and BAO data, we reconstruct $d_A$, $\mathcal{H}$, and their derivatives, enabling model-independent evaluation of FLRW relations and recovery of the sky-averaged density field over $z \in [0.38, \sim 2]$. Current data are too sparse to tightly constrain $\mathcal{H}(z)$, and the reconstructed density is consistent with both Planck and SH0ES $Λ$CDM. Reconstructed FLRW consistency tests show mild to moderate deviations from FLRW expectations at the $\sim 2$-$4σ$ level, although their significance depends on data selection and reconstruction stability.
  If these indicated deviations from an FLRW geometry are real, it would signify that most of the cosmological solutions considered for solving the cosmological tensions (evolving/interacting dark energy, new types of matter/energy, modified gravity, etc., within the FLRW framework) are ruled out. These preliminary indications highlight the importance of future, denser distance and expansion rate measurements, as well as further work toward standardizing uncertainty estimation for symbolic regression reconstructions.

### [76] [Forward analytical model for the optical selection bias on galaxy cluster lensing profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05833)
*M. Costanzi,H. Y. Wu,J. H. Esteves,S. Grandis,C. To,M. Aguena*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We present a predictive analytical model to quantify optical-selection biases in cluster catalogs due to line-of-sight projection effects, focusing on their impact on density profiles and two-halo contributions. The model uses a scale-dependent bias parametrization validated with simulations and applied to a DES Y3-like sample.

本文提出了一种可预测的解析模型，用于量化由于视线投影效应引起的光学选族目录中的选择偏差，重点关注其对密度轮廓和两晕成分的影响。该模型采用尺度依赖的偏置参数化方法，并通过模拟验证，应用于类似DES Y3的星系团样本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Optical cluster selections suffer from projection effects due to unresolved line-of-sight structures, leading to biased richness estimates and corrupted observables such as lensing signals and clustering statistics. A robust, predictive model is needed to link these selection biases directly to cosmology and survey design.

光学选族受制于未解析的视线方向结构引起的空间投影效应，导致丰度估计偏差以及弱引力透镜信号和成团性统计量的失真。需要一个稳健且具有预测能力的模型，将这些选择偏差直接与宇宙学和巡天设计联系起来。

Method: We introduce a scale-dependent optical cluster bias parametrization informed by the amplitude of projection effects. The two-halo term in the projected density profile is modeled analytically by accounting for contributions from off-axis halos along the line of sight. This forward model is tested against simulated DES Y3-like cluster samples.

我们引入了尺度依赖的光学星系团偏置参数化方案，其形式由投影效应的幅度决定。通过解析建模计入视线方向非中心晕（off-axis halos）的贡献来构建投影密度轮廓中的两晕项。该前向模型在类似DES Y3的模拟星系团样本上进行了测试。

Result: The model accurately captures the richness- and redshift-dependent behavior of the two-halo component, including enhancements due to richness boosts from projections. It reproduces the overall bias in the projected density profile relative to mass-matched random samples, validating its predictive power.

该模型准确捕捉了两晕成分随丰度和红移的变化行为，包括由投影引起的丰度增强效应。它重现了相对于质量匹配随机样本的投影密度轮廓的整体偏差，验证了其预测能力。

Conclusion: Our framework provides a consistent, analytical approach to modeling projection-induced selection biases in optically selected clusters, linking observed density profiles and richness to underlying cosmology and survey specifications through a physically motivated, scale-dependent bias model.

我们的框架提供了一种一致且解析的方法，用于建模光学选族中由投影引起的选择偏差，通过物理驱动的尺度依赖偏置模型，将观测到的密度轮廓和丰度与底层宇宙学及巡天参数联系起来。

Abstract: Cluster catalogs selected by optical properties are subject to selection biases, primarily arising from unresolved systems along the line of sight. These biases affect key observables for cluster cosmology, such as the lensing signal and clustering statistics. In this work, we present a fully predictive forward analytical model to quantify the impact of optical-selection bias due to projection effects on cluster density profiles. This is achieved by introducing a scale-dependent parametrization of the optical cluster bias, whose small- and large-scale behaviour is set by the amplitude of projection effects, and by expressing the two-halo component of the density profile in terms of the contributions from off-axis halos along the line of sight. As a case study, we consider a DES Y3-like cluster catalog and validate our model against simulated samples. Our model successfully captures the dependence of the two-halo component on richness boosts induced by projections, as well as its evolution with richness and redshift. It also recovers the overall bias in the projected density profile relative to a randomly selected sample with the same mass distribution. The framework presented here provides a consistent methodology for modeling the impact of line-of-sight structures on the observed richness and density profiles of optically selected clusters, directly linking selection biases to the underlying cosmology and survey specifications.

### [77] [Diagnostic Consistency Tests of the Concordance Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05836)
*S. M. Koksbang,A. Heinesen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We propose a model-independent framework to test the validity of the FLRW metric on large scales by combining derivatives of the angular diameter distance $d_A(z)$ and the expansion rate $\mathcal{H}(z)$, bypassing assumptions about dark energy or gravity. A new nonparametric estimator for the cosmic density field is also derived, enabling direct, observational tests of the foundational geometry of $\Lambda$CDM.

我们提出了一种模型无关的框架，通过结合角直径距离$d_A(z)$的导数与视线方向膨胀率$\mathcal{H}(z)$来检验大尺度上FLRW度规的有效性，避免了对暗能量或引力理论的假设。同时推导出一个新的非参数宇宙密度场估计量，使得可以直接通过观测检验$\Lambda$CDM模型的基础几何假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The $\Lambda$CDM model faces growing tensions between different cosmological observations, suggesting potential cracks in its core assumptions—particularly the use of a single FLRW metric to describe the universe's large-scale geometry. While dark energy and modifications to General Relativity are widely studied, the assumption of global FLRW symmetry remains less tested. This work aims to develop robust, model-independent tools to probe whether the standard geometric framework itself may be breaking down.

$\Lambda$CDM模型面临不同宇宙学观测之间的日益显著的张力，暗示其核心假设——特别是使用单一FLRW度规描述宇宙大尺度几何——可能存在缺陷。尽管暗能量和广义相对论修正已被广泛研究，但全局FLRW对称性的假设却较少被检验。本工作旨在发展稳健且模型无关的工具，以探测标准几何框架本身是否可能失效。

Method: We reformulate well-known FLRW consistency conditions (e.g., $\mathcal{H}(z) = d_A'(z)^{-1}$) into a hierarchy of model-independent differential relations involving higher-order derivatives of $d_A(z)$ and $\mathcal{H}(z)$. These are combined into a diagnostic function $\Omega_K^{\rm eff}(z)$ that vanishes if the FLRW assumption holds. We further construct a nonparametric estimator for the cosmic density contrast $\delta(z)$ directly from $d_A(z)$ and $\mathcal{H}(z)$, without invoking the Friedmann equations, enabling reconstruction of the density field independent of dynamical assumptions.

我们将已知的FLRW一致性条件（例如$\mathcal{H}(z) = d_A'(z)^{-1}$）重构为涉及$d_A(z)$和$\mathcal{H}(z)$高阶导数的模型无关微分关系层级，并组合成一个诊断函数$\Omega_K^{\rm eff}(z)$，当FLRW假设成立时该函数为零。进一步地，我们构建了一个从$d_A(z)$和$\mathcal{H}(z)$直接得到的宇宙密度对比$\delta(z)$的非参数估计量，无需使用Friedmann方程，从而实现不依赖动力学假设的密度场重建。

Result: The framework enables direct, observational tests of the FLRW geometry using current and future data (e.g., from BAO, SNIa, cosmic chronometers). The diagnostic $\Omega_K^{\rm eff}(z)$ provides a null test: any significant deviation from zero would indicate a breakdown of the FLRW metric. The nonparametric density estimator allows reconstruction of the growth of structure without assuming a specific form of dark energy or modified gravity, offering a new route to test homogeneity and isotropy.

该框架使得利用当前和未来的数据（如BAO、SNIa、宇宙计时器）直接进行FLRW几何的观测检验成为可能。诊断量$\Omega_K^{\rm eff}(z)$提供了一个零检验：任何显著偏离零的结果都表明FLRW度规失效。非参数密度估计量允许在不假设特定暗能量或修改引力形式的情况下重建结构增长，为检验均匀性和各向同性提供了新途径。

Conclusion: We present a novel, model-independent approach to test the fundamental geometric assumptions of $\Lambda$CDM. By decoupling geometry from dynamics, our method offers a powerful new class of consistency tests for the FLRW framework using existing cosmological probes, with the potential to identify systematics or new physics behind current cosmological tensions.

我们提出了一个新颖且模型无关的方法来检验$\Lambda$CDM模型的基本几何假设。通过将几何与动力学解耦，该方法利用现有的宇宙学探针为FLRW框架提供了一类强大的新型一致性检验，有望揭示当前宇宙学张力背后的系统误差或新物理。

Abstract: The $Λ$CDM cosmological model faces increasingly significant and robust tensions among independent cosmological probes, prompting renewed scrutiny of its foundational assumptions. While General Relativity and the nature of dark energy are now routinely tested with cosmological surveys, less progress has been made testing the space-time geometry at the largest scales, and in particular testing the assumption that observables (distances, redshifs, expansion of space, etc.) on the largest scales are described by a single Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) metric. In order to enable such tests, we introduce a model-independent framework that combines successive derivatives of the angular diameter distance, $d_A(z)$, with the line-of-sight expansion rate, $\mathcal{H}(z)$, to expose the physical content of well-known FLRW consistency relations. This allows us to perform diagnostic tests of the large-scale geometry, that are free of assumptions about dark energy and the theory of gravity on large scales. In addition, we derive a new nonparametric estimator for the cosmic density field that is independent of the Friedmann equations. This enables qualitatively new, observationally accessible tests of the FLRW framework and provides a stringent, model-independent diagnostic for departures from standard cosmology using current and forthcoming distance and expansion rate measurements.
