### [78] [Probing the Evolution of Dark Energy: A Joint Analysis of DESI DR2, Pantheon+, and Cosmic Chronometers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05849)
*Chanchal Kumari,Dinesh Kumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study explores dynamical dark energy models using a joint analysis of late-time cosmological data, including $H(z)$, BAO, and Pantheon+ SN Ia. Results indicate a better fit for time-varying dark energy compared to $\Lambda$CDM, with present-day equation-of-state $w_0 < -1$ and negative evolution parameter $w_a$, though uncertainties remain large. Information criteria favor simple one-parameter extensions, suggesting mild evidence for evolving dark energy.

该研究使用晚期宇宙学观测数据联合分析探讨了动力学暗能量模型，包括$H(z)$、BAO和Pantheon+超新星数据。结果表明，与$\Lambda$CDM相比，时变暗能量模型拟合更优，当前状态方程参数$w_0 < -1$，演化参数$w_a$为负，但误差仍较大。信息准则支持最简一参数扩展模型，暗示对暗能量演化的微弱偏好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To test whether dark energy is truly a cosmological constant ($\Lambda$) or exhibits time evolution, which has profound implications for fundamental physics and cosmic acceleration. The $\Lambda$CDM model, while successful, faces tensions (e.g., $H_0$, $S_8$), motivating exploration of dynamical dark energy alternatives.

为了检验暗能量是否真的是宇宙学常数($\Lambda$)，或是否存在时间演化，这对基础物理和宇宙加速膨胀具有深远意义。尽管$\Lambda$CDM模型成功，但仍面临一些张力（如$H_0$、$S_8$），因此有必要探索动力学暗能量的替代方案。

Method: A joint likelihood analysis of late-time cosmological probes: cosmic-chromatometer $H(z)$ measurements, DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) data, and the Pantheon+ Type Ia supernova (SN Ia) compilation. Several phenomenological dark energy equation-of-state parameterizations (e.g., $w(z) = w_0 + w_a z/(1+z)$) are tested against $\Lambda$CDM. Bayesian inference and information criteria (e.g., AIC, BIC) are used for model comparison and selection.

结合晚期宇宙学探针进行联合似然分析：宇宙色度计$H(z)$测量、DESI DR2重子声学振荡(BAO)数据和Pantheon+ Ia型超新星(SN Ia)样本。测试多种现象学暗能量状态方程参数化形式（如$w(z) = w_0 + w_a z/(1+z)$）并与$\Lambda$CDM对比。采用贝叶斯推断和信息准则（如AIC、BIC）进行模型比较与选择。

Result: Dynamical dark energy models provide a significantly improved fit to the data compared to $\Lambda$CDM. The present-day equation-of-state parameter is constrained to $w_0 < -1$ (phantom-like), while the redshift evolution parameter $w_a$ is negative, supporting a time-evolving dark energy density. However, statistical significance remains moderate, and current data cannot discriminate between different functional forms of $w(z)$. Model selection favors a simple one-parameter extension over more complex models.

相比$\Lambda$CDM，动力学暗能量模型显著改善了数据拟合。当前状态方程参数被限制为$w_0 < -1$（类幽灵型），红移演化参数$w_a$为负，支持暗能量密度随时间演化。然而统计显著性仍较弱，当前数据无法区分不同的$w(z)$函数形式。模型选择倾向于最简单的一参数扩展模型。

Conclusion: There is a mild but consistent preference for dynamical dark energy over the standard $\Lambda$CDM model based on current late-time observations. While not definitive, the results suggest that dark energy may evolve with time, motivating further theoretical and observational efforts. Future high-precision surveys (e.g., LSST, Euclid) will be crucial in confirming or ruling out such evolution.

基于当前晚期观测，存在对动力学暗能量相对于标准$\Lambda$CDM模型的微弱但一致的偏好。尽管结论尚不明确，结果提示暗能量可能随时间演化，激励进一步的理论与观测研究。未来的高精度巡天（如LSST、Euclid）将在确认或排除此类演化中起关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate several phenomenological dark energy parameterizations using a joint analysis of late-time cosmological observations, including cosmic-chromatometer measurements of the Hubble parameter, DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation data, and the Pantheon+ Type Ia supernova sample. Our results show that allowing for a time-varying dark energy equation of state significantly improves the overall fit compared to $Λ$CDM. The present-day equation-of-state parameter departs from the standard cosmological constant value. In contrast, the evolution parameter in two-parameter models tends to be negative, indicating a possible time dependence of dark energy. However, the constraints on the evolution remain moderate, and current data cannot clearly distinguish the specific functional form of dark energy. Model comparison using information criteria suggests that dynamical dark energy models are favored over $Λ$CDM, with the most straightforward one-parameter extension emerging as the most parsimonious scenario. These findings indicate a mild preference for dark energy evolution, though future high-precision observations will be required for definitive conclusions.

### [79] [Testing parity with composite-field spectra of BOSS and DESI luminous red galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06021)
*Zucheng Gao,Marina S. Cagliari,Azadeh Moradinezhad Dizgah,Zvonimir Vlah*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We present the first measurement of parity-odd kurtospectra $\mathcal{P}_{2\times2}$ and $\mathcal{P}_{3\times1}$ in galaxy survey data from BOSS DR12 and DESI DR1, finding no evidence for cosmological parity violation. The kurtospectrum formalism enables efficient compression of the trispectrum, reducing dimensionality and covariance-related systematics, with future DESI data promising sharper tests.

我们首次测量了来自BOSS DR12和DESI DR1星系巡天数据中的奇偶性破缺kurtospectrum $\mathcal{P}_{2\times2}$ 和 $\mathcal{P}_{3\times1}$，未发现宇宙学尺度上宇称破缺的证据。Kurtospectrum方法实现了对trispectrum的有效压缩，降低了数据维度并减少了协方差建模系统误差，未来DESI数据将提供更精确的检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Parity violation on cosmological scales would signal new physics beyond General Relativity and the Standard Model. Recent detections of parity-odd four-point correlation functions in galaxy surveys motivate a complementary analysis using kurtospectra, which offer improved statistical robustness and reduced sensitivity to covariance modelling. We aim to test for scalar- and vector-sector parity violation using spectroscopic data from BOSS and DESI.

宇宙学尺度上的宇称破缺将揭示超出广义相对论和标准模型的新物理。近期星系巡天中观测到的奇偶性破缺四点关联函数促使我们采用kurtospectrum这一互补方法，其具备更强的统计稳健性和更低的协方差建模敏感性。我们旨在利用BOSS和DESI的光谱数据检验标量与矢量 sector 的宇称破缺。

Method: We measure two parity-odd kurtospectra: $\mathcal{P}_{2\times2}$ (vector--pseudo-vector) and $\mathcal{P}_{3\times1}$ (scalar--pseudo-scalar), using composite-field estimators in Fourier space. The formalism compresses the full trispectrum into a lower-dimensional data vector, enabling direct covariance estimation from mock catalogues (e.g., Quick Particle Mesh and Outer Rim). We perform null-hypothesis $\chi^2$ tests and cross-patch consistency checks to assess significance, and compare results across high-fidelity and approximate mocks.

我们在傅里叶空间中使用复合场估计器测量两个奇偶性破缺kurtospectrum：$\mathcal{P}_{2\times2}$（矢量-赝矢量）和 $\mathcal{P}_{3\times1}$（标量-赝标量）。该方法将完整的trispectrum压缩为低维数据向量，从而可直接从模拟目录（如Quick Particle Mesh和Outer Rim）估计协方差矩阵。我们进行零假设$\chi^2$检验和跨区域一致性检查以评估显著性，并比较高保真与近似模拟目录的结果差异。

Result: No statistically significant detection of parity violation is found in either BOSS DR12 or DESI DR1 for both $\mathcal{P}_{2\times2}$ and $\mathcal{P}_{3\times1}$. Null-hypothesis $\chi^2$ tests show consistency with no signal. Cross-patch analyses confirm internal consistency. High-fidelity mocks match data better than approximate ones. DESI DR1 shows ~4× smaller scatter than BOSS DR12, consistent with higher tracer density and improved statistical precision.

在BOSS DR12和DESI DR1中均未发现$\mathcal{P}_{2\times2}$和$\mathcal{P}_{3\times1}$的显著宇称破缺信号。零假设$\chi^2$检验表明结果与无信号一致。跨区域分析验证了内部一致性。高保真模拟比近似模拟更好地匹配观测数据。DESI DR1的散射比BOSS DR12小约4倍，符合理论预期的更高示踪粒子密度带来的统计精度提升。

Conclusion: The kurtospectrum is a powerful tool for testing parity violation in large-scale structure, offering reduced dimensionality and robust covariance estimation. This first application to data shows no evidence for cosmological parity violation in BOSS or DESI. Future DESI data releases, with larger volume and number density, combined with high-fidelity mocks, will enable more sensitive searches using this formalism.

Kurtospectrum是检验大尺度结构中宇称破缺的有力工具，具有低维度和稳健协方差估计的优势。本次首次数据应用在BOSS和DESI中均未发现宇称破缺证据。未来的DESI数据发布，结合更大体积、更高示踪密度及高保真模拟，将能以该形式化方法实现更灵敏的探测。

Abstract: Detection of parity violation on cosmological scales would have profound implications for fundamental physics. Motivated in part by recent measurements of parity-odd four-point correlation functions in BOSS and DESI luminous red galaxy samples, which probe parity violation in the scalar sector, we present the first measurement of parity-odd kurto spectra in spectroscopic galaxy survey data. We analyse two composite-field spectra, $\mathcal{P}_{2\times2}$ (vector--pseudo-vector) and $\mathcal{P}_{3\times1}$ (scalar--pseudo-scalar). Compared with parity-odd four-point correlation function analyses, the kurto-spectrum formalism performs physically motivated compression on the trispectrum into a substantially lower-dimensional data vector, allowing direct estimation of covariance matrices from mock catalogues and reducing sensitivity to covariance-modelling systematics. Using null-hypothesis $χ^2$ tests and cross-patch consistency checks, we find no evidence for a cosmological parity-violating signal in either survey. We examine the impact of the adopted mock catalogues and find that the high-fidelity mocks provide a better match to the data of both surveys than the approximate mocks. The DESI DR1 measurements exhibit a scatter smaller than that of BOSS DR12 by about a factor of four, consistent with the improved statistical precision expected from the higher tracer number density. Future DESI data releases, with larger volume and number density, together with larger suites of high-fidelity mocks, can enable significantly sharper tests of parity violation using kurto spectra.

### [80] [Lyman-$α$ Forest Signatures of Mixed Fuzzy and Cold Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06038)
*Yourong Frank Wang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study examines Lyman-alpha forest flux statistics in mixed fuzzy dark matter (FDM) and cold dark matter (CDM) models using the Fluctuating Gunn-Peterson Approximation (FGPA) on hybrid Schrödinger-Poisson and N-body simulations. Despite similar nonlinear matter power spectra, the Ly α flux power differs by ~10% on intermediate scales due to suppressed small-scale velocity power in wave-mechanical FDM evolution, which N-body methods fail to capture. This shows that flux statistics depend on velocity field dynamics, not just the matter power spectrum, revealing unique kinematic imprints from FDM. Although based on an idealized FGPA framework, the results suggest that Ly α observables can break degeneracies in structure-based probes of mixed dark matter models.

该研究使用涨落耿-彼得森近似（FGPA）结合薛定谔-泊松与N体模拟，检验了混合模糊暗物质（FDM）和冷暗物质（CDM）模型中的莱曼α森林通量统计。尽管非线性物质功率谱高度简并，但由于波动力学FDM演化中小尺度速度功率被强烈抑制（N体方法无法捕捉），莱曼α通量功率谱在中间尺度上仍相差约10%。这表明通量统计不仅依赖于物质功率谱，还对速度场的动力学演化极为敏感，揭示了FDM独特的运动学印记。虽然基于理想化的FGPA框架，但结果说明莱曼α观测可打破结构探针中混合暗物质模型的简并性，值得进一步用流体动力学模拟深入研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To determine whether mixed fuzzy dark matter (FDM) and cold dark matter (CDM) cosmologies leave distinguishable imprints on Lyman-alpha forest statistics, particularly in cases where standard matter power spectrum analyses show near-degeneracy. The work aims to explore whether wave-mechanical effects in FDM, such as those arising from the Schrödinger-Poisson system, produce unique kinematic signatures in the velocity field that impact observables beyond initial power suppression.

为了确定混合模糊暗物质（FDM）与冷暗物质（CDM）宇宙学是否在莱曼α森林统计中留下可区分的印记，特别是在标准物质功率谱分析显示近乎简并的情况下。本研究旨在探索FDM中的波动力学效应（如来自薛定谔-泊松系统的效应）是否会产生产生于初态抑制之外的独特运动学信号，并影响可观测量。


Method: We perform cosmological simulations of mixed FDM+CDM models with axion mass $m_{22} = 0.01$ and FDM fraction $f_A = 0.1$, evolving the dark matter distribution from $z = 120$ to $z = 2$. Two simulation approaches are compared using identical initial conditions: (1) a particle-only N-body method with matched initial transfer functions, and (2) a full wave-mechanical treatment via the Schrödinger-Poisson equations. The Fluctuating Gunn-Peterson Approximation (FGPA) is applied to compute the Ly α forest flux statistics. Differences in the flux power spectra and underlying velocity fields are analyzed to isolate the impact of wave-mechanical dynamics.

我们对具有轴子质量$m_{22} = 0.01$和FDM比例$f_A = 0.1$的混合FDM+CDM模型进行了宇宙学模拟，将暗物质分布从$z = 120$演化至$z = 2$。在相同初始条件下比较两种模拟方法：(1) 使用匹配初始转移函数的纯粒子N体方法；(2) 通过薛定谔-泊松方程进行完整的波动力学处理。应用涨落耿-彼得森近似（FGPA）计算莱曼α森林通量统计，并分析通量功率谱与底层速度场的差异，以分离波动力学效应的影响。

Result: Despite near-degeneracy in the nonlinear matter power spectrum between the two simulations, the resulting Ly α flux power spectra differ by approximately 10 percent on intermediate scales ($k \sim 1 - 10~h/\mathrm{Mpc}$). This discrepancy originates from a strong suppression of small-scale velocity power in the Schrödinger-Poisson evolution, which is absent in the N-body simulation with matched initial conditions. Consequently, the Ly α flux statistics are sensitive not only to the matter power spectrum but also to the dynamical evolution of the velocity field. This indicates that wave-mechanical effects in FDM introduce distinct kinematic imprints that are not captured by standard structure formation probes based solely on density statistics.

尽管两种模拟的非线性物质功率谱高度简并，但其莱曼α通量功率谱在中间尺度（$k \sim 1 - 10~h/\mathrm{Mpc}$）上仍相差约10%。这一差异源于薛定谔-泊松演化中小尺度速度功率的强烈抑制，而匹配初始条件的N体模拟中无此现象。因此，莱曼α通量统计不仅依赖物质功率谱，还对速度场的动力学演化敏感。这表明FDM中的波动力学效应引入了独特的运动学印记，无法被仅基于密度统计的标准结构形成探针所捕捉。

Conclusion: Wave-mechanical effects in fuzzy dark matter, particularly in mixed FDM+CDM scenarios, leave detectable kinematic imprints in Lyman-alpha forest observables that go beyond initial-condition-based power suppression. These imprints arise from the suppression of small-scale velocity dispersion in the Schrödinger-Poisson dynamics and cannot be modeled accurately by conventional N-body simulations with adjusted initial power. Therefore, Ly α flux statistics provide a complementary probe to break degeneracies in structure-based dark matter constraints. While the current analysis uses an idealized FGPA framework, it highlights the need for full hydrodynamical simulations to quantify these effects in realistic observational contexts.

模糊暗物质中的波动力学效应——尤其是在混合FDM+CDM情景下——会在莱曼α森林观测中留下可探测的运动学印记，超越仅由初态引起的功率抑制。这些印记源于薛定谔-泊松动力学中小尺度速度弥散的抑制，无法通过调整初始功率的传统N体模拟准确建模。因此，莱曼α通量统计为打破基于结构的暗物质限制中的简并性提供了补充探针。尽管当前分析采用理想化的FGPA框架，但它凸显了在未来研究中使用全流体动力学模拟以量化现实观测情境下此类效应的必要性。

Abstract: We investigate Lyman-alpha forest flux statistics in mixed fuzzy dark matter (FDM) and cold dark matter (CDM) cosmologies using the Fluctuating Gunn-Peterson Approximation (FGPA) applied to hybrid Schrödinger-Poisson and N-body simulations. We evolve the dark matter distribution from z = 120 to z = 2 for an axion mass ( m_22 = 0.01) and FDM fraction (f_A = 0.1), and compare two realizations with identical initial conditions: one evolved with a particle-only approximation and one with full wave--mechanical dynamics.
  We find that, despite near-degeneracy in the nonlinear matter power spectrum, the corresponding Ly α flux power spectra differ at the 10 percent level on intermediate scales. This discrepancy arises from a strong suppression of small-scale velocity power in the Schrödinger--Poisson evolution, which is not captured by N-body treatments with matched initial transfer functions. As a result, the flux statistics cannot be fully characterized by the matter power spectrum alone, but depend sensitively on the dynamical evolution of the velocity field. These results demonstrate that wave-mechanical effects in FDM leave distinct kinematic imprints in Ly α observables beyond those associated with initial-condition suppression. While our analysis is based on an idealized FGPA framework, it isolates a mechanism by which mixed dark matter models can break degeneracies present in standard structure-based probes, motivating further investigation with full hydrodynamical simulations.

</details>


### [81] [Hunting Dark Matter with the Einstein Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06082)
*A. J. Iovino,M. Maggiore,N. Muttoni,A. Riotto*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Primordial black holes (PBHs) that are too light to survive Hawking evaporation can still account for dark matter if they form in strongly clustered environments, leading to halo collapse into heavier black holes. This scenario predicts a detectable flat stochastic gravitational wave background via the Einstein Telescope.

原初黑洞（PBHs）若质量过轻会因霍金蒸发而消失，但如果它们在高度成团的环境中形成，则其对应晕可坍缩为更重的黑洞，从而构成全部暗物质。该模型预言平坦的随机引力波背景，可在爱因斯坦望远镜中被探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Light primordial black holes are typically ruled out as dark matter candidates due to complete evaporation via Hawking radiation. The paper explores an alternative scenario where strong initial clustering allows the formation of heavier black holes through halo collapse, reviving light PBHs as viable dark matter constituents.

轻的原初黑洞通常因霍金辐射完全蒸发而被排除为暗物质候选者。本文探索了一种替代情景：强初始成团性可通过晕坍缩形成更重的黑洞，从而使轻PBHs重新成为可行的暗物质成分。

Method: The authors consider a model in which light PBHs are formed with strong spatial clustering, such that their associated dark matter haloes undergo gravitational collapse into more massive black holes. They compute the resulting stochastic gravitational wave background from mergers and collapses in this scenario using standard cosmological perturbation theory and gravitational wave emission models.

作者考虑了一个轻PBHs具有强空间成团性的模型，使其相关暗物质晕发生引力坍缩形成更大质量的黑洞。他们利用标准宇宙学扰动理论和引力波辐射模型，计算了此情景下由并合与坍缩产生的随机引力波背景。

Result: The model predicts a flat (white-noise-like) stochastic gravitational wave background in the frequency range accessible to the Einstein Telescope ($\sim 1-1000\,\mathrm{Hz}$), arising from the superposition of numerous unresolved merger and collapse events. This signal is distinguishable from astrophysical backgrounds and provides a testable prediction for the scenario.

该模型预测在爱因斯坦望远镜可探测频段（$\sim 1-1000\,\mathrm{Hz}$）存在平坦（类似白噪声）的随机引力波背景，源于大量未解析的并合与坍缩事件叠加。该信号可与天体物理背景区分，并为此情景提供了可检验的预言。

Conclusion: Strongly clustered light primordial black holes can evade evaporation constraints and serve as the totality of dark matter, with the key observational signature being a detectable flat spectrum of stochastic gravitational waves, offering a new pathway to test early-universe black hole formation.

高度成团的轻原初黑洞可逃避蒸发限制，并构成全部暗物质，其关键观测特征是可探测的平坦随机引力波谱，为检验早期宇宙黑洞形成提供了新途径。

Abstract: Too light primordial black holes evaporate and are therefore strongly constrained by various bounds, e.g. Cosmic Microwave Background distortion. However, if they are formed strongly clustered, the corresponding haloes may collapse in heavier black holes which may form the entirety of the dark matter of the universe. The indirect signal of such scenario is the production of a flat stochastic background of gravitational waves which is detectable by the Einstein Telescope.

</details>
